evam īkṣitvā asau gauḥ abhavat  utpādya prāṇi karmabhiḥ codyamānāyāḥ punar  punar  sā eva matiḥ śatarūpāyāḥ  manoḥ ca abhavat  tatas ca ṛṣabha itaraḥ tām sameva ābhat ityādi pūrvavat  tatas  gāvaḥ  ajāyanta tathā baḍa vetarā bhavat aśva vṛṣa itaraḥ tathā gardabhī itarā gardabha itaraḥ tatra baḍavā aśva vṛṣa ādīnām saṅgamāt tata ekaśapham ekagvuram aśva aśvatara gardabha ākhyam trayam ajāyata tathā aja itarā abhavat vastaḥ chāga itaraḥ tathā aviritarā meṣa itaraḥ tām sameva abhavat tām tām iti vīpsā tām ajām tām aviñcetisamabhavat eva iti arthaḥ tatas  aja aśva avayaḥ ca aja  ayaḥ ajāyanta evam eva yad idam kiñca yad kiṃñca idam mithunam srīpuṃsa lakṣaṇam dvandam ā pipīlikābhyaḥ pipīlikābhiḥ saha anena eva nyāyena tad sarvam asṛjata jagat sṛṣṭavān sa prajāpatiḥ sarvam idam jagat sṛṣṭvā avet  katham aham vā āvāham eva sṛṣṭiḥ sṛjyate iti sṛṣṭam jagat ucyate sṛṣṭiḥ iti yad mayā sṛṣṭam jagat mada bheda tvāt aham eva asmi na mattaḥ  vyatiricyate kuta etad  aham hi yasmāt idam sarvam jagat asṛkṣi sṛṣṭavān asmi tasmāt iti arthaḥ yasmāt sṛṣṭi śabdena ātmānam eva abhyadhāt prajāpatiḥ tatas tasmāt sṛṣṭiḥ abhavat sṛṣṭi nāmā bhavat sṛṣṭyām jagati hāsya prajāpategetasyām etasmin jagati sa prajāpativat sraṣṭā bhavati sva ātmanaḥ  ananya bhūtasya jagataḥ kaḥ ya evam prajāpativat yathā uktam sva ātmanaḥ  ananya bhūtam jagat sādhya ātma ādi bhūta adhidaivam jagat aham asmi iti veda evam sa prajāpatiḥ jagat idam mithuna ātmakam sṛṣṭā brahmaṇā ādi varṇa niyanvardevatāḥ sisṛkṣuḥ ādau ayā iti śabda dvayam abhinaya pradarśana artham anena prakāreṇa mukhe hastau prakṣityā abhyamanyat ābhimukhyena manyana pakarot  sa mukha hastābhyām mathitvā mukhāt ca yoneḥ hastābhyām ca yonibhyām agnim brāhmaṇa jāteḥ anugraha kartāram asṛjata sṛṣṭavān yasmāt dāhakasya agneḥ yoniḥ etad ubhayam hastau mukham ca tasmāt bhaya mapi etad alomakam loma vivarjitam kim sarvam eva na antarataḥ  abhyantarataḥ asti hi yonyā sāmānyam ubhayasya asya kim alomakā hi yoniḥ antaratas  strīṇām tathā brāhmaṇaḥ  api mukhāt eva jajhe prajāpateḥ tasmāt eka yoni tvāt jayeṣṭhena iva anujaḥ  anugṛhyate agninā brāhmaṇaḥ tasmāt brāhmaṇaḥ  agni devatyaḥ  mukha vīryaḥ ca iti śruti smṛti siddham tathā bala āśrayābhyām bāhubhyām balabhid ādikam kṣanni yaja ati niyantarām kṣanniyam ca tasmāt aindram kṣatram bāhu vīryam ca iti śrutau smṛtau ca avagatam tathā ūruta īhā ceṣṭā tad āśrayāt vasu ādi lakṣaṇam viśaḥ niyantāram viśam ca tasmāt kṛṣi ādi paraḥ  vasu ādi devatyaḥ ca vaiśyaḥ tathā pūṣaṇam pṛthvī daivatam śūdram ca padbhyām paricaraṇa kṣamam asṛjata iti śruti smṛti prasiddheḥ tatra kṣatra ādi devatā sargam iha anuktam vakṣyamāṇamam api uktavat upasaṃharati sṛṣṭi sākalya anukīrtyai yathā iyam śrutiḥ vyavasthitā tathā prajāpatiḥ eva sarve devāḥ  iti niścitor athaḥ sraṣṭuḥ ananya tvāt sṛṣṭānām prajāpatinā eva tu sṛṣṭa tvāt  devānām atha evam prakaraṇa arthe vyavasthite tad stuti abhiprāyeṇa avidvat matā antara nindā upanyāsaḥ anya nindā ani astutaye tad tatra karma prakaraṇe kevala yājñikā yāga kāle yad idam vaca āhuḥ aamum agnim yajāsum indram yaja aityādi nāma śastra stotra karma ādi bhinna tvāt bhinnam eva agni ādidevam eva ekam manyamānā āhuḥ iti abhiprāyaḥ tad na tathā vidyāt  yasmāt etasya eva prajāpateḥ sā visṛṣṭiḥ deva bhedaḥ sarva eṣa u hi eva prajāpatiḥ eva prāṇaḥ sarve devāḥ atra vipratipadyante para eva hiraṇyagarbhe iti eke saṃsārī iti apare param eva tu mantra varṇāt  indram mitram varuṇam agnim āhuḥ iti śruteḥ eṣa brahma eṣa indra eṣa prajāpatiḥ ete sarve devāḥ iti ca śruteḥ smṛteḥ ca etam eke vadanti agnim manum anye prajāpatim iti yaḥ  asau  atīndriyaḥ  agrāhyaḥ sūkṣmaḥ  avyaktaḥ sanātanaḥ sarva bhūta m ayaḥ  acintyaḥ sa eva svayam udbabhau iti saṃsāri iva vā syāt  sarvain pāpmana aupat iti śruteḥ na hi asaṃsāriṇaḥ pāpma dāha prasaṅgaḥ  asti bhaya arati saṃyoga śravaṇāt  atha yad martyaḥ san  amṛtān asṛjata iti ca hiraṇyagarbham paśyati jāyamānam iti ca mantra varṇāt  smṛteḥ ca karma vipāka prakriyāyām brahmā viśvasṛjaḥ  dharmaḥ  mahān avyaktam eva ca uttamām sātvikīm etām gatim āhuḥ manīṣiṇaḥ iti atha evam viruddha artha anupapatteḥ prāmāṇya vyāghāta iti ced  na kalpanā antara upapatteḥ avirodhāt upādhi viśeṣa sambandhāt viśeṣa kalpanā antaram upapadyate āsīnaḥ  dūram vrajati śayānaḥ  yāti sarvatas  kaḥ tam madāmadam devam mad anyaḥ  jñātum arhati iti evamādi śrutibhya upādhi vaśāt saṃsāri tvam na paramārthataḥ svatas  asaṃsāri iva evam eka tvam nānā tvam ca hiraṇyagarbhasya tathā sarva jīvānām tad tvam asi iti śruteḥ hiraṇyagarbhaḥ tu upādhi śuddhi atiśaya apekṣayā prāyaśas  para eva iti śruti smṛti vādāḥ pravṛttāḥ saṃsāri tvam tu kvacid eva darśayanti jīvānām upādhi gata aśuddhi bāhulyāt saṃsāri tvam eva prāyaśas  abhilapyate vyāvṛtta kṛtsnā upādhi bheda apekṣayā tu sarvaḥ paratvena abhidhīyate śruti smṛti vādaiḥ tārkikaiḥ tu parityakta āgama balaiḥ asti na asti kartā akartā ityādi viruddham bahu tarka padbhiḥ ākulīkṛtaḥ śāstra arthaḥ tena artha niścayaḥ  durlabhaḥ ye tu kevala śāstra anusāriṇaḥ śānta darpāḥ teṣām pratyakṣa viṣaya iva niścitaḥ śāstra arthe devatā ādi viṣayaḥ tatra prajāpateḥ ekasya devasya atra ādya lakṣaṇaḥ  bhedaḥ  vivakṣita iti tatra agniḥ uktaḥ  attā ādyaḥ soma idānīm ucyate atha yad kiñca idam loka ārdram drava ātmakam tad retasa ātmānaḥ  bījāt asṛjata retasa āpaḥ iti śruteḥ drava ātmakaḥ ca somaḥ tasmāt yad ārdram prajāpatinā retasaḥ sṛṣṭam tad u soma eva etāvat vai etāvat eva na atas  adhikam idam sarvam kim tad  annam ca eva somaḥ  drava ātmaka tvāt āpyāyakam anna ādaḥ ca agniḥ auṣṇyāt  rūkṣa tvāt ca tatra evadhriyate soma eva annam yad adyate tad eva soma iti arthaḥ ya eva āttā sa eva agniḥ artha balāt hi avadhāraṇam agniḥ api kvacid  hūyamānaḥ soma pakṣasya eva somaḥ  api ijyamānaḥ  agniḥ eva āttṛ tvāt evam agnīṣoma ātmakam jagat ātma tvena paśyanta kenacid doṣeṇa lipyate prajāpatiḥ ca bhavati sā eṣā brahmaṇaḥ prajāpateḥ atisṛṣṭiḥ ātmanaḥ  api atiśayā kā sā iti āha yad śreyasaḥ praśasyatarān ātmanaḥ sakāśāt yasmāt asṛjata devān  tasmāt deva sṛṣṭiḥ atisṛṣṭiḥ katham punar ātmanaḥ  atiśayā sṛṣṭiḥ iti ata āha atha yadi asmāt martyaḥ sat maraṇa dharmā sannamṛtāna maraṇa dharmiṇaḥ  devān karma jñāna vahninā sarvān ātmanaḥ pāpmana oṣitvā asṛjata tasmāt etām ati sṛṣṭim prajāpateḥ ātma bhūtām yaḥ  veda sa etasyām ati sṛṣṭyām prajāpatiḥ iva bhavati prajāpativat eva sraṣṭā bhavati sarvam vaidikam sādhanam jñāna karma lakṣaṇam kartṛ ādi aneka kāraka apekṣam prajāpatitva phala avasānam sādhyam etāvat eva yad etad vyākṛtam jagat saṃsāraḥ atha etasya eva sādhya sādhana lakṣaṇasya vyākṛtasya jagataḥ  vyākaraṇāt prāc bīja avasthā yā tām nirdidijñati aṅkura ādi kārya anumitām iva vṛkṣasya karma bījaḥ  avidyā kṣetraḥ  hi asau saṃsāra vṛkṣaḥ sa mūla uddhartavya iti tad uddharaṇe hi puruṣa artha parisamāptiḥ tathā ca uktam ūrdhva mūlaḥ  avāc śākhaḥ iti kāṭhake gītāsu ca ūrdhva mūlam adhas  śākham iti purāṇe ca brahmavṛkṣaḥ sanātanaḥ iti tad vedam tad iti bīja avastham jagat prāk utpatteḥ tarhi tasmin kāle  parokṣatva asarva nāmnā pratyakṣa abhidhānena abhidhīyate bhūta kāla sambandhi tvāt avyākṛta bhāvinaḥ  jagataḥ  sukha grahaṇa artham aitihya prayogaḥ  ha śabdaḥ evam ha tadā āsīt iti ucyamāne sukham tām parokṣām api jagataḥ  bīja avasthām pratipadyate yudhiṣṭhiraḥ  ha kila rājā āsīt iti ukte yadvat  idam iti vyākṛta nāma rūpa ātmakam sādhya sādhana lakṣaṇam yathāvarṇitam abhidhīyate tad idaṃśabdayoḥ parokṣa pratyakṣa avastha jagat vācakayoḥ sāmānādhikaraṇyāt eka tvam eva parokṣa prata yakṣa avasthasya jagataḥ  avagamyate tad eva idam idam eva ca tad avyākṛtam āsīt iti atha evam sati na asata utpattiḥ na sataḥ  vināśaḥ kāryasya iti avadhṛtam bhavati tad evambhūtam jagat avyākṛtam sat nāma rūpābhyām eva nāmnā rūpeṇa eva ca vyākriyata vyākriyata iti karma kartṛ prayogāt tad svayam eva ātmā eva vyākriyata vi ā akriyata vispaṣṭam nāma rūpa viśeṣa avadhāraṇa maryādam vyaktībhāvam āpadyata sāmarthyāt ākṣipta niyantṛ kartṛ sādhana kriyā nimittam asaunāma iti sarva nāmnā viśeṣa abhidhānena nāma mātram vyapadiśati devadattaḥ  yajñadatta iti vā nāma asya iti asaunāmāyam tathā idam iti śukla kṛṣṇa ādīnām aviśeṣaḥ idam śuklam idam kṛṣṇam vā rūpam asya iti idam rūpaḥ tad idam avyākṛtam vastu etarhi etasmin  api kāle nāma rūpābhyām eva vyākriyate asaunāmāyam idam rūpa iti yad arthaḥ sarva śāstra ārambhaḥ yasmin  avidyayā svābhāvikyā kartṛ kriyā phala adhyāropaṇā kṛta ā yaḥ kāraṇam sarvasya jagataḥ yad ātmake nāma rūpe salilāt iva su acchān malam iva phenam avyākṛte vyākriyete yaḥ ca tābhyām nāma rūpābhyām vilakṣaṇaḥ svatas  nitya śuddha buddha mukta svabhāvaḥ sa eṣaḥ  avyākṛte ātma bhūte nāma rūpe vyākurvan brahma ādi stamba paryanteṣu deheṣu iha karma phala āśrayeṣu aśanāya ādimatsu praviṣṭaḥ nanu avyākṛtam svayam eva vyākriyata iti uktam katham idam idānīm ucyate para eva tu ātma avyākṛtam vyākurvan  iha praviṣṭa iti na eṣa doṣaḥ parasya api ātmanaḥ  avyākṛta jagat ātma tvena vivakṣita tvāt  ākṣipta niyantṛ kartṛ kriyā nimittam hi jagat avyākṛtam vyākriyata iti avocāma idaṃśabda sāmānā adhikaraṇyāt ca avyākṛta śabdasya yathā idam jagat niyantra ādi aneka kāraka nimitta ādi viśeṣavat vyākṛtam tathā aparityakta anyatama viśeṣavat eva tad avyākṛtam vyākṛta avyākṛta mātram tu viśeṣaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ ca loke vivakṣātaḥ śabda prayogaḥ  grāma āgataḥ  grāmaḥ śūnya iti kadācid  grāma śabdena nivāsa mātra vivakṣāyām grāmaḥ śūnya iti śabda prayogaḥ  bhavati kadācid nivāsi jana vivakṣāyām grāma āgata iti kadācid ubhaya vivakṣāyām api grāma śabda prayogaḥ  bhavati grāmam ca na praviśet iti yathā tadvat iha api jagat idam vyākṛtam avyākṛtam ca iti abheda vivakṣāyām ātmānātmanoḥ bhavati vyapadeśaḥ tathā idam jagat utpatti vināśa ātmakam iti kevala jaga t vayapadeśaḥ tathā mahān aja ātmā asthūlaḥ  anaṇuḥ sa eṣa na iti na iti ityādi kevala ātma vyapadeśaḥ nanu pareṇa vyākartrā vyākṛtam sarvatas  vyāptam sarvadā jagat  sa katham iha praviṣṭaḥ parikalpyate apraviṣṭaḥ  hi deśaḥ paricchinnena praveṣṭum śakyate yathā puruṣeṇa grāma ādiḥ na ākāśena kiñcid nitya praviṣṭa tvāt pāṣāṇa sarpa ādivat dharma antareṇa iti ced  atha api syāt  na para ātmā svena eva rūpeṇa praviveśa kim tarhi tad stha eva dharma antareṇa upajāyate tena praviṣṭa iti upacaryate yathā pāṣāṇe sahajaḥ  antaḥsthaḥ sarpaḥ  nālikere vā toyam na tad sṛṣṭvā tad eva anuprāviśat iti śruteḥ yaḥ sraṣṭā sa bhāva antaram anāpanna eva kāryam sṛṣṭvā paścāt prāviśat iti hi śrūyate yathā bhuktvā gacchati iti bhujigami kriyayoḥ pūrva apara kālayoḥ itaretara vicchedaḥ  aviśiṣṭaḥ ca kartā tadvat iha api syāt  na tu tad sthasya eva bhāva antara upajanana etad sambhavati na ca sthāna antareṇa viyujya sthāna antara saṃyoga lakṣaṇaḥ praveśaḥ  niravayavasya aparicchinnasya dṛṣṭaḥ sāvayava eva praveśa śravaṇāt iti ced  na ṭha divyaḥ  hi amūrtaḥ puruṣaḥ niṣkalam niṣkriyam ityādi śrutibhyaḥ sarva vyapadeśya dharma viśeṣa pratiṣedha śrutibhyaḥ ca pratibimba praveśavat iti ced  na vastu antareṇa viprakarṣa anupapatteḥ dravye guṇa praveśavat iti ced  na anāśrita tvāt  nitya paratantrasya eva āśritasya guṇasya dravye praveśa upacaryate na tu brahmaṇaḥ svātantrya śravaṇāt tathā praveśa upapadyate phale bījavat iti ced  na sā avayavatva vṛddhi kṣaya utpatti vināśa ādi dharmavattva prasaṅgāt  na ca evam dharmavat tvam brahmaṇaḥ ajaḥ ajaraḥ ityādi śruti nyāya virodhāt  tasmāt anya eva saṃsārī paricchinna iha praviṣṭa iti ced  na  sā iyam daivatā aikṣata iti ārabhya ṭanāma rūpe vyākaravāṇi iti tasyāḥ  eva praveśa vyākaraṇa kartṛtva śruteḥ tathā atat sṛṣṭvā tad eva anuprāviśat asa etam eva sīmānam vidārya etayā dvārā prāpadyata asarvāṇi rūpāṇi vicitya dhīraḥ  nāmāni kṛtvā abhivadan yad āste tvam kumāra uta vā kumārī tvam jīrṇaḥ  daṇḍena vañcasi puras cakre dvipadaḥ rūpam rūpam iti ta mantra varṇān na parādanyasya praveśaḥ praviṣṭānām itaretara bhedāt parān ekatvam iti ced  na ekaḥ  devaḥ  bahudhā sanniviṣṭaḥ ekaḥ san bahudhā vicacāra tvam ekaḥ asi bahūn anupraviṣṭaḥ ekaḥ  devaḥ sarva bhūteṣu gūḍhaḥ sarva vyāpī sarva bhūta antarātmā ityādi śrutibhyaḥ praveśa upapadyate na upapadyata iti tiṣṭhatu tāvat  praviṣṭānām saṃsāri tvāt tad ananya tvāt na parasya saṃsāri tvam iti ced  na aśanāya ādi atyaya śruteḥ sukhitva duḥkhi tvā ādi darśanāt na iti ced na na lipyate loka duḥkhena bāhyaḥ iti śruteḥ pratyakṣa ādi virodhāt ayuktam iti ced  na upādhi āśraya janita viśeṣa viṣaya tvāt prakṣa ādeḥ na dṛṣṭeḥ draṣṭāram paśyeḥ vijñāta āram are kena vijānīyāt  avijñātam vijñātṛ ityādi śrutibhyaḥ  na ātma viṣayam vijñānam kim tarhi buddhi ādi upādhi ātma praticchāyā viṣayam eva sukhitaḥ  aham duḥkhitaḥ  aham iti evamādi pratyakṣa vijñānam ayam aham iti viṣayeṇa viṣayiṇaḥ sāmāna adhikaraṇya upacārāt na anyat atas  asti draṣṭrṛ iti anya ātma pratiṣedhāt ca deha avayava viśeṣya tvāt ca sukha duḥkhayoḥ viṣaya dharma tvam ātmānaḥ tu kāmāya iti ātma arthaḥ tu aśruteḥ yukta iti ced na yatra vā anyat iva syāt  iti avidyā viṣaya ātma arthatva abhyupagamāt tad kena kam paśyet  na iha nānā asti kiñcana tatra kaḥ  mohaḥ kaḥ śokaḥ eka tvam anupaśyataḥ ityādinā vidyā viṣaye tad pratiṣedhāt ca na ātma dharma tvam tārkika samaya virodhāt ayuktam iti ced  na  yuktyā api ātmanaḥ  duḥkhitvā anupapatteḥ na hi duḥkhena pratyakṣa viṣayeṇa ātmanaḥ  viśeṣya tvam pratyakṣa aviṣaya tvāt ākāśasya śabda guṇavat tvavat ātmanaḥ  duḥkhi tvam iti ced na eka pratyaya viṣayatva anupapatteḥ na hi sukha grāhakeṇa pratyakṣa viṣayeṇa pratyayena nitya anumeyasya ātmanaḥ  viṣayīkaraṇām upapadyate tasya ca viṣayīkaraṇe ātmana eka tvāt viṣayya bhāva prasaṅgaḥ ekasya eva viṣaya viṣayi tvam dīpavat iti ced  na  yuga pada sambhavātātmani aṃśa anupapatteḥ ca etena vijñānasya grāhya grāhaka tvam pratyuktam pratyakṣa anumāna viṣayayoḥ ca duḥkha ātmanoḥ guṇa guṇi tve na anumānam duḥkhasya nityam eva pratyakṣa viṣaya tvāt  rūpa ādi sāmāna adhikaraṇyāt ca manaḥ saṃyoga ja tve api ātmani duḥkhasya sāvayavatva vikriyāvattva anityatva prasaṅgāt  na hi avikṛtya saṃyogi dravyam guṇaḥ kaścid upayannapayan vā dṛṣṭaḥ kvacid  na ca niravayavam vikriyamāṇam dṛṣṭam kvacid anitya guṇa āśrayam vā nityam na ca ākāśa āgama vādibhiḥ nityatayā abhyupagamyate na ca anyaḥ  dṛṣṭāntaḥ  asti vikriyamāṇam api tad pratyaya anivṛtteḥ nityam eva iti ced  na dravyasya avayavān yathātva vyatirekeṇa vikriyā anupapatteḥ sāvayava tve api nitya tvam iti ced na sā avayavasya avayava saṃyoga pūrvaka tve sati vibhāga upapatteḥ vajra ādiṣu adarśanāt na iti ced na anumeya tvāt saṃyoga pūrva tvasya tasmāt na ātmānaḥ  duḥkha ādi nitya guṇa āśrayatva upapattiḥ parasya aduḥkhi tve anyasya ca duḥkhinaḥ  abhāve duḥkha upaśamanāya śāstra ārambhānarthakyam iti ced  na avidyā adhyāropita duḥkhitva bhrama apoha artha tvāt ātmani prakṛta saṅkhyā pūraṇa bhrama apohavat kalpita duḥkhya ātma abhyupagamāt ca jala sūrya ādi pratibimbavat ātma gra va īśaḥ ca pratibimbavat vyākṛte kārya upalabhya tvāt  prāk utpatteḥ anupalabdha ātmā paścāt kārye ca sṛṣṭa vyākṛte buddheḥ antar upalabhyamānaḥ sūrya ādi pratibimbavat jala ādau kāryam sṛṣṭvā praviṣṭa iva lakṣyamāṇaḥ  nirdiśyate sa eṣa iha praviṣṭaḥ tāḥ sṛṣṭvā tad eva anuprāviśata sa etam eva sīmānam vidārya etayā dvārā prāpadyata sā iyam devatā aikṣata hanta aham imāḥ tisraḥ  devatā anena jīvena ātmanā anupraviśya iti evamādibhiḥ na tu sarva gatasya niravayavasya diś deśa kāla antara apakramaṇa prāpti lakṣaṇaḥ praveśaḥ kadācid api upapadyate na ca parāda ātmanaḥ  anyaḥ  asti draṣṭā na anyat atas  asti draṣṭṛ na anyat atas  asti śrotṛ ityādi śruteḥ iti avocāma upalabdhi artha tvāt ca sṛṣṭi praveśa sthiti apyaya vākyānām upalabdheḥ puruṣa arthatva śravaṇāt ātmānam eva avet tasmāt tad sarvam abhavat bahma vid āpnoti param sa yaḥ  ha vai tad paramam brahma veda brahmā eva bhavati ācāryavān puruṣaḥ  veda tasya tāvat eva ciram ityādi śrutibhyaḥ tatas  mām tattvataḥ  jñātvā viśate tad anantaram tad hi agryam sarva vidyānām prāpyate hi amṛtam tatas  ityādi smṛtibhyaḥ ca bheda darśana apavādāt ca sṛṣṭi ādi vākyānām ātmā ekatva darśana artha paratva upapattiḥ tasmāt kārya sthasya upalabhya tvam eva praveśa iti upacaryate ānakha agrebhyaḥ  nakha agra maryādam ātmanaḥ caitanyam upalabhyate tatra katham iva praviṣṭaḥ iti āha yathā loke kṣura ādhāne kṣuraḥ  dhīyate asmin  iti kṣura dhānam tasmin   āpita upaskara ādhāne kṣuraḥ  antaḥstha upalabhyate avahitaḥ praveśitaḥ syāt  yathā vā viśvambharaḥ  agniḥ viśvasya bharaṇāt viśvambharaḥ kulāye nīḍe agniḥ kāṣṭhāda  ahitaḥ syāt iti anuvartate tatra hi sa mathyamāna upalabhyate yathā ca kṣuraḥ kṣura dhāna eka deśe avasthitaḥ  yathā ca agniḥ kāṣṭha ādau sarvatas  vyāpya avasthitaḥ evam sāmānyatas  viśeṣataḥ ca deham saṃvyāpya avasthita ātmā tatra hi sa prāṇana ādi kriyāvān darśana ādi kriyāvān  ca upalabhyate tasmāt tatra evam praviṣṭham tam ātmānam prāṇana ādi kriyā viśiṣṭam na paśyanti na upalabhante nanu aprāpta pratiṣedhaḥ  ayam tam na paśyanti iti darśanasya aprakṛta tvāt  na eṣa doṣaḥ sṛṣṭi ādi vākyānām ātmā ekatva pratipatti artha para tvāt prakṛtam eva tasya darśanam rūpam rūpam pratirūpaḥ  babhūva tad asya rūpam prati cakṣaṇāya iti mantra varṇāt  tatra prāṇana ādi kriyā viśiṣṭasya adarśane hetum āha akṛtsnaḥ  asamastaḥ  hi yasmāt sa prāṇana ādi kriyā viśiṣṭaḥ kutas  punar akṛtsna tvam iti ucyate prāṇān na iva prāṇana kriyām eva kurvan prāṇaḥ  nāma prāṇa samākhyaḥ prāṇa abhidhānaḥ  bhavati prāṇana kriyā kartṛ tvāt hi prāṇaḥ prāṇatī iti ucyate na anyām kriyām kurvan yathā lāvakaḥ pācaka iti tasmāt kriyā antara viśiṣṭasya anupasaṃhārāt akṛtsnaḥ  hi saḥ tathā vadan vadana kriyām kurvan vakti iti vāc  paśyan  cakṣuḥ caṣṭa iti cakṣuḥ draṣṭā śṛṇvan śṛṇoti iti śrotram prāṇān na iva prāṇaḥ vadan vāc  iti ābhyām kriyāśakti udbhavaḥ pradarśitaḥ  bhavati paśyan  cakṣuḥ śṛṇvan śrotram iti ābhyām vijñāna śakti udbhavaḥ pradarśyate nāma rūpa viṣaya tvāt vijñāna śakteḥ śrotra cakṣuṣī vijñānasya sādhane vijñānam tu nāma rūpa sādhanam na hi nāma rūpa vyatiriktam vijñeyam asti tayoḥ ca upalambhe karaṇam cakṣuḥ śrotre kriyā ca nāma rūpa sādhyā prāṇa samavāyinī tasyāḥ prāṇa āśrayāyā abhivyaktaḥ  vākkaraṇam tathā pāṇi pāda pāyu upaśtha ākhyāni sarveṣām upalakṣaṇa arthā vāc  etad eva hi sarvam vyākṛtam trayam vā idam nāma rūpam karma iti hi vakṣyati manvānaḥ  manaḥ  manuta iti jñāna śakti vikāsānām sādhāraṇam karaṇam manaḥ  manute anena iti puruṣaḥ tu kartā sat manvānaḥ  mana iti ucyate tāni etāni prāṇa ādīn i asya ātmanaḥ karma nāmāni karma jāni nāmāni karma nāmāni eva na tu vastu mātra viṣayāṇi atas  na kṛtsnā ātmavastu avadyotakāni evam hi asau  ātmā prāṇana ādi kriyayā tad tad kriyā janita prāṇa ādi nāma rūpābhyām vyākriyamāṇaḥ  avadyotyamānaḥ  api sa yaḥ  atas  asmāt prāṇana ādi kriyā samudāyāt  ekaikam prāṇam cakṣuḥ iti vā viśiṣṭam anupasaṃhṛta itara viśiṣṭa kriyā ātmakam manasā ayam ātmā iti upāste cintayati na sa veda nasa jānāti brahma kasmāt  akṛtsnaḥ  asamāptaḥ  hi yasmāt eṣa ātmā asmāt prāṇana ādi samudāyāt atas  pravibhakta ekaikena viśeṣaṇena viśiṣṭa itara dharma antara anupasaṃhārāt bhavati yāvat ayam evam veda paśyati śṛṇomi spṛśāmi iti vā svabhāva pravṛtti viśiṣṭam veda tāvat añjasā kṛtsnam ātmānam na veda katham punar  paśyan veda iti āha ātmā iti eva ātmā iti prāṇa ādīni viśeṣaṇāni yāni uktāni tāni yasya sa āpnuvan  tāni ātmā iti ucyate na tathā kṛtsna viśeṣola saṃhārī sankṛtsnaḥ  bhavati vastu mātra rūpeṇa hi prāṇa ādi upādhi viśeṣa kriyā janitāni viśeṣaṇāni vyāpnoti tathā ca vakṣyati dhyāyati iva lelāyati iva iti tasmāt ātmā iti eva upāsīta evam kṛtsnaḥ  hi asau svena vastu rūpeṇa gṛhyamāṇaḥ  bhavati kasmāt kṛtsnaḥ iti āśaṅkya āha atra asmin  ātmani hi yasmāt nirupādhika jala sūrya pratibimba bhedā iva ādi tve prāṇa ādi upādhi kṛtā viśeṣāḥ prāṇa ādikarma janāma abhidheyā yadyā uktā hi ete ekam abhinnatām bhavanti pratipadyante ātmā iti eva upāsīta iti na apūrva vidhiḥ pakṣe prāpta tvāt  yad sākṣāt aparokṣāt brahma katama ātmā iti yaḥ  ayam vijñāna mayaḥ iti evamādi ātma pratipādana parābhiḥ śrutibhiḥ ātma viṣayam vijñānam utpāditam tatra ātma svarūpa vijñānena eva tad viṣayān ātma abhimāna buddhiḥ kāraka ādi kriyā phala adhyāropaṇa ātmikā avidyā nivartitā tasyām nivartitāyām kāma ādi doṣa anupapatteḥ āna ātma cintā anupapattiḥ tasmāt tad upāsanam asmin pakṣe na vidhātavyam prāpta tvāt  tiṣṭhasu tāvat pākṣikya ātma upāsana prāptiḥ nityā vā iti apūrva vidhiḥ syāt  jñāna upāsanayoḥ ekatve satya prāpta tvāt  na sa veda iti vijñānam prastutya ātmā iti eva upāsīta iti abhidhānāt veda upāsana śabdayoḥ ekārtha tā avagamyate anena hi etad t sarvam veda ātmānam eva avet ityādi śrutibhyaḥ ca vijñānam upāsanam tasya ca aprāpta tvāt vidhi arha tvam na ca svarūpa anvākhyāne puruṣa pravṛttiḥ upapadyate tasmāt apūrva vidhiḥ eva ayam karma vidhi sāmānyāt ca yathā yajeta juhuyāt  ityādayaḥ karma vidhayaḥ na taiḥ asya ātmā iti eva upāsīta ātmā vā are draṣṭavyaḥ iti ādi ātma upāsana vidheḥ viśeṣaḥ  avagamyate mānasa kriyā tvāt ca vijñānasya tathā yasyai devatāyai haviḥ gṛhītam syāt tām manasā dhyāyet vaṣaṭkariṣyan ityādyā mānasī kriyā vidhīyate tathā ātmā iti eva upāsīta mantavyaḥ  nididhyāsitavyaḥ ityādyā kriyā eva vidhīyate jñāna ātmikā tathā avocāma veda upāsana śabdayoḥ ekārtha tvam iti bhāvāna aṃśa traya upapatteḥ ca yathā hi yajeta iti asyām bhāvanāyām kena katham iti bhāvya ādi ākāṅkṣa apanaya kāraṇam aṃśa trayam avagamyate tathā upāsīta iti asyām api bhāvanāyām vidhīyamānāyām kim upāsīta kena upāsīta iti asyām ākāṅkṣāyām ātmānam upāsīta manasā tyāga brahmacarya śama dama uparama titikṣā ādi iti kartavya tā saṃyuktaḥ ityādīśāstreṇa eva samarthyate aśa trayam yathā ca kṛtsnasya darśa pūrṇamāsa ādi prakaraṇasya darśa pūrṇamāsa ādi vidhi uddeśa tvena upayogaḥ evam aupaniṣadām ātma upāsana prakaraṇasya ātma upāsana prakaraṇasya ātma upāsana vidhi uddeśa tvena eva upayogaḥ na iti na iti asthūlam ekam eva advitīyam aśanāya ādi atītaḥ iti evamādi vākyānām upāsyātma svarūpa viśeṣa samarpaṇena upayogaḥṣa phalam ca mokṣaḥ  avidyā nivṛttiḥ vā apare varṇayanti upāsanena ātma viṣayam viśiṣṭam vijñāna antaram bhāvayet  tena ātmā jñāyate avidyā nivartakam ca tad eva na ātma viṣayam veda vākya janitam vijñānam iti etasmin  arthe vacanāni api vijñāya prajñām kurvīta draṣṭavyaḥ śrotavyaḥ  mantavyaḥ  nididhyāsitavyaḥ saḥ  anveṣṭavyaḥ sa vijijñāsitavyaḥ ityādīni na artha antara abhāvāt na ca ātmā iti eva upāsīta iti apūrva vidhiḥ kasmāt  ātma svarūpa kathanān ātma pratiṣedha vākya janita vijñāna vyatirekeṇa mānasasya bāhyasya vā abhāvāt  tatra hi vidheḥ sāphalyam yatra vidhi vākya śravaṇa mātra janita vijñāna vyatirekeṇa puruṣa pravṛttiḥ gamyate yathā darśa pūrṇamāsābhyām svarga kāmaḥ  yajeta iti evamādau na hi darśa pūrṇamāsa vidhi vākya janita vijñānam eva darśa pūrṇam āsām uṣṭhānam tad ca adhikāra ādi apekṣā anubhāvi na tu na iti na iti iti ādi ātma pratipādaka vākya janita vijñāna vyatirekeṇa darśa pūrṇamāsa ādivat puruṣa vyāpāraḥ sambhavati sarva vyāpāra upaśama hetu tvāt tad vākya janita vijñānasya na hi udāsīna vijñānam pravṛtti janakam abrahma anātma vijñāna nivartaka tvāt ca ekam eva advitīyam tad tvam asi iti evamādi vākyānām na ca tad nivṛttau pravṛttiḥ upapadyate  virodhāt  vākya janita vijñāna mātra anna abrahma anātma vijñāna nivṛttiḥ iti ced  na  tattvam asi na iti na iti ātmā eva idam ekam eva advitīyam brahma eva idam amṛtam na anyat atas  asti draṣṭaḥ tad eva brahma tvam viddhi ityādi vākyānām tad vādi tvāt draṣṭavya vidheḥ viṣaya samarpakāṇi etāni iti ced  na artha antara abhāvāt iti ukta uttaratvāt  ātma vastu svarūpa samarpakaiḥ eva vākyaiḥ tad tvam asi ityādibhiḥ śravaṇa kāla eva tad darśanasya kṛta tvāt  draṣṭavya vidheḥ na anuṣṭhāna antaram kartavyam iti ukta uttaram etad  ātma svarūpa anvākhyāna mātreṇa ātma vijñāne vidhim antareṇa na pravartata iti ced  na ātma vādi vākya śravaṇena ātma vijñānasya janita tvāt  kim bhaḥ kṛtasya karaṇam tad śravaṇe api na pravartata iti ced na anavasthā prasaṅgāt  yathā ātma vādi vākya artha śravaṇe vidhim antareṇa na pravartate tathā vidhi vākya artha śravaṇe api vidhim antareṇa na pravartiṣyata iti vidhi antara apekṣā tathā tad artha śravaṇe api iti anavasthā prasajyeta vākya janita ātma jñāna smṛti saṃtateḥ śravaṇa vijñāna mātrāt artha antara tvam iti ced  na artha prāpta tvāt  yadā eva ātma pratipādaka vākya śravaṇāt  ātma viṣayam vijñānam utpadyate tadā eva tad unpadya gānam tad viṣayam vijñānam utpadyate tadā eva tad unpadya gānam tad viṣayam mithyājñānam nivartayat eva utpadyate ātma viṣaya mithyā jñāna nivṛttau ca tad prabhavāḥ smṛtayaḥ na bhavanti svābhāvikyaḥ  anātma vastu bheda viṣayāḥ anarthatva avagateḥ ca ātma avagatau hi satyām anyat vastu anartha tvena ām agamyate anitya duḥkha aśuddhi ādi bahu doṣavat tvāt  ātma vastunaḥ ca tad vilakṣaṇa tvāt  tasmāt anātma vijñāna smṛtīnām ātma avagateḥ abhāva prāptiḥ pāriśeṣyāt ātmā ekatva vijñāna smṛti santateḥ arthata eva bhāvān na vidheya tvam śoka moha bhaya āyāsa ādi duḥkha doṣa nivartaka tvāt ca tad smṛteḥ viparīta jñāna prabhavaḥ  hi śoka moha ādi doṣaḥ tathā ca tatra kaḥ  mohaḥ vidvāṃma bibheti kutaścana abhayam vai janaka praptaḥ  asi bhidyate hṛdaya granthiḥ ityādi śrutayaḥ nirodhaḥ tarhi artha antaram iti ced  atha api syāt citta vṛtti nirodhasya veda vākya janita ātma vijñānāt artha antara tvāt tantra antareṣu ca kartavya tayā avagata tvāt vidheya tvam iti ced  na mokṣa sādhana tvena anavagamāt na hi vedānteṣu brahma ātma vijñānāt  anyat parama puruṣa artha sādhana tvena ām agamyate ātmānam eva avet tasmāt tad sarvam abhavat brahma vid āpnoti param sa yaḥ  ha vai tad paramam brahma veda brahmā eva bhavati ācāryavān puruṣaḥ  veda tasya tāvat eva ciram abhayam hi vai brahma bhavati evam veda iti evamādi śruti śatebhyaḥ ananya sādhana tvāt ca nirodhasya na hi ātma vijñāna tad smṛti santāna vyatirekeṇa citta vṛtti nirodhasya sādhanam asti abhyupagamya it am uktam na tu brahma vijñāna vyatirekeṇa anyat mokṣa sādhanam avagamyate ākāṅkṣā bhāvāt ca bhāvanā bhāvaḥ yad uktam yajeta iti ādau kim kena katham iti bhāvanā kāṅkṣāyām phala sādhana iti kartavyatābhiḥ ākāṅkṣa apanayanam yathā tadvat iha api ātma vijñāna vidhau  api upapadyata iti tad asat ekam eva advitīyam tad tvam asi na iti na iti anantaram abāhyam ayam ātmā brahma ityādi vākya artha vijñāna sama kālam eva sarva ākāṅkṣā vinivṛtteḥ na ca vākya artha vijñāne vidhi prayuktaḥ pravartate vidhi antara prayuktau ca anavasthā doṣam avocāma na ca ekam eva advitīyam brahma ityādi vākyeṣu vidhiḥ avagamyate ātma svarūpa anvākhyānena eva avasita tvāt vastu svarūpa anvākhyāna mātra tvāt aprāmāṇyam iti ced  atha api syāt yathā saḥ  arodīdyat ara udīt tad rudrasya rudra tvam iti evamādau vastu svarūpa anvākhyāna mātra tvāt aprāmāṇyam evam ātma artha vākyānām api iti ced  na  viśeṣāt  na vākyasya vastu anvākhyānam kriyā anvākhyānam vā prāmāṇya aprāmāṇya kāraṇam kim tarhi niścita phalavat vijñāna utpādaka tvam tad yatra asti tad pramāṇam vākyam yatra na asti tad apramāṇam kiṃñca bhaḥ pṛcchāmaḥ tvām ātma svarūpa anvākhyāna pareṣu vākyeṣu phalavat niścitam ca vijñānam utpadyate na vā utpadyate ced katham aprāmāṇyam iti kim vā na paśyasi avidyā śoka moha bhaya ādi saṃsāra bīja doṣa nivṛttim vijñāna phalam na śṛṇopi vā kim tatra kaḥ  mohaḥ kaḥ śoka eka tvam anupaśyataḥ mantra vid evā asmi na ātma vid saḥ aham bhagayaḥ śocāmi tam mā bhagavān śokasya pāram śocāmi tārayatu iti evamādi upaniṣad vākya śatāni evam vidyate kim saḥ  arodīt iti ādiṣu niścitam phalavat ca vijñānam na ced vidyate astu aprāmāṇyam tad aprāmāṇye phalavat niścita vijñāna utpādakasya kim iti aprāmāṇyam syāt  tad aprāmāṇye ta darśa pūrṇamāsa ādi vākyeṣu kaḥ  viśrambhaḥ nanu darśa pūrṇamāsa ādi vākyānām puruṣa pravṛtti vijñāna utpādaka tvāt  prāmāṇyam ātma vijñāna vākyeṣu tad na asti iti satyam evam na eṣa doṣaḥ prāmāṇaya kāraṇa upapatteḥ prāmāṇya kāraṇam ca yathā uktam eva na anyat  alaṅkāraḥ ca ayam yad sarva pravṛtti bīja virodha phalavat avijñāna utpādaka tvam ātma pratipādaka vākyānām na aprāmāṇya kāraṇam yad tu uktam vijñāya prajñām kurvīta ityādi vacanānām vākya artha vijñāna vyatirekeṇa upāsana artha tvam iti satyam etad  kintu na apūrva vidhi artha tā pakṣe prāptasya niyama artha tā eva katham punar upāsanasya pakṣa prāptiḥ yāvatā pāriśeṣyāt ātma vijñāna smṛti santatiḥ nityā eva iti abhihitam bāḍham yadi api evam  śarīra ārambhā kasya karmaṇaḥ  niyata phala tvāt  samyak jñāna prāptau  api avaśyambhāvinī pravṛttiḥ vāc manaḥ kāyānām labdha vṛtteḥ karmaṇaḥ  balīyaḥ tvāt  mukteṣu ādi pravṛttivat  tena pakṣe prāptam jñāna pravṛtti daurbalyam tasmāt tyāga vairāgya ādi sādhana bala avalambena ātma vijñāna smṛti santatiḥ niyantavyā bhavati na tu apūrvā kartavyā  prāpta tvāt  iti avecāma tasmāt  prāpta vijñāna smṛti santāna niyama vidhi arthāni vijñāya prajñām kurvīta ityādi vākyāni anya artha asambhavāt  nanu anātma upāsanam idam iti śabda prayogāt yathā priyam iti etad upāsīta iti ādau na priya ādi guṇā eva upāsyāḥ kim tarhi priya ādi guṇavat prāṇa ādi eva upāsyam tathā iha api iti para ātma śabda prayogāt  ātma guṇavat ana ātma vastu upāsyam iti gamyate ātma upāsyatva vākya vailakṣaṇyāt ca pareṇa ca vakṣyati ātmānam eva lokam upāsīta iti tatra ca vākye ātmā eva upāsya tvena abhipretaḥ  dvitīya aśravaṇāt ātmānam eva iti iha tu na dvitīyā śrūyate iti paraḥ ca ātma śabdaḥ ātmeni eva upāsīta iti atas  na ātma upāsya ātma guṇaḥ ca anya iti tu avagamyate na vākī aśeṣa ātmana upāsya tvena avagamāt  asya eva vākyasya śeṣe ātmā eva upāsya tvena avagamyate tad etad padanīyam asya sarvasya yad ayam ātmā antarataram yad ayam ātmā ātmānam eva avet iti praviṣṭasya darśana pratiṣedhāt anupāsya tvam iti ced  yasya ātmanaḥ praveśa uktaḥ tasya eva darśanam vāryate tam na paśyanti iti prakṛta upādānāt  tasmāt ātmanaḥ  anupāsya tvam eva it ced  na akṛt snatva doṣāt  darśana pratiṣedhaḥ  akṛtsnatva doṣa abhiprāyeṇa na ātma upāsya tvaṃpratiṣedhāya prāṇana ādi kriyā viśiṣṭa tvena viśeṣaṇāt  ātmanaḥ ced upāsya tvam anabhipetam prāṇana ādi ekaika kriyā viśiṣṭasya ātmanaḥ  akṛtsnatva vacanam anarthakam syāt  akṛtsnaḥ  hi eṣaḥ  ata ekaikena bhavati iti atas  anekaika viśiṣṭaḥ tu ātmā kṛtsna tvāt upāsya eva iti siddham yaḥ tu ātma śabdasya iti paraḥ prayogaḥ ātma śabda pratyayoḥ ātma tattvasya paramārtha taḥ  aviṣayatva jñāna artham anyathā ātmānam upāsīta iti evam avakṣyat tathā ca arthāt ātmani śabda pratyayau  anujñātau syātām  tad ca aniṣṭam na iti na iti vijñātāram arekena vijānīyāt  avijñātam vijñātṛ yatas  vācaḥ  nivartante aprāpya manasā saha ityādi śrutibhyaḥ yad tu ātmānam eva lokam upāsīta iti tad anātma upāsana prasaṅga nivṛtti para tvāt na vākya antaram anirjñātatva sāmānyāt ātmā jñātavyaḥ  anātmā ca tatra kasmāt ātma upāsane eva yatna āsthīyate ātmā iti eva upāsīta iti na itara vijñāna iti atra ucyate tad etad eva prakṛtam padanīyam gamanīyam na anyat  asya sarvasya iti nirdhāraṇa arthā ṣaṣṭhī asmin sarvasmin  iti arthaḥ yad ayam ātmā yad etad ātma tattvam kim na vijñātavyam eva anyat na kim tarhi jñātavya tve api na pṛthak jñāna antaram apekṣata ātma jñānāt kasmāt  anena ātmanā jñātena hi yasmāt etad sarvam anātma jātam anyat yad tad sarvam samastam veda jānāti nanu anya jñānena anyat na jñāyata iti asya parihāram dundubhi ādi granthena vakṣyāmaḥ katham punar etad  padanīyam iti ucyate yathā ha vai loke padena gavā ādi khura aṅkitaḥ  deśaḥ padam iti ucyate tena padena naṣṭam vivitsitam paśum padena anveṣamāṇaḥ  anuvindet labheta evam ātmani labdhe sarvam anulabhata iti arthaḥ nanu ātmani jñāte sarvam anyat jñāyata iti jñāne prakṛte katham lābhaḥ  aprakṛta ucyata iti na jñāna lābhayoḥ ekārtha tvasya vivakṣita tvāt  ātmanaḥ  hi alābhaḥ  ajñānam eva tasmāt jñānam eva ātmanaḥ  lābhaḥ nānā ātma lābhavat aprāpta prāpti lakṣaṇa ātma lābhaḥ labdhṛ labdha vyayarbheda abhāvāt  yatra hi ātmanaḥ  anātmā labdhā labdhavyaḥ  anātmā sa ca aprāpta utpādya ādi kriyā vyavahitaḥ kāraka viśeṣa upādānena kriyā viśeṣam utpādya labdhavyaḥ sa tu aprāpta prāpti lakṣaṇaḥ  anityaḥ mithyājñāna janita kāma kriyā prabhava tvāt svapne putrādi lābhavat ayam tu tad viparīta ātmā ātma tvāt eva na utpādya ādi kriyā vyavahitaḥ nitya labdha svarūpa tve api satya vidyā mātram vyavadhānam yathā gṛhyamāṇāyāḥ  api śuktikāyāḥ  viparyayeṇa rajata ābhāsāyāḥ  agrahaṇam viparīta jñāna vyavadhāna mātram tathā grahaṇam jñāna mātram eva viparīta jñāna vyavadhāna apoha artha tvāt jñānasya evam iha api ātmanaḥ  alābhaḥ  avidyā mātra vyavadhānam tasmāt vidyayā tad apohana mātram eva lābhaḥ  na anyaḥ kadācid api upapadyate tasmāt ātma lābhe jñānāt artha antara sādhanasya ānarthakyam vakṣyāmaḥ tasmāt nirāśaṅkam eva jñāna lābhayoḥ eka artha tvam vivakṣan  āha jñānam prakṛtya anuvindet iti vindateḥ lābha artha tvāt guṇa vijñāna phalam idam ucyate yathā ayam ātma ātmā nāma rūpa anupraveśena khyātim gata ātmā ityādi nāma rūpābhyām prāṇa ādi saṃhatim ca ślokam prāptavān iti evam yaḥ  veda sa kīrtim khyātim ślokam ca saṅghātam iṣṭaiḥ saha vindate labhate yad vā yathā uktam vastu yaḥ  veda mumukṣūṇām apekṣitam kīrti śabditam aikya jñānam tad phalam śloka śabditām muktim āpnoti iti mukhyam eva phalam kutas ca ātma tattvam eva jñeyam anāhatyā anyat iti āha tad etad ātma tattvam preyaḥ priyataram putrāt  putraḥ  hi loke priyaḥ prasiddhaḥ tasmāt api priyataram iti niratiśaya priya tvam darśayati tathā vittāt hiraṇya ratna ādeḥ tathā anyasya adyat loke priya tvena prasiddham tasmāt sarvasmāt iti arthaḥ tad kasmāt ātma tattvam eva priyataram na prāṇa ādi iti ucyate antarataram bāhyāt putra vitta ādeḥ prāṇa piṇḍa samudāyaḥ  hi antaraḥ  abhyantaraḥ sannikṛṣṭa ātmanaḥ tasmāt api antarāt antarataram yad ayam ātmā yad etad ātma tattvam yaḥ  hi loke niratiśaya priyaḥ sa sarva prayatnena labdhavyaḥ  bhavati tathā ayam ātmā sarva laukika priyebhyaḥ priyatamaḥ tasmāt tad lābhe mahān yatna āsthena iti arthaḥ karttavyatā prāptam api anya priya lābhe yatnam ujjhitvā kasmāt punar  ātmānātma priyayoḥ anyatara priya hānena itara priya upādāna prāptau ātma priya upādānena eva itara hānam kriyate na viparyayaḥ iti ucyate sa yaḥ kaścid anyam anātmamamamama viśeṣam putra ādikam priyataram ātmānaḥ sa ākāśāt  brūvāṇam brūyāt ātma priya vādī kim priyam tava abhimatam putra ādi lakṣaṇam rotsyati āvaraṇam prāṇa saṃrodham prāpsyati vinaṅkṣyati iti sa kasmāt evam bravīti yasmāt īśvaraḥ samarthaḥ paryāptaḥ  asau  evam vaktum ha yasmāt tasmāt tathā eva syāt yad tena uktam prāṇa saṃrodham prāpsyati yathābhūta vādī hi saḥ tasmāt sa īśvaraḥ  vaktum īśvara śabdaḥ kṣipra vācī iti kecid  bhavet yadi prasiddhiḥ syāt  tasmāt ujjhitvā anyat priyam ātmānam eva priyam upāsīta sa ya ātmānam eva priyam upāste ātmā eva priyaḥ  na anyaḥ  asti iti pratipadyate anyat laukikam priyam api apriyam eva iti niścitya upāste cintayati na ha asya evaṃvidaḥ priyam pramāyukam pramaraṇa śīlam bhavati nitya anuvāda mātram etad  ātma vidaḥ  anyasya priyasya apriyasya ca abhāvāt  ātma priya grahaṇa stuti artham vā priya guṇa phala vidhāna artham manda ātma darśinaḥ tāt śīlya pratyaya upādānāt  sūtritā brahma vidyā ātmā iti eva upāsīta iti yad artha upaniṣad kṛtasnā api tasya etasya sūtrasya vyācikhyāsuḥ prayojana abhidhitsayā upojjighāṃsati tad iti vakṣyamāṇam anantara vākye avadyotyam vastu āhuḥ brāhmaṇā brahma vividiṣavaḥ  janma jarā maraṇa prabandha cakra bhramaṇa kṛta āyāsa duḥkha udaka āpāra mahodadhi plava bhūtam gurum āsādya tad tīram uttitīrṣavaḥ  dharma adharma sādhana tad phala lakṣaṇāt  sādhya sādhana rūpān nirviṇṇāḥ tad vilakṣaṇa nitya niratiśaya śreyaḥ pratipitsavaḥ kim āhuḥ iti āha yad brahma vidyayā brahma paramātmā tayā brahma vidyayā sarvam niravaśeṣam bhaviṣyantaḥ  bhaviṣyāma iti evam manuṣyā yad manyante manuṣya grahaṇam viśeṣataḥ  adhikāra jñāpana artham manuṣyā eva hi viśeṣataḥ  abhyudaya niḥśreyasa sādhane adhikṛtā iti abhiprāyaḥ yathā karma viṣaye phala prāptim dhruvām karmabhyaḥ  manyante tathā brahma vidyāyāḥ  sarva ātma bhāva phala prāptim dhruvām eva manyante veda prāmāṇyasya ubhayatra aviśeṣāt  tatra vipratiṣiddham vastu lakṣyate atas  pṛcchāmaḥ kim u tad brahma yasya vijñānāt sarvam bhaviṣyantaḥ  manuṣyā manyante tad kim avedyasmāt vijñānāt tad brahma sarvam abhavat  brahma ca sarvam iti śrūyate tad yadi avijñāya kiñcid sarvam abhavat tathā anyeṣām api astu kim brahma vidyayā atha vijñāya sarvam abhavat  vijñāna sādhya tvāt karma phalena tulyam eva iti anityatva prasaṅgaḥ sarva bhāvasya brahma vidyā phalasya anavasthā doṣaḥ catat api anyat vijñāya sarevam abhavat tatas  pūrvam api anyat vijñāya iti na tāvat avijñāya sarvam abhavat  śāstra artha vairūpya doṣāt  phala anityatva doṣaḥ tarhi na ekaḥ api doṣoḥ atha viśeṣa upapatteḥ yadi kim api vijñāya eva tad brahma sarvam abhavat pṛcchāmaḥ kim u tad brahmāvet yasmāt tad sarvam abhavat iti evam codite sarva doṣān āgandhitam prativacanam āha brahmāparam sarva bhāvasya sādhyatva upapatteḥ na hi parasya brahmaṇaḥ sarva bhāva āpattiḥ vijñāna sādhyā vijñāna sādhyān ca sarva bhāva āpattiḥ vijñāna sādhyā vijñāna sādhyān ca sarva bhāva āpattim āha atasmāt tad sarvam abhavat aiti tad asmāt brahma vā idam agra āsīt iti aparam brahma iha bhavitum arhati manuṣya adhikārāt vā tad bhāvī brāhmaṇaḥ syāt  asarvam bhaviṣyantaḥ  manuṣyā manyante aiti hi manuṣyāḥ prakṛtāḥ teṣām ca abhyudaya niḥśreyasa sādhane viśeṣataḥ  adhikāra iti uktam na parasya brahmaṇaḥ  na api aparasya prajāpateḥ atas  dvaita ekatva apara brahma vidyayā karma sahitayā apara brahma bhāvam upasampannaḥ  bhojyāt apāvṛttaḥ sarva prāptyā ucchinna kāma karma bandhanaḥ para brahma bhāvī brahma vidyā hetoḥ brahma iti abhidhīyate dṛṣṭaḥ ca loke bhāvinīm vṛttim āśritya śabda prayogaḥ yathā aodanam pacati aiti śāstre ca aparivrājakaḥ sarva bhūta abhaya dakṣiṇām aityādi tathā iha iti kecid  brahma brahma bhāvī puruṣaḥ  brāhmaṇaḥ iti vyācakṣate tad na sarva bhāva āpatteḥ anityatva doṣāt na hi saḥ  asti loke paramārtha taḥ  yaḥ  nimitta vaśāt bhāva antaram āpadyate nityaḥ ca iti tathā brahma vijñāna nimitta kṛtā ced sarva bhāva āpattiḥ nityā ca iti viruddham anitya tve ca karma phala tulya tā iti uktaḥ  doṣaḥ avidyā kṛta asarvatva nivṛttim ced sarva bhāva āpattim brahma vidyā phalam manyase brahma bhāvi puruṣa kalpanā vyarthā syāt prāk brahma vijñānāt api sarvaḥ  jantu brahma tvāt nityam eva sarva bhāva āpannaḥ paramārthataḥ avidyayā tu abrahma tvam asarva tvam ca adhyāropitam yathā śuktikāyām rajatam vyomni vā tala malavattva ādi tathā iha brahmaṇi adhyoropitam avidyayā abrahma tvam asarva tvam ca brahma vidyayā nivartyata iti manyase yadi tadā yuktam yad paramārtha ta āsīt param brahma brahma śabdasya mukhya artha bhūtam abrahma vā idam agra āsīt aiti asmin vākye ucyate iti vaktum  yathā bhūta artha vādi tvāt vedasya na tu iyam kalpanā yuktā brahma śabda artha viparītaḥ  brahma bhāvī puruṣaḥ  brahma iti ucyata iti śruta hānya śruta kalpanāyā anyāyya tvāt mahattare prayojana antare asati avidyā kṛta vyatirekeṇa abrahma tvam asarva tvam ca vidyata eva iti ced na tasya brahma vidyayā apoha anupapatteḥ na hi kvacid sākṣāt vastu dharmasya apoḍhrī dṛṣṭā kartrī vā brahma vidyā avidyāya aḥ tu sarvatra eva nivartikā dṛśyate tathā iha api abrahma tvam asarva tvam ca avidyā kṛtam eva nivartyatām brahma vidyayā na tu pāramārthikam vastu kartum nivartayitum vā arhati brahma vidyā tasmāt vyarthā eva śruta hānya śruta kalpanā brahmaṇi avidyā anupapattiḥ iti ced  na brahmaṇi vidyā vidhānāt na hi śuktikāyām rajata adhyāropaṇe asati śuktikā tvam jñāpyate cakṣuḥ gocara āpannāyām iyam śuktikā na rajatam iti tathā sa deva idam sarvam brahma eva idam sarvam ātmā eva idam sarvam na idam dvaitam asti abrahma iti brahmaṇi ekatva vijñānam na vidhātavyam brahmaṇi avidyā adhyāropaṇāyām asatyām na brūmaḥ śuktikāyām iva brahmaṇi atad dharma adhyāropaṇā na asti iti kim tarhi na brahma sva ātmani atad dharma adhyāropanimittam avidyā kartṛ ca iti bhavatu evam na avidyā kartṛ bhrāntam ca brahma kiṃntu na eva abrahma avidyā kartā cetanaḥ bhrāntaḥ  anya iṣyate na anyaḥ  atas  asti vijñātā na anyat atas  asti vijñātṛ tad tvam asi ātmānam eva avet aham brahmā asmi anyaḥ  asau  anyaḥ  aham asmi iti na sa veda ityādi śrutibhyaḥ smṛtibhyaḥ ca samam sarveṣu bhūteṣu aham ātmā guḍākeśa śuni ca eva śvapāke ca yaḥ tu sarvāṇi bhūtāni ityādibhyaḥ yasmin sarvāṇi bhūtāni iti ca mantra varṇāt  nanu evam śāstra upadeśa ānarthakyam iti bāḍham evam avagate astu eva ānarthakyam avagamanarthakyam iti ced  na anavagama nivṛtteḥ dṛṣṭa tvāt  tad nivṛtteḥ api anupapattiḥ ekatva iti ced  na dṛṣṭa virodhāt  dṛśyate hi ekatva vijñānāt eva anavagama nivṛttiḥ dṛśyamānam api anupapannam iti bruvataḥ  dṛṣṭa virodhaḥ syāt na ca dṛṣṭa virodhaḥ kenacid api abhyupagamyate na ca dṛṣṭe anupapannam nāma dṛṣṭa tvāt eva darśana anupapattiḥ iti ced tatra api eṣā eva yuktiḥ puṇyam vai puṇyena karmaṇā bhavati tam vidyā karmaṇī samanvārabhete iti evamādi śruti smṛti nyāyebhyaḥ parasmāt vilakṣaṇaḥ  anyaḥ saṃsāri avagamyate tad vilakṣaṇaḥ ca paraḥ sa eṣa na iti na iti aśanāyāt yatyeti ya ātma apahata pāpmā vijaraḥ  vimṛtyuḥ etasya vā akṣarasya praśāsane ityādi śrutibhyaḥ kaṇā da akṣa pāda ādi tarka śāstreṣu ca saṃsāra vilakṣaṇa īśvara upapattitaḥ sādhyate saṃsāra duḥkha apanaya arthitva pravṛtti darśanāt sphuṭam anya tvam īśvarāt saṃsāriṇaḥ  avagamyate avākyanādaraḥ na me pārtha asti iti śrutibhyaḥ saḥ  anveṣṭavyaḥ sa vijijñāsitavyaḥ tam viditvā na lipyate brahma vid āpnoti param ekadhā eva anudraṣṭavyam etad  yaḥ  vā etad akṣaram gārgya viditvā tam eva dhīraḥ  vijñāya praṇavaḥ  dhanuḥ śaraḥ  hi ātmā brahma tad lakṣyam ucyate iti ādi karma kartṛ nirdeśāt ca mumukṣoḥ ca gati mārga viśeṣa deśa upadeśāt asati bhede kasya kutaḥ gatiḥ syāt  tad abhāve ca dakṣiṇa uttara mārga viśeṣa anupapattiḥ gantavya deśa anupapattiḥ ca iti bhinnasya tu parasmāt ātmanaḥ sarvam etad upapannam karma jñāna sādhana upadeśāt ca bhinnaḥ ced brahmaṇaḥ saṃsārī syāt  yuktaḥ tam pratyabhyudaya niḥśreyasādhanayoḥ karma jñānayoḥ upadeśaḥ  na īśvarasya āpta kāma tvāt  tasmāt yuktam brahma iti brahma bhāvī puruṣa ucyata iti ced  na brahma upadeśa anarthakya prasaṅgāt saṃsārī ced  brahma bhāvya brahma san viditvā ātmānam eva aham brahma asmi iti sarvam abhavat tasya saṃsārya ātma vijñānāt eva sarva ātma bhāvasya phalasya siddha tvāt para brahma upadeśasya dhruvam ānarthakyam prāptam tad vijñānasya kvacid puruṣa artha sādhane aviniyāgāt saṃsāriṇa eva aham brahma asmi iti brahmatva sampādana artha upadeśa iti ced  anirjñāte hi brahma svarūpe kim sampādayet aham brahma asmi iti nirjñāta lakṣaṇe hi brahmaṇi śakyā sampad kartum na  ayam ātmā brahma cat sākṣāt aparokṣāt brahma ya ātmā tad satyam sa ātmā brahma vid āpnoti param iti prakṛtya tasmāt vā etasmāt ātmanaḥ iti sahasraśas  brahma ātma śabdayoḥ sāmānādhikaraṇyāt eka artha tvam eva iti avagamyate anyasya hi anya tve sampad kriyate na ekatve idam sarvam yad ayam ātmā iti ca prakṛtasya eva draṣṭavyasya ātmana eka tvam darśayati tasmāt na ātmanaḥ  brahmatva sampad upapattiḥ na ca api anyat prayojanam brahma upadeśasya gamyate brahma veda brahmā eva bhavati abhayam vai janaka prāptaḥ  asi abhayam hi vai brahma bhavati iti ca tad āpatti śravaṇāt sampattiḥ ced tadāpattiḥ na syāt  na hi anyasyāmi abhāva upapadyate vacanāt  sampatteḥ api tad bhāva āpattiḥ syāt iti ced  na sampatteḥ pratyaya mātra tvāt  vijñānasya ca mithyājñāna nivartakatva vyatirekeṇa ākāraka tvam iti avocāma na ca vacanam vastunaḥ sāmarthya janakam jñāpakam hi śāstram na kārakam iti sthitiḥ sa eṣa iha praviṣṭaḥ ityādi vākyeṣu ca parasya eva praveśa iti sthitam tasmāt brahma iti na brahma bhāvi puruṣa kalpanā sādhvī iṣṭa artha bādhanāt ca saindhava dhanavat anantaram abāhyam eka rasam brahma iti vijñānam sarvasyām upaniṣadi pratipipādayiṣitor athaḥ kāṇḍa dvaye api ante avadhāraṇāt avagamyate iti anuśāsanam etāvat are khalu amṛta tvam iti tathā sarva śākhā upaniṣatsu ca brahma ekatva vijñānam niścitor athaḥ tatra yadi saṃsārī brahmaṇaḥ  anya ātmānam eva aved iti kalpyeta iṣṭasya arthasya na adhanam syāt  tathā ca śāstram upakrama upasaṃhārayoḥ virodhāt asamañjasam kalpitam syāt  vyapadeśa anupapatteḥ ca yadi ca ātmānam eva avet iti saṃsārī kalpyeta brahma vidyā iti vyapadeśaḥ  na syāt  ātmānam eva aved iti saṃsāriṇa eva vedyatva upapatteḥ ātmā iti vedituḥ anyat ucyata iti ced na aham brahma asmi iti viśeṣaṇāt  anyaḥ ced vedyaḥ syāt ayam asau  iti vā viśeṣyeta na tu aham asmi iti aham asmi iti viśeṣaṇāt ātmānam eva aved iti ca avadhāraṇāt niścitam ātmā eva brahma iti avagamyate tathā ca sati upapannaḥ  brahma vidyā vyapadeśaḥ  na anyathā saṃsāri vidyā hi anyathā syāt  na ca brahmatva abrahmatve hi ekasya upapanne paramārthataḥ tamaḥ prakāśau  iva bhānoḥ viruddha tvāt  na ca ubhaya nimitta tve brahma vidyā iti niścitaḥ  vyapadeśaḥ  yuktam tattva jñāna vivakṣāyām śrotuḥ saṃśayaḥ  hi tathā syāt  niścitam ca jñānam puruṣa artha sādhanam iṣyate yasya syāt ddhā na vicikitsā asti saṃśaya ātmā vinaśyati iti śruti smṛtibhyām atas  na saṃśayitaḥ  vākya arthaḥ  vācyaḥ para hita arthinā brahmaṇi sādhakatva kalpanā asmad ādiṣu iva apeśalā atadātmānam eva avet tasmāt tad sarvam abhavat aiti iti ced  na śāstra upālambhāt  na hi asmāt kalpanā iyam śāstra kṛtā tu tasmāt śāstrasya ayam upālambhaḥ na ca brahmaṇa iṣṭam cikīrṣuṇā śāstra atha viparīta kalpanā sva artha parityāgaḥ kāryaḥ na ca etāvatī eva akṣamā yuktā bhavataḥ sarvam hi nānā tvam brahmaṇi kalpitam eva ekadhā eva anudraṣṭavyam na iha nānā asti kiñcana yatra hi dvaitam iva bhavati ekam eva advitīyam ityādi vākya śatebhyaḥ sarvaḥ  hi loka vyavahāraḥ  brahmaṇi eva kalpitaḥ  na parama arthaḥ san iti atyalpam idam ucyate aiyam eva kalpanā apeśalā aiti tasmāt  yad praviṣṭam sraṣṭrṛ brahma tad brahma vaiśabdaḥ  avadhāraṇa arthaḥ idam śarīra stham yad  gṛhyate agre prāc pratibodhāt api brahma eva āsīt sarvam ca idam kintva pratibodhāt  abrahma asmi asarvam ca iti ātmani adhyāropāt akartā ahe kriyāvān phalānām ca bhoktā sukhī duḥkhaḥ  saṃsārī aiti ca adhyāropayati paramārthataḥ tu brahmā eva tad vilakṣaṇam sarvam ca tad kathañcid ācāryeṇa dayālunā pratibodhitam anāsi saṃsārī aitya ātmānam eva avetsvābhāvikam avidyā adhyāropita viśeṣa varjitam iti eva śabdasya arthaḥ brūhi kaḥ  asau  ātmā svābhāvikaḥ yam ātmānam viditavat brahma nanu na smarasya ātmānam darśitaḥ  hi asau ya iha praviśya prāṇityapān iti vyāniti udān iti samāniti iti nanu aasau gauḥ asau  aśvaḥ aiti evam asau vyapadiśyate bhavatā na ātmānam pratyakṣam darśayasi evam tarhi draṣṭā śrotā mantā vijñātā sa ātmā iti nanu atra api darśana ādi kriyā kartuḥ svarūpam na pratyakṣam darśayasi na hi gamiḥ eva gantuḥ svarūpam chidiḥ vā chettuḥ evam tarhi dṛṣṭeḥ draṣṭā śruteḥ śrotā mateḥ mantā vijñāteḥ vijñātā sa ātmā iti nanu atra kaḥ  viśeṣaḥ  draṣṭari yadi dṛṣṭardraṣṭā yadi vā ghaṭasya draṣṭā sarvathā api draṣṭā eva draṣṭavya eva tu bhavān viśeṣam āha dṛṣṭeḥ draṣṭā iti draṣṭā tu yadi dṛṣṭeḥ yadi vā ghaṭasya draṣṭā draṣṭā eva na viśeṣa upapatteḥ asti atra viśeṣaḥ dṛṣṭeḥ draṣṭā sa dṛṣṭim na kadācid api dṛṣṭiḥ na dṛśyate draṣṭā  tatra draṣṭuḥ dṛṣṭyā nityayā bhavitavyam anityā ced  draṣṭuḥ dṛṣṭiḥ tatra dṛśyā yā dṛṣṭiḥ sā kadācid na dṛśyeta api yathā anityayā dṛṣṭyā ghaṭa ādi vastu na ca tadvat  dṛṣṭeḥ draṣṭā kadācid api na paśyati dṛṣṭim kim dve dṛṣṭī draṣṭuḥ nityā adṛśyā anyā anityā dṛśyā iti bāḍham  prasiddhā tāvat anityā dṛṣṭiḥ andha anandhatva darśanāt nityā eva ced sarvaḥ  anandha eva syāt  draṣṭaḥ tu nityā dṛṣṭiḥ na hi draṣṭuḥ dṛṣṭeḥ viparilopaḥ  vidyate iti śruteḥ anumānāt ca andhasya api ghaṭa ādi ābhāsa viṣayā svapne dṛṣṭiḥ upalabhyate sā tarhi itara dṛṣṭi nāśe na paśyati sā draṣṭuḥ dṛṣṭiḥ tayā avipariluptayā nityayā dṛṣṭyā svarūpa bhūtayā svayan jyotiḥ samākhyathetām anityām dṛṣṭim svapna vuddha antayoḥ vāsanā pratyaya rūpām nityam eva paśyan dṛṣṭeḥ draṣṭā bhavati evaḥ ca sati dṛṣṭiḥ eva svarūpam asya agni auṣṇyavat  na kāṇādānām iva dṛṣṭi vyatiriktaḥ  anyaḥ cetanaḥ  draṣṭā tad brahma ātmānam eva nitya dṛś rūpam adhyāropita anitya dṛṣṭi ādi varjitam eva avedviditavat nanu vipratiṣiddham na vijñātevijñātāram vijānīyāḥ iti śruteḥ vijñātuḥ vijñānam na evam vijñānāt na vipratiṣedhaḥ evam dṛṣṭeḥ draṣṭā iti vijñāyata eva anya jñāna anapekṣa tvāt ca na ca draṣṭuḥ nitya eva dṛṣṭiḥ iti evam vijñāte draṣṭri viṣayām dṛṣṭim anyām ākāṅkṣate nivartate hi draṣṭu viṣaya dṛṣṭi ākāṅkṣā tad asambhavāt eva na hi avidyamāne viṣaya ākāṅkṣā kasyacid upajāyate na ca dṛśyā dṛṣṭiḥ draṣṭāram viṣayīkartum utsahate yatas tām ākāṅkṣeta na ca sva rūpa viṣaya ākhāṅkṣāsu asya eva tasmāt ajñāna adhyāropaṇa nivṛttiḥ eva aatmānam eva avet iti uktamna ātmanaḥ  viṣayīkaraṇam tad katham avet iti āha aham dṛṣṭeḥ draṣṭā ātmā brahmā asmi bhavāmi iti brahma iti yad sākṣāt aparokṣāt sarva antara ātmā aśanāya ādi atītaḥ  na iti na iti asthūla manaṇu iti evamādi lakṣaṇam tad eva aham asmi na anyaḥ saṃsārī yathā bhavān āha iti tasmāt evam vijñānāt tad brahma sarvam abhavat  tasmāt yuktam eva manuṣyā manyante yad brahma vidyayā sarvam bhaviṣyāma iti yad pṛṣṭam akimu tad brahma aved yasmāt tad sarvam abhavat aiti tad nirṇītam abrahma vā idam agra āsīt  tad ā ātmānam eva avedaham brahma asmi iti tasmāt tad sarvam abhavat aiti tad tatra yaḥ  yaḥ  devānām madhye pratyabudhyata pratibuddhvā anātmānam yathā uktena ātmā tad brahmā abhavat tathā rpīṇām tathā manuṣyāṇām ca madhye devānām ityādi loka dṛṣṭi apekṣayā na brahmatva buddhyā ucyate apuraḥ puruṣa āviśat aiti sarvatra brahma eva anupraviṣṭam ityādi ucyate paramārthataḥ tu tatra tatra brahma eva agra āsīt prāc pratibodhāt  deva ādi śarīra īśvanī athā eva vibhāvyamānam tadā ātmānam eva avet tathā eva ca sarvam abhavat  asyāḥ  brahma vidyāyāḥ sarva bhāva āpattiḥ phalam iti etasya arthasya draḍhimne mantrān udāharati śrutiḥ katham tad  brahma etad ātmānam eva aaham asmi aiti paśyan  etasmāt eva brahmaṇaḥ  darśanāt ṛṣṭiḥ vāmadeva ākhyaḥ pratipede ha pratipannavān kila sa etasmin mantrān dadarśa aaham manuḥ abhavam sūryaḥ ca aityādīn tad etad brahma paśyan iti brahma vidyā parāmṛśyate aaham manuḥ abhavam suryaḥ ca aityādinā sarva bhāva āpattim brahma vidyā phalam parāmṛśati paśyan sarva ātma bhāvam phalam pratipeda iti asmāt prayogāt  brahma vidyā sahāya sādhana sādhyam mokṣam darśayati bhuñjānaḥ tṛpyati iti yadvat  sā iyam brahma vidyayā sarva bhāva āpattiḥ āsīt mahatām deva ādīnām vīrya atiśayāt na ida ānīmaidaṃyugīnānām viśeṣataḥ  manuṣyāṇām alpa vīrya tvāt iti syāt kasyacid buddhiḥ tad utthāpanāya āha tad idam prakṛtam brahma yad sarva bhūta anupraviṣṭam dṛṣṭi kriyā ādi liṅgam etarhi etasmin  api vartamāna kāle yaḥ kaścid vyāvṛtta bāhya autsukya ātmānam eva evam veda aaham brahma asmi aiti apohya upādhi janita bhrānti vijñāna adhyāropitān viśeṣān saṃsāra dharmānāgandhitam anantaram abāhyam brahyeva aham asmi kevalam iti saḥ  avidyā kṛta asarvatva nivṛtteḥ braha avijhānāt idam sarva bhavati na hi mahā vīryeṣu vāma ḍheva ādiṣu hīna vīryeṣu vā vārtamānikeṣu manuṣya iṣu brahyaṇaḥ  viśeṣaḥ tad vijhānasya vā asti vārtamānikeṣu puruṣeṣu tu bahya vidyā phale anaikāntika tā śaḍkyata iti ata āha tasya ha brahya vijhātuḥ yathā utkena vidhinā devāḥ  mahā vīryāḥ ca na api abhūtatyaa bhavanāya brahyā sarvam āvasya na īśate na paryāptāḥ kim uta anye brahya avidyā phala prāpyau vidhna karaṇe deva ādaya īśata iti kā śaḍkā iti ucyate deva ādīn prati ṛṇavat tvāt martyānām brahya caryeṇa ṛpibhyaḥ  yajhena devabhyaḥ prajayā pitṛbhyaḥ iti hi jāyamānam eva ṛṇavantam puruṣam darśayati śrutiḥ paśu ni darśanāt ca athaḥ ayam vā ityāt loka śruteḥ ca ātmanaḥ  vṛtti paripipālayiṣayā adhamarṇānivam devāḥ paratantrāt manuṣyān pratyamṛtatva prāptim prati vidhnam kuryuḥ iti nyāyyā eva eṣā śaḍkā sva paśūn sva śarīrāṇi iva ca rakṣanti devāḥ mahattarām hi vṛttim karma adhīnām darśayṣyati deva ādīnām bahu paśu samatayā ekaikasya puruṣasya tasmāt depām tad na priyam yad etad manudhyā vidyāḥ iti hahi vakṣyati yathā ha vai svāya lokāya ariṣṭim icchet evam ha evaṃvide sarvāṇi bhūtāni ariṣṭim icchanti iti ca brahya āviśve pārārthya nivṛtteḥ na sva loka tvam paśu tvañca iti ami prāyaḥ  apriya ariṣṭi vacanābhyām avagamyate tasmāt brahya avidaḥ  brahya vidyā phalaṛprāpta prati kuryuḥ eva vidhnam devāḥ prabhāvavantaḥ ca hi te nanu evam sati anyāsu api karma phala prāpti pudevānām vidhna karaṇaṃpeya pāna samam hanta tarhi āvisrambhaḥ  abhyudaya niḥśreyasa sādhanā nuṣṭhāneṣu tathā īśvarasya acintaya śakti tvādvidhna karaṇe prabhu tvam tathā kāla karma mantra oṣadhi tapasām eṣām hi phala sampatti vipatti hetu tvam śāstre loke ca prasidvam atas  api anāśvāsaḥ śāstra artha anuṣṭhāne na  sarva padārthānām niyata nimitta upādānāt jagat vaicitrya darśanāt ca svabhāva pakṣe ca tad ubhaya anupapatteḥ asukha duḥkha ādi phala nimittam karma aiti etasmin pakṣe sthite veda smṛti nyāya loka parigṛhīte deva īśvara kālāḥ tāvat na karma phala viparyāsa kartāraḥ karmaṇām kāṅkṣita kāraka tvāt  karma hi śubha aśubham puruṣāṇām deva kāla īśvara ādi kārakam anapekṣya na ātmānam prati labhate labdha ātmakam api phala dāne asamartham kriyāyāḥ  hi kāraka ādi aneka nimitta upādāna sva abhāvyāt  tasmāt kriyā anuguṇā hi deveśvara ādaya iti karmasu tāvat na phala prāptim pratyavisrambhaḥ karmaṇām api eṣām vaśa aniga tvam kvacid  sva sāmarthyasya apraṇodya tvāt  karma kāla daiva dravya ādi svabhāvānām guṇa pradhāna bhāvaḥ tu aniyataḥ  durvijñeyaḥ ca iti tad kṛtaḥ  mohaḥ  lokasya karma eva kārakam na anyat phala prāptau  iti kecitaṃ daivam eva iti apare  kāla iti eke dravya ādi svabhāva iti kecit  sarva ete saṃhatā eva iti apare tatra karmaṇaḥ prādhānyam aṅgīkṛtya veda smṛti vādāḥ puṇyaḥ  vai puṇyena karmaṇā bhavati pāpaḥ pāpena ityādayaḥ yadi api eṣām sva viṣaye kasyacid prādhānya udbhava itareṣām tad kālīna prādhānya śakti stambhaḥ tathā api na karmaṇaḥ phala prāptim pratyanaikāntika tvam śāstra nyāya nirdhārita tvāt karma prādhānyasya na vidyā apagama mātra tvāt  brahma prāpti phalasya yad uktam brahma prāpti phalam prati devāḥ  vighnam kuryuḥ iti tatra na devānām vighna karaṇe sāmarthyam  kasmāt  vidyā kāla anantarita tvāt  brahma prāpti phalasya katham yathā loke draṣṭuḥ cakṣuṣa ālokena saṃyogaḥ  yad kālaḥ tad kāla eva rūpa abhivyaktiḥ evam ātma viṣayam vijñānam yad kālam tad kāla eva tad viṣaya jñāna tirobhāvaḥ syāt  atas  brahma vidyāyām satyām avidyā kārya anupapatteḥ pradīpa iva tamaḥ kāryasya kena kasya vighnam kuryuḥ devāḥ yatra ātma tvam eva devānām brahma vidaḥ tad etad āha ātmā svarūpam dhyeyam yad tad sarva śāstraiḥ vijñeyam brahma hi yasmāt  eṣām devānām sa brahma vid bhavati brahma vidyā sama kālam eva avidyā mātra vyavadhāna apagamāt śuktikāyāḥ  iva rajata ābhāsāyāḥ śuktikā tvam iti avocāma atas  na ātmanaḥ pratikūla tve devānām prayatnaḥ sambhavati yasya hi anātma bhūtam phalam deśa kāla nimitta antaritam tatra anātma viṣaye saphalaḥ prayatnaḥ  vighna ācaraṇāya devānām na tu iha vidyā sama kāla ātma bhūte deśa kāla nimitta an antarite avasara anupapatteḥ evam tarhi vidyā pratyaya santatyabhāvāt  viparīta pratyaya tad kāryayoḥ ca darśanāt  antya eva ātma pratyayaḥ avidyā nivartakaḥ  na tu pūrva iti na prathamena anaikāntika tvāt  yadi hi prathama  ātma viṣayaḥ pratyayaḥ avidyām na nivartayati tathā antyaḥ  api tulya viṣaya tvāt  evam tarhi santatas  avidyā nivartakaḥ  na vicchinna iti na jīvana ādau sati santati anupapatteḥ na hi jīvana ādi hetuke pratyaye sati vidyā pratyaya santatiḥ upapadyate virodhāt  atha jīvana ādi pratyaya tiraskaraṇena eva āmaraṇa antāt vidyā āsantatiḥ iti ced na pratyayeyattā samantānānavadhāraṇāt śāstra artha an avadhāraṇa doṣāt  iyatām pratyayānām santatiḥ avidyāyā nivartikā iti anavadhāraṇāt śāstra arthaḥ  na avadhriyeta tad ca aniṣṭam santati mātra tve avadhārita eva iti ced  na ādi antayoḥ aviśeṣāt prathamā vidyā pratyaya santatiḥ maraṇa kāla antā vā iti viśeṣa abhāvāt ādi antayoḥ pratyayoḥ pūrva uktau doṣau prasajyeyātām evam tarhi anivartaka eva iti ced  na tasmāt tad sarvam abhavat iti śruteḥ bhidyate hṛdaya granthiḥ tatra kaḥ  mohaḥ ityādi śrutibhyaḥ ca arthavāda iti ced  na sarva śākhā upaniṣadaḥ pratyakṣa pramita ātma viṣaya tvāt asti eva iti ced  na ukta parihāra tvāt  avidyā śoka moha bhaya ādi doṣa nivṛtteḥ pratyakṣa tvāt iti ca uktaḥ parihāraḥ tasmāt ādyaḥ  antyaḥ santatas  asantatas cetyacodyam etad  avidyā ādi doṣa nivṛtti phala avasāna tvāt vidhāyāḥ ya eva avidyā ādi doṣa nivṛtti phala kṛt pratyaya ādyaḥ  antyaḥ santatas  asantatas  vā sa eva vidyā iti abhyupagamāt na codyasya avatāra gandhaḥ  api asti yad tu uktam viparīta pratyaya tad kāryayoḥ ca darśanāt iti na tad śeṣa sthiti hetu tvāt  yena karmaṇā śarīram ārabdham tad viparīta pratyaya doṣa nimitta tvāt tasya tathābhūtasya eva viparīta pratyaya doṣa saṃyuktasya phala dāne sāvarthyam iti yāvat śarīra pātaḥ tāvat phala upabhoga aṅga tayā viparīta pratyayam rāga ādi doṣam ca tāvat mātram ākṣipati eva mukta iṣuvat pravṛtta phala tvāt tad hetukasya karmaṇaḥ tena na tasya nivartukā vidyā avirodhāt  kim tarhi sva āśrayāt eva sva ātma virodhya vidyā kāryam yad utpitsu tad niruṇāddhi anāgata tvāt  atītam hi itarat  kiñca na ca viparīta pratyayaḥ vidyāvata utpadyate nirviṣaya tvāt  anavadhṛta viṣaya viśeṣa svarūpam hi sāmānya mātram āśritya viparīta pratyaya utpadyamāna utpadyate yathā śuktikāyām rajatam iti sa ca viṣaya viśeṣa avadhāraṇavataḥ  aśeṣa viparīta pratyaya āśrayasya upamardita tvāt na pūrvavat sambhavati śuktikā ādau samyak pratyayāt pattau punagdarśanāt  kvacid tu vidyāyāḥ pūrva utpanna viparīta pratyaya janita saṃskārebhyaḥ  viparīta pratyaya avabhāsāḥ smṛtayaḥ jāyamānā viparīta pratyaya bhrāntim akasmāt kurvanti  yathā vijñāta diś vibhāgasya api akasmāt diś viparyaya vibhramaḥ samyak jñānavataḥ  api ced pūrvavat viparīta pratyaya utpadyate samyak jñāne api avisrambhāt śāstra artha vijñāna ādau pravṛttiḥ asamañjasā syāt sarvam ca pramāṇam apramāṇam sampadyeta pramāṇa apramāṇayoḥ viśeṣa anupapatteḥ etena asamyak jñāna anantaram eva śarīra pāta abhāvaḥ kasmāt  aiti etad  parihṛtam jñāna utpatteḥ prāk ūrdhvam tad kāla janma antara sañcitānām vināśaḥ siddhaḥ  bhavati phala prāpti vighna niṣedha śruteḥ eva kṣīyante ca asya karmāṇi tasya tāvat eva ciram sarve pāpmānaḥ pradrūyante tam viditvā na lipyate karmaṇā pāpakena etam u ha eva ete na tarataḥ na enam kṛta akṛte tapataḥ etam ha vāva na tapati na bibheti kutaścana ityādi śrutibhyaḥ ca jñāna agniḥ sarva karmāṇi bhasmasāt kurute ityādi smṛtibhyaḥ ca yad tu ṛṇaiḥ pratibadhyata iti tad na avidyāvat vipaya tvāt avidyāvān hi ṛṇī tasya kartṛtva ādi upapatteḥ ayatra vā anyat iva syāt tatra anyaḥ  anyat paśyet iti hi vakṣyati ananyat sat vastu ātma ākhyam yatra avidyāyām satyām anya divasyāt timira kṛta dvitīya candravat tatra avidyā kṛta aneka kāraka apekṣam darśana ādi karma tad kṛtam phalam ca darśayati tatra anyaḥ  anyat paśyet  ityādinā yatra punar vidyāyām satyām avidyā kṛta anekatva bhrama prahāṇam tad kena kam paśyet  iti karma asambhavam darśayati tasmāt avidyāvat viṣaya eva ṛṇi tvam karma sambhavāt nā itaratra etad ca uttaratra vyācikhyāsiṣyamāṇaiḥ eva vākyaiḥ vistareṇa pradarśayiṣyāmaḥ tad yathā iha eva tāvat  atha yaḥ kaścid abrahma vid anyām ātmānaḥ  vyatiriktām yām kāñcid devatām upāste stuti namaskāra yāga bali upahāra praṇidhāna ādinā upa āste anyaḥ  asau  anātmā mattaḥ pṛthak  anyaḥ  aham asmi adhikṛtaḥ mayā asmai ṛṇivat pratikartavyam iti evam pratyayaḥ  veda vijānāti tattvam na sa kevalam evaṃbhūtaḥ  avidvān avidyā doṣavān eva kim tarhi yathā paśuḥ gavādiḥ vāhana dohana ādi upakāraiḥ upabhujyate evam sa ijyā ādi aneka upakāraiḥ upabhoktavya tvāt ekaikena deva ādīnām atas  paśuḥ iva sarva artheṣu karmasu adhikṛta iti arthaḥ etasya hi aviduṣaḥ  varṇa āśrama ādi pravibhāgavataḥ  adhikṛtasya karmaṇaḥ  vidyā sahitasya kevalasya ca śāstra uktasya kāryam manuṣyatva ādikaḥ  brahmānta utkarṣaḥ śāstra ukta viparītasya ca svābhāvikasya kāryam manuṣyatva ādika eva sthāvara antaḥ  apakarṣaḥ yathā ca etad tathā atha trayaḥ  vāva lokāḥ ityādinā vakṣyāmaḥ kṛtsnena eva adhyāya śeṣeṇa vidyayāḥ ca kāryam sarva ātma bhāva āpattiḥ iti etad saṅkṣepataḥ  darśitam sarvāhi iyam upaniṣad  vidyā avidyā vibhāga pradarśanena eva upakṣīṇā yathā ca eṣor athaḥ kṛtsnasya śāstrasya tathā pradarśayiṣyāmaḥ yasmāt evam tasmāt avidyāvantam puruṣam prati devāḥ  īśata eva vighnam kartum anugraham ca iti etad darśayati yathā ha vai loke bahavaḥ  gaḥ aśva ādayaḥ paśavaḥ  manuṣyam svāminam ātmanaḥ  adhiṣṭhātāram bhuñjyuḥ pālayeyuḥ evam bahu paśu sthānīya ekaikaḥ  avidvān puruṣaḥ  devān devān iti pitṛ ādi upalakṣaṇa artham bhunakti pālayati iti ima indra ādayaḥ  anye mattaḥ  mama īśita āraḥ  bhṛtya iva aham eṣām stuti namaskāra ijyā ādinā ārādhanam kṛtvā abhyudayam niḥśreyasam ca tad prattaṃphalam prāpsyāmi iti evam abhisandhiḥ tatra loke bahu paśumataḥ  yathā ekasmin  eva paśāvādīyamāne vyāghra ādinā apahiyamāṇe mahat apriyam bhavati tathā bahu paśu sthānīya ekasmin puruṣe paśu bhāvāt  vyuttiṣṭhati apriyam bhavati iti kim citram devānām bahu paśu apa haraṇa iva kuṭuṃbinaḥ tasmāt eṣām devānām tad na priyam kim tad  yad etad brahma ātma tattvam kathañcana manuṣyā vidyuḥ vijānīyuḥ tathā ca smaraṇam anugītāsu bhagavataḥ  vyāsasya kriyāvadbhiḥ hi kaunteya deva lokaḥ samāvṛtaḥ na ca etad iṣṭam devānām maryaiḥ upari vartanam atas  devāḥ paśūn iva vyāghra ādibhyaḥ  brahma vijñānāt vighnam ācikīrṣanti asmad upabhogya tvāt māvyuttiṣṭheyuḥ iti yam tu mumocayiṣanti tam śraddhā ādibhiḥ yokṣyanti viparītam aśraddhā ādibhiḥ tasmāt mumukṣuḥ deva ārādhana paraḥ śraddhā bhakti paraḥ praṇaya u apramādī syāt vidyā prāptim ati vidyām prati iti vā kākva etad pradarśitam bhavati deva apriya vākyena sūtritaḥ śāsra arthaḥ ātmā iti eva upāsīta iti tasya ca vyāci khya asitasya sārtha vādena tad āhuḥ yad brahma vidyayā ityādinā sambandha prayojane abhihite avidyāyāḥ ca saṃsāra adhikāra kāraṇa tvam uktam atha yaḥ  anyām devatām upāste ityādinā tatra avidvānṛṇī paśavat deva ādi karma kartavya tayā paratantra iti uktam kim punar deva ādi karmavya tvenimittam varṇā āśramāḥ ca tatra ke varṇāḥ iti ataidam ārabhyate yad nimitta sambaddheṣu karma svayam paratantra eva adhikṛtaḥ saṃsārī iti etasya eva arthasya pradarśanāya agni sarga anantaram indra ādi sargaḥ  na uktaḥ agneḥ tu sargaḥ prajāpateḥ sṛṣṭi paripūraṇāya pradarśitaḥ ayam ca indra ādi sargaḥ tatra eva draṣṭavyaḥ tad śeṣa tvāt iha tu sa eva āmidhīyate aviduṣaḥ karma adhikāra hetu pradarśanāya brahma vā idam agra āsīt yad agnim sṛṣṭvā agni rūpāpannam brahma brāhmaṇa jātyam i mānād brahma iti abhidhīyate vai idam kṣatra ādit jātam brahma eva abhinnam āsīt ekam eva na āsīt kṣatra ādi bhedaḥ tad brahma ekam kṣatra ādi paripālayitra ādi śūnyam sadam na vyabhavat  na vibhūtavat  karmaṇe na alam āsīt iti arthaḥ tatas tad brahma abrāhmaṇaḥ  asmi mama ittham kartavyam aiti brāhmaṇa jāti nimittam karma cikīrṣu ātmanaḥ karma kartṛtva vibhūtyai śreyaḥ rūpam praśasta rūpam ati asṛjata atiśayena asṛjata sṛṣṭavat  kim punar tad yad sṛṣṭam kṣatram kṣatriya jātiḥ tad vyakti bhedena pradarśayati yāni etāni prasiddhāni loke devatrā deveṣu kṣatrāṇi iti jāti ākhyāyām pakṣe bahuvacana smaraṇāt  vyakti bahutvāt vā bheda upacāreṇa bahuvacanam kāni punar tāni iti āha tatra abhipiktā eva viśeṣataḥ  nirdiśyante indraḥ  devānām rājā varuṇaḥ  yādasām somaḥ  brāhmaṇānām rudraḥ paśūnām parjanyaḥ  vidyut ādīnām yamaḥ pitṝṇām mṛtyu roga ādīnām īśānaḥ bhāsām iti evamādīni deva iṣu kṣatrāṇi tadanu indra ādi kṣatra devatā adhiṣṭhitāni purūravaḥ prabhṛtīni sṛṣṭāni eva draṣṭavyāni tad artha eva hi devakṣatra sargaḥ prastutaḥ yasmāt brahmaṇā atiśayena sṛṣṭam kṣatram tasmāt kṣatrāt param na asti brāhmaṇa jāteḥ api niyansṛ tasmāt brāhmaṇaḥ kāraṇa bhātaḥ  api kṣatriyasya kṣatriyam adhastāt vyavasthitaḥ san  uparisthitam upāste kka rājasūye kṣatra eva tad ātmīyam yaśaḥ khyāti rūpam brahma iti dadhāti sthāpayati rājasūya abhiṣiktena āsandyām sthitena rājñā āmantritaḥ  brahman  iti ṛtvij punar tam pratyāha tvam rājan brahmā asi iti tad etad abhidhīyate kṣatra eva tad yaśaḥ  dadhāti iti sā eṣā prakṛtā kṣatrasya yoniḥ eva yad brahma tasmāt yad yati rājā parama tām rājasūya abhiṣeka guṇam gacchati āpnoti brahmā eva brāhmaṇa jāti medha antatas  ante karma parisamāptau  upanikṣayati āśrayati svām yonim purohitam puraḥ nidhatta iti arthaḥ yaḥ tu punar bala abhimānāt svām yonim brāhmaṇa jātim brāhmaṇam ya u enam hinasti hiṃsati nyagbhāvena paśyati svāma ātmāyām eva sa yonim ṛcchati svam prasavam vicchinatti vināśayati svam prasavam vicchinatti vināśayati sa etad kṛtvā pāpīyān pāpa taraḥ  bhavati pūrvam api kṣatriyaḥ pāpa eva krūra tvāt ātma prasava hiṃsayā sutarām yathā loke śreyāṃsam praśastataram hiṃsitvā paribhūya pāpa taraḥ  bhavati tadvat  kṣatre sṛṣṭe api sa na eva vyabhavat  karmaṇe brahma tathā navī abhavat vitta upārjayituḥ abhāvāt  sa viśam asṛjata karma sādhana vitta upārjanāya kaḥ punar asau viṣ  yāni etāni deva jātāni sva arthe niṣṭhā ya ete deva jāti bhedā iti arthaḥ  gaṇaśas  gaṇam gaṇam ākhyāyante kathyante gaṇa prāyā hi viśaḥ prāyeṇa saṃhatā hi vitta upārjane samarthāḥ na ekaikaśas  vasavaḥ aṣṭa saṅkhyaḥ  gaṇaḥ tathā ekādaśa rudrāḥ dvādaśa ādityāḥ viśvedeva asrayodaśa viśvāyā apatyāni sarve vā devāḥ marutaḥ sapta sapta gaṇāḥ sa paricāraka bhāvāt punar api na eva vyabhavat  sa śaudram varṇam asṛjata śūdra eva śaudraḥ sva arthe aṇi vṛddhiḥ kaḥ punar asau śaudraḥ  varṇaḥ  yaḥ sṛṣṭaḥ pūṣaṇam puṇyati iti pūṣā kaḥ punar asau pūṣā iti viśeṣataḥ tad nirdiśati iyam pṛthivī pūpā svayam eva nirvacanam āha iyam hi idam sarvam puṣyati yad idam kiñca sa caturaḥ sṛṣṭvā api varṇān na eva vyabhavat  ugra tvāt kṣatrasya aniyata āśaṅkayā tad śreyaḥ rūpam atyasṛjata kim tad  dharmam  tad etad śreyaḥ rūpam sṛṣṭam kṣatrasya kṣatram kṣatrasya api niyantṛ ugrāt api ugram yad dharmaḥ  yaḥ  dharmaḥ tasmāt kṣatrasya api niyantṛ tvāt dharmāt param na asti tena hi niyamyante sarve tad katham iti ucyate athaḥ api abalīyān durbala taraḥ  balīyāṃsam ātmanaḥ  balavattaram api āśaṃsate kāmayate jetum dharmeṇa balena yathā loke rājñā sarva balavattamena api kuṭumbikaḥ  evam  tasmāt siddham dharmasya sarva balavattara tvāt sarva niyantṛ tvam yaḥ  vai sa dharmaḥ  vyavahāra lakṣaṇaḥ  laukikaiḥ vyavahriyamāṇaḥ satyam vai tad satyam iti yathā astra artha tā  sa eva anuṣṭhīyamānaḥ  dharma nāmā bhavati śāstra artha tvena jñāyamānaḥ tu satyam bhavati yasmāt evam tasmāt satyam yathāśāstram vadantam vyavahāra kāla āhuḥ samīpa sthā ubhaya viveka jñāḥ dharma vadati iti prasiddham laukikam nyāyam vadati iti tathā viparyayeṇa dharma vā laukikam vyavahāram vadantam āhuḥ satyam vadati śāstrāt anapetam vadati iti etad yad uktam ubhayam jñāyamānam anuṣṭhīyamānam ca etad dharma eva bhavati tasmāt sa dharmaḥ  jñāna anuṣṭānalakṣaṇaḥ śāstra jñāna nitarān  ca sarvān eva niyamayati tasmāt sa kṣatrasya api kṣatram atas tad abhimānaḥ  avidvān  tad viśeṣa anuṣṭhānāya brahma kṣatra viś śūdra nimitta viśeṣam abhimanyate tāni ca nisargata eva karma adhikāra nimittāni tad etad cāturvarṇyam sṛṣṭam brahma kṣatram viś śūdra iti uttara artham upasaṃhāraḥ yad tad sraṣṭṛ brahma tad agninaivana anyena rūpeṇa deveṣu brahma brāhmaṇa jātiḥ abhavat  brāhmaṇā brāhmaṇa svarūpeṇa manuṣyeṣu brahmā abhavat itareṣu varṇeṣu vikāra antaram prāpya kṣatriyeṇa kṣatriyaḥ  abhavat indra ādi devatā adhiṣṭhitaḥ vaiśyena vaiśyaḥ śūdreṇa śūdraḥ yasmāt kṣatra ādiṣu vikāra āpannam agnau brāhmaṇa e ca avikṛtam sraṣṭṛ brahma tasmāt agnau  eva deveṣu devānām madhye lokam karma phalam icchanti agni sambaddham karma kṛtvā iti arthaḥ tad artham eva hi tad brahma karma adhikaraṇa tvena agni rūpeṇa vyavasthitam tasmāt  tasmin  agnau karma kṛtvā tad phalam prārthayanta iti etad upapannam brahmaṇe manuṣyeṣu manuṣyāṇām punar madhye karma phala icchāyām na agni ādi nimitta kriyā apekṣā kim tarhi jāti mātra svarūpa pratilambhena eva puruṣa artha siddhiḥ yatra nu deva adhīnā puruṣa artha siddhiḥ tatra eva agni ādi sambaddha kriyā apekṣā smṛteḥ ca japyena eva tu saṃsidhyet brāhmaṇaḥ  na atra saṃśayaḥ kuryāt anyat na vā kuryāt maitraḥ  brāhmaṇa ucyate iti pārivrājya darśanāt ca tasmāt brahmaṇatva eva manuṣyeṣu lokam karma phalam icchanti yasmāt etābhyām hi brāhmaṇa agni rūpābhyām karma kartṛ adhi karaṇa rūpābhyām yad sraṣṭṛ brahma sākṣāt abhavat atra tu paramātma lokam agnau brāhmaṇe ca icchanti iti kecid  tad asat  avidyā adhikāre karma adhikāra artham varṇa vibhāgasya prastuta tvāt  pareṇa ca viśeṣaṇa at ya di hi atra loka śabdena para eva ātmocyeta pareṇa viśeṣaṇam anarthakam syāt asvam lokam adṛṣṭvā aiti sva loka vyatiriktaḥ ced agni adhīna tayā prārthyamānaḥ prakṛtaḥ  lokaḥ tatas  svam iti yuktam viśeṣaṇam prakṛta para loka nivṛtti artha tvāt sva tvena ca avyabhicārāt paramātma lokasya avidyā kṛtānām ca svatva vyabhicārāt  bravīti ca karma kṛtānām vyabhicāram akṣīyata eva aiti brahmaṇā sṛṣṭā varṇāḥ karma artham  tad ca karma dharma ākhyam sarvān eva kartavya tayā niyantṛ puruṣa artha sādhanam va tasmāt tena eva ced karmaṇā svar  lokaḥ paramātma ākhyaḥ  aviditaḥ  api prāpyate kim tasya eva padanīya tvena kriyata iti ata āha atha iti pūrva pakṣa vinivṛtti arthaḥ yaḥ kaścid  ha vai asmāt saṃsāri kāmakarma hetukāt agni adhīna karma abhimāna tayā vā brāhmaṇa jāti mātra karma abhimāna tayā vā āgantukāt asvabhūtāt lokāt  svam lokam ātma ākhyam ātma tvena avyabhicāri tvāt adṛṣṭā aaham brahma asmi aiti praiti mriyate  sa yadi api svar  lokaḥ aviditaḥ  avidyayā vyavahitaḥ  asva iva ajñātaḥ enam saṅkhyā pūraṇa iva laukika ātmānam na bhunakti na pālayati śoka moha bhaya ādi doṣa apanayena yathā ca loke vedaḥ  ananuktaḥ  anadhītaḥ karma ādi avabodhaka tvena na bhunakti anyat vā laukikam kṛṣi ādi karma akṛtam sva ātmanā anabhivyañjitam ātmīya phala pradānena na bhunakti evam ātmā svar  lokaḥ svena eva nitya ātma svarūpeṇa anabhivyañjitaḥ  avidyā ādi prahāṇena na bhunakti eva nanu kim sva loka darśana nimitta paripālanena karmaṇaḥ phala prāpti dhrauvyāt  iṣṭa phala nimittasya ca karmaṇaḥ  bāhulyāt  tad nimittam pālanam akṣayam bhaviṣyati tad na kṛtasya kṣayavat tvāt iti etad āha yad iha vai saṃsāre adbhutavat kaścid mahātmā api anevaṃvid  svam lokam yathā uktena vidhinā avidvān mahat bahu aśvamedha ādi puṇyam karma iṣṭa phalam eva nairantaryeṇa karoti aanena eva ānantyam mama bhaviṣyati aiti tad karma hāsya avidyāvataḥ  avidyā janita kāma hetu tvāt svapna darśana vibhrama udbhūta vibhūtivat antataḥ ante phala upabhogasya kṣīyata eva tad kāraṇayoḥ avidyā kāmayoḥ cala tvāt  kṛta kṣaya ghnauvya upapattiḥ tasmāt na puṇya karma phala pālana ānanti āśā asti eva ata ātmānam eva svam lokam aātmānam aiti asvam lokam aityasmin  arthe svam lokam iti prakṛta tvāt  iha ca sva śabdasya aprayogāt  upāsīta sa ya ātmānam eva lokam upāste tasya kim iti ucyate na hāsya karma kṣīyate  karma abhāvāt eva iti nitya anuvādaḥ yathā viduṣaḥ karma kṣaya lakṣaṇam saṃsāra duḥkham santatam evana tathā tad asya vidyata iti arthaḥ mithilāyām pradīptāyām na me dahyati kiñcana iti yadvat  sva ātma loka upāsakasya viduṣaḥ  vidyā saṃyogāt karma eva na kṣīyata iti apare varṣayanti loka śabda artham ca karma samavāyinam dvidhā parikalpayanti kila ekaḥ  vyākṛta avasthā karma āśrayaḥ  lokaḥ  hairaṇyagarbha ākhyaḥ tam karma samavāyinam lokam vyākṛtam paricchinnam ya upāste tasya kila paricchinnam ya upāste tasya kila paricchinna karma ātma darśinaḥ karma kṣīyate tam eva karma samavāyinam lokam avyākṛta avastham kāraṇa rūpam āpādya yaḥ tu upāste tasya aparicchinna karma ātma darśi tvāt tasya yaḥ tu upāste tasya aparicchinna karma ātma darśi tvāt tasya karma na kṣīyata iti bhavati iyam śobhanā kalpanā na tu śrautī sva loka śabdena prakṛtasya paramātmanaḥ  abhihita tvāt  svam lokam iti prastutya sva śabdam vihāya ātma śabda prakṣepeṇa punar tasya eva pratinirdeśāt ātmānam eva lokam upāsīta iti tatra karma samavāyi loka kalpanāyā anavasara eva pareṇa ca kevala vidyā viṣayeṇa viśeṣaṇāt  kim prajayā kariṣyāmaḥ  yeṣām naḥ ayam ātmāyam lokaḥ ithi putra karma apara vidyā kṛtebhyaḥ  hi lokebhyaḥ  viśinaṣṭi aayam ātmā naḥ lokaḥ aiti na hāsya kenacana karmaṇā lokaḥ  mīyata eṣaḥ  asya paramaḥ  lokaḥ iti ca taiḥ sa viśeṣaṇaiḥ asya eka vākyatā yuktā iha api svam lokam iti viśeṣaṇa darśanāt  asmāt kāmayata iti ayuktam iti ced  iha svar  lokaḥ paramātmā tad upāsanāt sa eva bhavati iti sthite yad yad kāmayate tad tad asmāt ātmanaḥ sṛjata ithi tad ātma prāpti vyatirekeṇa phala vacanam ayuktam iti ced  na sva loka upāsana stuti paratvat svasmāt eva lokāt sarvam iṣṭam sampadyata iti arthaḥ  na anyadataḥ prārthanīyam āpta kāma tvāt  ātmataḥ prāṇa ātmataḥ  āśā ityādi śruti antare yathā sarva ātma bhāva pradarśana arthaḥ  vā pūrvavat  yadi hi para eva ātmā sampadyate tadā yuktaḥ asmāt hi eva ātmanaḥ iti ātma śabda prayogaḥ svasmāt eva prakṛtāt ātmanaḥ  lokāt iti evam arthaḥ anyathā aavyākṛta avasthāt karmaṇaḥ  lokāt aiti sa viśeṣaṇam avakṣyāt  prakṛta paramātma loka vyāvṛttaye vyākṛta avasthā vyāvṛttaye ca na hi asmin prakṛte viśeṣite aśru tā antarāla ava sthā pratipattum śakyate athaḥ ayam vā ātmā atra avidvān varṇa āśrama ādi abhimānaḥ  dharmeṇa niyamyamānaḥ  deva ādi karma kartavya tayā paśuvat paratantra iti uktam kāni punar tāni karmāṇi yad kartavya tayā paśuvat paratantraḥ  bhavati ke vā te deva ādayaḥ  yeṣām karmabhiḥ paśuvat upakaroti iti tad ubhayam prapañcayati athaḥ iti ayam vākya upanyāsa arthaḥ ayam yaḥ prakṛtaḥ  gṛhī karma adhikṛtaḥ  avidvān śarīra indriya saṅghāta ādi viśiṣṭaḥ piṇḍa ātmā iti ucyate  sarveṣām varṇa āśrama ādi vihitaiḥ karmabhiḥ upakāri tvāt  kaiḥ punar  karma viśeṣaiḥ upakurvan keṣāṃ bhūta viśeṣāṇām lokaḥ iti ucyate sa gṛhī yad juhoti yad yajate yāgaḥ  devatām uddiśya svatva parityāgaḥ sa eva parityāgaḥ sa eva āsecana adhikaḥ  homaḥ tena homa yāga lakṣaṇena karmaṇā vaśya kartavya tvena devānām paśuvat paratantra tvena pratibaddha iti lokaḥ atha yad anubrūte svādhyāyam adhīte ahara hastena ṛṣīṇām lokaḥ atha yad pitṛbhyaḥ  nipṛṇāti prayacchati piṇḍa udaka ādi yad ca prajām icchati prajā artham udyamam karoti icchā ca utpatti upalakṣaṇa arthā prajām ca utpādayati iti arthaḥ tena karmaṇā vaśya kartavya tvena pitṛṇām bhogya tvena paratantraḥ  lokaḥ atha yad manuṣyān vāsayate gṛhe yad ca tebhyaḥ  vasadbhyaḥ  avasadbhyaḥ  vā arthibhyaḥ  aśanam dadāti tena manuṣyāṇām  atha yad paśubhyaḥ tṛṇa udakam vindati lambhayati tena paśūnām  ya dasya gṛheṣu śvāpadā vayāṃsi ca pipīlikābhiḥ saha kaṇa bali bhāṇḍa kṣālana ādi upajīvanti tena teṣām lokaḥ yasmāt ayam etāni karmāṇi kurvan  upakaroti deva ādibhyaḥ tasmāt yathā ha vai loke svāpya lokāya svasmai dehāya ariṣṭam avināśam svatva bhāva apracyutim icchet  svatva bhāva pracyuti bhayāt poṣaṇa rakṣaṇa ādibhiḥ sarvatas  paripālayet  evam ha evaṃvide asarva bhūta bhogyaḥ  aham anena prakāreṇa mayā avaśyam ṛṇivat pratikartavyam aiti evam ātmānam parikalpitavate sarvāṇi bhūtāni deva ādīni yathā uktāni ariṣṭim avināśam icchanti svatva apracyutyai sarvatas  saṃrakṣanti kuṭumbina iva paśūn tasmāt eṣām tad na priyam iti uktam tad vā etad tad etad yathā uktānām karmaṇām ṛṇavat avaśya kartavya tvam pañca mahāyajña prakaraṇe viditam kartavya tayā mīmāṃsitam vicāritam ca avadāna prakaraṇe brahma vidvān  ced tasmāt paśu bhāvāt kartavya tā bandhana rūpāt pratimucyate kena ayam kāritaḥ karma vandhana adhikāre avaśa iva pravartate na punar tad vimokṣṇa upāye vidyā adhikāra iti nanu uktam devāḥ  rakṣanti iti bāḍham karma adhikāra sva gocara ārūḍhān eva te api rakṣanti anyathā akṛta abhyāgama kṛta nāśa prasaṅgāt  na tu sāmānyam puruṣa mātram viśiṣṭa adhikārān ārūḍham  tasmāt bhavitavyam tena yena preritaḥ  avaśa eva bahirmukhaḥ  bhavati svasmāt lokāt  nanu avidyāsā avidyāvānihi bahirmukhībhūtaḥ pravartate sā api na eva pravartikā  vastu svarūpāvarṇa ātmikā hi sā pravartaka bīja tvam tu pratipadyate andha tvam iva garta ādi patana pravṛtti hetuḥ evam tarhi ucyatām kim tad  yad pravṛtti hetuḥ iti tad iha abhidhīyate eṣaṇā kāmaḥ saḥ asvābhāvikyām avidyāyām vartamānā bālāḥ parācaḥ kāmān anuyanti aiti kāṭhaka śrutau smṛtau ca kāma eṣa krodha eṣaḥ ityādi mānave ca sarvā pravṛttiḥ kāma hetukī eva iti sa eṣor athaḥ sa vistaraḥ pradarśyata iha ā adhyāya parisamāpteḥ ātmā eva idam agra āsīt  ātmā eva svābhāvikaḥ  avidvān kārya karaṇa saṅghāta lakṣaṇaḥ  varṇī agre prāc dāra sambandhātātmā iti abhidhīyate  tasmāt ātmanaḥ pṛthak bhūtam kāmyamānam jāyā ādi bheda rūpam na āsīt sa eva eka āsīt  jāyā ādi eṣaṇā bīja bhūtāḥ  vidyāvān eka eva āsīt  svābhāvikyā sva ātmani kartṛ ādi kāraka kriyā phala ātmaka tā dhyāra upalakṣaṇayā avidyā vāsanayā vāsitaḥ saḥ  akāmayata kāmitavān katham jāyā karma adhikāra hetu bhūtā me mama kartuḥ syāt tayā vinā aham anadhikṛta eva karmaṇi atas karma adhikāra sampattaye bhavet jāyā atha aham prajāyeya prajā rūpeṇa aham eva utpadyeya atha vittam me syāt karma sādhanam gavā ādi lakṣaṇam atha aham abhyudaya niḥśreyasa sādhanam karma kurvīya yena aham anṛṇī bhūtvā deva ādīnām lokān prāpnuyām tad karma kurvīya  kāmyāni ca putra vitta svarga ādi sādhanāni etāvān vai kāma etāvat viṣaya paricchinna iti arthaḥ etāvān eva hi kāmayitavyaḥ  viṣayaḥ  yad uta jāyā putra vitta karmāṇi sādhana lakṣaṇa eṣaṇā   lokāḥ ca trayaḥ  manuṣya lokaḥ pitṛ lokaḥ  deva loke  iti phala bhūtāḥ sādhana eṣaṇā tasmāt sā ekaiva eṣaṇā yā loka eṣaṇā sā ekā eva satyeṣaṇā sādhana apekṣā iti dvidhā atas avadhārayiṣyati ubhe hi ete eṣaṇe eva   iti phala artha tvāt sarva ārambhasya loka eṣaṇa artha prāptā uktā eva iti etāvān vā etāvān eva kāma iti avadhriyate bhojane abhihite tṛptiḥ na hi pṛthak abhidheyā tad artha tvāt bhojanasya te ete eṣaṇe sādhya sādhana lakṣaṇe kāmaḥ yena prayuktaḥ  avidvān avaśa eva kośakāravat ātmānam veṣṭayati karma mārga eva ātmānam praṇidadhat bahirmukhībhūtaḥ  na svam lokam pratijānāti tathā ca taittirīyake agnimugdhaḥ  ha eva dhūma tāntaḥ svam lokam na pratijānāti iti katham punar etāvat tvam avadhāryate kāmānām ananta tvāt  anantā hi kāmāḥ iti etad āśaṅkya hetum āha yasmāt  na icchan ca na icchan  api atas  asmāt phala sādhana lakṣaṇāt  bhūyaḥ adhikāram na vindet na labheta na hi loke phala sādhana vyatiriktam dṛṣṭam adṛṣṭam vā labdhavyam asti labdhavyaviṣayaḥ  hi kāmaḥ tasya ca etad vyatirekeṇa abhāvāt  yuktam vaktum aetāvān vai kāmaḥ aiti etad uktam bhavati dṛṣṭa artham adṛṣṭa artha  vā sādhya sādhana lakṣaṇam avidyāvat puruṣa adhikāra viṣayam eṣaṇā dvayam kāmaḥ atas  asmāt viduṣā vyutthātavyam iti yasmāt evam avidvān ātmā kāmaḥ  pūrvam kāmayāmāsa tathā pūrvataraḥ  api eṣā loka sthitiḥ prajāpateḥ ca evam eṣa sargam āsīt  saḥ  abibhet avidyayā tatas  kāma prayukta ekākyaramamāṇaḥ  asti upaghātāya striyam aicchat  tām samabhavat  tatas  sargaḥ  ayam āsīt iti hi uktam tasmāt tad sṛṣṭau etarhi etasmin  api kāla ekākī san prāc dāra kriyātaḥ kāmayate jāyā me syāt  atha prajāyeya atha vittam me syāt  atha karma kurvīya iti ukta artham vākyam sa evam kāmayamānaḥ sampādayan  ca jāyā ādīn yāvat sa eteṣām yathā uktānām jāyā ādīnām ekaikam api na prāpnoti akṛtsnaḥ  asampūrṇaḥ  aham iti evam tāvat ātmānam manyate pāriśeṣyāt samastān eva etān sampādayati yadā tadā tasya kṛtsna tā yadā tu na śaknoti kṛtsna tām sampādayitum tadā asya kṛtsnatva sampādanāya āha tasya u tasya ākṛtsna tu abhimāninaḥ kṛtsna tā iyam evam bhavati katham ayam kārya karaṇa saṅghātaḥ pravibhajyate  tatra manaḥ  anuvṛtti hi itarat sarvam kārya karaṇa jñātam iti manaḥ pradhānatva aja ātmā iva ātmā yathā jāyā ādīnām kuṭumba patiḥ ātmā iva tad anukāri tvān jāya ādi catuṣṭi asya evam iha api mana ātmā parikalpate kṛtsna tāyai tathā vāc jāyā manaḥ  anuvṛttitva sāmānyāt vācaḥ vāc iti śabdaḥ codana ādi lakṣaṇaḥ manasā śrotra dvāreṇa gṛhyate avadhāryate prasṛjyate ca iti manasaḥ  jāyā iva vāc  tābhyām ca vāc manasābhyām jāyā pati sthānīyābhyām prasūyate prāṇaḥ karma artham iti prāṇaḥ prajā iva tatra prāṇa ceṣṭā ādi lakṣaṇam karma cakṣuḥ mānuṣam vittam tad  dvividham vittam mānuṣam itarat ca atas viśinaṣṭi itara vitta nivṛtti artha mānuṣam iti gavā ādi hi manuṣya sambandhi vittam cakṣuḥ grāhyam karma sādhanam tasmāt tad sthānīyam tena sambandhāt cakṣuḥ grāhyam vittam  cakṣuṣā hi yasmāt tad mānuṣam vittam vindate gavā ādi upalabhata iti arthaḥ kim punar itarat vittam śrotram daivam deva viṣaya tvāt vijñānasya vijñānam daivam vittam  tad iha śrotram eva sampatti viṣayam kasmāt  śrotreṇa hi yasmāt tad daivam vittam vijñānam śṛṇoti  atas  śrotram eva tad iti kim punar etaiḥ ātma ādi vitta antaiḥ iha nirvartya karma iti ucyate ātmā eva ātmā iti śarīram ucyate katham punar ātmā karma sthānīyaḥ asya karma hetu tvāt  katham karma hetu tvam ātmanā hi śarīreṇa yatas  karma karoti tasya ākṛt snatva abhimānina evam kṛtsna tā sampannā yathā bāhyā jāyā ādi lakṣaṇā evam tasmāt sa eṣa pāṅktaḥ pañcabhiḥ nirvṛttaḥ pāṅktaḥ  yajñaḥ  darśana mātra nirvṛttaḥ  akarmiṇaḥ  api katham punar asya pañcatva sampatti mātreṇa yajña tvam ucyate yasmāt bāhyaḥ  api yajñaḥ paśu puruṣa sādhyaḥ sa ca paśuḥ puruṣaḥ ca pāṅkta eva yathā ukta manaa ādi pañcatva yogāt tad āha pāṅktaḥ paśu garva ādiḥ pāṅktaḥ puruṣaḥ paśu tve api adhikṛta tvena asya viśeṣaḥ puruṣasya iti pṛthak puruṣa grahaṇam kim bahunā pāṅktam idam sarvam karma sādhanam phalam ca yad idam kiñca yad kiñcid idam sarvam evam pāṅktam yajñam ātmānam yaḥ sampādayat  sa tad idam sarvam jagat ātma tvena āpnoti ya evam veda iti prathama adhyāye caturtham sṛṣṭi ādi sarva ātma tā brāhmaṇam yad sapta annāni medhayā avidyā prastutā tatra avidvān anyām devatām upāste aanyaḥ  asau  anyaḥ  aham asmi aiti sa varṇa āśrama abhimānaḥ karma kartavya tayā niyataḥ  juhoti ādi karmabhiḥ
