anyathā adhigata tvāt vastunaḥ na ca pramāṇam pramāṇa antareṇa virudhyate pramāṇa antara aviṣayam eva hi pramāṇa antaram jñāpayati na ca laukika pada padārtha āśrayaṇa vyatirekeṇa āgamena śakyam ajñātam vastu antaram avagamayitum tasmāt prasiddha nyāyam anusara tā na śakyā paramātmanaḥ sa avayava aṃśa aṃśitva kalpanā paramārthataḥ pratipādayitum kṣudrā visphuliṅgāḥ mama eva aṃśaḥ iti ca śrūyate smaryate ca iti ced na ekatva pratyaya artha paratvāt agneḥ hi visphuliṅgaḥ  agniḥ eva iti ekatva pratyaya arhe dṛṣṭaḥ  loke  tathā ca aṃśoṃ aśina ekatva pratyaya arhaḥ  tatra evam sati vijñāna ātmanaḥ paramātma vikāra aṃśatva vācakāḥ śabdāḥ paramātma vikāra aṃśatva vācakāḥ śabdāḥ paramātmā ekatva pratyaya ādhitsavaḥ upakrama upasaṃhārābhyām ca sarvāsu hi upaniṣatsu pūrvam eka tvam pratijñāya dṛṣṭāntaiḥ hetubhiḥ ca paramātmanaḥ  vikāra aṃśa ādi tvam jagataḥ pratipādya punar eka tvam upasaṃharati  tad yathā iha eva tāvat  idam sarvam yad ayam ātmā iti pratijñāya utpatti sthiti laya hetu dṛṣṭāntaiḥ vikāra vikāritva ādi ekatva pratyaya hetūn prati pādya anantaram abāhyam ayam ātmā brahma iti upasaṃhariṣyati tasmāt upakrama upasaṃhariṣyati tasmāt upakrama upasaṃhārābhyām ayam arthaḥ  niścīyate paramātmā ekatva pratyaya draḍhimna utpatti sthiti laya pratipādakāni vākyāni iti anyathā vākya bheda prasaṅgāt ca sarva upaniṣatsu hi vijñāna ātmanaḥ paramātmanā ekatva pratyayaḥ vidhīyata iti avipratipattiḥ sarveṣām upaniṣad vādinām tad vidhi eka vākya yoge ca sambhavati utpatti ādi vākyānām na pramāṇam asti phala antaram ca kalpayitavyam syāt  tasmāt utpatti ādi śrutaya ātmā ekatva pratipādana parāḥ atra ca sampradāya vida ākhyāyikām sampracakṣate kaścid kila rāja pitraḥ jāta mātra eva mātā pitṛbhyām apaviddhaḥ  vyādha gṛhe saṃvardhitaḥ saḥ  amuṣya vaṃśyatām ajānan vyādha jāti pratyayaḥ vyādha jāti karmāṇi eva anuvartate  na rājā asmi iti rāja jāti karmāṇi anuvartate yadā punar  kaścid parama kāruṇikaḥ  rāja putrasya rāja śrī prāpti yogyatām jānan  amuṣya putra tām bodhayati na tvam vyādhaḥ  amuṣya rājñaḥ putraḥ kathañcid vyādha gṛham anupraviṣṭaḥ iti sa evam bodhitaḥ tyaktvā vyādha jāti pratyaya karmāṇi pitṛpaitāmahīm ātmanaḥ padavīm anuvartate rājā aham asmi iti tathā kila ayam parasmāt agni visphuliṅga ādivat tad jātiḥ eva vibhakta iha deha indriya ādi gahane praviṣṭaḥ  asaṃsārī san deha indriya ādi saṃsāra dharmam anuvartate deha indriya saṅghātaḥ  asmi kṛśaḥ sthūlaḥ sukhī duḥkhī iti paramātma tām ajānan  ātmanaḥ na tvam etad ātmakaḥ param eva brahma āsya saṃsārī iti pratibodhita ācāryeṇa hitvā eṣaṇā traya anuvṛttim brahma eva asmi iti pratipadyate atra rāja putrasya rāja pratyayavat brahma pratyayaḥ dṛḍhībhavati visphuliṅgava deva tvam parasmāt brahmaṇaḥ  bhraṣṭa iti ukte visphuliṅgasya prāc agneḥ bhraṃśāt agni ekatva darśanāt tasmāt ekatva pratyaya dārḍhyāya suvarṇa maṇi loha agni visphuliṅga dṛṣṭāntāḥ na utpatti ādi bheda pratipādana parāḥ saindhava dhanavat prajñapti eka rasa nairantarya avadhāraṇāt ekadhā eva anudraṣṭavyam iti ca yadi ca brahmaṇaḥ citra paṭavat  vṛkṣa samudra ādivat ca utpatti ādi aneka dharma vicitra tā vijigrāhayiṣitā eka rasam saindhava ghanavat anantaram abāhyam iti na upasamahariṣyat ekadhā eva anudraṣṭavyam iti ca na prāyokṣyata ya iha na anā iva paśyati iti nindā vacanam ca tasmāt eka rūpa ekatva pratyaya dārḍhyāya eva sarva veda anteṣu utpatti sthiti laya ādi kalpanā na tad pratyaya karaṇāya na ca niravayavasya paramātmanaḥ  asaṃsāriṇaḥ saṃsāri eka deśa kalpanānyāyyā svatas  adeśa tvāt paramātmanaḥ adeśasya parasya eka deśa saṃsāritva kalpanāyām para eva saṃsārī iti kalpitam bhavet  atha para upādhikṛta eka deśaḥ parasya ghaṭa karaka ādi ākāśavat na tadā tatra vivekinām paramātmā eka deśaḥ pṛthak saṃvyavahāra bhāj iti buddhiḥ utpadyate avivekinām vivekinām ca upacaritā buddhiḥ dṛṣṭā iti ced  na vivekinām mithyā buddhi tvāt  vivekinām ca saṃvyavahāra mātra ālambana artha tvāt yathā kṛṣṇaḥ  raktaḥ ca ākāśa iti vivekinām api kadācid kṛṣṇa tā rakta tā ca ākāśasya saṃvyavahāra mātra ālambana artha tvam pratipadyata iti na paramārthataḥ kṛṣṇaḥ  raktaḥ  vā ākāśaḥ  bhavitum arhati atas  na paṇḍitaiḥ brahma svarūpa pratipatti viṣaye brahmaṇoṃ aśāṃśi eka deśa eka deśi vikāra vikāritva kalpanā kāryā sarva kalpanā apanayana artha sāra paratvāt sarva upaniṣadām atas  hitvā sarva kalpanām ā ākāśasya iva nirviśeṣa tā pratipattavyā ākāśavat sarva gataḥ ca nityaḥ na lipyate loka duḥkhena bāhyaḥ ityādi śruti śatebhyaḥ  na ātmānam brahma vilakṣaṇam kalpayet  uṣṇa ātmaka iva agnau śīta eka deśam prakāśa ātmake vā savitari tam eka deśam sarva kalpanā apanayana artha sāra paratvāt sarva upaniṣadām tasmāt nāma rūpa upādhi nimittā eva ātmani asaṃsāra dharmiṇi sarve vyavahārāḥ  rūpam rūpam pratirūpaḥ  babhūva sarvāṇi rūpāṇi vicitya dhīraḥ  nāmāni kṛtvā abhivadan yad āste iti evamādi mantra varṇebhyaḥ na svata ātmanaḥ saṃsāri tvam alaktaka ādi upādhi saṃyoga janita rakta sphaṭika ādi buddhivat bhrāntam eva na paramārthataḥ dhyāyati iva lelāyati iva na vardhate karmaṇā naḥ kanīyān na lipyate karmaṇā pāpakena samam sarveṣu bhūteṣu tiṣṭhantam śuni ca eva śvapāke ca ityādi śruti smṛti nyāyebhyaḥ paramātmanaḥ  asaṃsāritā eva ata eka deśaḥ  vikāraḥ śaktiḥ vā vijñāna ātmā anyaḥ  vā iti vikalpayitum niravayavatva abhyupagame viśeṣataḥ  na śakyate aṃśa ādi śruti smṛti vādāḥ ca ekatva arthāḥ na tu bheda pratipādakāḥ vivakṣita artha eka vākya yogāt iti avocāma sarva upaniṣadām paramātmā ekatva jñāpana paratve atha kimartham tad pratikūlor athaḥ vijñāna ātma bhedaḥ parikalpyata iti karma kāṇḍa prāmāṇya virodha parihārāya iti ekeca karma pratipādakāni hi vākyāni aneka kriyā kāraka phala bhoktṛ kartrāśrayāṇi vijñāna ātma bheda abhāve hi asaṃsāriṇa eva paramātmana ekatve katham iṣṭa phalāsu kriyāsu pravartayeyuḥ aniṣṭa phala abhyaḥ  vā kriyā abhyaḥ  nivartayeyuḥ kasya vā baddhasya mokṣāya upaniṣadā ārabhyeta api ca paramātmā ekatvau  ādi pakṣe katham paramātmā ekatva upadeśaḥ katham vā tad upadeśa grahaṇa phalam baddhasya hi bandha nāśāya upadeśaḥ tad abhāva upaniṣad śa asram nirviṣayam eva evam tarhi upaniṣad u ādi pakṣasya karma kāṇḍava ādi pakṣeṇa codya parihārayoḥ samānaḥ panthāḥ yena bheda abhāve karma kāṇḍam nirālambanam ātmānam na labhte prāmāṇyam prati tathā upaniṣad api evam tarhi yasya prāmāṇye sva artha vidhātaḥ  na asti tasya eva karma kāṇḍasya astu prāmāṇyam  upaniṣadām tu prāmāṇya kalpanāyām sva artha vighātaḥ  bhavet iti mā bhūt prāmāṇyam na hi karma kāṇḍam pramāṇam sat apramāṇam bhavitum arhati na hi pradīpaḥ prakāśyam prakāśayati na prakāśayati ca iti pratyakṣa ādi pramāṇa vipratiṣedhāt ca na kevalam upaniṣadaḥ  brahma eka tvam pratipādayantyaḥ sva artha vighātam karma kāṇḍa prāmāṇya vighātam ca kurvanti  pratyakṣa ādi niścita bheda pratipatti artha pramāṇaiḥ ca virudhyante tasmāt aprāmāṇyam eva upaniṣadām anya artha tā vāstu na tu eva brahma ekatva pratipatti artha tā na ukta uttara tvāt  pramāṇasya hi pramāṇa tvam apramāṇa tvam vā pramā utpādana anutpādana nimitm anyathā ced stambha ādīnām prāmāṇya prasaṅgāt śabda ādau prameye kiñcātas  yadi tāvat upaniṣadaḥ  brahma ekatva pratipatti pramām kurvanti katham apramāṇam bhaveyuḥ sa bhavān evam vadan vaktavyaḥ upaniṣad prāmāṇya pratiṣedha artham bhavataḥ  vākyam upaniṣad prāmāṇya pratiṣedham kim na karoti eva agniḥ vā rūpa prakāśam atha karoti yadi karoti bhavatu tadā pratiṣedha artham pramāṇam bhavat vākyam agniḥ ca rūpa prakāśa kaḥ  bhavet  pratiṣedha vākya prāmāṇye bhavati eva upaniṣadām prāmāṇyam atra bhavantaḥ  bruvantu kaḥ parihāra iti nanu atra pratyatrā mada avākya upaniṣad prāmāṇya pratiṣedha artha pratipattiḥ agnau ca rūpa prakāśana pratipattiḥ pramā kaḥ tarhi bhavataḥ pradveṣaḥ  brahma ekatva pratyaye pramām pratyakṣam kurvati iṣu upaniṣad su upalabhyamānāsu pratiṣedha anupapatteḥ śoka moha ādi nivṛttiḥ ca pratyakṣam phalam brahma ekatva pratipatti pāramparya janitam iti avocāma tasmāt ukta uttara tvāt upaniṣadam pratyaprāmāṇya śaṅkā tāvat na asti yad ca uktam sva artha vighāta kara tvāt aprāmāṇyam iti tad api na tad artha pratipatteḥ bādhaka abhāvāt na hi upaniṣadbhyaḥ brahma ekam eva advitīyam na eva ca iti pratipattiḥ asti yathā agniḥ uṣṇaḥ śītaḥ ca iti asmāt vākyāt viruddha artha dvaya pratipattiḥ abhyupagamya ca etad avocāma na tu vākya prāmāṇya samaya eṣa nyāyaḥ yad uta ekasya vākyasya aneka artha tvam sati ca aneka artha tve sva arthaḥ ca syāt  tad vighāta kṛt ca viruddhaḥ  anyor athaḥ na tu etad  vākya pramāṇakānām viruddham aviruddham ca evam vākyam anekam artham pratipādayati iti eṣa samayaḥ artha eka tvāt vyeka vākyatā na ca kānicid upaniṣad vākyāni brahma ekatva pratiṣedham kurvanti yad tu laukikam vākyam agniḥ uṣṇaḥ śītaḥ ca iti na tatra eka vākyatā tad eka deśasya pramāṇa antara viṣaya anuvādi tvāt agniḥ śīta iti etad ekam vākyam  agniḥ uṣṇa iti tu pramāṇa antara anubhava smārakam na tu svayam artha avabodhakam atas  na agniḥ śīta iti anena eka vākyatā pramāṇa antara anubhava smāraṇena eva upakṣīṇa tvāt yad tu viruddha artha pratipādakam idam vākyam iti manyate tad śīta uṣṇa padābhyām agni padasā mānādhikaraṇya prayoga nimittā bhrāntiḥ na tu eva ekasya vākyasya aneka artha tvam laukikasya vaidikasya vā yad ca uktam karma kāṇḍa prāmāṇya vighāta kṛt upaniṣad vākyam iti tad na  anya artha tvāt  brahma ekatva pratipādana parā hi upaniṣadaḥ  na iṣṭa artha prāptau sādhana upadeśam tasmin vā puruṣa niyogam vārayanti aneka arthatva anupapatteḥ eva na ca karma kāṇḍa vākyānām sva arthe pramā na utpadyate asādhāraṇe ced sva arthe pramām utpādayati vākyam kutaḥ anyena virodhaḥ syāt  brahma eka tve nirviṣaya tvāt pramāna utpadyata eva iti ced  na pratyakṣa tvāt pramāyāḥ darśa pūrṇamāsābhyām svarga kāmaḥ  yajeta brāhmaṇaḥ  na hantavyaḥ iti evamādi vākyebhyaḥ pratyakṣā pramā jāyamānā  asau na eva bhaviṣyati yadi upaniṣadaḥ  brahma eka tvam bodhayiṣyanti iti anumānam  na ca anumānam pratyakṣa virodhe prāmāṇyam labhate  tasmāt asat eva etad gīyate pramā eva na utpadyata iti api ca yathā prāptasya eva avidyā pratyupasthāpitasya kriyā kāraka phalasya āśrayaṇena iṣṭa aniṣṭa prāpti parihāra upāya sāmānye pravṛttasya tad viśeṣam ajānataḥ tad ācakṣāṇā śrutiḥ kriyākāraka phala bhedasya loka prasiddhasya satya tām asatya tām vā na ācaṣṭe na ca vārayati iṣṭa aniṣṭa phala prāpti parihāra upāya vidhi paratvāt yathā kāmyeṣu pravṛttā śrutiḥ kāmānām mithyājñāna prabhava tve sati api yathāprāptān eva kāmān upādāya tad sādhanāni eva vidhatte na tu kāmānām mithyājñāna prabhava tvāt anartha rūpa tvam ca iti na vidadhāti tathā nitya agnihotra ādi śāsram api mithyājñāna prabhavam kriyākāraka bhedam yathāprāptam eva ādāya iṣṭa viśeṣa prāptim aniṣṭa viśeṣa parihāram vā kim api prayojanam paśyat agni hotra ādīni karmāṇi vidhatte na avidyā gocarāsa dvastu viṣayam iti na pravartate yathā kāmyeṣu na ca puruṣā na pravarteḥ an  vidyāvantaḥ dṛṣṭa tvāt yathā kāminaḥ vidyāvatām eva karma adhikāra iti ced  na brahma ekatva vidyāyām karma adhikāra virodhasya ukta tvāt etena brahma eka tve nirviṣaya tvāt upadeśena tad grahaṇa phala abhāva doṣa parihāra uktaḥ  veditavyaḥ puruṣa icchā rāga ādi vaicitryāt ca anekā hi puruṣāṇam icchāḥ rāga ādayaḥ ca doṣā vicitrāḥ tatas ca bāhya viṣaya rāga ādi apahṛta cetasaḥ  na śāsram nivartayitum śaktam nā api svabhāvataḥ  bāhya viṣaya virakta cetasaḥ  viṣayeṣu pravartayitum śaktam  kintu śāsrāt etāvat eva bhavati idam iṣṭa sādhanam idam aniṣṭa sādhanam iti sādhya sādhana sambandha viśeṣa abhivyaktiḥ pradīpa ādivat tamasi rūpa ādi jñānam na tu śāsram bhṛtyān iva balāt nivartayati niyojayati vā dṛśyante hi puruṣā rāga ādi gauravāt śāsram api atikrāmantaḥ tasmāt  puruṣam ati vaicitryam apekṣya sādhya sādhana sambandha viśeṣān anekadhā upadiśati tatra puruṣāḥ svayam eva yathāruci sādhana viśeṣeṣu pravartante śāsram tu savitṛ pradīpa ādivat udāsta eva tathā kasyacid paraḥ  api puruṣa arthaḥ  apuruṣa arthavat avabhāsate  yasya yathā avabhāsaḥ sa tathārūpam puruṣa artham paśyati  tad anurūpāṇi sādhanāni upāditsate tathā ca artha vādaḥ  api trayāḥ prājāpatyāḥ prajāpatau pitari brahmacaryam ūṣuḥ ityādiḥ tasmāt na brahma eka tvam jñāpayiṣyantaḥ  vedāntā vidhi śāsrasya bādhakāḥ na ca vidhi śāsram etāvatā nirviṣayam syāt  na api ukta kāraka ādi bhedam vidhi śāsram upaniṣadām brahma eka tvam prati prāmāṇyam nivartayati sva viṣaya śūrāṇi hi pramāṇāni śrotra ādivat  tatra paṇḍitaṃmanyāḥ kecid sva citta vaśāt sarvam pramāṇam itaretara viruddham manyante tachā pratyakṣa ādi virodham api codayanti brahma eka tve śabda ādayaḥ kila śrotra ādi viṣayā bhinnāḥ pratyakṣata upalabhyante brahma eka tvam bruvatām pratyakṣa virodhaḥ sya at  tathā śrotra ādibhiḥ śabda ādi upalabdhāraḥ kartāraḥ ca dharma adharmayoḥ pratiśarīram bhinnā anumīyante saṃsāriṇaḥ  tatra brahma eka tvam bruvatām anumāna virodhaḥ ca tathā ca āgama virodham vadanti grāma kāmaḥ  yajeta paśu kāmaḥ  yajeta svarga kāmaḥ  yajeta iti evamādi vākyebhyaḥ  grāma paśu svarga ādi kāmāḥ tad sādhana ādi anuṣṭhātāraḥ ca bhinnā avagamyante atra ucyate te tu kutarka dūṣita antaḥkaraṇā brāhmaṇa ādi varṇa apasadā anukampanīyā āgama artha vicchinna sampradāya buddhaya iti katham śrotra ādi dvāraiḥ śabda ādibhiḥ pratyakṣata upalabhyamānaiḥ brahmaṇa eka tvam virudhyata iti vadantaḥ  vaktavyāḥ kim śabda ādīnām bhedena ākāśa eka tvam virudhyata iti atha na viruddhyate na tarhi pratyakṣa virodhaḥ yad ca uktam pratiśarīram śabda ādi upalabdha āraḥ  dharma adharmayoḥ ca kartāraḥ  bhinnā anumīyante tathā ca brahma eka tve anumāna virodha iti bhinnā kaiḥ anumīyanta iti praṣṭavyāḥ atha yadi brūyuḥ sarvaiḥ asmābhiḥ anumāna kuśalaiḥ iti ke yūyam anumāna kuśalā iti evam pṛṣṭānām kim uttaram śarīra indriya mana ātmasu ca pratyekam anumāna kauśala pratyākhyāne śarīra indriya manaḥ sādhanā ātmānaḥ  vayam anumāna kuśalāḥ aneka kāraka sādhya tvāt kriyāṇām iti ced  evam tarhi anumāna kauśalebhavatām anekatva prasaṅgaḥ  aneka kāraka sādhyā hi kriyā iti bhavadbhiḥ eva abhyupagatam tatra anumānam ca kriyā  sā śarīra indriya mana ātma sādhanaiḥ kārakaiḥ ātma kartṛkā nirvartyata iti etad pratijñātam tatra vayam anumāna kuśalā iti evam vadadbhiḥ śarīra indriya manaḥ sādhanā ātmānaḥ pratyekam vayam aneka  iti abhyupagatam syāt  ahaḥ anumāna kauśalam darśitam apuccha śṛṅgaiḥ tārkika balī vardaiḥ yaḥ  hi ātmānam eva na jānāti sa katham mūḍhaḥ tad gatam vā jānīyāt  tatra kim anuminoti kena vā liṅgena na hi ātmanaḥ svatas  bheda pratipādakam kiñcid liṅgam asti yena liṅgena ātma bhedam sādhayet   yāni liṅgāni ātma bheda sādhanāya nāma rūpavanti upanyasyanti tāni nāma rūpa gatāni upādhaya eva ātmanaḥ  ghaṭa karaka apavaraka bhūt chidrāṇi iva ākāśasya yad ākāśasya bheda liṅgam paśyati tad ā ātmanaḥ  api bheda liṅgam labheta saḥ  na hi ātmanaḥ paratas  api viśeṣam abhyupagacchadbhiḥ tārkika śataiḥ api bheda liṅgam ātmanaḥ  darśayitum śakyate  svatas tu dūrāt apanītam eva aviṣaya tvāt ātmanaḥ yad yad para ātma dharma tvena abhyupagacchati tasya tasya nāma rūpābhyām ca ātmanaḥ  anyatva abhyupagamāt  ākāśaḥ  vai nāma nāma rūpayoḥ nirvahitā te yad antarā tad brahma iti śruteḥ nāma rūpe vyākaravāṇi iti ca utpatti pralaya ātmake hi nāma rūpe tad vilakṣaṇam ca brahma atas  anumānasya eva aviṣaya tvāt kutaḥ anumāna virodhaḥ etena āgama virodhaḥ pratyuktaḥ yad uktam brahma eka tve yasmā upadeśaḥ yasya ca upadeśa grahaṇa phalam tad abhāvāt ekatva upadeśa ānarthakyam iti tad api na aneka kāraka sādhya tvāt kriyāṇām kaḥ ca udyaḥ bhavati ekasmin brahmaṇi nirupādhike na upadeśaḥ na upadeṣṭā na ca upadeśa grahaṇa phalam  tasmāt upaniṣadām ca ānarthakyam iti etad abhyupagatam eva atha aneka kāraka viṣaya ānarthakyam codyate na svatas  ñabhyupagama virodhāt ātma vādinām tasmāt tārkika cāṭa bhaṭa rājā praveśyam abhayam durgam idam alpabuddhi agamyam śāsra guru prasāda rahitaiḥ ca kaḥ tam madāmadam devam mad anyaḥ  jñātum arhati devaiḥ atra api vicikitsitam purā na eṣā tarkeṇa matiḥ āpaneyā vara prasāda labhyatva śruti smṛti vādebhyaḥ ca  tad ejati tad na ejati tad dūre tad vantike ityādi viruddha dharma samavāyitva prakāśaka mantra varṇebhyaḥ ca gītāsu ca mad sthāni sarva bhūtāni ityādi tasmāt para brahma vyatirekeṇa saṃsārī nāma na anyat vastu antaram asti tasmāt suṣṭhu ucyate brahma vā idam agra āsīt  tad ā ātmānam eva aved aham brahmā asmi na anyat atas  asti draṣṭṛ na anyat atas  asti śrotṛ ityādi śruti śatebhyaḥ tasmāt parasya eva brahmaṇaḥ satyasya satyam nāma upaniṣad parā yaḥ  ha vai śiśum sa ādhānam sa pratyādhānam sa sthūṇam sadā amam veda tasya idam phalam  kim tad  sapta sapta saṃkhyākān ha dviṣataḥ  dveṣa kartṝn bhrātṛvyān bhrātṛvyā hi dvividhā bhavanti dviṣantaḥ  adviṣantaḥ ca tatra dviṣantaḥ  ye bhrātṛvyāḥ tān dviṣataḥ  bhrātṛ vyāna varuṇaddhi  sapta ye śīrṣaṇyāḥ prāṇā viṣaya upalabdhi dvārāṇi tad prabhavā viṣaya rāgāḥ sahaja tvāt  bhrātṛvyāḥ te hi asya sva ātma sthām dṛṣṭim viṣaya viṣayām kurvanti tena te dveṣṭāraḥ  bhrātṛvyāḥ pratyak ātma īkṣaṇa pratiṣedha kara tvāt kāṭhake ca uktam parāñci khāni vyatṛṇat svayambhūḥ tasmāt parāṅpaśyati na antarātman ityādi tatra yaḥ śiśva ādīn veda teṣām yāthātmyam avadhārayati sa etān bhrātṛ vyāna varuṇaddhi apāvṛṇoti vināśayati tasmai phala śravaṇena abhimukhībhūtāya āha ayam vāva śiśuḥ kaḥ  asau yaḥ  ayam madhyamaḥ prāṇaḥ śarīra madhye yaḥ prāṇaḥ  liṅga ātmā yaḥ pañcadhā śarīram āviṣṭaḥ bṛhan pāṇḍara vāsaḥ soma rājan  iti uktaḥ yasmin vāc manaḥ prabhṛtīni karaṇāni viṣaktāni paḍvīśa śaṅku ni darśanāt  sa eṣa śiśuḥ iva viṣayeṣu itara karaṇavat apaṭutva at  śiśum sādhānam iti uktam kim punar tasya śiśoḥ vatsa sthānīyasya karaṇa ātmana ādhānam tasya idam eva śarīram ādhānam kārya ātmakam ādhīyate asmin  iti ādhānam  tasya hi śiśoḥ prāṇasya idam śarīram adhiṣṭhānam asmin hi karaṇāni adhiṣṭhitāni labdha ātmakāni upalabdhi dvārāṇi bhavanti na tu prāṇa mātre viṣaktāni tathā hi darśitam ajāta śatruṇā upasaṃhṛteṣu karaṇeṣu vijñānam ayaḥ  na upalabhyate śarīra deśa vyūḍheṣu tu karaṇeṣu vijñāna maya upalabhamāna upalabhyate tad ca darśitam pāṇi peṣa pratibodhanena idam pratyādhānam śiraḥ  pradeśa viśeṣeṣu prati pratyādhīyata iti pratyādhānam prāṇaḥ sthūṇā anna pāna janita aśaktiḥ prāṇaḥ  balam iti paryāyaḥ bala avaṣṭambhaḥ  hi prāṇaḥ  asmin śarīre sa yatra ayam ātma abalyam nyetya saṃmoham iva iti darśanāt  yathā vatsaḥ sthūṇā avaṣṭambha evam śarīra pakṣapātī vāyuḥ prāṇaḥ sthūṇā iti kecid  annam dāma annam hi bhuktam tredhā pariṇamate ya  sthūlaḥ pariṇāmaḥ sa etad dvayam bhūtvā imām apyeti mūtram ca purīṣam ca yaḥ  madhyamaḥ  rasaḥ sa rasaḥ  lohita ādi krameṇa sva kāryam śarīram sāptadhātukam upacinoti  sva yoni anna āgame hi śarīram upacīyate anna mayatva at viparyaye apakṣīyate patati yaḥ tu aṇiṣṭhaḥ  rasaḥ amṛtam ūrk prabhāvaḥ iti ca kathyate sa nābheḥ ūrdhvam hṛdaya deśam āgatya hṛdayāt viprasṛteṣu dvāsaptati nāḍī sahasreṣu anupraviśya yad tad karaṇa saṅghāta rūpam liṅgam śiśu sañjñakam tasya śarīre sthiti kāraṇam bhavati balam upajanayat sthūṇa ākhya m tena annam ubhayatas  pāśavat sadāmavat  prāṇa śarīrayoḥ nibandhanam bhavati tam etāḥ sapta akṣitaya upatiṣṭhantetam karaṇa ātmakam prāmam śarīre anna bandhanam cakṣuṣyūḍham etā vakṣyamāṇāḥ sapta sapta saṅkhyākā akṣitayaḥ  akṣiti hetu tvāt upatiṣṭhante yadi api mantra karaṇe tiṣṭhatiḥ upapūrva ātmanā īpadī bhavati iha api sapta devatā abhidhānāni mantra sthānīyāni karaṇā ni tiṣṭhateḥ atas  atra api ātmanepadam na viruddham kāḥ tā akṣitayaḥ iti ucyante tad tatra yā imāḥ prasiddhāḥ akṣat nakṣaṇi lohinyaḥ  lohitā rājayaḥ rekhāḥ tābhiḥ dvāra bhūtābhiḥ enam madhyamam prāṇam rudraḥ  anvāyattaḥ  anugataḥ  atha yā akṣat nakṣaṇya apaḥ  dhūma ādi saṃyogena abhivyajyamānāḥ tābhiḥ adbhiḥ dvāra bhūtābhiḥ parjanyaḥ  devatā ātmā anvāyattaḥ  ñanugata upatiṣṭhata iti arthaḥ sa ca anna bhūtaḥ  akṣitiḥ prāṇasya  parjanye varṣati ānandinaḥ prāṇā bhavanti iti śruti antarāt yā kanīnakā dṛś chaktiḥ tayā kanīnakayā dvāreṇa ādityaḥ  madhyamam prāṇam upatiṣṭhate yad kṛṣṇam cakṣuṣi tena enam agniḥ upatiṣṭhate yad śuklam cakṣuṣi tena indraḥ adharayā vartanyā pakṣmaṇa enam pṛthivī anvāyattā adharatva sāmānyāt  etāḥ sapta anna bhūtāḥ prāṇasya santatam upatiṣṭhante iti evam yaḥ  veda tasya etad phalam na asya annam kṣīyate ya evam veda tad tatra etasmin  arthe eṣa ślokaḥ  mantraḥ  bhavati arvāc bilaḥ camasa ityādiḥ tatra mantra artham ācaṣṭe śrutiḥ arvāc bilaḥ camasa ityādiḥ tatra mantra artham ācaṣṭe śrutiḥ arvāc bilaḥ camasa ūrdhva budhna iti kaḥ punar asau  arvāc bilaḥ camasa ūrdhva budhnaḥ idam tad  śiraḥ camasa ākāram hi tad  katham eṣa hi arvāc bilaḥ mukhasya bila rūpa tvāt  śirasaḥ  budhna ākāra tvāt ūrdhva budhnaḥ tasmin yaśaḥ  nihitam viśvarūpam iti yathā somaḥ camase evam tasmin śirasi viśvarūpam nānā rūpam nihitam sthitam bhavati kim punar tad  yaśaḥ prāṇā vai yaśaḥ  viśva rūpam prāṇāḥ śrotra ādayaḥ  vāyavaḥ ca marutaḥ saptadhā teṣu prasṛtā yaśaḥ iti etad āha mantraḥ śabda ādi jñāna hetu tvāt  tasya āsata ṛṣayaḥ sapta tīra  iti prāṇāḥ parispanda ātmakāḥ ta eva ca ṛṣayaḥ prāṇau  etad āha mantraḥ vāc aṣṭamī brahmaṇā saṃvidānā iti brahmaṇā saṃvādam kurvatī aṣṭamī bhavati tad hetum āha vāc hi aṣṭamī brahmaṇā saṃvitta iti imau  eva gotama bharadvājau karṇau ayam eva gotamaḥ  ayam bharadvājaḥ  dakṣiṇaḥ ca uttaraḥ ca viparyayeṇa vā tathā cakṣuṣī upadiśan  uvāca imau  eva viśvāmitra jamadagnī dakṣiṇam viśvāmitra uttaram jamadagniḥ viparyayeṇa vā imau  eva vasiṣṭha kaśyapau nāsike upadiśan  uvāca  dakṣiṇaḥ puṭaḥ  bhavati vasiṣṭhaḥ uttaraḥ kaśyapaḥ pūrvavat  vāc eva atriḥ adana kriyā yogāt saptamaḥ vācā hi annam adyate tasmāt attiḥ ha vai prasiddham nāma etad  attṛ tvā adattiḥ iti attiḥ eva san yad atriḥ iti ucyate parokṣeṇa sarvasya etasya anna jātasya prāṇasya atri nirvacana vijñāna ādattā bhavati atta eva bhavati na amuṣmin  annena punar  pratipadyata iti etad uktam bhavati sarvam asya annam bhavati iti ya evam etad yathā uktam prāṇayāthātmyam veda sa evam madhyamaḥ prāṇaḥ  bhū tvā aādhāna pratyādhāna gataḥ  bhoktā eva bhavati na bhojyam bhojyād vyāvartata iti arthaḥ iti dvitīyam brāhmaṇam tatra dvi rūpam brahma pañcabhūta janita kārya karaṇa sambaddham mūrta amūrta ākhyam martya amṛta svabhāvam tad janita vāsanā rūpam ca sarvan jñam sarva śakti sā upākhyam bhavati kriyā kāraka phala ātmakam ca sarva vyavahāra āspadam tad eva brahma vigata sarva upādhi viśeṣam samyak darśana viṣayam ajam ajaram amṛtam abhayam vāc manasayoḥ api aviṣayam advaita tvāt  aneti na iti aiti nirdiśyate tatra yad apoha dvāreṇa aneti na iti aiti nirdiśyate brahma te ete dve vāva vāvaśabdaḥ  avadhāraṇa arthaḥ dve eva iti arthaḥ brahmaṇaḥ paramātmanaḥ  rūpe rūpyate yābhyāma rūpam param brahma avidyā adhyāropyamāṇābhyām ke te dve mūrtam ca eva mūrtam eva ca tathāmūrtam ca amūrtam eva ca iti arthaḥ antarṇītasvātma viśeṣaṇe mūrta amūrte dve eva iti avadhāri ete kāni punar tāni viśeṣaṇāni mūrta amūrtayoḥ iti ucyante martyam ca martyam maraṇa dharmi amṛtam ca tad viparītam sthitam ca paricchinnam gati pūrvakam yad sthāsnu yad ca yāti iti yad  vyāpi aparicchinnam sthita viparītam sat ca sat iti anyebhyaḥ  viśeṣyamāṇa āsādhāraṇa dharma viśeṣavat tyat ca tad viparītam atyat aiti iva sarvadā parokṣa abhidhāna arham tad etad mūrtam mūrcchita avayavam itaretara anupraviṣṭa avayavam ghanam saṃhatam iti arthaḥ kim tad  yad anyat kasmāt anyat  vāyoḥ ca antarikṣāt ca bhūta dvayāt  pariśeṣāt  pṛthivī ādi bhūta trayam etad martyam yad etad mūrta ākhyam bhūta trayam idam martyam maraṇa dharmi  kasmāt  yasmāt sthitam etad paricchinnam hi artha antareṇa samprayujyamānam virudhyate yathā ghaṭaḥ stambha kuṇḍya ādinā  tathā mūrtam sthitam paricchinnam artha antara sambandhi tator atha antara virodhāt martyam  etad sat viśeṣya māṇāsa ādhāraṇa dharmavat tasmāt hi paricchinnam paricchinna tvāt martyam atas  mūrtam mūrta tvāt vā martyam martya tvāt sthitam sthita tvāt sat atas  anyonya avyabhicārāt caturṇām dharmāṇām yatheṣṭam viśeṣaṇa viśeṣya bhāvaḥ  hetu hetum at bhāvaḥ ca darśayitavyaḥ sarvathā api tu bhūta trayam catuṣṭaya viśeṣaṇa viśiṣṭam mūrtam rūpam brahmaṇaḥ tatra caturṇām ekasmin gṛhīte viśeṣaṇe itarat gṛhītam eva viśeṣaṇam iti āha tasya etasya mūrtasya etasya martyasya etasya sthitasya etasya sataḥ catuṣṭaya viśeṣaṇasya bhūta trayasya iti arthaḥ eṣa rasaḥ sāra iti arthaḥ trayāṇām hi bhūtānām sāriṣṭhaḥ savitā etad sārāṇi trīṇi bhūtāni yata etad kṛta vibhajyamāna rūpa viśeṣaṇāni bhavanti  ādhidaivikasya kāryasya etad rūpam yad savitā yad etad maṇḍalam tapati sataḥ  bhūta trayasya hi yasmāt eṣa rasa iti etad  gṛhyate mūrtaḥ hi eṣa savitā tapati sāriṣṭhaḥ ca yadtva adhidaivikam karaṇam maṇḍalasya abhyantaram tad vakṣyāmaḥ atha amūrtam atha adhunā amūrtam ucyate vāyuḥ ca antarikṣam ca yad pariśeṣitam bhūta dvayam etad amṛtam amūrta tvāt sthitam atas  avirudhyamānam kenacid  amṛtam amaraṇa dharmi etad yad sthita viparītam vyāpi aparicchinnam yasmāt  ayat aetat  anyebhyaḥ  apravibhajyamāna viśeṣam atas tyat atyat aiti parokṣa abhidhāna arham eva pūrvavat  tasya etasya amūrtasya tasya amṛtasya etasya yata etasya tyasya catuṣṭaya viśeṣaṇasya amūrtasya eṣa rasaḥ kaḥ  asau yaeṣa etasmin maṇḍale puruṣaḥ karaṇa ātmakaḥ  hiraṇyagarbhaḥ prāṇa iti abhidhīyate yaḥ sa eṣaḥ  amūrtasya bhūta dvayasya rasaḥ pūrvavat sāriṣṭhaḥ etad puruṣa sāram cāmūrtam bhūta dvayamhairaṇyagarbha liṅga ārambhāya hi bhūta dvaya abhivyaktiḥ avyākṛtāt  tasmāt tad arthyāt tad sāram bhūta dvayam tyasya hi eṣa rasaḥ yasmāt yaḥ  maṇḍala sthaḥ puruṣaḥ  maṇḍalavat na gṛhyate sāraḥ ca bhūta dvayasya tasmāt asti maṇḍala sthasya puruṣasya bhūta dvayasya ca sādharmyam tasmāt yuktam prasiddhavat vetu upādānam tyasya hi eṣa rasa iti rasaḥ kāraṇam hiraṇyagarbha vijñāna ātmā cetana iti kecid  tatra ca kila hiraṇyagarbha vijñāna ātmanaḥ karma vāyu antarikṣayoḥ prayoktṛ tad karma vāyu antarikṣa ādhāram sat anyeṣām bhūtānām prayoktṛ bhavati tena sva karmaṇā vāyu antarikṣayoḥ prayoktā iti tayaḥ rasaḥ kāraṇam ucyata iti tad na mūrta rasena atulya tvāt  mūrtasya tu bhūta trayasya rasaḥ  mūrtam eva maṇḍalam dṛṣṭam bhūta trayasya rasaḥ  mūrtam eva maṇḍalam dṛṣṭam bhūta traya samāna jātīyam na cetanaḥ  tathā mūrtayoḥ api bhūtayoḥ tad samāna jātīyena eva amūrtasena yuktam bhavitum  vākya pravṛtteḥ tulya tvāt yathā hi mūrta amūrte catuṣṭaya dharmavatī vibhajyete tathā rasa rasavatoḥ api mūrta amūrtayoḥ tulyena eva nyāyena yuktaḥ  vibhāgaḥ na tu ardha vaiśasam mūrta rase api maṇḍala upādhiḥ cetanaḥ  vivakṣyata iti ced  atyalpam idam ucyate sarvatra eva tu mūrta amūrtayoḥ brahma rūpeṇa vivakṣita tvāt  puruṣa śabdaḥ  acetane anupapanna iti ced   na pakṣa puccha ādi viśiṣṭasya eva liṅgasya puruṣa śabda darśanāt  na vā ittham santaḥ śakṣyāmaḥ prajāḥ prajanayitum imān sapta puruṣān ekam puruṣam karavāma iti ta etān sapta puruṣān ekam puruṣam akurvan iti ādau anna rasa maya ādiṣu ca śruti antare puruṣa śabda prayogāt  iti adhidaivatam iti ukta upasaṃhāraḥ  adhyātma vibhāga ukti arthaḥ atha adhunā adhyātmam mūrtā mūrtayoḥ vibhāga ucyate kim tad mūrtam idam eva kim ca idam yad anyat prāṇāt cavāyoḥ yaḥ ca ayam antarabhyantare ātman  ātmani ākāśaḥ kham śarīra sthaḥ ca yaḥ prāṇa etad  dvayam varjayitvā yad anyat śarīra ārambhakam bhūta trayam etad martyam ityādi samānam anyat pūrveṇa etasya sataḥ  hi eṣa rasaḥ yad cakṣuḥ iti  ādhyātmikasya śarīra ārambhakasya kāryasya eṣa rasaḥ sāraḥ  tena hi sāreṇa sāravat idam śarīram samastam yathā adhidaivatam āditya maṇḍalena prāthamyāt ca cakṣuṣī eva prathame sambhavataḥ sambhavata iti tejaḥ  rasaḥ  niranartatā agniḥ iti liṅgāt   taijasam hi cakṣuḥ  etad sāram  taijasam hi cakṣuḥ  etad sāram ādhyātmikam bhūta trayam  sataḥ  hi eṣa rasa iti mūrtatva sāra tve hetu arthaḥ atha adhunā amūrtam ucyate yad pariśeṣitam bhūta dvayam prāṇaḥ ca yaḥ ca ayam antarātman  ākāśaḥ etad amūrtam anyat pūrvavat  etasya tyasya eṣa rasaḥ sāraḥ yaḥ  ayam dakṣiṇe akṣan puruṣaḥ dakṣiṇe akṣan  iti viśeṣa grahaṇam śāstra pratyakṣa tvāt liṅgasya hi dakṣiṇe akṣṇi viśeṣataḥ  adhiṣṭhātṛ tvam śāsatrasya pratyakṣam sarva śrutiṣu tathā prayoga darśanāt  tyasya hi eṣa rasa iti pūrvavat viśeṣataḥ agrahaṇāt amūrtatva sāra tve eva hetu arthaḥ tasya ha etasya puruṣasya karaṇa ātmanaḥ  liṅgasya rūpam vakṣyāmaḥ  vāsanā mayam mūrta amūrta vāsanā vijñāna maya saṃyoga janitam vicitram paṭa bhitti citravat māya indrajāla mṛga tṛṣṇikā upamam sarva vyāmoha āspadam etāvat mātram eva ātmā iti vijñāna vādinaḥ  vaināśikā yatra bhrāntāḥ etad eva vāsanā rūpam paṭa rūpavat ātmanaḥ  dravyasya guṇa iti naiyāyikā vaiśeṣikāḥ ca sampratipannāḥ idam ātma artham triguṇam svatantram pradhāna āśrayam puruṣa arthena hetunā pravartata iti sāṅkhyāḥ aupaniṣadaṃmanyā api kecid prakriyām racayanti mūrta amūrta rāśiḥ ekaḥ paramātma rāśiḥ uttamaḥ tābhyām anyaḥ ayam madhyamaḥ kila tṛtīyaḥ kartrā bhoktrā vijñāna mayena ajāta śatru pratibodhitena saha vidyā karma pūrva prajñā samudāyaḥ  prayoktā karmarāśiḥ prayojyaḥ pūrva uktaḥ  mūrta amūrta bhūta rāśiḥ sādhanam ca iti tatra ca tārkikaiḥ saha sandhim kurvanti liṅga āśrayaḥ ca eṣa karma rāśiḥ iti uktvā punar tatasrasyantaḥ sāṅkhyatva bhayāt sarvaḥ karmarāśiḥ puṣpa āśraya iva gandhaḥ puṣpa viyoge api puṭa taila āśrayaḥ  bhavati tadvat  liṅga viyoge api paramātmā eka deśam āśrayati sa paramātmā eka deśaḥ kila anyata āgatena guṇena karmaṇā sa guṇaḥ  bhavati nirguṇaḥ  api san sa kartā bhoktā badhyate mucyate ca vijñāna ātmā iti vaiśeṣika cittam api anusaranti  sa ca karma rāśiḥ bhūta rāśeḥ āgantukaḥ svatas  nirguṇa eva paramātma eka deśatva at svata utthitā avidyā anāgantukā api ūṣara vadanātma dharmaḥ iti anayā kalpanayā sāṅkhya cittam anuvartante sarvam etad tārkikaiḥ saha sāmañjasya kalpanayā ramaṇīyam paśyanti lopa niṣad siddhāntam sarva nyāya virodham ca paśyanti  katham uktā eva tāvat sāva yava tve paramātmanaḥ saṃsāritva sa vraṇatva karma phala deśa saṃsāritva sa vraṇatva karma phala deśa saṃsaraṇa anupapatti ādayaḥ  doṣāḥ nitya bhede ca vijñāna ātmanaḥ pareṇa ekatva anupapattiḥ liṅgam eva iti ced paramātmana upacarita deśa tvena kalpitam ghaṭa karaka bhū chidra ākāśa ādivat  tathā liṅga viyoge api paramātma deśa āśrayaṇam vāsanāyāḥ avidyāyāṣca svata utthānam ūṣaravat  ityādi kalpanā anupapannā eva na ca vā asya deśa vyatirekeṇa vāsanāyā vastu antara sañcaraṇam manasā api kalpayitum śakyam na ca śrutayaḥ gacchanti kāmaḥ saṅkalpaḥ  vicikitsā hṛdaye hi eva rūpāṇi dhyāyati iva lelāyati iva kāmā ye asya hṛdi śritāḥ tīrṇaḥ  hi tadā sarvān śokān hṛdayasya ityādyāḥ na ca āsām śrutīnām śrutādartha antara kalpanā nyāyyā ātmanaḥ para brahmatva upapādana artha para tvāt āsām etāvat mātra artha upakṣaya tvāt ca sarva upaniṣadām tasmāt śruti artha kalpanā kuśalāḥ sarva eva upaniṣad artham anyathā kurvanti tathā api veda arthaḥ ced syāt kāmam bhavatu na me dveṣaḥ na ca adva vāva brahmaṇaḥ  rūpe aiti rāśi traya pakṣe samañjasam yadā tu mūrta amūrte tad janita vāsanāḥ ca mūrta amūrte dve rūpe brahma ca rūpi tṛtīyam na ca anyat caturtham antarāletadā etad anukūlam avadhāraṇam dve eva brahmaṇaḥ  rūpe iti anyathā brahma eka deśasya vijñāna ātmanaḥ  rūpe iti kalpyam paramātmanaḥ  vā vijñāna ātma dvāreṇa iti tadā ca rūpe eva iti dvivacanam asamañjasam rūpāṇi iti vāsanābhiḥ saha bahuvacanam yuktataram syāt  dve ca mūrta amūrte vāsanāḥ ca tṛtīyam iti atha mūrta amūrte eva paramātmanaḥ  rūpe vāsanāḥ tu vijñāna ātmana iti ced  tadā vijñāna ātma dvāreṇa vikriyamāṇasya paramātmanaḥ iti iyam vācā uyuktiḥ anarthikā syāt  vāsanāyā api vijñāna ātma dvāra tvasya aviśiṣṭa tvāt na ca vastu vaḥ tu antara dvāreṇa vikriyata iti mukhyayā vṛttyā śakyam kalpayitum na ca vijñāna ātmā paramātmanaḥ  vastu antaram tathā kalpanāyām siddhānta hānāt tasmāt  veda artha mūḍhānām sva citta prabhavā evamādi kalpanā akṣara bāhyāḥ na hi akṣara bāhyaḥ  veda arthaḥ  veda artha upakārī vā nirapekṣa tvāt vedasya prāmāṇyam prati tasmāt rāśi traya kalpanā asamañjasā ayaḥ  ayam dakṣiṇe akṣan puruṣaḥ aiti liṅga ātmā prastutaḥ  adhyātme adhidaive ca aya eṣa etasmin maṇḍale puruṣaḥ aiti atasya aiti prakṛta upādānāt sa eva upādīyate yaḥ  asau tyasya amūrtasya rasaḥ  na tu vijñāna mayaḥ nanu vijñāna mayasya eva etāni rupāṇi kasmāt na bhavanti vijñāna mayasya api prakṛta tvāt  atasya aiti ca prakṛta upādānāt  na evam vijñāna mayasya arūpi tvena vijijñāpayiṣita tvāt ya di hi tasya eva vijñāna mayasya etāni māhārajana ādīni rūpāṇi syuḥ tasya ava aneti na iti aityana ākhyeya rūpa tayā ādeśaḥ  na syāt  nanu anyasya eva āsādeśaḥ  na tu vijñāna mayasya iti na ṣaṣṭha ante upasaṃhārāt  vijñāta āram are kena vijānīyāt  iti vijñāna mayam prastutya sa eṣa na iti na iti iti vijñāpayiṣyāmi iti ca pratijñāyā arthavat tvāt  yadi ca vijñāna mayasya eva asaṃvyavahāryam ātma svarūpam jñāpayitum iṣṭam syāt pradhvasta sarva upādhi viśeṣam tatas  iyam pratijñā arthavatī syāt  yena asau jñāpitaḥ  jānāti ātmānam eva aham brahma asmi iti śāsra niṣṭhām prāpnoti na bibheti kutas ca atha punar anyaḥ  vijñāna mayaḥ anyaḥ aneti na iti iti vyapadiśyate tadā anyadadaḥ  brahma anyaḥ  aham asmi iti viparyayaḥ gṛhītaḥ syāt  na aātmānam eva avedaham brahmā asmi iti tasmāt  atasya ha etasya iti liṅga puru śasyai vaitāni rūpāṇi satyasya ca satye paramātma svarūpe vaktavye niravaśeṣam satyam vaktavyam  satyasya ca viśeṣa rūpāṇi vāsanāḥ tāsām imāni rūpāṇi ucyante etasya puruṣasya prakṛtasya liṅga ātmana etāni rūpāṇi kāni tāni iti ucyante yathā loke mahārajanam haridrā tayā raktam māhāra janam yathā vāsaḥ  loke evam strī ādi viṣaya saṃyoge tādṛśam vāsanā rūpam rañjana ākāra mutpadyate cittasya yena asau puruṣaḥ  rakta iti ucyate vasra ādivat  yathā ca loke pāṇḍu āvikam averidam āvikam ūrṇa ādi yathā ca tad pāṇḍuram bhavati tathā anyat vāsanā rūpam yathā ca loke indragopa u atyanta raktaḥ  bhavati evam asya vāsanā rūpam kvacid viṣaya viśeṣa apekṣayā rāgasya tāratamyam kvacid puruṣa citta vṛtti apekṣayā yathā ca loke agni arciḥ bhāsvaram bhavati tathā kvacid kasyacid vāsanā rūpam bhavati yathā pumḍarīkam śuklam tadvat api ca vāsanā rūpam kasyacid bhavati yathā sakṛt vidyuktam yathā loke sakṛt vidyotanam sarvatas  prakāśakam bhavati tathā jñāna prakāśa vivṛddhi apekṣayā kasyacid vāsanā rūpam upajāyate na eṣām vāsanā rūpāṇām ādiḥ antaḥ  madhyam saṅkhyā vā deśaḥ kālaḥ  nimittaṃvā avadhāryate asaṅkhyeya tvāt vāsanāyāḥ vāsanā hetūnām ca anantyāt  tathā ca vakṣyati ṣaṣṭhe idaṃmayaḥ  adomayaḥ ityādi tasmāt na svarūpa saṅkhyā avadhāraṇa arthā dṛṣṭāntāḥ ayathā māhāra janam vāsaḥ aitya ādayaḥ kim tarhi prakāra pradarśana arthāḥ evamprakārāṇi hi vāsanā rūpāṇi iti yad tu vāsanā rūpam abhihitam ante sakṛt vidyotanam iva iti tad kila hiraṇyagarbhasya avyākṛtāt prādurbhavataḥ taḍitvat sakṛt eva vyaktiḥ bhavati iti tad tadīyam vāsanā rūpam hiraṇyagarbhasya yaḥ  veda tasya sakṛt vidyut teva ha vai iti avadhāraṇa arthau evam eva asya śrīḥ khyātiḥ bhavati iti arthaḥ yathā hiraṇyagarbhasya evam etad yathā uktam vāsanā rūpamantyam yaḥ  veda evam niravaśeṣam satyasya sva rūpam abhidhāya yad tad satyasya satyam avocāma tasya eva svarūpa avadhāraṇa artham brahmaṇa idam ārabhyate atha anantaram satya svarūpa nirdeśa anantaram yad satyasya satyam tad eva avaśiṣyate yasmāt atas tasmāt satyasya satyam svarūpam nirdekṣyāmaḥ ādeśaḥ  nirdeśaḥ  brahmaṇaḥ kaḥ punar asau nirdeśaḥ iti ucyate na iti na iti iti evam nirdeśaḥ nanu katham ābhyām aneti na iti aiti śabdābhyām satyasya satyam nirdidikṣitam iti ucyate sarva upādhi viśeṣa apohena yasmin  kaścid viśeṣaḥ  asti nāma vā rūpam vā karma vā bhedaḥ  vā jātiḥ vā guṇa u vā tad dvāreṇa hi śabda pravṛttiḥ bhavati na ca eṣām kaścid  viśeṣaḥ  brahmaṇi asti atas  na nirdeṣṭum śakyate idam tad iti gauḥ asau spandate śuklaḥ  viṣāṇi iti yathā loke nirdiśyate tathā adhi āropita nāma rūpa karma dvāreṇa brahma nirdiśyate avijñānam ānandam brahma avijñāna ghana eva brahma ātmā aiti evamādi śabdaiḥ yadā punar  svarūpam eva nirdidikṣitam bhavati nirasta sarva upādhi viśeṣam tadā na śakyate kenacid api prakāreṇa nirdeṣṭum  tadā ayam eva abhyupāyaḥ yad uta prāpta nirdeśa pratiṣedha dvāreṇa aneti na iti aiti nirdeśaḥ idam ca nakāra dvayam vīpsā avyāpti artham  yadyat prāptam tad tad niṣidhyate tathā ca sati anirdiṣṭa āśaṅkā brahmaṇaḥ parihṛtā bhavati anyathā hi nakāra dvayena prakṛta dvaya pratiṣedhe yad anyat prakṛtāt pratiṣiddha dvayāt brahma tad na nirdiṣṭam kīdṛśam nu khalu iti āśaṅkā na nivartiṣyate  tathā ca anarthakaḥ ca sa nirdeśaḥ puruṣasya vividiṣāyāḥ  anivartaka tvāt  abrahma jñapayiṣyāmi aiti ca vākyam aparisamāpta artham syāt  yadā tu sarva diś kāla ādi vividiṣā nivartitā syāt  sarva upādhi nirākaraṇa dvāreṇa tadā saindhava ghanavat eka rasam prajñāna ghanam anantaram abāhyam satyasya satyam ahaṃbrahma asmi iti sarvatas  nivartate vividiṣā ātmani eva avasthitā prajñā bhavati tasmāt vīpsā artham na iti na iti iti nakāra dvayam nanu mahatā yatnena parikara bandham kṛtvā kim yuktam evam nirdeśṭum brahma bāḍham  kasmāt  na hi yasmāt  aiti na iti na aityetasmāt  iti iti vyāptavya prakārā nakāra dvaya viṣayā nirdiśyante yathā grāmaḥ  grāmaḥ  ramaṇīya iti anyat param nirdeśanam na asti tasmāt ayam eva nirdeśaḥ  brahmaṇaḥ yad uktam atasya upaniṣad satyasya satyam aiti evaṃprakāreṇa satyasya satyam tad param brahma atas  yuktam uktam nāmadheyam brahmaṇaḥ nāma eva nāmadheyam  kim tad  satyasya satyam prāṇā vai satyam teṣām eṣa satyam iti iti tṛtīyam brāhmaṇam maitreyī iti ha uvāca yājñavalkyaḥ maitreyīm sva bhāryām āmantritavān yājñavalkyaḥ  nāma ṛṣiḥ udyāsyan  ūrdhvam yā asyan pārivrājya ākhyam āśrama antaram vai are iti sambodhanam aham asmāt gārhasthyāt  sthānāt āśramāt ūrdhvam gantum icchan  asmibhava āmi atas hanta anumatim prārthayāmi te tava  kiñcā anyatte tava anayā dvitīyayā bhāryayā kātyāyanyā antam vicchedam karavāṇi pati dvāreṇa yuvayoḥ mayā sambandhasya vicchedam karavāṇi dravya vibhāgam kṛtvā vittena saṃvibhajya yuvām gamiṣyāmi sā evam uktā ha uvāca yad yadi anu aiti vitarke me mama iyam pṛthivī bhagoḥ bhagavan sarvā sāgara parikṣiptā vittena dhanena pūrṇā syāt katham na kathañcana iti ākṣepa arthaḥ praśna arthaḥ  vā tena pṛthivī pūrṇa vitta sādhyena karmaṇā agni hotra ādinā amṛtā kim syām iti vyavahitena sambandhaḥ pratyuvāca yājñavalkyaḥ katham iti yadi ākṣepa artham anumodanam na iti ha uvāca yājñavalkyaḥ katham iti yadi ākṣepa artham anumodanam na iti ha uvāca yājñavalkya iti praśnaḥ ced prativacana artha m na eva syā amṛtā kim tarhi yathā eva loke upakaraṇavatām sādhanavatām jīvitam sukha upāya bhoga sampannam  tathā eva tadvat eva tava jīvitam syāt amṛta tvasya tu nāśā manasā api asti vittena vitta sādhyena karmaṇā iti sā ha uvāca maitreyī  evam uktā pratyuvāca maitreyī yadi evam yena aham na amṛtā syām kim aham tena vittena kuryām yad eva bhagavān kevalam amṛtatva sādhanam veda tad eva amṛtatva sādhanam me mahyam brūhi sa ha uvāca yājñavalkyaḥ evam vitta sādhye amṛtatva sādhane pratyākhyāte yājñavalkyaḥ sva abhiprāya sampattau tuṣṭa āha sa ha uvāca priyeṣāṭā bata iti anukampya āha are maitreyi naḥ asmākam pūrvam api priyā satī bhavantī idānīm priyam eva citta anukūlam bhāṣase ata ehyāḥ sva upaviśa vyākhyāsyāmi yad te tava iṣṭam amṛtatva sādhanam ātma jñānaṃkathayiṣyāmi vyācakṣāṇasya tu me mama vyākhyānam kurvataḥ  nididhyāsasva vākyāni arthataḥ  niścayena dhyātum iccha iti sa ha uvāca amṛtatva sādhanam vairāgyam upadidikṣuḥ jāyā pati putra ādibhyaḥ  virāgam utpādayati tad saṃnyāsāya na vai vaiśabdaḥ prasiddha smaraṇa arthaḥ  prasiddham eva etad loke patyuḥ bhartuḥ kāmāya prayojanāya jāyāyāḥ patiḥ priyaḥ  na bhavati kim tarhi ātmanaḥ tu kāmāya prayojanāya eva bhāryāyāḥ patiḥ priyaḥ  bhavati tathā na vā are jāyāyāḥ  ityādi samānam anyat  na vā are putrāṇām na vā are vittasya na vā are brahmaṇaḥ na vā are kṣatrasya na vā are devānām na vā are bhūtānām na vā are sarvasya pūrvam pūrvam yathā āsanne prīti sādhane vacanam  tatra tatra iṣṭatara tvāt vairāgyasya  sarva grahaṇa muktā anukta artham tasmāt loka prasiddham etad  ātmā eva priyaḥ na anyat  atat etad preyaḥ putrāt aiti upanyastam tasya etad  vṛtti sthānīyam prapañcitam tasmāt ātma prīti sādhana tvāt gauṇī anyatra prītiḥ ātmani eva mukhyā tasmāt ātmā vai are draṣṭavyaḥ  darśana arhaḥ darśana viṣayam āpādayitavyaḥ  śrotavyaḥ pūrvam ācāryata āgamataḥ ca paḥ cāt mantavyaḥ tarkataḥ tatas  nididhya asitavyaḥ  niścayena dhyātavyaḥ evam hi asau dṛṣṭaḥ  bhavati śravaṇa manana nididhi āsana sādhanaiḥ nirvartitaiḥ yadā ekatva matāni upagatāni tadā samyak darśanam brahma ekatva viṣayam prasidati na anyathā śravaṇa mātreṇa yad brahma kṣatra ādi karma nimittam varṇa āśrama ādi lakṣaṇam ātma vidyā adhyāropita pratyaya viṣayam kriyā kāraka phala ātmakam avidyā pratyaya viṣayam rajjavāmva sarpa pratyayaḥ tad upamardana artham āha ātmani khalvare maitreyi dṛṣṭe śrute mate vijñāte idam sarvam viditam vijñātam bhavati nanu katham anyasmin vidite anyat viditam bhavati na eṣa doṣaḥ na hi ātma vyatirekeṇa anyat kiñcid asti  yadi asti na tad viditam syāt na tu anyat asti  ātmā eva tu sarvam  tasmāt sarvam ātmani vidite viditam syāt  katham punar ātmā eva sarvam iti etad śrāvayati brahma brāhmaṇa jātiḥ tam puruṣam parādāt parādadhyāt parākuryāt kam yaḥ  anyatra ātmana ātma svarūpa vyatirekeṇa ātmā eva na bhavati iyam brāhmaṇa jātiḥ iti tām yaḥ  veda tam parādadhyāt sa abrāhmaṇa jātiḥ anātma svarūpeṇa mām paśyati iti paramātmā ahi sarveṣām ātmā tathā kṣatram kṣatriya jātiḥ tathā lokāḥ devāḥ bhūtāni sarvam idam brahma iti yāni anukrāntāni tāni sarvāṇi ātmā eva yad ayam ātmā yaḥ  ayam ātmā draṣṭavyaḥ śrotavya iti prakṛtaḥ yasmāt ātmanaḥ  jāyata ātmani eva līyata ātma mayam ca sthiti kāle ātma vyatirekeṇa agrahaṇāt  ātmā eva sarvam katham punar idānīm idam sarvam ātmā eva iti grahītum śakyate cit mātra anugamāt sarvatra cit svarūpa tā eva iti gamyate tatra dṛṣṭānta ucyate tatra dṛṣṭānta ucyate yad svarūpa vyatirekeṇa agrahaṇam yasya tasya tad ātma tvam eva loke dṛṣṭam sa yathā sa iti dṛṣṭāntaḥ loke yathā dundubheḥ bherī ādeḥ hanyamānasya tāḍyamānasya daṇḍa ādinā na bāhyān śabdān bahis bhūtān śabda viśeṣān dundubhi śabda sāmānyāt niṣkṛṣṭān dundubhi śabda viśeṣān na śaknuyād grahaṇāya grahītum  dundubheḥ tu grahaṇena dundubhi śabdā eta iti śabda viśeṣā gṛhītā bhavanti dundubhi śabda sāmānya vyatirekeṇa abhāvāt teṣām dundubhi āghātasya vā dunduberāhananam āghātaḥ dundubhi āghāta viśiṣṭasya śabda sāmānyasya grahaṇena tad gatā viśeṣā gṛhītā abhavanti na tu ta eva nirbhidya grahītum śakyante viśeṣa rūpeṇa abhāvāt teṣām tathā prajñāna vyatirekeṇa svapna jāgaritayoḥ na kaścid vastu viśeṣaḥ  gṛhyate tasmāt prajñāna vyatirekeṇa abhāvaḥ  yuktaḥ teṣām tathā sa yathā śaṅkhasya dhmāyamānasya śabdena saṃyojyamānasya āpūryamāṇasya na bāhyān śabdān śaknuyāt iti evamādi pūrvavat  tathā vīṇāyai vādyamānāyai vīmāyā vādyamānāyāḥ aneka dṛṣṭānta upādānam iha sāmānya bahutva khyāpana artham aneke hi vilakṣaṇāḥ cetana acetana rūpāḥ sāmānya viśeṣāḥ teṣām pāramparya gatyā yathā ekasmin mahā sāmānye antarbhāvaḥ prajñāna ghane katham nāma pradarśayitavya iti dundubhi śaṅkha vīṇā śabda sāmānya viśeṣāṇām yathā śabda tve antarbhāvaḥ evam sthiti kāle tāvat sāmānya viśeṣa avyatirekāt  brahma eka tvam śakyam avagantum sa yathā ārdra edha agneḥ ārdraiḥ edhobhiḥ iddhaḥ  agniḥ ārdra edha agniḥ tasmāt  abhyāhitāt pṛthak dhūmāḥ pṛthak nānā prakāram dhūma grahaṇam visphulihgādi pradarśana artham dhūma visphuliṅga āt ayaḥ  viniścaranti vinirgacchanti evam yathā ayam dṛṣṭāntaḥ are maitreyī asya paramātmanaḥ prakṛtasya mahataḥ  bhūtasya niśvasitam etad  niśvasitam iva niśvasitam  yathā aprayatnena eva puruṣa niśvāsaḥ  bhavati evam vā are kim tad niśvasitam iva tatas  jātam iti ucyate yadṛgvedaḥ  yajurvedaḥ sāmavedaḥ  atharva aṅgirasaḥ caturvidham mantra jātam itihāsa iti urvaśī purūra vasoḥ saṃvāda ādiḥ uru aśī iha apsarāḥ ityādi brāhmaṇam eva purāṇam asat vā idam agra āsīt  ityādi vidyā deva jana vidyā vedaḥ saḥ  ayam iti ādyā upaniṣadaḥ priyam iti etad upāsīta ityādyāḥ ślokā brāhmaṇa prabhavā mantrāḥ tad ete ślokāḥ ityādayaḥ  sūtrāṇi vastu saṅgraha vākyāni vede yathā ātmā iti eva upāsīta ityādīni anuvyākhyānāni mantra vivaraṇāni vyākhyānāni artha vādāḥ athavā vastu saṅgraha vākya vivaraṇāni anuvyākhyānāni yathā caturtha adhyāye aātmā iti eva upāsīta iti asya yathā vā aanyaḥ  asau  anyaḥ  aham asmi iti na sa veda yathā paśuḥ evam iti asya ayam eva adhyāya śeṣaḥ mantra vivaraṇāni vyākhyānāni evam aṣṭavidham brāhmaṇam evam mantra brāhmaṇayoḥ eva grahaṇam niyata racanāvataḥ  vidyamānasya eva vedasya abhivyaktiḥ puruṣa niśvāsavat  na ca puruṣa buddhi prayatna pūrvakaḥ  atas  pramāṇam nirapekṣa eva sva arthe  tasmāt yad tena uktam tad tathā eva pratipattavyam ātmanaḥ śreya icchadbhiḥ jñānam vā karma vā iti nāma prakāśa vaśā hi rūpasya vikriyā vyavasthā nāma rūpayoḥ eva hi paramātma upādhi bhūtayoḥ vyākriyamāṇayoḥ salila phenavat tattva anya tvena anirvaktavyayoḥ sarva avasthayoḥ saṃsāra tvam iti atas  nāmna eva niśvasita tvam uktam tad vacanena eva itarasya niśvasitatva siddheḥ athavā sarvasya dvaita jātasya avidyā viṣaya tvam uktam brahma tam parādāti dam sarvam yad ayam ātmā iti tena vedasya aprāmāṇyam āśaṅkyate tad āśaṅkā nivṛtti artham idam uktam puruṣa niśvāsavat aprayatna utthita tvāt pramāṇam vedaḥ na yathā anyaḥ  grantha iti kiñca anyat na kevalam sthiti utpatti kālayoḥ eva prajñāna vyatirekeṇa abhāvāt jagataḥ  brahma tvam pralaya kāle ca jala budbuda phena ādīnām iva salila vyatirekeṇa abhāvaḥ evam prajñāna vyatirekeṇa tad kāryāṇām nāma rūpa karmaṇām tasmin  eva līyamānānām abhāvaḥ tasmāt ekam eva brahma prajñāna ghanam eka rasam pratipattavyam iti ata āha pralaya pradarśanāya dṛṣṭāntaḥ sa iti dṛṣṭāntaḥ yathā yena prakāreṇa sarvāsām nadī ivāpī taḍāga ādi gatānām apām samudraḥ  abdhiḥ ekāyanam eka gamanam eka pralayaḥ  avibhāga prāptiḥ iti arthaḥ yathāyām dṛṣṭāntaḥ evam sarveṣām sparśānām mṛdu karkaśa kaṭhina picchila ādīnām vāyoḥ ātma bhūtānām tvac ekāyanam tvak iti tvac viṣayam sparśa sāmānya mātram tasmin praviṣṭāḥ sparśa viśeṣāḥ āpa iva samudram tad vyatirekeṇa abhāva bhūtāḥ  bhavanti tasya eva hi te saṃsthāna mātrā āsan tathā tad api sparśa sāmānya mātram tvac śabda vācyam manaḥ saṅkalpe manaḥ viṣaya sāmānya mātre tvac viṣaya iva sparśa viśeṣāḥ praviṣṭam tad vyatirekeṇa abhāva bhūtam bhavati  evam manaḥ viṣayaḥ  api buddhi viṣaya sāmānya mātre praviṣṭaḥ tad vyatirekeṇa abhāva bhūtaḥ  bhavati vijñāna mātram eva bhūtvā prajñāna ghane pare brahmaṇi āpa iva samudre pralīyate evam paramparā krameṇa śabda ādau saha grāhakeṇa karaṇena pralīne prajñāna ghane upādhi abhāvāt saindhava ghanavat  prajñāna ghanam ekarasam anantam apāram nirantaram brahma vyavatiṣṭhate tasmāt ātmā eva ekam advayam iti pratipattavyam tathā sarveṣām gandhānām pṛthivī viśeṣāṇām nāsike ghrāṇa viṣaya sāmānyam tathā sarveṣām rasānām abviśeṣāṇām cakṣuḥ cakṣuḥ viṣaya sāmānyam tathā śabdānām śrotra viṣaya sāmānyam pūrvavat  tathā śrotra ādi viṣaya sāmānyānām manaḥ viṣaya sāmānye saṅkalpe  manaḥ viṣaya sāmānyasya api buddhi viṣaya sāmānye vijñāna mātre vijñāna mātram bhūtvā parasmin prajñāna ghane pralīyate tathā karmendriyāṇām viṣayā vadana ādāna gamana visarga ānanda viśeṣāḥ tad tad kriyā sāmānyeṣu eva praviṣṭā na vibhāga yogyā bhavanti samudra iva abviśeṣāḥ  tāni ca sāmānyāni prāṇa mātram prāṇaḥ ca prajñāna mātram eva yaḥ  vai prāṇaḥ sā prajñā yā vai prajñā sa prāṇaḥ iti kauṣītakinaḥ adhīyate nanu sarvatra viṣayasya eva pralayaḥ  abhihitaḥ na tu karaṇasya tatra kaḥ  abhiprāya iti bāḍham  kintu viṣaya samāna jātīyam karaṇam manyate śrutiḥ na tu jāti antaram  viṣayasya eva sva ātma grāhaka tvena saṃsthāna antaram karaṇam nāma yathā rūpa viśeṣasya eva saṃsthānam pradīpaḥ karaṇam sarva rūpa prakāśane evam sarva viṣaya viśeṣāṇām eva sva ātma viśeṣa prakāśaka tvena saṃsthāna antarāṇi karaṇāni pradīpavat  tasmāt na karaṇānām pṛthak pralaye yatnaḥ kāryaḥ viṣaya sāmānya ātmaka tvāt viṣaya pralayena eva pralayaḥ siddhaḥ  bhavati karaṇānām iti tatra aidam sarvam yad ayam ātmā iti pratijñātam tatra hetuḥ abhihitaḥ ātma sāmānya tvam ātmaja tvam ātma pralaya tvam ca tasmāt utpatti sthiti pralaya kāleṣu prajñāna vyatirekeṇa abhāvāt  prajñānam brahma ātmā eva idam sarvam iti pratijñātam yad  tad tarkatas  sādhitam svābhāvikaḥ  ayam pralaya iti paurāṇikā vadanti yaḥ tu buddhi pūrvakaḥ pralayaḥ  brahma vidām brahma vidyā nimittaḥ ayam ātyantika iti ācakṣate avidyā nirodha dvāreṇa yaḥ  bhavati  tad arthaḥ  ayam viśeṣa ārambhaḥ tatra dṛṣṭānta upādīyate sa yathā iti saindhava khilyaḥ sindhoḥ vikāraḥ saindhavaḥ sindhu śabdena udakam abhidhīyate syandanāt sindhuḥ udakam tad vikāraḥ tatra bhavaḥ  vā saindhavaḥ saindhavaḥ ca asau khilyaḥ ca iti saindhava khilyaḥ khila eva khilyaḥ sva arthe yad pratyayaḥ udeka sindhau sva yonauprastaḥ prakṣiptaḥ udakam eva vilīyamānam anuvilīya ita yad tad bhauma taijasa samparkāt kāṭhinya prāptiḥ khilyasya sva yoni samparkāt apagacchati tad udakasya vilayanam tadanu saindhava khilyaḥ  vilīyata iti ucyate tad etad āha udakam eva anuvilīyeta iti na ha na eva asya khilyasya udgrahaṇāya uddhṛtya pūrvavat grahaṇāya grahītum na eva samarthaḥ kaścid syāt su nipuṇaḥ  api iva śabdaḥ  anarthakaḥ grahaṇāya na eva samarthaḥ  kasmāt  yatas  yatas  yasmāt yasmāt deśā tad udakam ādadīta gṛhītvā svādayet  lavaṇa āsvādam eva tad udakam na tu khilyam āvaḥ yathā ayam dṛṣṭāntaḥ evam eva vā are maitreyidam paramātma ākhyam mahat bhūtam yasmāt mahataḥ  bhūtāt avidyayā paricchinnā satī kārya karaṇa upādhi sambandhāt khilyam āvam āpannā asi martyā janma maraṇa aśanāyā pipāsā ādi saṃsāra dharmavatī asi nāma rūpa kārya ātmikā amuṣya an va yā aham iti sa khilya bhāvaḥ tava kārya karaṇa bhūna upādhi samparka bhrānti janitaḥ  mahati bhūte sva yonau mahā samudrasya ānīye parama ātmani ajare amare abhaye śudve saindhava vanavat eka rase prajñāna ghane anante apāre nirantare avidyā janita bhrānti meda varjite praveśitaḥ tasmin praviṣṭe sva yoni graste khilya bhāve avidyā kṛte bheda bhāve praṇāśite idam ekam advaitam mahat bhūtam mahat ca tad  bhūtam ca mahat bhūtam sarva mahattara tvāt ākāśa ādi kāraṇa tvāt ca bhūtam viṣu api kālepu svarūpa adhi abhicārāt sarvadā eva pariniṣpannam iti vaikālikaḥ  niṣṭhā pratyayaḥ athavā bhūta śabdaḥ parama artha vācī mahat ca pāramārthikam ca iti arthaḥ laukikam tu yadi api mahat bhavati svapna māyā kṛtam himavat ādi parvata upamam na parama artha vastu atas  viśinaṣṭi idam tu mahat ca tad abhūtam ca iti anantam na asya antaḥ  vidyata iti anantam  kadācid āpekṣikam syāt iti atas viśinaṣṭaya pāramiti vijñaptiḥ vijñānam vijñānam ca tad ghanaḥ ca iti vijñāna ghanaḥ ghana śabdaḥ jāti antara pratiṣedha arthaḥ yathā suvarṇa ghanaḥ  ayaḥ ghana iti  eva śabdaḥ  avadhāraṇa arthaḥ na anyan jāti antaram antarāle vidyata iti arthaḥ yadi idam ekam advaitam paramārthataḥ svaccham saṃsāra duḥkha asampṛttkam kinnimitaḥ  ayam khilya bhāva ātmanaḥ  jātaḥ  mṛtaḥ sukhī duḥkhī aham mama iti evamādi lakṣaṇaḥ  aneka saṃsāra dharma upadrutaḥ iti ucyate etebhyaḥ  bhūtebhyaḥ  yāni etāni kārya karaṇa vipaya ākāra pariṇatāni nāma rūpa ātmakāni salliphena vudvuda upamāni svacchasya paramātmanaḥ salila upamasya yepām viṣaya paryantānām prajñāna ghane brahmaṇi parama artha viveka jñānena pravilāpanam uttakam nadī samudravata etabhyaḥ  hetu bhūtebhyaḥ  bhūtebhyaḥ satya śabda vācyebhyaḥ samutthāya saindhava khilyavat  yathā adbhayaḥ sūrya candra ādi pratibimbaḥ yathā vā svacchasya sphaṭikasya alattaka ādi upādhibhyaḥ  rattka ādi bhāvaḥ evam kārya karaṇa bhūta bhūta upādhibhyaḥ  viśepa ātma khilya bhāvena samutthāya samyak utthāya yebhyaḥ  bhūtebhya utthitaḥ tāni yadā akārya karaṇa viṣaya ākāra pariṇatāni bhūtāni ātmanaḥ  viśepa ātmakhilya hetu bhūtāni śāstra ācārya upadeśena brahma vidyāyāḥ  nadī samudravat pravilāpitāni vinaśyanti salila phena budbuda ādivat teṣu vinaśyatsu anu eva eṣa viśeṣa ātma khilya bhāvaḥ  vinaśyati yathā udakālattphaka ādi hetu apanaye sārya candra sphaṭika ādi pratibimbaḥ  vinaśyati candra ādi svarūpam eva paramārtha taḥ  vyavatiṣṭhate tadvat prajñāna ghanam anantam apāram svaccham vyavatiṣṭhate na tatra pretya viśepa saṃjñā asti kārya karaṇa saṅghātebhyaḥ vimuttkasya iti evam are maitreyi bravīmi na asti viśeṣa saṃjñā iti aham asau  amuṣya putraḥ  mama idam kṣetram dhanam sukhī duḥkhī iti evamādi lakṣaṇā avidyā kṛta tvāt tasyāḥ avidyāyāḥ cabrahma vidyayā niranvayataḥ  nāśita tvāt kutaḥ viśeṣa saṃjñā sambhavaḥ  brahma vidaḥ caitanya svabhāva avasthitasya śarīra avasthitasya api viśeṣa saṃjñā na upapadyate kim uta kārya karaṇa vimuttkasya sarvatas  iti ha uvāca uttkavān kila parama artha darśanam maitreyyai bhāryāyai yājñavalkyaḥ evam pratibodhitā sā ha kila uvācā uttkavatī maitreyī atra eva etasmitreva ekasmin vastuni brahmaṇi virudva dharmavattavam ācakṣaṇena bhagavatā mama moha kṛtaḥ tad āha atra eva mā bhagavān pūjāvān am ūmuhat moham kṛta cān katham tena virudva dharmavat tvam utkam iti ucyate pūrva vijñāna ghana eva iti pratiśāya punar na pretya saṃśāsti iti katham vijñāna ghana eva katham vā na pretya saṃjñā asti iti na hi uṣṇaḥ śītaḥ ca agniḥ eva ekaḥ bhavati atas  mūḍha asmi atra sa ha uvāca yājñavalkyaḥ na vā are maitreyī aham moham bravīmi mohanam vākyam na bravīm iti arthaḥ nanu katham virudva dharma tvam avocaḥ vijñāna ghanam saṃjñā abhāvam ca na mayā idam ekasmin vamiṃṇyamihitam tvayā eva idam virudva dharma tvena ekam vastu parigṛhītam bhrāntyā na tu mayā uttkam mayā tu idam uttkam yaḥ tu avidyā pratyupasya apitaḥ kārya karaṇa sambandhī ātmanaḥ khilya bhāvaḥ yasmin vidyayā nāśite tad nimittā yā viśeṣa saṃjñā śarīra ādi sambandhinī anyatva darśana lakṣaṇā sā kārya karaṇa saṅghāta upādhau pravilāpite naśyati hetu abhāvāt  udaka ādi ādhāra nāśāt iva candra ādi pratibimba stad nimittaḥ ca prakāśa ādiḥ  na punar  parama artha candra āditya svarūpā nāśavat saṃsāri brahma svarūpasya vijñāna ghanasya nāśaḥ  tad vijñā ghana iti uttkam  sa ātmā sarvasya jagataḥ paramārtha taḥ  bhūta nāśān na vināśī vināśī tu avidya kṛtaḥ khilya bhāvaḥ vācā ārambhaṇam vikāraḥ  nāmadheyam iti śruti antarāt ayam tu pāramārthikaḥ avināśī vā are ayam ātmā atas  alam paryāptam vai are idam mahat bhūtam anantam apāram ya yāvi ākhyātam vijñānāya vijñātum katham tarhi pretya saṃjñā na asti iti ucyate śṛṇu yatra yasmin  avidyā kalpite kārya karaṇa saṃghāta upādhi janite viśeṣa ātmani khilya bhāve hi yasmāt at dvaitam iva pāramārthataḥ  advaite brahmaṇi dvaitam iva bhinnam iva vastu antaram ātmana upalakṣyate nanu dvaitena upamīyamāna tvāt dvaitasya pāramārthika tvam iti na avācā arambhaṇam vikāraḥ  nāmadheyam i ati śruti antarā adekam evā advitīyam ātmā eva idam sarvām iti ca tad tatra yasmāt dvaitam iva tasmāt eva itaraḥ  asau paramātmanaḥ khilya bhūta ātma aparama arthaḥ candra udeḥ iva udaka candra ādi pratibimba itaraḥ  ghrāta itareṇa dhrāṇena itaram ghrātavyam jighrati itara itaram iti kāraka pradarśana artham jighrati iti kriyā phalayoḥ abhidhānam yathā chintti iti yathā udyamya udyamya nipātanam chedasya ca dvaidhībhāva ubhayam chinatti iti ekena eva śabdena abhidhīyate kriyā avasāna tvāt kriyā vyatirekeṇa ca tad phalasya anupalambhāt  itaraḥ  ghrāṇa itareṇa ghrāṇena itaram ghratavyam jighrati tathā sarvam pūrvavat vijānāti iyam avidyāvat avasthā yatra tu brahma vidyayā avidyā nāśam upagamitā tatrā atma vyatirekeṇa anyasya abhāvaḥ yatra vā asya brahma vidaḥ sarvam nāma rūpa ādi ātmani eva pravilāpitam ātmā eva saṃvṛttam yatra evam ātmā eva abhūt tatra kena karaṇena kam dhrātavyam kaḥ  jighret tathā paśya udvijānīyāt sarvatra hi kāraka sādhyā kriyā atas  kāraka abhāve anupapattiḥ kriyāyāḥ kriyā bhāve ca phala abhāvaḥ tasmāt avidyāyām eva satyām kriyā kāraka phala vyavahāraḥ  na brahma vidaḥ ātma tvāt eva sarvasya nā atma vyatirekeṇa kārakam kriyā phalam vā asti nacānātmā san sarvam ātmā eva bhavati kasyacid  tasmāt avidyayā eva anāttma tvam parikalpitam na tu paramārtha ta ātma vyatirekeṇa asti kiñcid  tasmāt parama artha ātmā ekatva pratyaye kriyā kāraka phala pratyaya anupapattiḥ atas  virodhāt brahma vidaḥ kriyāṇām tad sādhanānām ca antyantam eva nivṛttiḥ kena kim iti kṣepa artham vacanam prakāra antara anupapatti darśana artham kenacid api prakāreṇa kriyā karaṇa ādi kāraka anupapatteḥ kenatcit kañcitkāścid katham cit na jivret eva iti arthaḥ yatra api avidyā avasthāyām anyaḥ anyam paśyati tatra api yena idam sarvam vijānāti tam kena vijānīyāt yena vijānāti tasya karaṇasyavijñeye viniyukta tvāt  jñātuśva jñeya eva hi jijñāsā nā atmani na ca agneḥ ivā atmā atmanaḥ  viṣayaḥ  na ca aviṣaye jñātuḥ jñānam upapadyate tasmāt yena idam vijānāti tam vijñātāram kena karaṇena kaḥ  vā anyaḥ  vijānīyāt  yadā tu punar  parama artha vivekinaḥ  brahma vidaḥ  vijñātā eva kevalaḥ  advayaḥ vartate tam vijñāta āram are kena vijānīyāt iti iyam pṛthivī prasiddhā sarveṣām bhūtānām madhu sarveṣām brahma ādi stamba paryantānām bhūtānām prāṇinām madhu kāryam madhu iva madhu yathā ekaḥ madhu apūpaḥ  anekaiḥ madhukaraiḥ nirvartita evam iyam pṛthivī sarva bhūta nirvartitā tathā sarvāṇi bhūtāni pṛthivyai pṛthivyāḥ  asyāḥ  madhu kāryam kiñca yaśva ayam puruṣaḥ  asyām pṛthivyām tejaḥ maya śvin mātra prakāśam ayaḥ  amṛtam ayaḥ  amaraṇa dharmā puruṣaḥ  yaḥ ca ayam adhyātmam śārīraḥ śarīre bhavaḥ pūrvavat tejaḥ mayaḥ  amṛta mayaḥ puruṣaḥ sa ca liṅga abhimānī sa ca sarveṣām bhūtānām upakāra karaṇa tvena madhu sarvāṇi ca bhūtāni asya madhu caśabda sāmarthyāt  evam etad catuṣṭayam tāvat ekam sarva bhūta kāryam sarvāṇi ca bhūtāni asya kāryam atas  asya eka kāraṇa pūrvaka tā yasmāt ekasmāt kāraṇāt etad jātam tad eva ekam paramārtha taḥ  brahma itarat kāryam vācā arambhaṇam vikāraḥ  nāmadheya mātram iti eṣa madhu paryāyāṇām sarveṣām arthaḥ saṃkṣepataḥ ayam eva sa yaḥ  ayam pratijñāta idam sarvam yad ayam ātmā iti idam amṛtam yad maitreyyā amṛtatva sādhanam uktam ātma vijñānam idam tad amṛtam idam brahma yad brahmā te bravāṇi jñapayiṣyāmi iti adhyāya ādau prakṛtam yad viṣayā ca vidyā brahma vidyā iti ucyata idam sarvam yasmāt brahmaṇaḥ  vijñānāt sarvam bhavati tathā apaḥ adhyātmam retasi apām viśeṣataḥ  avasthānam tathā agniḥ vāci agneḥ viśeṣataḥ  avasthānam tathā vāyuḥ adhyātmam prāṇaḥ  bhūtānām śarīra ārambhaka tvena upakārān madhu tvam tad antargatānām tejaḥ maya ādīnām karaṇa tvena upakārāt madhu tvam tathā ca uktam tasya eva vācaḥ pṛthivī śarīram jyotīrūpa mayam agniḥ iti tathā adityaḥ  madhu cākṣuṣaḥ  adhyātmam tathā diśaḥ  madhu diśām yadi api śrotram adhyātmam śabda pratiśravaṇa velāyām tu viśeṣataḥ saṃnihitaḥ  bhavati iti adhyātmam prātiśrutkaḥ pratiśrutkāyām pratiśravaṇa velāyām bhavaḥ prātiśrutkaḥ tathā candraḥ adhyātmam mānasaḥ tathā vidyut  tvac tejasi bhavaḥ taijasaḥ  adhyātmam tathā stanayitnaḥ śabde bhavaḥ śābdaḥ  adhyātmam yadi api tathā api svare viśeṣataḥ  bhavati iti sauvaraḥ  adhyātmam tathā akāśaḥ adhyātmam hi adya ākāśaḥ ayam dharmaḥ  ayam iti apratyakṣaḥ  api dharmaḥ kāryeṇa tad prayuktena pratyakṣeṇa vyapadiśyate ayam dharma iti pratyakṣavat  dharmaḥ ca vyākhyātaḥ śruti smṛti lakṣaṇaḥ kṣatra ādīnām api niyantā jagataḥ  vaicitrya kṛt pṛthivī ādīnām pariṇāma hetu tvāt prāṇibhiḥ anuṣṭhīyamāna rūpaḥ ca tena ca ayam dharma iti pratyakṣeṇa vyapadeśaḥ satya dharmayoḥ ca abhedena nirdeśaḥ kṛtaḥ śāsra ācāra lakṣaṇayoḥ idda tu bhedena vyapadeśa ekatve sati api dṛṣṭa adṛṣṭa bheda rūpeṇa kārya ārambhaka tvāt  yaḥ tu adṛṣṭaḥ  apūrva ākhyaḥ  dharmaḥ sa sāmānya viśeṣa ātmanā adṛṣṭena rūpeṇa kāryam ārabhate sāmānya rūpeṇa pṛthivī ādīnām prayoktā bhavati viśeṣa rūpeṇa ca adhyātmam kārya karaṇa saṃghātasya tatra pṛthivī ādīnām prayoktari yaḥ ca ayam asmin dharme tejaḥ mayaḥ tathā adhyātmam kārya karaṇa saṃghāta kartari dharme bhavaḥ  dhārmaḥ tathā dṛṣṭena anuṣṭhīyamānenā acāra rūpeṇa satya ākhyaḥ  bhavati sa eva dharmaḥ saḥ  api dvi prakāra eva sāmānya viśeṣa ātma rūpeṇa sāmānya rūpaḥ pṛthivī ādi samavetaḥ  viśeṣa rūpaḥ kārya karaṇa saṃghāta samaveta tatra pṛthivī ādi samavete vartamāna kriyā rūpe satye tathā adhyātmam kārya karaṇa saṃghāta sa mavete satye bhavaḥ satyaḥ satyena vāyuḥ āvāti iti śruti antarāt dharma satyābhyām prayuktaḥ  ayam kārya karaṇa saṃghāta viśeṣaḥ sa yena jāti viśeṣeṣa saṃyuktaḥ  bhavati sa jāti viśeṣaḥ  mānuṣa ādiḥ tatra mānuṣa ādi jāti viśiṣṭā eva sarve prāṇi nikāyāḥ paraspara upakārya upakāraka bhāvena vartamānā dṛśyante atas  mānuṣa ādi jātiḥ api sarveṣām bhūtānām madhu tatra mānuṣa ādi jātiḥ api bāhyā adhyātmikī ca iti ubhayathā nirdeśa bhāj bhavati yaḥ tu kārya karaṇa saṃghātaḥ  mānuṣa ādi jāti viśiṣṭaḥ saḥ  ayam ātmā sarveṣām bhūtānām madhu nanu ayam śārīra śabdena nirdiṣṭaḥ pṛthivī paryāya eva na pārthiva aṃśasya eva tatra grahaṇāt  idam tu sarva ātmā pratyasta mita adhyātma adhibhūta ādi sarva viśeṣaḥ sarva bhūta devatā gaṇa viśiṣṭaḥ kārya karaṇa saṃghātaḥ saḥ  ayam ātmā iti ucyate tasmin  asmin  ātmani tejaḥ mayaḥ  amṛta mayaḥ puruṣaḥ  ayamūrta rasaḥ sarva ātmakaḥ  nirdiśyate eka deśena tu pṛthivī ādiṣu nirdiṣṭaḥ  atra adhyātma viśeṣa abhāvāt sa na nirdiśyate yaḥ tu pariśiṣṭaḥ  vijñānam ayaḥ  yad arthaḥ  ayam deha liṅga saṃghāta ātmā sa yaḥ ca ayam ātmā iti ucyate yasmin  ātmani pariśiṣṭaḥ  vijñānam ayaḥ  amātmā tasmin  avidyā kṛta kārya karaṇa saṅghāta upadhi viśiṣṭe brahma vidyāyāḥ  parama artha ātmani praveśite sa evam uttkaḥ anantaraḥ  abāhyaḥ kṛtastraḥ prajñāna ghana bhūtaḥ sarveṣām bhūtānām ayam ātmā sarvairūpāsyaḥ sarveṣām bhūtānām adhipatiḥ sarva bhūtānām svatantraḥ  na kumāra mātyavat  kim tarhi sarveṣām bhūtānām rājā rājatva viśeṣaṇam adhipatiḥ iti bhavati kaścid rāja ucitaṣṭattim āśritya rājā na tu adhipatiḥ atas  viśinaṣṭi adhipatiḥ iti evam sarva bhūta ātmā vidvān brahma vid muttkaḥ bhavati yad uttkam abrahma vidyayā sarvam bhaviṣyantaḥ  manuṣyā manyante kim u tad brahmā vedyasmāt tad sarvam abhavat aiti idam tad  vyākhyātam evam ātmānabheva sarva ātma tvena ācārya gamābhyām śrutvā matvā tarkataḥ vijñāya sākṣāt evam yathā madhu brāhmaṇe darśitam tathā tasmāt brahma vijñānāt evaṃlakṣaṇāt  pūrvam apibrahema eva sat avidyayā abrahma āsīt  sarva bheva ca sat asarvam āsīt tāntu avidyām asmāt vijñanāt tiraskṛtya brahma vid brahmā eva san brahmā abhavat sarvaḥ sa sarvam abhavat  parisamāptaḥ śāstra arthaḥ  yad arthaḥ prastutaḥ tasmin  etasmin sarva ātma bhūte brahma vidi sarva ātmani sarvam jagat  samarpitam iti etasmin  arthe dṛṣṭānta upādīyate tad yathā ratha nābhau ca rathena imau cārāḥ sarve samarpitā iti prasidvor athaḥ evam eva asmin  ātmani paramātma bhūte brahma vidi sarvāṇi bhūtāni brahma ādi stambarī antāni sarve devāḥ  agni ādayaḥ sarve loka abhūḥ ādayaḥ sarve praṇā vāc ādayaḥ sarva eta ātmānaḥ  jala candravat  prati śarīra anupraveśinaḥ  avidyā kalpitāḥ sarvam jagat asmin samarpitam yad uttkam brahma vid vāmadevaḥ pratipede aaham manuḥ abhavam sūryaḥ ca aiti sa eṣa sarva ātma bhāvaḥ  vyākhyātaḥ sa eṣa vidvān brahma vid  sarva upādhiḥ sarva ātmā sarvaḥ  bhavati nirupādhiḥ nirupākhyaḥ anantaraḥ  abāhyaḥ kṛtsnaḥ prajñāna ghanaḥ  aja ajaraḥ  amṛta ubhayaḥ acalaḥ  na iti na iti asthūlaḥ  anaṇuḥ iti evaṃviśeṣaṇaḥ  bhavati tam etam artham aja anantaḥ tārkikāḥ kecid  paṇḍitaṃmanyāḥ ca āgama vidaḥ śāstra artha virudvam manyamānā vikalpayantaḥ  moham agādham upayānti tam etam artham etau manetrau  anuvadataḥ anejat ekam manasaḥ  javīyaḥ tad ejati tad na ejati iti tathā ca taittirīyake yasmāt param na apāram asti kiñcat  etad sāma gāyan  āste aham annam aham annam aham annam ityādi tathā ca cchāndogye jakṣat  krīḍa n ramamāṇaḥ sayadi pitṛ loka kāmaḥ sarva gandhaḥ sarva rasaḥ ityādi āyarvaṇe ca sarvajñaḥ sarva vid  dūrāta sudūre tad iha antike ca kaṭhavallīṣu api aṇoḥ aṇīyān mahataḥ  mahīyān kaḥ tam madāmadam devam tad vāvataḥ  anyānatyeti tiṣṭhat  iti ca tathā gītāsu aham kratuḥ aham yajñaḥ pitā aham asya jagataḥ na ādatte kasyacid  pāpam samam sarveṣu bhūteṣu avimattkam vibhatt kepu grasiṣṇu prabhaviṣṇu ca iti evamādi āgama artha virudvam iva pratibhā antam manyamānāḥ sva citta sāmarthyāt artha nirṇayāya vikalpayantaḥ asti ātmā na asti ātmā kartā akartā muttkaḥ badvaḥ kṣaṇikaḥ  vijñāna mātram śūnyam ca iti evam vikalpayantaḥ  na pāram adhigacchanti avidyāyāḥ virudvarrma darśi tvāt  sarvatra tasmāt tatra ya eva śruti ācārya darśita mārga anusāriṇaḥ ta eva avidyāyāḥ pāram adhigacchanti ta eva vā asmān moha samudrāt agādhāt uttariṣyanti na itare sva vudvi kauśala anusāriṇaḥ idam iti anantara nirdiṣṭam vyapadiśati budvau sannihita tvāt  vaiśabdaḥ smaraṇa arthaḥ tad iti ākhyāyikā nirvṛttaṃprakaraṇa antara abhihitam parokṣam vaiśabdena smārayan  iha vyapadiśati yad tad pravargya prakaraṇe mūcitam na āviṣkṛtam madhu tad idam madhu iha anantaram nirdiṣṭam aiyam pṛthivī aityādinā katham tatra prakaraṇa ante sūcitam dadhi aṅ ha vā ābhyām ātharvaṇaḥ  madhu nāma brāhmaṇam uvāca tad enayoḥ priyam dhāma tad eva enayoḥ etena upagacchati sa ha uvāca indreṇa vā uttkaḥ asmayetat ced anyasmā anuvrūyāḥ tata eva te śiraḥ chindyām iti tasmāt vai bibhemi yad vai me sa śiraḥ  na chindyāt  tadvām upaneṣya iti tau hocaturāvām tvā tasmāt  trāsyāvahe iti katham mā trāsyethe iti yadā na  upaneṣyase atha te śiraḥ chittvā anyatra āhratya upanidhāsyāvaḥ atha aśvasya śira āhrati tad te pratidhāsya avaḥ tena na avanuvakṣyasi yadā na avanuvakṣyasi atha te tad indraḥ śiraḥ chetsyati atha te svam śira āhrati tad te pratidhāsyāva iti tathā iti tau ha upaninye tau yadā upaninye atha asya śirat chittvā anyatra upanidadhutuḥ  atha aśvasya śira āhrati tad vā asya pratidadhatuḥ tena hābhyām anuvāca sa yadā ābhyām anuvāca atha asya tad indraḥ śiraḥ cit cheda atha asya svam śira āhrati tad vā asya pratidadhatuḥ iti yāvat tu pravargya karma aṅga bhūtam madhu tāvat eva tatra abhihitam na tu kakṣyam ātmā ajñāna ākhyam tatra yā ākhyāyikā abhihitā sā iha stuti arthā pradarśyate idam vai tad madhu dadhi aṅṅātharvaṇaḥ  anena prapañcena aśvibhyām uvāca tad etad ṛpiḥ tad etad karma śṛpiḥ mantraḥ paśyan  upalabhamānaḥ avocat  uttkavān katham tad daṃsa iti vyavahitena sambandhaḥ daṃsa iti karmaṇaḥ  nāmadheyam tad ca daṃsaḥ ki viśiṣṭam ugram krūram vām yuvayoḥ he narā nara ākārau  aśvinau tad ca karma kinnimitam sanaye lābhāya  lāma lubdha u hi loke api krūram karma ācarati tathā eva etau  upalabhyete yathā soke tadāviḥ prakāśam kṛṇomi karomi yad rahasi bhavat bhayām kṛtam kim iva iti ucyate tanyatuḥ parjanyaḥ na iva na kāraḥ tu upariṣṭāt upacāra upamā arthīyaḥ  vede na pratipedha arthaḥ yathāśvam na aśvam iva iti yadvat  tanyatuḥ iva vṛrṣṭi yathā parjanyaḥ  vṛrṣṭi prakāśayati stanayitnu ā ādi śabdaiḥ tadvat aham yuvayoḥ krūram karma āviṣkṛṇomi iti sambandhaḥ nanu aśvinoḥ stuti arthau katham imau mantrau syātām nindā vacanau hi imau na epa doṣaḥ stutiḥ eva eṣā na nindā vacanau yasmāt īdṛśam api atikrūram karma kurvatoḥ yuvayoḥ na loma ca mīyata iti na ca anyat kiñcid vīyata eva iti stutau  etau bhavataḥ nindām praśaṃsām hi laukikāḥ smaranti tathā praśaṃsā rūpā ca nindā loke prasidvā dadhyak nāma ātharvaṇaḥ hā iti anartha kaḥ  nipātaḥ yad madhu kakṣyam ātma jñāna lakṣaṇam āthavaṇaḥ  vām yukābhyām aśvasya śīrṣṇā śirasā prayat īm uvāca yad  provāca madhu īm iti anartha kaḥ  nipātaḥ idam vai tad madhu ityādi pūrvavat mantra antara darśana artham tathā anyaḥ  mantraḥ tām eva ākhyāyikām anusaratisma ātharvaṇaḥ  dadhyak nāma ātharvaṇaḥ  anyaḥ  vidyata iti atas  viśinaṣṭi dadhyak nāma ātharvaṇaḥ tasmai dadhīca ātharvaṇāya he aśvinau  iti mantra dṛśaḥ  vacanam aśvyama śvasya sva bhūtam śiraḥ brāhmaṇasya śira si  chinne aśvasya śiraḥ chittvā īdṛśam ati krūram karma kṛtvā aśvayam śiraḥ  brāhmaṇam prati erayatam gamitavantau yuvām sa ca atharvaṇaḥ  vām yuvābhyām tad madhu pravocat  yad  pūrvam pratijñātam vakṣyāmi iti sa kimartham evam jīvita sandeham āruhya pravocat  iti ucyate śṛtāyan yata pūrvam pratijñātam satyam tad  paripālayitum icchan jīvitāt api hi satya dharma paripālanā gurutarā ityesya liṅgam etad  ki tad madhu pravocat  iti ucyate tvāṣṭram tvaṣṭā ādityaḥ tasya sambandhi yajñasya śiraḥ chinnam tvaṣṭā abhavat tad pratisandhāna artha pravargya karma tatra pravargya karma aṅga bhūtam yad  vijñānam tad tvāṣṭram madhu yajñasya śiraḥ chedana pratisandhāna ādi viṣayam darśanam tad tvāṣṭram yad madhu he dastraḥ dastrau  iti para balānām upakṣa payitārau śatrūṇām vā ahiṃsitārau api ca na kevalam tvāṣṭram eva madhu karma sambandhi yuvābhyām avocat  api ca kakṣyam gopyam rahasyam parama ātma sambandhi yad  vijñānam madhu madhu brāhmaṇena uttkama dhyāya dvaya prakāśitam tad ca vām yuvābhyām pravocat iti anuvartate idam vai tad madhu iti pūrvavat  uttkau dvau mantrau pravargya sambandhyākhyāyi kā upasaṃhartārau dvayoḥ pravargya karma arthayoḥ adhyāyayoḥ artha ākhyāyikā bhūtābhyām mantrābhyām prakāśitaḥ brahma vidyā arthayoḥ tu adhyāyayoḥ artha auttarābhyām ṛgbhyām prakāśayitavyaḥ iti atas  pravartate yad  kakṣyam ca madhuttkavān ātharvaṇaḥ  yuvābhyām iti uttkam kim punar dat madhu iti ucyate puras cakre puras  purāṇi śarīrāṇi yata iyam acya akṛta vyākaraṇa prakriyā sa parameśvaraḥ  nāma rūpe avyākrate vyākurvāṇaḥ prathamam bhūḥ ādīm llokān sṛṣṭvā cakre kṛtavān dvipadaḥ  dvi pāda palakṣitāni manuṣya śarīrāṇi pakṣi śarīrāṇi tavā puras  śarīrāṇi cakre catuṣpadaḥ catuṣpād upalakṣitāni paśu śarīrāṇi puras  purastān sa īśvaraḥ pakṣī liṅga śarīram bhūtvā puras  śarīrāṇi puruṣa āviśat iti asya artham ācaṣṭe śrutiḥ sa vā ayam puruṣaḥ sarva asuyūrṣu sarva śarīreṣu puriśayaḥ puriśeta iti puriśayaḥ san puruṣa iti ucyate na enena anena kiñacana kiñcid api anāvṛta manāt śaditam tathā na enena kiñcana asaṃvṛtam antarananu praveśitam bāhya bhūtena antarbhūtena ca na anāvṛtam evam sa eva nāmakhya ātmanā antarvahiḥ bhāvena kārya karaṇa rūpeṇa vyavasthitaḥ puras cakre ityādi mantraḥ saṅkṣepata ātmā eka tvam ācaṣṭā eti arthaḥ idam vai tad madhu ityādi pūrvavat  rūpam rūpam pratirūpaḥ  rūpa antaram babhūva iti arthaḥ pratirūpaḥ  anurūpaḥ  vā yādṛś saṃmathānau mātā pitarau tad saṃsthānaḥ tad anurūpa eva putraḥ  jāyate na hi catuṣpadaḥ  dvipād jāyate dvipadaḥ  vā catuṣpād  sa eva hi parameśvaraḥ  nāma rūpe vyākurvāṇaḥ  rūpam rūpam pratirūpaḥ  babhūva kimartha punar  pratirūpam āgamanam tasya iti ucyate tad asya ātmanaḥ  rūpam praticakṣaṇāya pratikhyāpanāya yadi hi nāma rūpe na vyākriyete tadā asya ātmanaḥ  nirūpa adhikam rūpam prajñā ana ghana ākhyam na pratikhyāyeta yadā punar  kārya karaṇa ātmanā nāma rūpe vyāka te bhavataḥ tadā asya rūpam pratikhyāyeta indraḥ parameśvaraḥ  māyābhiḥ prajñābhiḥ nāma rūpa bhūta kṛta mithyā abhimānaiḥ vā na tu paramārthataḥ  puru rūpaḥ  bahu rūpa īyate gabhyate eka rūpa eva prajñāna ghanaḥ sanna vidyā prajñābhiḥ kasmāt  punar  kāraṇāt  yuttkā ratha iva vājinaḥ sva vipaya prakāśanāya hi yasmāt dasya harayaḥ  haraṇāt indriyāṇi śatā śatāni daśa ca prāṇi bheda bāhulyāt śatāna daśa ca bhavanti tasmāt indriya vipaya bāhulyāt tad prakāśanāyā iva ca yuttkāna tāni na ātma prakāśanāya parāñci khāni vyatṛṇat  svayambhūḥ iti hi kāṭhake tasmātaiḥ eva vipaya svarūpaiḥ īyate na prajñāna ghana eka rasena sva rūpeṇa evam tahi ayam anyaḥ parameśvaraḥ  anye haraya iti evam prāpte ucyate ayam vai harayaḥ  ayam vai daśa ca sahasrāṇi bahūni ca anantāni ca prāṇi bhedasya anantyāt  kim bahunā tad etad brahma ya ātmā apūrvam na asya kāraṇam pūrva vidyata iti apūrvam na asya aparam kāryam vidyata iti anaparam na asya jāti antaram antarāle vidyata iti analtaram tathā bahis asya na vidyata iti avāhyam kim punar tad nirantaram brahma ayam ātmanā kaḥ  asau yaḥ pratyagātmā draṣṭā śrotā mantā bodvā vijñātā sarva anubhūḥ sarva ātmanā sarvam anubhavati iti sarvam anubhūḥ iti etad anuśāsanam sarva vedānta upadeśaḥ eṣa sarva vedāntānām upasaṃhrator athaḥ etad amṛtam abhayam parisamāptaḥ ca śāstra arthaḥ iti pañcamam brāhmaṇam ayedānīm brahma vidyā arthasya madhuka aṇḍasya vaṃśaḥ stuti arthaḥ  brahma vidyāyāḥ mantraḥ ca ayam svādhyāya arthaḥ  japa arthaḥ ca tatra vaṃśa iva vaṃśaḥ yathā veṇuḥ vaṃśaḥ parvaṇaḥ parvaṇaḥ  hi bhidyate tadvat agrat prabhṛti āmūla prāpteḥ ayam vaṃśaḥ adhyāya catuṣṭayasya ācārya paramparā kramaḥ  vaṃśa iti ucyate tatra prathama antaḥ śiṣyaḥ pañcamayantaḥ ācāryaḥ parameṣṭhī virāj  brāhmaṇaḥ  hiraṇyagarbhāt  tatas  parama ācārya paramparāna asti yad punar brahma tad nityam svayambhū tasmai brahmaṇai svayambhuve namaḥ ayedānīm brahma vidyā arthasya madhuka aṇḍasya vaṃśaḥ stuti arthaḥ  brahma vidyāyāḥ mantraḥ ca ayam svādhyāya arthaḥ  japa arthaḥ ca tatra vaṃśa iva vaṃśaḥ yathā veṇuḥ vaṃśaḥ parvaṇaḥ parvaṇaḥ  hi bhidyate tadvat agrat prabhṛti āmūla prāpteḥ ayam vaṃśaḥ adhyāya catuṣṭayasya ācārya paramparā kramaḥ  vaṃśa iti ucyate tatra prathama antaḥ śiṣyaḥ pañcamayantaḥ ācāryaḥ parameṣṭhī virāj  brāhmaṇaḥ  hiraṇyagarbhāt  tatas  parama ācārya paramparāna asti yad punar brahma tad nityam svayambhū tasmai brahmaṇai svayambhuve namaḥ iti ṣaṣṭham brāhmaṇam                                                                        ādhḥYāYā janakaḥ  ha vaideha ityādi yājñavalkoyam kāṇḍam ārabhyate upapatti pradhāna tvāt atikrāntena madhuka aṇḍena samāna artha tve api sati na punarukta tā madhu ka aṇḍam hi āgema pradhānam āgama upapattī hi ātmā ekatva prakāśanāya pravṛtte śaknutaḥ kara tala gata bilvam iva darśayitum śrotavyaḥ  mantavya iti hi uktam tasmāt āgama arthasya eva parīkṣā pūrvakam nirdhāraṇāya yājñavalkīyam kāṇḍam upapatti pradhānam ārabhyate ākhyāyikā tu vijñāna stuti artha upāya vidhi parā vā prasiddhaḥ  hi upāyaḥ vidvadbhiḥ śāstreṣu ca dṛṣṭaḥ  dānam dānena hṛyupanam ante prāṇinaḥ prabhūtam hiraṇyam gaḥ sahasra dānam ca iha upalabhyate tasmāt anya pareṇa api śāstreṇa vidyā prāpti upāya dāna pradarśana arthā akhyāyikā arabdhā api ca tad vidya saṃyogaḥ taiśva saha vāda karaṇam vidyā prāpti upāyaḥ  nyāya vidyāyām dṛṣṭaḥ tad ca asmin  adyāye prābalyena pradarśyate pratyakṣā ca vidvat saṃyoge prajñā vṛddhiḥ tasmāt vidyā prāpti upāya pradarśana arthā eva ākhyāyikā janakaḥ  nāma ha kila samrāj rājā babhūva videhānām tatra bhavaḥ  vaidehaḥ sa ca bahu dakṣiṇena yajñena śākhā antara prasiddhaḥ  vā bahu dakṣiṇaḥ  nāma yajñaḥ  aśvamedhaḥ  vā dakṣiṇā bāhulyāt bahu dakṣiṇa iha ucyate teneje ayajat  tatra tasmin yajñe nimantritā darśana kāmā vā kurūṇām deśānām pañcālānām ca brāhmaṇāḥ teṣu hi viduṣām bāhulyam prasiddham abhisametā abhisaṃgatā babhūvuḥ tatra mahāntam vidvat sa mudāyam dṛṣṭvā tasya ha kila janakasya vaidehasya yajamānasya kaḥ  nu khalu atra brahmiṣṭha iti viśeṣeṇa jñātum icchā vijijñāsā babhūva katham kaḥ svid kaḥ nu khalu eṣām brāhmaṇānām anūcānatamaḥ sarva ime anūcānāḥ kaḥ su ideṣām atiśayena anūcāna iti sa hānu ūcānatam aviṣaya utpad nijijñāsaḥ san  tad vijñāna upāya artham gavām sahasram prathama vayasām avaru rodha goṣṭhe avarodham kārayāmāsa kiṃviśiṣṭāḥ tā gāvaḥ  avaruddhā iti ucyate pala caturtha bhāgaḥ pādaḥ suvarṇasya daśa daśa pādā ekaikasya goḥ śṛṅgayoḥ ābaddhā babhūvuḥ pañca pañca pādā ekaikasmin śṛṅge gā evam avarudhya brāhmaṇān  tān ha uvāca he brāhmaṇā bhagavanta iti āmantratha yaḥ  vaḥ  yuṣmākam brahmiṣṭhaḥ sarve yūyam brahmāṇaḥ  atiśayena yuṣmākam brahmā yaḥ sa etā gā udajatām utkālayatu sva gṛham prati te ha brāhmaṇā na dadhṛṣuḥ ha kila evam uktā brāhmaṇā brahmiṣṭha tām ātmanaḥ pratijñātum na dadhṛ puḥ na pragalbhāḥ saṃvṛttāḥ apragalbha bhūteṣu brāhmaṇeṣu atha ha yājñavalkyaḥ sva mātmīyam eva brahmacāriṇam antevāsinam uvāca etā gā he somya udaja udgamayā asmad gṛhān prati he sāmaśravaḥ sāma vidhim hi śṛṇoti ator ayāt catur vedaḥ  yājñavalkyaḥ tā gā ha udācakāra utkālitavān ācārya gṛham prati yājñavalkyena brahmiṣṭha paṇa svīkaraṇena ātmanaḥ  brahmiṣṭha tā pratijñātā iti te ha cukrudhuḥ kruddhavantaḥ  brāhmaṇāḥ teṣām krodha abhiprāyam ācaṣṭe katham naḥ asmākam ekaika pradhānānām brahmiṣṭhaḥ  asmi iti bruvīta iti atha ha evam kruddheṣu brāhmaṇeṣu janakasya yajamānasya hotā ṛtvij aśvalaḥ  nāma babhūva āsīt  sa enam yājñavalkyam brahmiṣṭha abhimānī rāja āśraya tvāt ca dhṛṣṭaḥ yājñavalkyam papraccha pṛṣṭavān katham tvam nu khalu naḥ yājñavalkya brahmiṣṭhaḥ  asī iti plutiḥ bhartsana arthā sa ha uvāca yājñavalkyaḥ namaskarmaḥ  vayam brahmiṣṭhāya idānīm gaḥ kāmāḥ sma u vayam iti tam brahmiṣṭha pratijñam santam tatas  eva brahmiṣṭha paṇa svīkaraṇāt  praṣṭum dadhre dhṛtavān manaḥ  hotā aśvalaḥ yājñavalkya iti ha uvāca tatra madhu kāṇḍe pāḍaktena karmaṇā darśana saptuccitena yajamānasya mṛtyoḥ atyayaḥ  vyākhyāta udgītha prakaraṇe saṅkṣepataḥ tasya eva parīkṣā viṣayaḥ  ayamiti tadgata darśana viśeṣa arthaḥ  ayam vistara ārabhyate yad idam sādhana jātam asya karmaṇa ṛtvigagni ādi mṛtyunā karma lakṣaṇena svābhāvika āsaṅga sahitena āptam jyāptam na kevalam vyāptam abhiṣannam ca mṛtyunā baśīkṛtam ca kena darśana lakṣaṇena sādhanena yajamānaḥ  mṛtyoḥ āptimati mṛtyu gacara tvam atikramya mucyate svatantraḥ  mṛtyoḥ avaśaḥ bhavati iti arthaḥ nanu udgītha eva abhihitam yena atimucyatemukhya prāṇa ātma darśanena iti bāḍham uktam yaḥ  anuktaḥ  viśeṣaḥ tatra tad arthaḥ  ayam ārambha iti adoṣaḥ hotrā ṛtvijā agninā vācā iti āha yājñavalkyaḥ etasya arthaṃvyācaṣṭe kaḥ punar hetā yena mṛtyum atikāmati iti ucyate vāc vai yajñasya yajamānasya yajñaḥ  vai yajamānaḥ iti śruteḥ yajñasya yajamānasya yāvāc sā eva hotā adhiyajñe katham tatatrayeyaṃvan ga yajñasyayajamānasya saḥ  ayam prasiddhaḥ  agniḥ adhidaivatam tad etad vyanna prakaraṇā ivyākhyātam sa ca agniḥ hetā agniḥ vai hotā iti śruteḥ yad etad  yajñasya sādhana dvayam hotā catviṅg adhiyajñam adhyātmam ca vāc  etad ubhayam sādhana dvayam paricchinnam mṛtyunā āptam svābhāvikā jñāna āsaṅga prayuktena karmaṇā mṛtyunā pratikṣaṇam anyathātvam āpadyamānam vaśīkṛtam tad  anena adhidaivata rūpeṇa agninā adṛśyamānaṃ ayajamānasya yajñasya sṛtyorati muktaye bhavati tad etad āha sa muktiḥ sa hotā agniḥ muktiḥ agni svarūpa darśanam eva muktiḥ yadā eva sādhana dvayam agni rūpeṇa gaśyati tadānīm eva hi svābhāvikādāsaṅgāt mṛtyoḥ vimucyate ādhyātmikāt  paricchinna rūpā dādhibhautikāt ca tasmāt  sa hotā agni rūpeṇa dṛṣṭaḥ  muktiḥ mukti sādhanam yajamānasya sā atimuktiḥ yā eva ca muktiḥ sā atimuktiḥ ati mukti sādhanam iti arthaḥ sādhana dvayasya paricchinnasya yā adhidevatā rūpeṇa aparicchinnena agni rūpeṇa dṛṣṭiḥ sā muktiḥ yā asau muktiḥ adhidevatā dṛṣṭiḥ sā eva adhyātma adhibhūta pariccheda viṣaya āsaṅga āspadam mṛtyum atikramya adhidevatā tvasya agni bhāvasya prāptiḥ yā phala bhūtā sā atimuktiḥ iti ucyate tasyāḥ  atimukteḥ muktiḥ eva sādhanam iti kṛtvā sā atimuktiḥ iti āha yajamānasya hi ati muktiḥ vāc ādīnām agni ādi bhāva iti udgītha prakaraṇe vyākhyātam tatra sāmānyena mukhya prāṇa darśana mātram mukti sādhanam uktam na tad viśeṣaḥ vāc ādīnām agni ādi darśanam iha viśeṣaḥ  varṇyate mṛtyu prāpti atimuktiḥ tu sā eva phala bhūtā yodgītha brāhmaṇena vyākhyātā amṛtyu pratikrāntaḥ  dīpyate ityādyā yājñavalkya iti ha uvāca svābhāvikāda jñāna āsaṅga prayuktāt  karma lakṣaṇāt mṛtyoḥ ati muktiḥ vyākhyātā tasya karmaṇaḥ sāsaṅgasya mṛtyoḥ āśraya bhūtānām darśa pūrṇamāsa ādi karma sādhanānām yaḥ  vipariṇāma hetuḥ kālaḥ tasmāt  kālāt  pṛthak ati nuṣṭhāna vyatirekeṇa api prāk ūrdhvam ca kriyāyāḥ sādhana vipariṇāma hetu tvena vyāpāra darśanāt  kālasya tasmāt  pṛthak kālāt ati muktiḥ vaktavyā ityata āha yad idam sarvam ahorātrābhyām āptam sa ca kālaḥ  dvi rūpaḥ ahorātra ādi lakṣaṇāḥ tithi ādi lakṣaṇaḥ ca tatra ahorātra ādi lakṣaṇāt tāvat atimuktim āha ahorātrābhyām hi sarvam jāyate vardhate vinaśyati ca tathā yajña sādhanam ca yajñasya yajamānasya cakṣuḥ adhvaryuḥ ca śiṣṭāni akṣarāṇi pūrvavat neyāni yajamānasya cakṣuḥ adhvaryuḥ ca sādhana dvayam adhyātma adhibhūta paricchedam hitvā adhidaivata ātmanā dṛṣṭam yad  sa muktiḥ saḥ  adhvaryuḥ āditya bhāvena dṛṣṭaḥ  muktiḥ sā eva muktiḥ eva atimuktiḥ iti pūrvavat  āditya ātma bhāvam āpannasya hi na ahorātre sambhavataḥ idānīm tithi ādi lakṣaṇāt ati muktiḥ ucyate idānīm tithi ādi lakṣaṇāt ati muktiḥ ūcyate yad idam sarvam ahorātrayoḥ aviśiṣṭayoḥ ādityaḥ kartā na prati pada ādīnām tithīnām  tāsām tu vṛddhi kṣaya upagamanena pratipad prabhṛtīnām candramāḥ kartā atas tadā apācyā pūrva pakṣa apara pakṣa atyayaḥ āditya apacyā ahorātra atyayavat  tatra yajamānasya prāṇaḥ  vāyuḥ sa eva audgātā iti udgītha brāhmaṇe avagatam avācā ca hi eva sa prāṇena ca udak āyat aiti ca nirdhāritam aatha etasya prāṇasya apaḥ śarīram jyotīrūpam asau candraḥ aiti ca prāṇauvāyu candramasām eka tvāt candramasā vāyunā ca upasaṃhāre na kaścid  viśeṣaḥ evam manyamānā śrutiḥ vāyunā adhidaivata rūpeṇa upasaṃharati api ca vāyu nimittau hi vṛddhi kṣayau candramasaḥ tena tithi ādi lakṣaṇasya kālasya kartuḥ api kārayitā vāyuḥ atas  vāyu rūpa āpannaḥ tithi ādi kālāt atītaḥ  bhavati iti upapannataram bhavati tena śruti antare candra rūpeṇa dṛṣṭiḥ muktiḥ atimuktiḥ ca iha tu kāṇvānām sādhana dvayasya tad kāraṇa rūpeṇa vāyu ātmanā dṛṣṭiḥ muktiḥ atimuktiḥ ca iti na śrutyoḥ virodhaḥ mṛtyoḥ kālāt ati muktiḥ vyākhyātā yajamānasya saḥ  atimucyamānaḥ kena avaṣṭambhena pariccheda viṣayam mṛtyum atotya phalam prāpnoti atimucyata iti ucyate yad idam prasiddham antarikṣam ākāśaḥ  anārambaṇam anālambanam iva śabdāt asti eva tatrā alambanam tad tu na jñāyata iti abhiprāyaḥ yad tu tad ajñāyamānam ālambanam tad sarva nāmnā kena iti pṛcchyate anyathā phala prāpteḥ asaṃbhavāt yena avaṣṭambhenā akrameṇa yajamānaḥ karma phalam pratipadyamānaḥ  atimucyate kim tad iti praśna viṣaya kenā akrameṇa yajamānaḥ svargam lokam ākramata iti svargam lokam phalam prāpnoti atimucyata iti arthaḥ brahmaṇā ṛtvijā manasā candreṇa iti akṣara nyāsaḥ pūrvavat  tatra adhyātmam yajñasya yajamānasya yad idam prasiddham manaḥ saḥ  asau candraḥ  adhidaivatam manaḥ  adhyātmam candramā adhidaivatam iti hi prasiddham sa eva candramā brahmaṛtviktena adhibhūtam brāhmaṇaḥ paricchinnam rūpam adhyātmam ca manasa etad dvayam aparicchinnena candramasaḥ  rūpeṇa paśyati tena candramasā manasā avalambanena
