karma phalam svargam lokam prāpnoti atimucyata iti abhiprāyaḥ iti iti upasaṃhārātham vacanam iti evaṃprakārā mṛtyoḥ ati mokṣāḥ sarvāṃṇi hi darśana prakārāṇi yajña aṅga viṣayāṇi asmin  avasara uktāni iti kṛtvā upasaṃhāra iti ati mokṣāḥ evaṃprakārā atimokṣā iti arthaḥ atha saṃpadaḥ atha adhunā saṃpada ucyante saṃpad nāma kenacid sāmānyena agnihotra ādīnām karmaṇām mahatām phalavatām tad phalāya saṃpādanam saṃpad  phalasya eva vā sarva utsāhena phala sādhana anuṣṭhāne prayatatām kenacid vaiguṇyena asaṃbhavaḥ tad idānīm āhitāgniḥ sanyat kiñcit karma agnihotra ādīnām yathāsaṃbhavam ādāyā alambanīkṛtya karma phala vidvattāyām satyām yad karma phala kāmaḥ  bhavati tad eva saṃpādayati anyathā rājasūya aśvamedha puruṣa medha sarva medha lakṣaṇānām adhikṛtānām traivarṇikānām api asaṃbhavaḥ teṣām tad pāṭhaḥ svādhyāya artha eva kevalaḥ syāt  yadi tad phala prāpti upāyaḥ kaścana na syāt  tasmāt teṣām sepadā eva tad phala prāptiḥ tasmāt saṃpadām api phalavat tvam atas  saṃpada ārabhyante yājñavalkya iti ha uvāca abhimukhīkaraṇāya katibhiḥ aya madya rgbhiḥ hetā asmin yajñe katibhiḥ kati saṅkhyā abhiḥ ṛgbhiḥ ṛc jātibhiḥ ayaṃha utar tvigasmin yajñe kariṣyati śastram śaṃsati āha itaraḥ tisṛbhiḥ ṛc jātibhiḥ iti ukkavantam pratyā hetaraḥ katamāḥ tāstiḥ tra iti saṅkhyeya viṣayaḥ  ayam praśnaḥ pūrvaḥ tu saṅkhyā viṣayaḥ puronuvākyāca prāc yāga phālāt  yāḥ prayujyante ṛcaḥ sā ṛc jātiḥ puronuvākyā iti ucyate yāga artham yāḥ prayujyante ṛcaḥ sā ṛc jātiḥ yājyā śastra artham yāḥ prayujyante ṛcaḥ sā ṛc jātiḥ śasyā sarvāḥ tu yāḥ kāścana ṛcaḥ tāḥ stotriyā vā anyā vā sarvā etāsu eva tisṛṣu ṛc jātiṣu antarbhavanti kim tābhiḥ jayati iti yad kiñca idam prāṇabhṛt iti atas ca saṅkhyā sāmānyāt  yad kiñcid prāṇabhṛt jātam tad  sarvam jayati tad  sarvam phala jātam sampādayati saṅkhī ā ādi sāmānyena yājñavalkya iti hovāva iti pūrvavat  katyaya madya adhvaryuḥ asmin yajña āhutīḥ heṣyati iti kati āhuti prakārāḥ tastra iti katamāḥ tāstiḥ tra iti pūrvavat  itara āha yā hūtā ujjvalanti samidh ājya āhutayaḥ yā hutā atinedante atīva śabdam kuvanti māsa ādi āhutayaḥ yā hutā adhiśerate adhyādhaḥ gatvā bhūmeḥ adhiśerate payaḥ soma āhutayaḥ kim tābhiḥ jayati iti tābhiḥ evam nirvartitābhiḥ āhutibhiḥ kim jayati iti yā āhutayaḥ  hutā ujjvalanti ujjvalana yuktā āhutayaḥ  nirvartitāḥ phalam ca deva loka ākhyam ujjvalam eva tena sāmānyena yā maya tā ujjvalantya āhutayaḥ  nirvartyamānāḥ tā etāḥ sākṣāt deva lokasya karma phalasya rūpam deva loka ākhyam phalam eva mayā nirvartyata iti evam sampādayati yā hutā atinedante āhutayaḥ pitṛ lokam eva tābhiḥ jayati kutsita śabda kartṛtva sāmānyena pitṛ lokam eva tābhiḥ jayati kutsita śabda kartṛtva sāmānyena pitṛ loka sambaddhāyām hi saṃyamanyām puryām vaivasvatena yātyamānānāṃ ahā hatāḥ sma muñca muñca aiti śabda ubhavati tathā avadāna āhutayaḥ tena pitṛ loka sāmānyāt  pitṛ loke  eva mayā nirvartyata iti sampādayati yā hutā adhiśerate manuṣya lokam eva tām ijayati bhūmi upari sambandha sāmānyāt  adha iva hi agha eva hi manuṣya lokaḥ uparitanān sādhyān  lokān apekṣya athavā adhas gamanam apekṣya atas  manuṣya loke  eva mayā nirvartyata iti sampādayati yā hutā adhiśerate manuṣya lokam eva tābhijayati bhūmi upari sambandha sāmānyāt  adha iva hi adha eva hi manuṣya lokaḥ uparitanān sādhyān  lokān apekṣya athavā adhas gamanam apekṣya atas  manuṣya loke  eva mayā nirvartyata iti sampādayati payaḥ soma āhuti nirvartana kāle yājñavalkya iti ha uvāca iti pūrvavat  ayam ṛtvij brahmā dakṣiṇatas  brahmāsane sthitvā yajñam gopāyati katibhiḥ devatābhiḥ gopāyati iti prāsaṅgikam etad vahuvacanam ekayā hi devatayā gopāyati asau evam jñāte bahuvacanena praśnaḥ  na upapadyate svayam jānataḥ tasmāt pūrvayoḥ kaṇḍikayoḥ praśna prativacaneṣu katibhiḥ kati tisṛbhiḥ tistra iti prasaṅgam dṛṣṭvā iha api bahuvacanena eva praśna upakramaḥ kriyate athavā prativādivyāmoha artha bahuvacanam itara āha ekayā iti ekā sā devatā yayā dakṣiṇatas  sthitvā brahmā asane yajñam gopāyati katamā sā ekā iti mana eva iti manaḥ sā devatā manasā hi brahmā vyāpriyate dhyānena eva tasya yajñasya manaḥ ca vāc ca vartanī tayoḥ anyatarām manasā saṃskaroti brahmā iti śruti antarāt tena mana eva devatā tayā manasā hi gopāyati brahmā yajñam tad ca manaḥ  vṛtti bhedena anantam vaiśabdaḥ prasiddha avadyotana arthaḥ prasiddham manasa ānantyma tad ā ānantyā abhimāninaḥ  devāḥ sarve devāḥ  yatra ekam bhavanti ityādi śruti antarāt tena ānantya sāmānyāt anantam eva sa tena lokam jayati yājñavalkya iti ha uvāca iti pūrvavat  kati stotriyāḥ stopyati iti ayam udgātā stotriyā nāma ṛc sāma samudāyaḥ katipayānām ṛcām stotriya avāśamyāvāyāḥ kāścana ṛcaḥ tā sarvāstiḥ tra eva iti āha tāḥ ca vyākhyātāḥ muronuvākyā ca yājyā ca śasya eva tṛtīyā iti tatra pūrvam uktam yad kiñca idam prāṇabhṛta sarve jayati iti tad  kena sāmānyena iti ucyate katamāḥ tāstiḥ tra ṛcaḥ  yā adhyātmam bhavanti iti prāṇa eva puronuvākyā paśabda sāmānyāt  avānaḥ yājyā ānantaryāt  apānena hi prattam haviḥ devatā grasanti yāgaḥ ca pradānam vyānaḥśasyā aprāṇan  anapānat nṛcam abhivyāharati iti śrati antarāt  kim tābhiḥ jayati iti vyākhyātam tatra viśeṣa sambandha sāmānyam anuktam iha ucyate sarvam anyat  vyākhyātam loka sambandha sāmānyena pṛthivī lokam eva puronuvākyayā jayati antarikṣa lokam yājyayā madhyamatva sāmānyāt  dyulokaṃśasyayā ūrdhvatva sāmānyāt tatas  ha tasmāt ātmanaḥ praśna nirṇayāt asau hotā aśvala upararāma na ayam asmad gecara iti iti tṛtīyā adhyāye prathamam aśvala brāhmaṇam ākhyāyikā sambandhaḥ prasiddha eva mṛtyoḥ ati muktiḥ vyākhyātā kāla lakṣaṇāt  karma lakṣaṇāt ca kaḥ punar asau mṛtyuḥ yasmāt ati muktiḥ vyākhyātā sa ca svābhāvikā jñāna āsaṅga āspadaḥ  adhyātma adhibhūta aviṣaya paricchinnaḥ  graha atigraha lakṣaṇaḥ  mṛtyuḥ tasmāt  paricchinna rūpāt mṛtyoḥ atimuktasya rūpāṇi aganyāt ityādīn yudgītha prakaraṇe vyākhyātāni aśvala praśneca tadgataḥ  viśeṣaḥ kaścid  tad ca etad  karmaṇām jñāna sahitānām phalam etasmāt  sādhya sādhana rūpāt  saṃsārāt mokṣaḥ kartavya iti atobandhana rūpasya mṛtyoḥ svarūpam ucyate baddhasya hi mokṣaḥ kartavyaḥ yad api atimuktasya sva rūpam uktam tatra api graha atigraha abhyām avinirmukta eva mṛtyu rūpābhyām tathā ca uktam aśanāya ahi mṛtyuḥ eṣa eva mṛtyuḥ iti āditya stham puruṣam aṅgīkṛtya āha ekaḥ  mṛtyuḥ vahavā iti ca tad ātma bhāva āpannaḥ  hi mṛtyoḥ āptimatimucyata iti ucyate na ca tatra graha atigrahau mṛtyu rūpau nastas  atha etasya manasaḥ  dyauḥ śarīram jyotīrūpam asau  ādityaḥ amanaśva agrahaḥ sa kāmena atigrāheṇa gṛhītaḥ iti vakṣyati prāṇaḥ  vai grahaḥ saḥ  apānena atigrāheṇa iti vāc vai grahaḥ sa nāmnā atigrāheṇa iti ca tathā vyanna vibhāge vyākhyātam asmābhiḥ su vicāritam ca etad  yad eva pravṛtti kāraṇam tad eva nivṛtti kāraṇam na bhavati iti kecid tu sarvam eva nivṛtti kāraṇam manyante atas  kāgṇāt  pūrvasmāt pūrvasmāt mṛtyoḥ mucyate uttaram uttaram pratipadyamānaḥ  vyāvṛtti artham eva prati padyate na tu tādarthyam iti ata ā dvaita kṣayāta sarvam mṛtyuḥ dvaina kṣaye tu paramārtha tā mṛtyoḥ āptimatimucyate atas ca āpekṣikī gauṇī muktiḥ antarāle sarvam etad  evat  abārhat āraṇyakam nanu sarva eka tvam mokṣaḥ tasmāt tad sarvam abhavat iti śruteḥ bāḍham bhavati etad api na tu grāma kāmaḥ  yajeta paśu kāmaḥ  yajeta ityādi śrutīnām tādarthyam yadi hi advaita artha tvam eva āsām grāma paśu svarga ādi artha tvam na asti iti grāma paśu svargāt ayaḥ  na gṛhyeran gṛhyante tu karma phala vaicitrya viśeṣāḥ yadi ca vaidikānām karmaṇām tādarthyam eva saṃsāra eva na abhaviṣyat atha tādarthye api anuniṣpādita padārtha svabhāvaḥ saṃsāra iti ced  yathā ca rūpa darśana artha āloke sarvaḥ  api tatrasthaḥ prakāśyata eva na  pramāṇa anupapatteḥ advaita artha tve vaidikānām karmaṇām vidyā sahitānām anya spānu niṣpādita tve pramāṇa anupapattiḥ na pratyakṣam na anumānam ata eva ca na āgamaḥ ubhayam ekena vākyena pradarśyata iti ced  kulyā praṇayana āloka ādivat  tad nevam  vākya dharma anupapatteḥ na ca eka vākya gatasya arthasya pravṛtti nivṛtti sādhana tvam avagantum śakyate kulyā praṇayana āloka ādau  arthasya pratyakṣa tvāt adoṣaḥ yad api ucyate mantrā asmin  artheḥ dṛṣṭā iti ayam eva tu tāvat arthaḥ pramāṇa agamyaḥ mantrāḥ punar  kim asmin  artha āhosvit anyasmin  artha iti mṛgyam etad  tasmāt  graha ati praha lakṣaṇaḥ  mṛtyuḥ bandhaḥ tasmāt bhokṣaḥ  vaktavya iti ata idam ārabhyate na ca jānīmaḥ  viṣaya sandhau  iva antarāle avasthānam ardha jaratīyam kauśalam yad tu mṛtyoḥ atimucyata iti ukatvā graha atigrahau  ucyete tacu artha sambandhāt sarvaḥ  ayam sādhya sādhana lakṣaṇaḥ  bandhaḥ graha atigraha avinirmokāt nigaḍe hi nirjñāte nigaḍitasya mokṣāya yatnaḥ kartavyaḥ  bhavati tasmātādarthyena ārambhaḥ atha ha enam ha śabda aitihya arthaḥ atha anantaram aśvala uparate prakṛtam yājñavalkyam jaratkāru gotraḥ  jāratkārava ṛta bhāgasya apatyam ārta bhāgaḥ papraccha yājñavalkya iti ha uvāca iti abhimukhokaraṇāya pūrvavat praśnaḥ kati grahāḥ kati atigrahā iti iti śabdaḥ  vākya parisamāpti arthaḥ tatra nirjñāteṣu vā graha atigraheṣu praśnaḥ syāt anirjñāteṣu vā yadi tāvat grahā atigrahāḥ ca nirjñātāḥ tadā tad gatasya api guṇasya saṃkhyāyāḥ  nijñāta tvāt kati grahāḥ kati atigrahā iti saṃkhyā viṣayaḥ praśnaḥ  na upapadyate atha nirjñātāḥ tadā saṃkhyeya viṣaya praśna iti ke grahāḥ ke atigrahā iti praṣṭavyam na tu kati grahāḥ kati atigrahā iti praśnaḥ api ca nirjñāta sāmānya keśu viśeṣa vijñānāya praśnaḥ  bhavati yathā katame atra kaṭhāḥ katame atra kāla apā iti na ca atra graha atigrahā nāma padārthāḥ kecana loke prasiddhāḥ yena viśeṣa arthaḥ praśnaḥ syāt  nanu ca atimucyata iti uktam graha gṛha utasya hi mokṣaḥ sa muktiḥ sā atimuktiḥ iti hi dvis uktam tasmāt prāptā grahā atigrahāḥ ca nanu tatra api catvāraḥ  grahā atigrahāḥ ca nirjñātā vāc cakṣuḥ prāṇa manāṃsi tatra kati iti praśnaḥ  na upapadyate nirjñāta tvāt  na anavadhāraṇa artha tvāt na hi catuṣṭvam tatra vivakṣitam iha tu graha atigraha adarśane aṣṭhatva guṇa vivakṣayā katoti praśna upapadyata eva tasmāt sa muktiḥ sā atimuktiḥ iti mukti atiktī dvis ukte graha atigrahā api siddhāḥ atas  kati saṃkhyākā grahāḥ kati vā atigrahā iti pṛcchati itara āha aṣṭau grahā aṣṭau  atigrahā iti ye te aṣṭau grahā abhihitāḥ katame te niyamena grahītavyā iti tatrā aha prāṇaḥ  vai grahaḥ prāṇa iti ghrāṇam ucyate prakaraṇāt  vāyu sahitaḥ saḥ apānena iti gandhena iti etad  apāna saciva tvāt apānaḥ  gandha ucyate apāna upahṛtam hi gandham ghrāṇena sarvaḥ  lokaḥ  jighrati tad etad ucyate apānena hi gandhān jighrati iti vāc vai grahaḥ vācā hi adhyātma paricchinnayā asaṅga viṣaya āspadayā asatya anṛta asabhya bībhatsād ivacaneṣu vyāpṛtayā gṛhītaḥ  lokaḥ  apahṛtaḥ tena vāggrahaḥ sa nāmnā atigrāreṇa gṛhītaḥ sa vāc ākhyaḥ  grahaḥ  nāmnā vaktavyena viṣayeṇa atigraheṇa atigrāheṇa iti daighyam chāndasam nāma vaktavya arthā hi vāktena vaktavyena arthena tādarthyena prayuktā vāktena vaśīkṛtā tena tad kāryam akṛtvā na eva tasyāḥ  mokṣaḥ atas  nāmnā atigrāheṇa gṛhītā vāc iti ucyate vakta vyāsaṅgena hi pravṛttā sarva anarthaiḥ yujyate samānam anyat  iti ete tvac paryantā aṣṭau grahāḥ sparśa paryantāḥ ca ete aṣṭau  atigrahā iti upasaṃhṛteṣu graha atigraheṣu āha punar  yājñavalkya iti ha uvāca yad idam sarvam mṛtyoḥ annam yad idam vyākṛtam sarvam mṛtyoḥ annam sarvam jāyate vipadyate ca graha atigraha lakṣaṇena mṛtyunā grastam kāsvitkā nu syāt sā devatā yasyāḥ  devatāyāḥ  mṛtyuḥ api annam bhavet  mṛtyuḥ yasya upasecanam iti śruti antarāt ayam abhiprāyaḥ praṣṭuḥ yadi mṛtyoḥ mṛtyum vakṣyati anavasthā syāt  atha na vakṣyati asmāt graha atigraha lakṣaṇāt mṛtyoḥ mokṣaḥ  na upapadyate graha atigraha mṛtyu vināśe hi mokṣaḥ yāt  sa yadi mṛtyoḥ api mṛtyuḥ syāt bhavet graha atigraha lakṣaṇasya mṛtyoḥ vināśaḥ atas  durvacanam praśnam manvānaḥ pṛcchati kāsvitsā devatā iti asti tāvat mṛtyoḥ mṛtyuḥ nanu anavasthā syāt tasya api anyaḥ  mṛtyuḥ iti na anavasthā sarva mṛtyoḥ mṛtyu antara anupapatteḥ katham punar avagamyate asti mṛtyoḥ mṛtyuḥ iti dṛṣṭa tvāt  agniḥ tāvat sarvasya dṛṣṭaḥ  mṛtyuḥ vināśaka tvāt  saḥ  adbhiḥ bhakṣyate saḥ  agniḥ apām annam gṛhāṇa tarhi asti mṛtyoḥ mṛtyuḥ iti tena sarvam graha atigraha jātam bhakṣyate mṛtyoḥ mṛtyunā tasmin bandhane nāśite mṛtyunā bhakṣite saṃsārāt mokṣa upapannaḥ  bhavati bandhanam hi graha atigraha lakṣaṇam uktam tasmāt ca mokṣa upapadyata iti etad prasādhitam atas  bandha mokṣāya puruṣa prayāsaḥ saphalaḥ  bhavati atas  apajayati punar mṛtyum pareṇa mṛtyunā mṛtyau bhakṣite paramātma darśanena yaḥ  asau muktaḥ  vidvān saḥ  ayam puruṣaḥ  yatra yasmin kāle mriyata udūrdhvam asmāt brahma vidaḥ  mriyamāṇāt prāṇā vā agadayaḥ  grahā nāma ādayaḥ ca atigrahā vāsanā rūpā antasthāḥ prayojakāḥ kāmatnī ūrdhvam utkrāmanti āhosvit na iti na iti ha uvāca yājñavalkyaḥ  na utkrāmanti atra eva asmin  eva pareṇā atmanā vibhāgam gacchanti viduṣi kāryāṇi karaṇāni ca sva yonau para brahma sa tattave samavanīyanta ekībhāvena samavasṛjyante pralīyanta iti arthaḥ ūrmaya ida samudre tathā ca śruti antaram kalā śabda vācyānām prāṇānām parasmin  ātmani pralayam darśayati evam eva asya paridraṣṭuḥ imāḥ ṣoḍaśa kalāḥ puruṣāyaṇāḥ puruṣam prāpya astam gacchantī ti iti pareṇā atmanā vibhāgam gacchanti iti darśitam na tarhi mṛtaḥ  na hi mṛtaḥ ca ayam yasmāt sa ucchvayati ucchūnatām pratipadyata ādhmāyati bāhyena vāyunā pūryate dṛtivat ādhmātaḥ  mṛtaḥ śete niśceṣṭaḥ bandhana nāśe muktasya na kvacid gamanam iti vākya arthaḥ muktasya kim prāṇā eva samavanoyanta āhosvit tad prayojakam api sarvam atha prāṇā eva na tad prayojakam sarva prayojake vidyamāne punar  prāṇānām prasaṅgaḥ atha sarvam eva kāma karma ādi tatas  mokṣa upapadyata iti evam artha uttaraḥ praśnaḥ yājñavalkya iti ha uvāca yatra ayam puruṣaḥ  mriyate kim enam na jahāti iti āha itaraḥ  nāma iti sarvam samavanīyata iti arthaḥ nāma mātram tu na līyata ākṛti sambandhāt  nityam hi nāma anantam vai nāma nitya tvam evā anantyam nāmnaḥ tad ānantyā adhikṛtā anantā bai viśve devāḥ  anantam eva sa tena lokam jayati tad nāma ānantya adhikṛtān viśvān devān ātma tvena upetya tenā anantya darśanena anantam eva lokam jayati graha atigraha rūpam bandhanam uktam mṛtyu rūpam tasya ca mṛtyoḥ mṛtyu sadbhāvāt mokṣaḥ ca upapadyate sa ca mokṣaḥ  graha atigraha rūpāṇām iha eva pralayaḥ pradīpa nirvāṇavat  yadvat graha atigraha ākhyam bandhanam mṛtyu rūpam tasya yad prayojakam tad svarūpa nirdhāraṇa artham idam ārabhyate yājñavalkya iti ha uvāca atra kecid varṇayanti graha atigrahasya sa prayojakasya vināśe api kila na mucyate nāma avaśiṣṭaḥ  avidya yā uṣara sthānīyayā sva ātma prabhavayā pa mā ātmanaḥ paricchinnaḥ  bhojyāt ca jagataḥ  vyāvṛtta ucchinna kāma karma antarāle vyavatiṣṭhate tasya paramātmā ekatva darśane dvaita darśanam apanetavyam iti atas  param paramātma darśanam ārabdhavyam iti evam apavarga ākhyām antarāla avasthām parikalya uttara grantha saṃbandham kurvanti tatra vaktavyam viśīrṇeṣu karaṇeṣu videhasya paramātma darśana śravaṇa manana nididhi āsanāni katham iti samavanīta prāṇasya hi nāma mātra avaśiṣṭasya iti taiḥ ucyate mṛtaḥ śeta iti hayuktam na manorathena api etad upapādayitum śakyate atha jīvan  eva avidyā mātra avaśiṣṭaḥ  bhojyāt apāvṛtta iti parikalpyate tad tu kiṃnimittam iti vaktavyam samasta dvaita ekatva ātma prāpti nimittam iti yadi ucyate tad pūrvam eva nirākṛtam karma sahitena dvaita ekatva ātma darśanena sampannaḥ  vidvān mṛtaḥ samavanīta prāṇaḥ  jagat ātma tvam hiraṇyagarbha svarūpam vā prāpnuyāt asamavanīta prāṇaḥ  bhojyāt jīvan  eva vyāvṛttaḥ  viraktaḥ paramātma darśana abhimukhaḥ syāt  na ca ubhayam eka prayatna niṣpādyena sādhanena labhyam hiraṇyagarbha prāpti sādhanam ced na tatas  vyāvṛtti sādhanam paramātma abhimukhīkaraṇasya bhojyā dvaya āvṛtteḥ sādhanam ced na hiraṇyagarbha prāpti sādhanam na hi yad gati sādhanam tad gati nivṛtteḥ api atha mṛtvā hiraṇyagarbham prāpya tatas  samavanīta prāṇaḥ  nāma avaśiṣṭaḥ paramātma jñāne adhikriyate tatas  asmad ādi artham paramātma jñāna upadeśaḥ  anarthakaḥ syāt  sarveṣām hi brahma vidyā puruṣa arthāya upadiśyate tad yaḥ yaḥ  devānām ityādyayā śrutyā tasmāt atyanta nikṛṣṭā śāstra bāhya eva iyam kalpanā prakṛtam tu vartayiṣyāma tatra kena prayuktam graha atigraha lakṣaṇam bandhanam iti etad nirdidha ārayiṣayā aha yatra asya puruṣasya asamyak darśinaḥ śiraḥ pāṇi ādimataḥ  mṛtasya vāc agnim apyeti vātam prāṇaḥ  apyeti cakṣuḥ ādityam api eti iti sarvatra sambadhyate manaḥ candram diśaḥ śrotram pṛthivīm śarīram ākāśam ātmā iti atrā atma adhiṣṭhānam hṛdaya ākāśam ucyate sa ākāśam apyeti oṣadhīḥ apiyati lomāni vanaspatīn apiyanti keśāḥ apsu lohitam ca retaḥ ca nidhīyata iti punar ādāna liṅgam sarvatra hi vāc ādi śabdena devatāḥ parigṛhyante na tu karaṇāni eva apakrāmanti prāk mokṣāt  tatra devatābhiḥ anadhiṣṭhitāni karaṇāni nyasta dātrā ādi upamānāni videhaḥ ca kartā puruṣaḥ  asvatantraḥ kim āśritaḥ  bhavati iti pṛcchayate kva ayam tadā puruṣaḥ  bhavati iti kim āśritaḥ tadā puruṣaḥ  bhavati iti yam āśrayam āśritya punar  kārya karaṇa saṃghātam upādatte yena graha atigraha lakṣaṇam bandhanam prayujyate tad kim iti praśnaḥ atra ucyate svabhāvayadṛcchā kāla karma daiva vijñāna mātra śūnyāni vādibhiḥ parikalpitāni atas  aneka vipratipatti sthāna tvāt na eva jalpa nyāyena vastu nirṇayaḥ atra vastu nirṇayam ced icchasyāhara sobhya hasta sārtabhāga ha āvām eva etasya tvad pṛṣṭasya veditavyam yad tad vediṣyāvaḥ  nirūpayiṣyāvaḥ kasmāt  na na avāvayoḥ etad vastu sa jane jana samudāye nirṇetum śakyate ata ekānta gamiṣyāvaḥ  vicāraṇāya tau hā ityādi śruti vacanam tau yājñavalkya ārta bhāgau  ekāntam gatvā kim cakratuḥ iti ucyate tau ha utkramya sa janāt deśān mantrayāñca krāte ādau laukika vādi pakṣāṇām ekaikam parugṛhya vicāritavantau tau ha vicārya yad ū catuḥ apohya pūrva pakṣān sarvān eva tad śṛṇu karma ha evā aśrayam punar  punar  kārya karaṇa upādāna hetum tad tatra ūcatur uktavantau na kevalam kāla karma dā eva īśvareṣu abhyupagateṣu hetuṣu yad praśaśaṃsatuḥ tau karma ha eva tad praśaśaṃsatuḥ yasmāt nirdhāritam etad karma prayuktam graha atigraha ādi kārya karaṇa upādānam punar  punar tasmāt puṇyaḥ  vai śāstra vihitena puṇyena karmaṇā bhavati tad viparotena viparītaḥ  bhavati pāpaḥ pāpena iti evam yājñavalkyena praśneṣu nirṇīteṣu tatas  aśakya prakampya tvāt yājñavalkyasya ha jaratkārava ārtabhāga upararāma iti tṛtīyā adhyāye dvitīyam ārta bhāga brāhmaṇam atha ha enam bhujyuḥ lāhyāyaniḥ papraccha graha atigraha lakṣaṇam bandhanam uktam yasmāt sa prayojakāt muktaḥ  mucyate yena vā baddhaḥ saṃsarati sa mṛtyuḥ tasmāt ca mokṣa upapadyate yasmāt mṛyoḥ mṛtyuḥ asti muktasya ca na gatiḥ kvacid  sarva utsādaḥ  nāma mātra avaśeṣaḥ pradīpa nirvāṇavat iti ca avadhṛtam tatra saṃsaratām mucyamānānām ca kārya karaṇānām sva kāraṇa saṃsarge samāne muktānām atyantam eva punar anupādānam saṃsaratām tu punar  punar upādānam yena prayuktānām bhavati tad karma iti avadhāritam vicāraṇā pūrvakam tad kṣaye ca nāma avaśeṣeṇa sarva utsādaḥ  mokṣaḥ tad ca puṇya pāpa ākhyam karma puṇyaḥ  vai puṇyena karmaṇā bhavati pāpaḥ pāpena iti avadhārita tvāt etad kṛtaḥ saṃsāraḥ tatra apuṇyena sthāvara jaṅgameṣu svabhāva duḥkha bahuleṣu naraka tiryak preta ādiṣu ca duḥkham anubhavati punar  punar jāyamānaḥ  mriyamāṇaḥ ca iti etad rāja vartmavat sarva loka prasiddham yad tu śāstrī iyam puṇyaḥ  vai puṇyena karmaṇā bhavati tatra eva ādaraḥ kriyata iha śrutyā puṇyam eva ca karma sarva puruṣa artha sādhanam iti sarve śruti smṛti vādāḥ mokṣasya api puruṣa artha tvāt tad sādhyatā prāptā yāvat yāvat puṇya utkarṣaḥ tāvat tāvat phala utkarṣa prāptiḥ tasmāt uttam eva puṇya utkarṣeṇa mokṣaḥ  bhaviṣyati iti āśaṅkā syāt  sā nivartayitavyā jñāna sahitasya ca prakṛṣṭasya karmaṇa etāvatī gatiḥ vyākṛta nāma rūpa āspada tvāt karmaṇaḥ tad phalasya ca na tu akārye nitye avyākṛta dharmiṇya nāma rūpa ātmake kriyā kāraka phala svabhāva varjite karmaṇaḥ  vyāpāraḥ  asti yatra ca vyāpāraḥ sa saṃsāra eva iti asya arthasya pradarśanāya brahmaṇam ārabhyate yad tu kaiścid ucyate vidyā sahitam karma nirabhisaṃdhi mantra śarkarā ādi yukta viṣada dhyādivat kārya antaram ārabhata iti tad na anārabhya tvāt mokṣasya bandha nāśa eva hi mokṣaḥ  na kārya bhūtaḥ bandhanam ca avidyā iti avocāma avidyāyāḥ ca na karmaṇā nāśa upapadyate dṛṣṭa viṣayatva acva karma sāmarthyasya utpatti āpti vikāra saṃskārā hi karma sāmarthyasya viṣayāḥ utpādayitum prāpayitum vikartum ca sāmarthyam karmaṇaḥ  na atas  vyatirikta viṣayaḥ  asti karma sāmarthyasya loke aprasiddha tvāt  na ca mokṣa eṣām padārthānām anyatamaḥ avidyā mātra vyavahita iti avocāma bāḍham bhavatu kevalasya eva karmaṇa evaṃsvabhāva tā vidyā saṃyuktasya tu nirabhisaṃdheḥ bhavati anyathā svabhāvaḥ dṛṣṭam hi anya śakti tvena nirjñātānām api padārthānām viṣa dadhi ādīnām vidyā mantra śarkarā ādi saṃyuktānām anya viṣaye sāmathyam tathā karmaṇaḥ  api astu iti ced  na pramāṇa abhāvāt  tatra hi karmaṇa ukta viṣaya vyatirekeṇa viṣaya antare sāmarthya astitve pramāṇam na pratyakṣam na anumānam na upamānam na arthāpattiḥ na śabdaḥ  asti nanu phala antara abhāve codanāni atha anupapattiḥ pramāṇam iti na hi nityānām karmaṇām viśva jit nyāyena phalam kalpyate na api śrutam phalam asti codyante ca tāni pāriśeṣyāt mokṣaḥ teṣām phalam iti gamyate anyathā hi puruṣā na pravarteran nanu viśvajit nyāya evā ayātaḥ  mokṣasya phalasya kalpita tvāt  mokṣe vā anyasmin vā phale akalpite puruṣā na pravarteran  iti mokṣaḥ phalam kalpyate śruta artha āpattyā yathā viśvajiti nanu evam sati katham ucyate viśvajit nyāyaḥ  na bhavati iti phalam ca kalpyate viśva jit nyāyaḥ ca na bhavati iti vipratiṣiddham abhidhīyate mokṣaḥ phalam eva na bhavati iti ced  na pratijñāhānāt  karma kārya antaram viṣadadhi ādivat ārabhata iti hi pratijñātam sa ced mokṣaḥ karmaṇaḥ kāryam phalam eva na bhavati iti sā pratijñā hīyeta karma kārya tve ca mokṣasya svarga ādi phalebhyaḥ  viśeṣaḥ  vaktavyaḥ atha karma kāryam na bhavati nityānām karmaṇām phalam mokṣa iti asyā vacana vyakteḥ kor atha iti vaktavyam na ca kārya phala śabda bheda mātreṇa viśeṣaḥ śakyaḥ kalpayitum aphalam ca mokṣaḥ  nityaiḥ ca karmabhiḥ kriyate nityānām karmaṇām phalam na kāryam iti ca eṣor athaḥ vipratiṣiddhaḥ  abhidhīyate yathā agniḥ śīta iti jñānavat iti ced  yathā jñānasya kāryam mokṣaḥ  jñānena akriyamāṇaḥ  api ucyate tadvat karma kāryatvam iti ced  na ajñāna nivartaka tvāt jñānasya ajñāna vyavadhāna nivartaka tvāt jñānasya mokṣaḥ  jñāna kāryam iti upacaryate na tu karmaṇā nivartayitavyam ajñānam na ca ajñāna vyatirekeṇa mokṣasya vyavadhāna antaram kalpayitum śakyam nitya tvāt mokṣasya sādhaka svarūpa avyatirekāt ca yad karmaṇā nivartyeta ajñānam eva nivartayati iti ced  na vilakṣaṇa tvāt  anabhivyaktiḥ ajñānam abhivyakti lakṣaṇena jñānena virudhyate karma tu tājñānena virudhyate tena jñāna vilakṣaṇam karma yadi jñāna abhāvaḥ  yadi saṃśaya jñānam yadi viparīta jñānam vā ucyate ajñānam iti sarvam hi tad jñānena eva nivartyate na tu karmaṇā anyatamena api virodha abhāvāt atha adṛṣṭam karmaṇām ajñāna nivartaka tvam kalpyam iti ced  na jñānena ajñāna nivṛttau gamyamāna āyām dṛṣṭa nivṛtti kalpanā anupapatteḥ yathā avaghātena vrīhīṇām tuṣa nivṛttau gamyamānāyām agni hotra ādi nityakarma kārya adṛṣṭā na kalpyate tuṣa nivṛttiḥ tadvat ajñāna nivṛttiḥ api nitya karma kārya adṛṣṭā na kalpyate jñānena viruddha tvam ca asakṛt karmaṇām avocāma yad aviruddham jñānam karmabhiḥ tad deva loka prāpti nimittam iti uktam vidyayā deva lokaḥ iti śruteḥ kiñca anyat kalpye ca phale nityānām karmaṇām śrutānām yad karmabhiḥ virudhyate dravya guṇa karmaṇām kāryam eva na bhavati kim tad kalpyatām iti yasmin karmaṇaḥ sāmarthyam eva na dṛṣṭam kiṃvā yasmin dṛṣṭam sāmarthyam yad ca karmaṇām phalam aviruddham tad kalpyatām iti puruṣa pravṛtti jananāya avaśyam ced karma phalam kalpayitavyam karma aviruddha viṣaya eva śruta arthāpatteḥ kṣīṇa tvāt nityaḥ  mokṣaḥ phalam kalpayitum na śakyaḥ tad vyavadhāna ajñāna nivṛttiḥ vā aviruddha tvāt dṛṣṭa sāmarthya viṣaya tvāt ca iti pāriśeṣya nyāyāt mokṣa eva kalpayitavya iti ced  sarveṣām hi karmaṇām sarvam phalam na ca anyat itara karma phala vyatirekeṇa phalam kalpanā yogyam asti pariśiṣṭaḥ ca mokṣaḥ sa ceṣṭaḥ veda vidām phalam tasmāt sa eva kalpayitavya iti ced  na karma phala vyaktonām ānantyāt pāriśeṣī anyāya anupapatteḥ na hi puruṣa icchā viṣayāṇām karma phalānām etāvat tvam nāma kenacid asarva jñena avadhṛtam tad sādhanānām vā puruṣa icchānām vā aniyata deśa kāla nimitta tvāt puruṣa icchā viṣaya sādhanānām ca puruṣa iṣṭa phala prayukta tvāt  pratiprāṇi ca icchā vaicitryāt phalānām tad sādhanānām cā anantya siddhiḥ tad ānantyāt ca aśakyam etāvat tvam puruṣaiḥ jñātum ajñāte ca sādhana phala etāvat tve katham mokṣasya pariśeṣa siddhiḥ iti karma phala jāti pāriśeṣyam iti ced  sati api icchā viṣayāṇām tad sādhanānām cā anantye karma phala jāti tvam nāma sarveṣām tulyam mokṣa satva karma phala tvāt pariśiṣṭaḥ syāt  tasmāt pariśeṣāt sa eva yuktaḥ kalpayitum iti ced  na tasya api nitya karma phalatva abhyupagame karma phala samāna jātīyatva upapatteḥ pariśeṣa anupapattiḥ tasmāt anyathā api upapatteḥ kṣīṇā śruta arthāpattiḥ utpattaya āpti vikāra saṃskārāṇām anyatam api nityānām karmaṇām phalam upapadyata iti kṣīṇā śruta arthāpattiḥ caturṇām anyatama eva mokṣa iti ced  na tāvat utpādyaḥ  nitya tvāt  ata eva avikāryaḥ  asaṃskāryaḥ ca āta eva asādhana dravya ātmaka tvāt ca sādhana ātmakam hi dravyam saṃskriyate yathā pātra ājya ādi prokṣaṇa ādinā na ca saṃskriyamāṇaḥ saṃskāra nirvartyaḥ  vā yūpa ādivat  pāriśeṣyāt āpyaḥ syāt  nā api aḥ  api ātma svabhāva tvāt ekatvāt ca itaraiḥ karmabhiḥ vailakṣaṇyāt nityānām karmaṇām tad phalena api vilakṣaṇena bhavitavyam iti ced  na karma tvasā lakṣaṇyāt sa lakṣaṇam kasmāt phalam na bhavati itara karma phalaiḥ nimitta vailakṣaṇyāt iti ced  na kṣāmavatī ādibhiḥ samāna tvāt  yathā hi gṛha dāha ādau nimitte kṣāmavatī ādi iṣṭiḥ yathā bhinne juhoti skanne juhoti iti evamādau naimittikeṣu karmasu na mokṣaḥ phalam kalpyate taiḥ ca aviśeṣāt naimittika tvena jīvana ādi nimitte ca śravaṇāt  tathā nityānām api na mokṣaḥ phalam ālokasya sarveṣām rūpa darśana sādhanatva ulūka ādaya ālokena rūpam na paśyanti iti ulukā ādi cakṣuṣaḥ  vailakṣaṇyāditara loka cakṣurbhiḥ na rasa ādi viṣaya tvam parikalpyate rasa ādi viṣaye sāmarthyasya adṛṣṭa tvāt su dūram api gatvā yad viṣaye dṛṣṭam sāmarthyam tatra eva kaścid viśeṣaḥ kalpayitavyaḥ yad punaruktam vidyā mantra śarkarā ādi saṃyukta viṣada dadhi ādivat nityāni kārya antaram ārabhanta iti ārabhyatām viśiṣṭam kāryam tad iṣṭa tvāt avirodhaḥ nirabhisaṃdheḥ karmaṇaḥ  vidyā saṃyuktasya viśiṣṭa kārya antara ārambhe na kaścid virodhaḥ deva yājya ātma yājinoḥ ātma yājinaḥ  viśeṣa śravaṇāt deva yājinaḥ aśreyān ātma yājī atyādau ayat eva vidyayā karotī atyādau ca yaḥ tu paramātma darśana viṣaye manunā ukta ātma yāji śabdaḥ asamam paśyan  ātma yājī atyatra samam paśyan  ātma yājī bhavati iti arthaḥ athavā bhūta pūrva gatyā ātmayājya ātma saṃskāra artham nityāni karmāṇi karoti idam me anena aṅga saṃskriyate iti śruteḥ tathā gārbhaiḥ hemaiḥ iti ādi prakaraṇe kārya karaṇa saṃskāra artha tvam nityānām karmaṇām darśayati saṃskṛtaḥ ca ya ātma yājī taiḥ karmabhiḥ samam draṣṭum samarthaḥ  bhavati tasya iha vā janmāntare vā samam ātma darśanam utpadyate samam paśyan svārājyam adhigacchati iti eṣor athaḥ ātma yāji śabdaḥ tu bhūta pūrva gatyā prayujyate jñāna yuktānām nityānām karmaṇām jñāna utpatti sādhanatva pradarśana artham kiñca anyat brahmā viśvasṛjaḥ  dharmaḥ  mahān avyaktam eva ca uttamām sāttvikīm etām gatim āhuḥ manīṣiṇaḥ iti ca deva sārṣṭi vyatirekeṇa bhūta apyayam darśayati bhūtāni apyeti pañca vai bhūtāni atyeti iti pāṭham ye kurvanti teṣām veda viṣaye paricchinna buddhi tvāt adoṣaḥ na ca arthavāda tvam adhyāyasya brahmānta karma vipāka arthasya tadvayati rikta ātma jñāna arthasya ca karma kāṇḍa upaniṣad bhayām tulya arthatva darśanāt vihita akaraṇa pratiṣiddha karmaṇām ca sthāvara śva sūkara ādi phala darśanāt vānta āśya ādi preta darśanāt ca na ca śruti smṛti vīrīta pratiṣiddha vyatirekeṇa vihitāni vā pratiṣiddhān ivā karmāṇi kenacid avagantum śakyante yeṣām akaraṇāt anuṣṭhānāt ca preta śva sūkara sthāvara ādīni karma phalāni pratyakṣa anumānābhyām upalabhyante na ca eṣām akarma phala tvam kenacid abhyupagamyate tasmāt vihita akaraṇa pratiṣiddha sevānām yathā ete karma vipākāḥ preta tiryak sthāvara ādayaḥ tathā utkṛṣṭeṣu api brahma anteṣu karma vipāka tvam veditavyam tasmāt  sa ātmanaḥ  vapām udakhidat  saḥ  arodīdi tyādi vannā bhūta arthavāda tvam tatra api abhūta arthavat atvam mā bhūt iti ced  bhavatu evam na ca etāvatā asya nyāyasya bādhaḥ  bhavati na ca asmad pakṣaḥ  vā duṣyati na ca brahmā viśvasṛja ityādīnām kāmya karma phala tvam śakyam vaktum teṣām deva sārṣṭitāyāḥ phalasya ukta tvāt  tasmāt sa abhisaṃdhīnām nityānām karmaṇām sarvamedha aśvamedha ādīnām ca brahmatva ādīni phalāni yeṣām punar nityāni nirabhisaṃdhīni ātma saṃskāra arthāni teṣām jñāna utpatti arthāni tāni brāhmī iyam kriyate tanuḥ iti smaraṇāt  teṣām ārāt upakāraka tvāt mokṣa sādhanāni api karmāṇi bhavanti iti na virudhyate yathā ca ayam arthaḥ ṣaṣṭhe janaka ākhyāyikā samāptau vakṣyāmaḥ yad tu viṣadadhi ādivat iti uktam tatra pratyakṣa anumāna viṣaya tvāt avirodhaḥ yaḥ tu atyanta śabda gamyoḥ athaḥ tatra vākyasya abhāve tad artha pratipādakasya na śakyam kalpayitum viṣa dadhi ādi sādharmyam na ca pramāṇa antara viruddha artha viṣaye śruteḥ prāmāṇyam kalpyate yathā śītaḥ  agniḥ kledayati iti śrute tu tādarthye vākyasya pramāṇa antarasyā abhāsa tvam yathā khadyotaḥ  agniḥ iti tala malinam antarikṣam iti bālānām yad pratyakṣam api tad viṣaya pramāṇa antarasya yathārtha tve niścite niścita artham api bāla pratyakṣam ābhāsībhavati tasmāt veda prāmāṇyasya avyabhicārāt tādarthye sati vākyasya tathā tvam syāt  na tu puruṣam ati kauśalam na hi puruṣamati kauśalāt savitā rūpam na prakāśayati tathā veda vākyāni api na anya arthāni bhavanti tasmāt na mokṣa arthāni karmāṇi iti siddham atas  karma phalānām saṃsāratva pradarśanāya eva brāhmaṇam ārabhyate atha anantaram uparate jārat kārave bhujyuḥ iti nāmataḥ  lahyasya apatyam lāhyaḥ tad apatyam lāhyāyaniḥ papraccha yājñavalkya iti ha uvāca ādābuktam aśvamedha darśanam samaṣṭi vyaṣṭi phalaḥ ca aśvamedha kratuḥ jñāna samuccitaḥ  vā kevala jñāna sampāditaḥ  vā sarva karmaṇām parā kāṣṭhā  bhraṇa hatyā aśvamedhābhyām na param puṇya pāpayoḥ iti hi smaranti tena hi samaṣṭim vyaṣṭīḥ ca prāpnoti tatra vyaṣṭayaḥ  nirjñātā antaraṇḍa viṣayā aśvamedha yāga phala bhūta aḥ  amṛtyuḥ asya ātmā bhavati etāsām devatānām ekā bhavati iti uktam mṛtyuḥ ca aśanāya alakṣaṇaḥ  buddhayā ātmā samaṣṭiḥ prathama jaḥ  vāyuḥ sūtram satyam hiraṇyagarbhaḥ tasya vyākṛtaḥ  viṣayaḥ yad ātmakam sarvam dvaita eka tvam yaḥ sarva bhūta antarātmā liṅgam amūrta rasaḥ  yad āśritāni sarva bhūta karmāṇi yaḥ karmaṇām karma sambaddhānām ca vijñānānām parā gatiḥ param phalam tasya kiyān gocaraḥ kiyati vyāptiḥ sarvatas  parimaṇḍalībhūtā sā vaktavyā tasyām uktāyām sarvaḥ saṃsāraḥ  bandha gocara uktaḥ  bhavati tasya ca samaṣṭi vyaṣṭi ātma darśanasya alaukikatva pradarśana artham ākhyāyikām ātmanaḥ  vṛttām prakurute tena ca prativādi buddhiṃvyāmohayiṣyāmi iti manyate madreṣu madrā nāma janapadāḥ teṣu carakā adhyayana artha vrata caraṇāt carakā adhvaryavaḥ  vā paryavrajāma paryaṭitavantaḥ te patañcalasya nāmataḥ kāpyasya kapi gotrasya gṛhān aima gatavantaḥ tasya āsīt  duhitā gandharva gṛhītā gandharveṇa amānuṣeṇa sacvena kenacid āviṣṭā  gandharvaḥ  vā dhiṣṇyaḥ  agniḥ ṛtvij adevatā viśiṣṭa vijñāna tvāt avasīyate na hi sacva mātrasya īdṛśam vijñānam upapadyate tam sarve vayam parivāritāḥ santaḥ  apṛcchāma kaḥ  asi iti kaḥ tvam asi kinnāmā kiṃsatacvaḥ saḥ  abravīt  gandharvaḥ sudhanvā nāmataḥ āṅgirasaḥ  gotrataḥ tam yadā yasmin kāle lokānām antān paryavasānāni apṛcchāma atha enam gandharvam abrūma bhū vana kośa parimāṇa jñānāya pravṛtteṣu sarveṣu ātmānam ślāghayantaḥ pṛṣṭavantaḥ  vayam katham kva pārikṣitā abhavan  iti sa ca gandharvaḥ sarvam asmabhi abravīt tena divyebhyaḥ  mayā labdham jñānam tad tava na asti atas  nigṛhītaḥ  asi iti abhiprāyaḥ saḥ  aham vidyā sampannaḥ  labdha āgamaḥ  gandharvāt  tvā tvām pṛcchāmi yājñavalkya kva pārikṣitā abhavantat  tvam kim jānāsi he yājñavalkya akathaya pṛcchāmi kva pārikṣitā abhavan  iti sa ha uvāca yājñavalkya uvāca vai saḥ vaiśbdaḥ smaraṇa arthaḥ uvāca vai sa gandharvaḥ tubhyam agacchan vai te pārikṣitāḥ tad tatra kva yatra yasmin  aśvamedha yājinaḥ gacchanti iti nirṇote praśna āha kva nu kasmin  aśvamedha yājinaḥ  gacchanti iti teṣām gati vivakṣayā bhuvana kośa parimāṇam āha dvātriṃśatam vai dve adhike triṃśat dvātriṃśatam vai deva ratha āhrayāni deva ādityaḥ tasya rathaḥ  deva rathaḥ tasya rathasya gati āhrā yāvat paricchidyate deśa parimāṇa  tad deva ratha āhrayam tad dvātriṃśat guṇitam deva ratha āhrayāni tāvat parimāṇaḥ  ayam lokaḥ  lokāloka giriṇā parikṣiptaḥ yatra vairājam śarīram yatra ca karma phala upabhogaḥ prāṇinām sa eṣa loka etāvān  lokaḥ  atas  parama lokaḥ tam lokam samantam samantatas  loka vistārāt dviguṇa parimāṇa vistāreṇa parimāṇena tam lokam parikṣiptā paryeti pṛthivī tām pṛthivīm tathā eva samantam dvis tāvat dviguṇena parimāṇena samudraḥ paryeti yam ghanodam ācakṣate paurāṇikāḥ tatraṇḍa kapālayoḥ vivara parimāṇam ucyate yena vivareṇa mārgeṇa vahiḥ nirgacchantaḥ  vyāpnuvanti aśvamedha yājinaḥ tatra yāvatī yāvat parimāṇa  kṣurasya dhārā agram yāvat vā saukṣmyeṇa yuktam makṣikāyāḥ patram tāvān  tāvat parimāṇaḥ  antareṇa madhye aṇḍakapālayoḥ ākāḥ chidram tenā akāśena iti etad  tān pārikṣitān aśvamedha yājinaḥ prāpta anidraḥ parameśvaraḥ  yaḥ  aśvam eve agniḥ citaḥ suparṇaḥ  yad viṣayam darśanamuktam tasya prāci diviśara ityādinā suparṇaḥ pakṣī bhūtvā pakṣa puccha ādi ātmakaḥ suparṇaḥ  bhūtvā vāyave prāyacchat mūrta tvāt na asti ātmanaḥ  gatiḥ tatra iti tān pārikṣita anvāyuḥ ātmani dhitvā sthāpayitvā sva ātma bhūtān kṛtvā tatra tasmin  agamayat  kva yatra pūrve atikrāntāḥ pārikṣitā aśvamedha yājinaḥ  abhavan  iti evam iva vā evam eva sa gandharvaḥ  vāyum eva praśaśaṃsa pārikṣitānām gatim samāptā akhyāyikā ākhyāyikā nirvṛttam tu artham ākhyāyikātaḥ  apasutya śrutiḥ sva mukhena evā acaṣṭe asmabhyam yasmāt vāyuḥ sthāvara jaṅgamānām bhūtānām antarātmā bahis ca sa eva tasmāt adhyātma adhibhūta adhidaiva bhāvena vividhā yāṣṭiḥ vyāptiḥ sa vāyuḥ eva tathā samaṣṭiḥ kevalena sūtra ātmanā vāyuḥ eva evam vāyum ātmānam samaṣṭi vyaṣṭi rūpa ātmaka tvena upagacchati ya evam veda tasya kim phalam iti āhi apa punar mṛtyum jayati sakṛt mṛtvā punanam mriyate tatas  ātmanaḥ praśna nirṇayāt bhujyuḥ lāhyāya nirupararāma atha ha enam uṣastaḥ cākrāyaṇaḥ papraccha puṇya pāpa prayuktaiḥ graha atigrahaiḥ gṛhītaḥ punar  punar graha atigrahān  tyajan  upādadat saṃsarati iti uktam puṇyasya ca para utkarṣaḥ  vyākhyātaḥ  vyākṛta viṣayaḥ samaṣṭi vyaṣṭi rūpaḥ  dvaita ekatva ātma prāptiḥ yaḥ tu graha atigrahaiḥ grastaḥ saṃsarati saḥ  asti vā na asti astitve ca kiṃlakṣaṇa iti ātmana eva viveka adhigamāya uṣasta praśna ārabhyate tasya ca nirupādhi svarūpasya kriyā kāraka vinirmukta svabhāvasya adhigamāt i athā uktāt vandhanāt vimucyate sa prayojakāt  ākhyāyikā saṃbandhaḥ tu prasiddhaḥ atha ha enam prakṛtam yājñavalkya muṣaḥ taḥ  nāmataḥ cakrasya apatyam cākrāyaṇaḥ papraccha yad brahma sākṣāt avyavahitam kenacid draṣṭuḥ aparokṣāt agauṇam na śrotra brahma ādivat  kim tad  ya ātmā ātma śabdena pratyagātmā ucyate tatrā atma śabdasya prasiddha tvāt  sarvasya abhyantaraḥ sarva antaraḥ yad yaḥ śabdābhyām prasiddha ātmā brahma iti tam ātmānam me mahyam vyācakṣva iti viṣpaṣṭam śṛṅge gṛhītvā yathā gām darśayati tathā acakṣva saḥ  ayam iti evam kathayasva iti arthaḥ evam uktaḥ pratyāha yājñavalkyaḥ eṣu te tavā atmā sarva antaraḥ sarvasya abhyantaraḥ sarva viśeṣaṇa upalabhaṇa artha sarva antara grahaṇam yad sākṣāt avyavahitam aparokṣāt agauṇam brahma bṛhattamam ātmā sarvasya abhyantara etaiḥ guṇaiḥ samastaiḥ ukta eṣaḥ kaḥ  asau tavā atmā yaḥ  ayam kārya karaṇa saṃghātaḥ tava yenā atmanā atmavān sa eṣa tava ātmā tava kārya karaṇa saṃghātasya iti arthaḥ tatra piṇḍaḥ tamya abhyantare liṅga ātmā karaṇa saṃghātaḥ tṛtīyaḥ  yaḥ ca saṃdihyamānaḥ teṣu katamaḥ  mama āatmā sarva antaraḥ tvayā vivakṣita iti ukta itara āha yaḥ prāṇena mukha nāsikā saṃcāriṇā prāṇiti prāṇa ceṣṭām karoti yena prāṇaḥ praṇīyata iti arthaḥ sa te taba kārya karaṇa saṃghātasyā atmā vijñāna mayaḥ samānam anyat  yaḥ  apānena apāni iti yaḥ  vyānena vyāni iti iti cchānda sam dairdhyam sarvāḥ kārya karaṇa saṃghāta gatāḥ prāṇana ādi ceṣṭā dāru yantrasya iva yena kriyante na hi cetanā vadana dhiṣṭhatasya dāru yantrasya iva prāṇana ādi ceṣṭā vidyante tasmāt vijñāna mayena adhiṣṭhitam vilakṣaṇena dāru yantravat prāṇana ādi ceṣṭām pratipadyate tasmāt saḥ asti kārya karaṇa saṃghāta vilakṣaṇaḥ  yaḥ ciṣṭayati sa ha uvāca uṣastaḥ ca ākrāyaṇaḥ  yathā kaścid anyathā pratijñāya pūrvam punar vipratipannaḥ  brūyāt anyathā asau gaurasau  aśvaḥ  yaḥ calati dhāvati iti vā pūrvam pratyakṣam darśayām iti pratijñāya paścāt calana ādi liṅgaiḥ vyapadiśati evam eva etad brahma prāṇana ādi liṅgaiḥ vyapadiṣṭam bhavati tvayā kim bahunā tyaktvā gaḥ tṛṣṇā nimittam vyājam yad eva sākṣāt aparokṣāt brahma ya ātmā sarva antaraḥ tam me vyācakṣva iti itara āha yathā mayā prathamam pratijñātaḥ tavā atmava lakṣaṇa iti tām pratijñām anuvarta eva tad tathā eva yathā ukta mayā yad punaruktam tam ātmānam ghaṭa ādivat viṣayīkuru iti tad aśakya tvāt na kriyate kasmāt punar tad aśakyam iti āha vastu svābhāvyāt  kim punar tad vastu svābhāvyam dṛṣṭayā ādi draṣṭṛ tvam dṛṣṭeḥ draṣṭā hi ātmā dṛṣṭiḥ iti dvividhā bhavati laukikī pāramārthikī ca iti tatra laukikī cakṣuḥ saṃyukta antaḥkaraṇa vṛttiḥ sā kriyata iti jāyate vinaśyati ca yā tu ātmanaḥ  dṛṣṭiḥ agni uṣṇa prakāśa ādi vatsā ca draṣṭaḥ svarūpa tvāt na jāyate na vinaśyati ca sā kriyamāṇayā upādhi bhūtayā saṃsṛṣṭā iva iti vyapadiśyate draṣṭā iti bhedavat ca draṣṭā dṛṣṭiḥ iti ca yā asau laukikī dṛṣṭiḥ cakṣuḥ dvārā rūpa uparaktā jāyamānā eva nityayā atma dṛṣṭyā saṃsṛṣṭā iva tad praticchāyā tayā vyāptā eva jāyate tathā vinaśyati ca tena upacaryate draṣṭā sadā paśyan  api paśyati na paśyati ca iti na tu punar draṣṭuḥ dṛṣṭeḥ kadācid api anyathātvam tathā ca vakṣyati ṣaṣṭhe dhyāyati iva lelāyati iva na hi draṣṭuḥ dṛṣṭeḥ viparilopaḥ  vidyata iti ca tam imam artham āha laukikyā dṛṣṭeḥ karma bhūtāyā draṣṭāram svakīyayā nityayā dṛṣṭyā vyāptāram na paśyeḥ yā asau laukikī dṛṣṭiḥ karma bhūtāḥ  sā rūpa uparaktā rūpa abhivyañjikā nā atmānam sva ātmanaḥ  vyāptāram pratyañcam vyāpnoti tasmāt tam pratyak ātmānam dṛṣṭet raṣṭāram na paśyeḥ tathā śruteḥ śrotāram na śṛṇuyāḥ tathā mateḥ manaḥ vṛtteḥ kevalāyāḥ  vyāptāram na manvīthāḥ tathā vijñāteḥ kevalāyāḥ  buddhi vṛtteḥ vyāpta āram na vijānīyāḥ eṣa vastunaḥ svabhāvaḥ  atas  na eva darśayitum śakyate gavā ādivat  na dṛṣṭeḥ draṣṭāram iti atra akṣarāṇi anyathā vyācakṣate kecid  na dṛṣṭeḥ draṣṭāram dṛṣṭeḥ kartāram dṛṣṭi bhedam akṛtvā dṛṣṭi mātrasya kartāram na paśyeḥ iti dṛṣṭeḥ iti karmaṇi ṣaṣṭhī sā dṛṣṭiḥ kriyamāṇā ghaṭavat karma bhavati draṣṭāram iti tṛjantena draṣṭuḥ dṛṣṭi kartṛ tvam ācaṣṭe tena asau dṛṣṭeḥ draṣṭā dṛṣṭeḥ kartā iti vyākhyātṛṇām abhiprāyaḥ tatra dṛṣṭeḥ iti ṣaṣṭhī antena dṛṣṭi grahaṇam nirarthakam iti doṣam na paśyanti paśyatām vā punaruktam asāraḥ pramāda pāṭha iti vā nā adaraḥ katham punar ādhikyam tṛjantena eva dṛṣṭi kartṛ tvasya siddha tvāt dṛṣṭeḥ iti nirarthakam tadā draṣṭāram na paśyeḥ iti etāvat eva vaktavyam yasmāt dhātoḥ paraḥ tṛt śūyate tad dhātu artha kartari hi tṛcsmaryate gantāram bhattāram vā nayati iti etāvān eva hi śabdaḥ prayujyate na tu gateḥ gantāram bhideḥ bhettāram iti asatyartha viśeṣe prayoktavyaḥ na ca artha vāda tvena hātavyam satyām gatau na ca pramāda pāṭhaḥ sarveṣām avigānāt tasmāt vyākhyātṛṇām eva buddhi daurbalyam na adhyetṛ pramādaḥ yathā tu asmābhiḥ vyākhyātam laukika dṛṣṭeḥ vivicya nitya dṛṣṭi viśiṣṭa ātmā pradarśayitavyaḥ tathā kartṛ karma viśeṣaṇa tvena dṛṣṭi śabdasya dvis prayoga upapadyata ātma svarūpa nirdhāraṇāya anahi draṣṭuḥ dṛṣṭeḥ i ati ca pradeśa antara vākyena eva eka vākyatā upapannā bhavati tathā ca cakṣūṃṣi paśyati śrotram idam śrutam iti śruti antareṇa eka vākyatā upapannā nyāyāt ca evam eva hi ātmanaḥ  nitya tvam upapadyate vikriyā abhāve vikriyāvat ca nityam iti ca vipratiṣiddham dhyāyati iva lelāyati iva na hi draṣṭuḥ dṛṣṭeḥ viparilopaḥ  vidyate eṣa nityaḥ  mahimā brāhmaṇasya iti ca śruti akṣarāṇi anyathā na gacchanti nanu draṣṭā śrotā mantā vijñāta iti evamādīni api akṣarāṇi ātmanaḥ  avikriya tve na gacchanti iti na yathā prāpta laukika vākya anuvādi tvāt teṣām nā atma tattva nirdhāraṇa arthāni tāni dṛṣṭeḥ draṣṭāram iti evamādīnām anya artha asambhavāt i athā ukta artha paratvam avagamyate tasmāt anavabodhāt eva hi viśeṣaṇam parityaktam dṛṣṭeḥ draṣṭāram iti evamādīnām anya artha asambhavāt i athā ukta artha paratvam avagamyate tasmāt anavabodhāt eva hi viśeṣaṇam parityaktam dṛṣṭeḥ iti eṣa te tavā atmā sarvaiḥ uktaiḥ viśeṇaṇaiḥ viśiṣṭaḥ ata etasmāt ātmanaḥ  anyat ārta kārya vā śarīram karaṇa ātmakam vā liṅgam etad eva ekam anārtamavināśi kūṭastham tatas  ha uṣastaḥ ca ākrāyaṇa upararāma vandhanam sa prayojakam uktam yaḥ ca baddhaḥ tasya api astitvam adhigatam vyatirikta tvam ca tasya idānīm bandha mokṣa sādhanam sa saṃnyāsam ātma jñānam vaktavyam iti kahola praśna ārabhyate atha ha enam kaholaḥ  nāmataḥ kuṣītakasya apatyam kauṣītakeyaḥ papraccha yājñavalkya iti ha uvāca iti pūrvavat  yad eva sākṣāt aparokṣāt brahma ya ātmā sarva antaraḥ tam me vyācakṣva iti yam viditvā bandhanāt pramucyate yājñavalkya āha eṣa te tavā atmā kim uṣastaka holābhyām eka ātmā pṛṣṭaḥ kiṃvā bhinnau  ātmānau tulya lakṣaṇau  iti bhinnau  iti yuktam praśnayoḥ apunaruktatva upapatteḥ yadi hi eka ātma uṣasta kahola praśnayoḥ vivakṣitaḥ tatra ekena eva praśnena adhigata tvāt tad viṣayaḥ  dvi toyaḥ praśnaḥ  anarthakaḥ syāt  na ca artha vāda rūpa tvam vākyasya tasmāt bhinnau  etau  ātmānau kṣetrajña parama ātma ākhyau  iti kecid vyācakṣate tad na ta iti pratijñānāt  eṣa ta ātmā iti hi prativacane pratijñātam na ca ekasya kārya karaṇa saṃghātasya dvau  ātmānau  upapadyete ekaḥ  hi kārya karaṇa saṃghāta ekenā atmanā atmavān na coṣaḥ tasya anyaḥ kaholasya anyaḥ  jātitaḥ  bhinna ātmā bhavati dvayoḥ agauṇatva ātmatva sarva antaratva anupapatteḥ yadi ekam agauṇam brahma dvayoḥ itareṇa vaśyam gauṇena bhavitavyam tathā atma tvam sarva antara tvam ca viruddha tvāt padārthānām yadi ekam sarva antaram brahmā atmā mukhya  itareṇa asarva antareṇa anātmanā mukhyena avaśyam bhavitavyam tasmāt ekasya eva dvis śravaṇam viśeṣa vivakṣayā yad tu pūrva uktena samānam dvitīye praśna antara uktam tāvat mātram pūrvasya eva anuvādaḥ tasya eva anuktaḥ kaścid viśeṣaḥ  vaktavya iti kaḥ punar asau viśeṣa iti ucyate pūrvasmin praśne asti vyatirikta ātmā yasya ayam sa prayojakaḥ  bandha ukta iti dvitīye tu tasya evā atmanaḥ  aśanāya ādi saṃsāra dharma atīta tvam viśeṣa ucyate yad viśeṣa parijñānāt saṃnyāsa sahitāt pūrva uktāt vandhanāt vimucyate tasmat praśna prativacanayoḥ eṣa ta ātmā iti evam antayoḥ tulya artha tā eva nanu katham ekasya evā atmanaḥ  aśanāya ādi atīta tvam tad vatvam ca iti viruddha dharma samavāyi tvam iti na parihṛta tvāt  nāma rūpa vikara kārya karaṇa lakṣaṇa saṃghāta upādhi bheda saṃparka janita bhrānti mātram hi saṃsāri tvam iti asakṛt avocāma viruddha śrati vyākhyāna prasaṅgena ca yathā rajju śuktikā gagana ādayaḥ sarpa rajata malinā bhavanti parādhi āropita dharma viśiṣṭāḥ svatas  kevalā eva rajju śuktikā gagana ādayaḥ na ca evam viruddha dharma samavāyi tve padārthānām kaścana virodhaḥ nāma rūpa upādhyastitve ekam eva advitīyam na iha nānā asti kiñcana iti śrutayaḥ virudhyeran  iti ced  na salila phena dṛṣṭāntena parihṛta tvāt mṛdā ādi haṣṭa antaiḥ ca yadā tu parama artha dṛṣṭyā parama ātma tattvāt śrati anusāribhiḥ anya tvena nirupyamāṇe nāma rūpe mṛd ādi vikāravat vastu antare tattvataḥ  na staḥ salila phena ghaṭa ādi vikāravat eva tadā tad apekṣya aekam eva advitīyaṃ aneha nānā asti kiñcane tyadiparama artha darśana gocara tvam pratipadyate yadā tu svābhāvikyā avidyayā brahma svarūpam rajju śuktikā gagana svarūpavat eva svena rūpeṇa vartamānam kenacid aspṛṣṭa svabhāvam api sat nāma rūpa kṛta kārya karaṇa upādhibhyaḥ  vivekena na avadhāyate nāma rūpa upādhi dṛṣṭiḥ eva ca bhavati svābhāvikī tadā sarvaḥ  ayam vastu antara astitva vyavahāraḥ asti ca ayam bheda kṛtaḥ  mithyā vyavahāraḥ  yeṣām brahma tattvāt anya tvena vastu vidyate yeṣām ca na asti parama artha vādibhiḥ tu śruti anusāreṇa nirūpyamāṇe vastuni kim tattvataḥ  asti vastu kiṃvā na asti iti brahma ekam eva advitīyam sarva saṃvyahāra śūnyam iti nirdhāryate tena na kaścid virodhaḥ na hi parama artha avadhāraṇa niṣṭhāyām vastu antara astitvam pratipadyāmahe ekam eva advitīyam anantaram abāhyam iti śruteḥ na ca nāma rūpa vyavahāra kāle tu avivekinām kriyā kāraka phala ādi saṃvyavahāraḥ  na asti iti pratiṣidhyate tasmāt jñāna ajñāne apekṣya sarvaḥ saṃvyavahāraḥ jñāstrīyaḥ laukikaḥ ca atas  na kācana virodha śaṅkā sarva vādinām api aparihāryaḥ parama artha savyavahāra kṛtaḥ  vyavahāraḥ tatra parama artha ātma svarūpam apekṣya praśnaḥ punar  katamaḥ  yājñavalkya sarva antara iti pratyāha itaraḥ  yaḥ  aśanāyā pipāsaḥ  aśitum icchā aśanāyā pātum icchā pipāsā te aśanāyā pipāse yaḥ  atyeti iti vakṣyamāṇena sambandhaḥ avivekibhiḥ tala malavat iva gaganam gamyamānam eva tala male atyeti paramārthataḥ tābhyām asaṃsṛṣṭa svabhāva tvāt tathā mūḍhaiḥ aśanāya apipāsā ādimat brahma gamyamānam api kṣudhitaḥ  aham pipāsitaḥ  aham iti te atyeti eva paramārthataḥ tābhyām asaṃsṛṣṭa svabhāva tvāt na lipyate loka duḥkhena bāhyaḥ iti śruteḥ avidvat loka adhyāropita duḥkhena iti arthaḥ prāṇa eka dharma tvāt samāsa karaṇam aśanāyā pipāsayoḥ śokam moham śoka iti kāmaḥ iṣṭam vastu uddiśya cintayataḥ  yad aramaṇam tad tṛṣṇā abhibhūtasya kāmabījam tena hi kāmaḥ  dīpyate mohaḥ tu vaparīta pratyaya prabhavaḥ  avivekaḥ  bhramaḥ sa ca avidyā sarvasya anarthasya prasava bījam bhinna kārya tvāt tayoḥ śoka mohayoḥ asamāsa karaṇam tau manodhikaraṇau tathā śarīra adhikaraṇau jarām mṛtyum ca atyeti jarā iti kārya karaṇa saṃghāta vipariṇāmaḥ  valī palita ādi liṅgaḥ mṛtyuḥ iti tad vicchedaḥ  vipariṇāma avasānaḥ tau jarā mṛtyū śarīra adhikaraṇāvatyā iti ye te aśanāya ādayaḥ prāṇa manaḥ śarīra adhikaraṇāḥ prāṇiṣu anavaratam vartamānā ahorātra ādivat samudra ūrmivat ca prāṇiṣu saṃsāra iti ucyate yaḥ  asau dṛṣṭeḥ draṣṭa ityādi lakṣaṇaḥ sākṣāt avyavahitaḥ  aparokṣāt agauṇaḥ sarva antara ātmā brahma ādi stamba paryantānām bhūtānām aśanāya api pāsā ādibhiḥ saṃsāra dharmaiḥ sadā na spṛśyata ākāśa iva ghana ādi malaiḥ tam etam vā ātmānam svam tattvam viditvā jñātvā ayam aham asmi param brahma sadā sarva saṃsāra vinirmuktam nitya tṛptam iti brāhmaṇāḥ brāhmaṇānām eva adhikāraḥ  vyutthāne atas  brāhmaṇa grahaṇam vyutthāya vaiparītyena utthānam kṛtvā kuta iti āha putra eṣaṇāyāḥ putra artha eṣaṇā putra eṣaṇā putreṇa imam lokam jayeyam iti loka jaya sādhanam putram pratīccha eṣaṇā dāra saṃgrahaḥ dāra saṃgraham akṛtvā iti arthaḥ vitta eṣaṇāyāḥ ca karma sādhanasya gavā ādeḥ upādānam anena karma kṛtvā pitṛ lokam jeṣyāmi iti vidyā saṃyuktena vā deva lokam kevalayā vā hiraṇyagarbha vidyayā daivena vittena deva lokam daivāt vittāt vyutthānam eva na asti iti kecid  yasmāt tad valena hi kila vyutthānam iti tad asat  etāvān vai kāma iti paṭhita tvāt eṣaṇā madhye daivasya vittasya hiraṇyagarbha ādi devātā viṣayā eva vidyā cittam iti ucyate deva loka hetu tvāt  na hi nirupādhika prajñāna ghana viṣayā brahma vidyā deva loka prāpti hetuḥ tasmāt tad sarvam abhavat ātmā hi eṣām sa bhavati iti śruteḥ tad balena hi vyutthānam etam vai tam ātmānam viditvā iti viśeṣa vacanāt  tasmāt tribhyaḥ  api atebhyaḥ  anātma loka prāpti sādhanebhya eṣaṇā viṣayebhyaḥ  vyutthāya eṣaṇā kāmaḥ etāvān vai kāmaḥ iti śruteḥ etasmiḥ trividhe anātma loka prāpti sādhane tṛṣṇām akṛtvā iti arthaḥ sarvā hi sādhana icchā phala icśā eva atas  vyācaṣṭe śrutiḥ ekā eva eṣaṇa iti katham yā hi eva putra eṣaṇā sā vitta eṣaṇā dṛṣṭa phala sādhanatva tulya tvāt yā vitta eṣaṇā sā loka eṣaṇā phala arthā eva sā sarvaḥ phala artha prayukta eva hi sarvam sādhanam upādatte ata ekaiva eṣaṇā yā loka eṣaṇā sā sādhanam antareṇa sampādayitum na śakyata iti sādhya sādhana bhedena ubhe hi yasmāt ete eṣaṇe eva bhavataḥ tasmāt brahma vidaḥ  na asti karma karma sādhanam vā atas  ye atikrāntā brāhmaṇāḥ sarva karma karma sādhanam ca sarva deva pitṛ mānuṣa nimittam yajñopavīta ādi tena hi daivam pitryam mānuṣam ca karma kriyate nivītam manuṣyāṇām ityādi śruteḥ tasmāt pūrva brāhmaṇā brahma vidaḥ  vyutthāya karmabhyaḥ karma sādhanebhyaḥ ca yajñopavīta ādibhyaḥ paramahaṃsa pārivrājyam pratipadya bhikṣā carya caranti bhikṣā artha caraṇam bhikṣā carya caranti tyaktvā smārta liṅgam kevalam āśrama mātra śaraṇānām jīvana sādhanam parivrājya vyañjakam viddhān  liṅga varjitaḥ tasmāt aliṅgaḥ  dharma jñaḥ  avyakta liṅgaḥ  avyakta ācāraḥ ityādi smṛtibhyaḥ atha parivra ḍavi varṇa vāsāḥ  muṇḍaḥ  aparigrahaḥ ityādi śruteḥ sa śikhān keśān nikṛtya visṛjya yajñopavītam i ti ca nanu vyutthāya atha bhikṣā carya caranti iti vartamāna apadeśāt artha vādaḥ  ayam na vidhāyakaḥ pratyayaḥ kaścid śrūyate liṅloṭtavyānām anyatamaḥ  api tasmāt arthavāda mātreṇa śruti smṛti vihitānām yajñopavīta ādonām sādhanānām na śakyate parityāgaḥ kārayitum yajñopavīti eva adhayīta yājayet yajeta vā pārivrājye tāvat adhyayanam vihitam veda saṃnyasanāt śūdraḥ tasmāt vedam na saṃnyaset  iti svādhyāya eva utsṛjamānaḥ  vācam iti cā apastambaḥ brahma ujjhaṃ veda nindā ca kauṭa sākṣyam suhṛd vadhaḥ garhitān na adyayoḥ jagdhiḥ surā pāna samni ṣaḍ  iti veda parityāge doṣa śravaṇāt  upāsane gurūṇām vṛddhānām atithīnām home japya karmaṇi bhojana ācamane svādhyāye ca yajña upavītī sya ādi ti parivrājaka dharmeṣu ca guru upāsana svādhyāya bhojana ācamāna ādīnām karmaṇām śruti smṛtiṣu kartavya tayā codita tvāt guru ādi upāsana aṅga tvena yajñopavītasya vihita tvāt tad parityāgaḥ  na eva avagantum śakyate yadi api eṣaṇābhyaḥ  vyutthānam vidhīyata eva tathā api putra ādi eṣaṇābhyaḥ tisṛbhya eva vyutthānam na tu sarvasmāt karmaṇaḥ karma sādhanāt ca vyutthānam sarva parityāge ca aśrutam kṛtam syāt śutam ca yajñopavīta ādi hāpitam syāt  tathā ca mahān aparādhaḥ  vihita akaraṇa pratiṣiddha ācaraṇa nimittaḥ kṛtaḥ syāt  tasmāt yajñopavīta ādi liṅga parityāgaḥ  andha paramparā eva na yajñopavītam vedān  ca sarva tad varjayet yatiḥ iti śruteḥ api cā atma jñāna paratva ātmarvasyā upaniṣadaḥ ātmā draṣṭavyaḥ śrotavyaḥ  mantavya iti hi prastutam sa cā atmā eva sākṣāt aparokṣāt sarva antaraḥ  aśanāya ādi saṃsāra dharma varjita iti evam vijñeya iti tāvat prasiddham sarvā hi iyam upaniṣad evaṃpara iti vidhi antara śeṣatva tāvat na asti atas  na artha vādaḥ ātma jñānasya kartavya tvāt  ātmā ca aśanāya ādi dharmavān na bhavati iti sādhana phala vilakṣaṇaḥ  jñātavyaḥ ate avyatirekeṇā atmanaḥ  jñānam avidyā anyaḥ  asau  anyaḥ  aham asmi iti na sa veda mṛtyoḥ sa mṛtyum āpnoti ya iha na anā iva paśyati ekadhā eva anudraṣṭavyam ekam eva advitīyam tad tvam asi ityādi śrutibhyaḥ kriyā phalam sādhanam ca aśanāya ādi saṃsāra dharma atītāt ātmanaḥ  anyat avidyā viṣayam yatra hi dvaitam iva bhavati anyaḥ  asau  anyaḥ  aham asmi iti na sa veda atha ye anyathā atas  viduḥ ityādi vākya śatebhyaḥ na ca vidyā avidye ekasya puruṣasya yaha bhavataḥ  virodhāt tamaḥ prakāśau  iva tasmāt ātma vidaḥ  avidyā viṣayaḥ  adhikāraḥ  na draṣṭavyaḥ kriyā kāraka phala bheda rūpaḥ mṛtyoḥ sa mṛtyum āpnoti ityādi nindita tvāt  sarva kriyā sādhana phalānām ca avidyā viṣayāṇām tad viparīta ātma vidyayā hātavya tvena iṣṭa tvāt yajñopavīta ādi sādhanānām ca tad viṣaya tvāt tasmāt asādhana phala svabhāvāt ātmanaḥ  anya viṣayā vilakṣaṇa eṣaṇā ubhe hi ete sādhana phale eṣaṇe eva bhavataḥ yajñopavīta ādeḥ tad sādhya karmaṇām ca sādhana tvāt  ubhe hi ete eṣaṇe eva iti hetu vacanena avadhāraṇāt yajñopavīta ādi sādhanāt tad sādhyebhyaḥ ca karmabhyaḥ  avidyā viṣaya tvāt eṣaṇā rūpa tvāt ca jihāsitavya rūpa tvāt ca vyutthānam vidhitsitam eva nanu upaniṣada ātma jñāna paratvāt  vyutthāna śrutiḥ tad stuti arthā na vidhiḥ na  vidhitsita vijñānena samāna kartṛkatva śravaṇāt na hi akartavyena kartavyasya samāna kartṛka tvena vede kadācid api śravaṇam sambhavati kartavyānām eva hi abhipava baha uma bhakṣāṇām yathā śravaṇam abhiputya hutvā bhakṣayanti iti tadvat ātma jñāna eṣaṇā vyutthāna bhikṣā caryāṇām kartavyānām eva samāna kartṛkatva śravaṇam bhavet  avidyā viṣaya tvāt eṣaṇā tvāt ca artha prāpta ātma jñāna vidheḥ eva yajñopavīta ādi parityāgaḥ na tu vidhātavya iti cet sutarām ātma jñāna vidhinā eva vihitasya samāna kartṛkatva śravaṇena dārḍhyepapattiḥ tathā bhikṣā caryasya ca yad  punaruktam vartamāna apadeśāt arthavāda mātram iti na audumbara yūpa ādi vidhi samāna tvāt adoṣaḥ avyutthāya bhikṣā caryam caranti aityanena pārivrājyam vidhīyate pārivrājya āśrame ca yajñopavīta ādi sādhanāni vihitāni liṅgam ca śrutibhiḥ smṛtiḥ ca atas tad  varjayitvā anyasmāt  vyutthānam eṣaṇātve api iti ced  na vijñāna samāna kartṛkāt  pārivrājyāt eṣaṇā vyutthāna lakṣaṇāt  pārivrājya antara upapatteḥ yad dhi tad eṣaṇā abhyaḥ  vyutthāna lakṣaṇam pārivrājyam tad ātma jñāna aṅgam ātma jñāna virodhi eṣaṇā parityāga rūpa tvāt avidyā viṣaya tvāt ca eṣaṇāyāḥ tad vyatirekeṇa ca asti āśrama rūpam pārivrājyam brahma loka ādi phala prāpti sādhanam yad viṣayam yajñopavīta ādi sādhana vidhānam siṅga vidhānam ca na ca eṣaṇā rūpa sādhana āpādānasya āśrama dharma mātreṇa pārivrājya antare viṣaye sambhavati sati sarva upaniṣad vihitasya ātma jñānasya bādhanam yuktam yajñopavīta ādi vidyā viṣaya eṣaṇā rūpa sādhana upāditsāyām ca avaśyam asādhana phala rūpasya aśanāya ādi saṃsāra dharma varjitasya aham brahmā asmi ithi vijñānam bādhyate na ca tad rādhanam yuktam sarva upaniṣadām tad artha paratvāt abhikṣā caryam caranti aityeṣaṇām grāhayantī śrutiḥ svayam eva bādhata iti ced  atha api syāt eṣaṇābhyaḥ  vyutthānam vidhāya punar eṣaṇaka deśam bhikṣā carya grāhayantī tad sambaddham anyat api grāhayati iti ced  na bhikṣā caryasya aprayojaka tvāt  hutvā uttara kāla bhakṣaṇāt  śeṣa pratipatti karma tvāt aprayojakam hi tad  asaṃskāram api syāt  na tu bhikṣā caryam niyama adṛṣṭasya api brahma vidaḥ  aniṣṭa tvāt  niyama adṛṣṭasya aniṣṭa tve kim bhikṣā ācaryeṇa iti ced   na anya sādhanāt  vyutthānasya vihita tvāt  tathā api kim tena iti ced  yadi syāt  bādham abhyupagamyate hi tad  yāni pārivrājye abhihitāni vacanāni ayajña upavīti eva adhīyīta aitya ādīni tāni avidvat pārivrājya mātra viṣayāṇi iti parihṛta ani ita rathā ātma jñāna bādhaḥ syāt iti hi uktam nirāśiṣam anārambham nirnamaḥ tāram astutim akṣīṇam kṣīṇa karmāṇam tam devāḥ  brāhmaṇe viduḥ iti sarva karma abhāvam darśayati smṛtiḥ viduṣaḥ vidvānliṅgaḥ  dharma jñaḥ iti ca tasmāt  parama haṃsa pārivrājyam eva vyutthāna lakṣaṇam pratipadyeta ātma vid  sarva karma sādhana parityāga rūpam iti yasmāt  pūrve brāhmaṇā etam ātmānam asādhana phala svabhāvam viditvā sarvasmāt  sādhana phala svarūpa ādeṣaṇā lakṣaṇāt  vyutthāya bhikṣā caryam caranti sma dṛṣṭa adṛṣṭa artham karma tad sādhanam ca hitvā tasmāt  adyatve api brāhmaṇaḥ  brahma vid  pāṇḍityam paṇḍita bhāvam etad ātma vijñānam pāṇḍityam nirvidya niḥśeṣam viditvā ātma vijñānam niravaśeṣam kṛtvā iti arthaḥ ācāryata āgamataḥ ca eṣaṇābhyaḥ  vyutthāya eṣaṇa avyutthāna avasānam eva hi tad  pāṇḍityam eṣaṇa atiraskāra udbhava tvāt eṣaṇā virudvatva at eṣaṇā matiraskṛtya na hi ātma jñānena eva vihita m eṣaṇā vyutthānam ātma jñāna samāna kartṛkatva apratyaya upādāna liṅga śruti ād daḍhīkṛtam tasmāt epaṇābhyaḥ  vyutthāya jñāna bana bhāvena bālyena tiṣṭhāset  sthātum icchet  sādhana phala āśrayaṇam hi balam itareṣām anātma vidām tad  balam hitvā vidvān asādhana phala svarūpa ātma vijñānam eva balam tad bhāvam eva kevalam āśrayet  tad āśrayaṇe hi karaṇāni eṣaṇa avipaye enam hratvā sthāpayitum nīt sahante  jñāna bala hīnam hi mūḍhaṃd daṣṭa adṛṣṭa viṣayāyām eṣaṇāyām eva enam karaṇāni niyojayanti  balam nāma ātma vidyayā aśeṣa viṣaya dṛṣṭi tiraskaraṇam  atas tad bhāvena bālyena tiṣṭhāset  tathā ātmanā bindate vīryam iti śruti antarāt na ayam ātmā bala hīnena labhyaḥ iti ca bālyam ca pāṇḍityam ca nirvidya niḥśeṣam kṛtvā atha mananāt muniḥ yogī bhavati  etāvat vi brāhmaṇena kartavyam yad uta sarvān ātma pratyaya tiraskaraṇam  etad  kṛtvā kṛtakṛtyaḥ  yogī bhavati amaunam ca ātma jñāna an ātma pratyaya tiraskārau pāṇḍitya bālya saṃjñakau niḥśeṣam kṛtvā maunam nāma anātma pratyaya tiraskaraṇasya parthavasānam phalam tad ca nirvidya atha brāhmaṇaḥ kutakṛtyaḥ  bhavati brahmā eva sarvam iti pratyaya upajāyate sa brāhmaṇaḥ kutakṛtyaḥ atas  brāhmaṇaḥ nirūpa caritam hi tadā tasya brāhmaṇyam prāptam kena syāt  kena caraṇena bhavet  yena syāt  yena caraṇena bhavet  tena īdṛśa eva ayam yena kenacid caraṇena syāt  tena īdṛśa eva ukta lakṣaṇa eva brāhmaṇaḥ  bhavati yena kenacid caraṇena iti stuti artham yā iyam brāhmaṇyā avasthā sā iyam stūyate na tu caraṇe anādaraḥ ata etasmāt  brāhmaṇya avasthānāt aśanāya ādi atīta ātma svarūpa āt  nitya tṛptāt  anyat  avidyā vipayam eṣaṇā lakṣaṇam vastu antaram ārta vināśi ārti parigṛhītam svapna māyā marīci udaka samam asāram ātmā evākaḥ kevalaḥ  nitya mukta iti tatas  ha kaholaḥ kaupātakeyaḥ upararāma yad  sākṣāt aparokṣāt  brahma sarvantara ātmā iti uktam tasya sarva antarasya svarūpa adhigamāya ā śākalya brāhmaṇāt  grantha ārabhyate pṛthivī ādīni hi ākāśa antāni bhūtāni antarvahiḥ bhāvena vyavasthitāni teṣām yad  bāhyam bādyam avigamya adhigamya nirākurvan draṣṭuḥ sākṣāt  sarva antaraḥ  agauṇa ātmā sarva saṃsāra dharma vinirmuktaḥ  darśayitavya iti ārambhaḥ atha ha enam gārgī nāmataḥ vācaknavī ivacakroḥ duhitā papraccha yājñavalkya iti ha uvāca yad idam sarvam pārthivam dhātu jātam apsūdake otam ca protam ca otam dīrghapaṭa tantuvat protam tiryak tantuvat  viparītam vā adbhiḥ sarvatas  antar bahis bhūtābhiḥ vyāptam iti arthaḥ anyathā saktu muṣṭivat  viśīryeta idam tāvat anumānam upanyastam yad  kāryam paricchinnam sthūlam kāraṇena aparicchinnena sūkṣmeṇa vyāptam itid daṣṭam yathā pṛthivī adbhiḥ tathā apūrvam pūrvam uttareṇa uttareṇa vyāpinā bhavitavyam iti eṣa ā sarva antarāt ātmanaḥ praśna arthaḥ tatra bhūtāni pañca saṃhatāni eva uttaram uttaram sūkṣam abhāvena vyāpakena kāraṇa rūpeṇa ca vyavatiṣṭhante na ca paramātmanor avāk  tad vayatirekeṇa vastu antaram asti satyasya satyam iti śruteḥ satyam ca bhūta pañcakam satyasya satyam ca para ātmā kasmin nu khalvāpa otāḥ ca protāḥ ca iti tāsām api kāryatvāt  sthūla tvāt  paricchinna tvāt ca kacid vi ota prota bhāvena bhavitavyam  kva tāsā metayota bhāva iti evam utara uttara prakṣaṇa saṅgaḥ yojayitavyaḥ vāyau gārgi iti nanu agnau  iti vaktavyam  naipa doṣaḥ agneḥ pārthivam vā āpyam vā dhātum anāśritya itara bhūtavat  svātantryeṇa ātma lābhaḥ  na asti iti tasminnota prota bhāvaḥ  na upadiśyate kasmin nu khalu vāyurotaḥ ca protaḥ ca iti antarikṣa lokeṣu gārgi iti tāni eva bhūtāni saṃhatāni antarikṣa lokāḥ tāni api gandharva lokeṣu gandharva lokā āditya lokeṣu āditya lokāḥ candra lokeṣu candra lokā nakṣatra lokeṣu nakṣatra lokā deva lokeṣu deva lokā indra lokeṣu indra lokā virāj śarīra āraṃmakeṣu bhūteṣu prajāpati lokeṣu prajāpati lokā brahma lokeṣu brahma lokā nāma aṇḍa āraṃmakāṇi bhūta ani sarvatra hi sūkṣma tāratamya krameṇa prāpyu bhoga āśraya ākāra pariṇatāni bhūtāni saṃhatāni tāni eva pañca iti bahuvacana māñji kasmin nu khalu brahma lokā otāḥ ca protāḥ ca iti sa ha uvāca yājñavalkyaḥ  he gārgī mā atiprākṣīḥ svam praśnam nyāya prakāram atītya āgamena praṣṭabyām devatām anumānena mā prākṣīḥ iti arthaḥ pṛcchantyāḥ ca mā te tava mūrdhā śiraḥ  vyapatat  vispaṣṭam patet devatāyāḥ sva praśna āgama viṣayaḥ tam praśna viṣayam atikrāntaḥ  gārgyāḥ praśnaḥ ānumānika tvāt sa yasyāḥ  devatāyāḥ praśnaḥ sā ati praśnyā na ati praśnyā anati praśnyā sva praśraviṣayā eva kevala āgama gamyā iti arthaḥ tām anati praśnyām vai devatām atipṛcchasi atas  gārgi mā atiprākṣīḥ martum ced na icchasi tatas  ha gārgī vācaknavī upararāma iti tṛtīyā adhyāye ṣaṣṭham gārgī brāhmaṇam idānīm brahma lokānām antaratamam sūtram va ktavyam iti tad artha ārambhaḥ tad ca āgamena eva praṣṭavyam iti itihāsena āgama upanyāsaḥ kriyate atha ha enam uddālakaḥ  nāmataḥ aruṇasya apatyam āruṇiḥ papraccha yājñavalkya iti ha uvāca madreṣu deśeṣu avasāma uṣitavantaḥ patañcalasya patañcalaḥ  nāmataḥ tasya eva kapi gotrasya kāpyasya gṛheṣu yajñam adhīyānā yaśaśāstra adhyayanam kurvāṇāḥ tasya āsīt  bhāryā gandharva gṛhīta ā tam apṛcchāma kaḥ  asi iti saḥ  abravīt  kabandhaḥ nāmataḥ atharvaṇaḥ  apatyam ātharvaṇa iti saḥ  abravīt  gāndharvaḥ patan calam kāpyam yājñikān  ca tad śipyān vettha nu tvam he kāpya jānīṣe tad  sūtram kim tad  yena sūtreṇa ayam ca leka idam ca janma paraḥ ca lokaḥ param ca pratipattavyam janma sarvāṇi ca bhūtāni brahma ādi stamba paryantāni sandṛbdhāni saṅgrathitāni sraj iva sūtreṇa viṣṭabdhāni bhavanti yena tad  kim sūtram vettha saḥ  abravīt evam pṛṣṭaḥ kāpyaḥ na aham tad  bhagavan veda iti tad  sūtram na aham jāne he bhagavan  iti sampūjayan  āha saḥ  abravīt  punar gandharva upādhyāyam asmān  ca vettha na tvam kāpya tam antaryāmiṇam antaryāmi iti viśeṣyate ya imam ca lokam param ca lokam sarvāṇi ca bhūtāni yaḥ  antara abhyantaraḥ san yamayati niyamayati dāruyantram iva brāmayati svam sva mucita vyāpāram kārayati iti saḥ  abravīt evam uktaḥ patañcalaḥ kāpyaḥ na aham tam jāne bhagavan  iti sampūjayan  āha saḥ  abravīt  punar gandharvaḥ sūtra tad antargata antaryāmiṇoḥ vijñānam stūyate yaḥ kaścid  vai tad  sūtram he kāpya bavidyāt  vijānīyāt  tam ca antaryāmiṇam sūtra antargatam tasya eva sūtrasya niyantāram vidyāt  yaḥ iti evam uktena prakāreṇa sa hi brahma vita paramātma vid  sa lokān  ca bhūḥ ādīn antaryāmiṇā niyamyamānān  lokān vetti sa devān  ca agni ādīn  lokinaḥ  jānāti vedān  ca sarva pramāṇa bhūtān vetti bhūtāni ca brahma ādīni sūtreṇa dhiyamāṇāni tad antargatena antaryāmiṇā niyamyamānāni vetti sa ātmānam ca kartṛtva bhoktṛtva viśiṣṭam tena eva antaryāmiṇā niyamyamānam vetti sarvam ca jagata tathābhūtam vetti iti evam stute sūtrāntaryāmi vijñāne pralubdhaḥ kāpyaḥ  abhimukhībhūtaḥ vayam ca tebhyaḥ ca asmabhyam abhimukhībhūtebhyaḥ bravīt  gandharvaḥ sūtram antaryāmiṇam ca tad aham sūtrānitaryāmi vijñānam veda gandharvāt labdha āgamaḥ san tad ced  yājñavalkya sūtram tam ca antaryāmiṇam avidvān  cebrahma vid  san yadi brahma gavīru dajatase brahma vidām sva bhūtā gā udajase unnayasi tvam anyāyena tatas  mad śāpa dagdhasya mūrdhā śiraḥ te tava vispaṣṭam ṣatiṣyati evam uktaḥ  yājñavalkya āhavet jānāmi aham he gautama iti gotrataḥ tad  sūtram yad  gandharvaḥ tubhyam uktavān yam ca antaryāmiṇam gandharvāt  viditavantaḥ  yūyam tam ca antaryāmiṇam veda aham iti evam uktaḥ  pratyāha gautamaḥ yaḥ kaścid  prākṛta idam yad tavaya uktam brūyāt  katham veda veda iti ātmānam ślāghayan kim tena garjitena kāryeṇa darśaya yathā vā itya tathā brūhi iti sa ha uvāca yājñavalkyaḥ brahma lokā yasmin notāḥ ca protāḥ ca vartamānekāle yathā pṛthivī apsu tad  sūtram āgama gamyam vattavyam iti tad artham praśna antaram utthāpitam  atas tad nirṇayāya āha vāyuḥ vai gautama tad  sūtram na anyat va āyuḥ iti sūkṣmam ākāśavat viṣṭambhakam pṛthivī ādīnām yad ātmakam saptadaśavidham liṅgam karma vāsanā samavāyi prāṇinām yad tad samaṣṭi vyaṣṭi ātmakam yasya bāhyā medāḥ sapta sapta marut raṇāḥ samudrasya iva ūrmayaḥ tad etad  vāyavyam tattvam sūtrām iti abhidhīyate vāyunā vai gautama sūtreṇa ayam ca lokaḥ paraḥ ca lokaḥ sarvāṇi ca bhūtāni sandṛbdhāni bhavanti saṅprathitāni bhavanti iti prasiddham etad  asti ca loke prasiddhiḥ katham yasmāt  vāyuḥ sūtram vāyunā vidhṛtam sarvam tasmāt  vai gautama puruṣam pretam āhuḥ kathayanti vyasraṃsipata visrastāni asya puruṣasya aṅgāni iti sūtra apagame hi maṇyādīnām protāni yad  yasya aṅgāni syuḥ tatas  yuktam etad  vāyu apagame avasraṃsanam aṅgānām atas  vāyunā hi gautama sūtreṇa sandṛbdhāni bhavanti iti nigamayati evam eva etad  yājñavalkya samyak uktam sūtram  tad antargatam tu idānīm tasya eva sūtrasya niyantāram antaryāmiṇam brūhi iti ukta āha yaḥ pṛthivyām tiṣṭhan bhavati saḥ  antaryāmī sarvaḥ pṛthivyām tiṣṭhati iti sarvatra prasaṅgaḥ  mā bhūt iti viśinaṣṭi pṛthivyāḥ  antaraḥ  abhyantaraḥ tatra etad  syāt  pṛthivī devatā eva antaryāmī iti ata āha yam antaryāmiṇam pṛthivī devatā api na veda mayi anyaḥ kaścid vartata iti yasya pṛthivī śarīram yasya ca pṛthivī eva śarīram na anyat  pṛthivī devatāyāḥ  yad śarīram tad eva śarīram yasya śarīra grahaṇam ca upalakṣaṇa artham karaṇam ca pṛthivyāḥ tasya sva karma prayuktam hi kāryam ca pṛthivī devatāyāḥ tad asya sva karma abhāvāt antaryāmiṇaḥ  nitya mukta tvāt  para artha kartavyatā svabhāva tvāt parasya yad  kāryam karaṇam ca tad eva asya na svatas  tad āha yasya pṛthivī śarīram iti devatā kārya karaṇasya īśvara sākṣi mātra sānnidhyena hi niyamena pravṛtti nivṛttī syātām ya īdṛś īśvaraḥ  nārāyaṇa ākhyaḥ pṛthiḥ vī pṛthivī devatām yamayati niyamayati sva vyāpāre antaraḥ  abhyantaraḥ tiṣṭhan eṣa ta ātmā te tava mama ca sarva bhūtānām ca iti upalakṣaṇa artham etad  antaryāmī yaḥ tvayā āpṛṣṭaḥ amṛtaḥ sarva saṃsāra dharma varjita iti etad  yaḥ  agnau tiṣṭhan   agneḥ  antaraḥ  yam agniḥ  na veda yasya agniḥ śarīram yaḥ  agnim antaraḥ  yamayati  eṣa ta ātmā antaryāmy amṛtaḥ bhrhūp yaḥ  antarikṣe tiṣṭhan   antarikṣāt  antaraḥ  yam antarikṣam na veda yasya antarikṣam śarīram yaḥ  antarikṣam antaraḥ  yamayati  eṣa ta ātmā antaryāmy amṛtaḥ bhrhūp yaḥ  vāyau tiṣṭhan vāyoḥ  antaraḥ  yam vāyuḥ  na veda yasya vāyuḥ śarīram yaḥ  vāyum antaraḥ  yamayati  eṣa ta ātmā antaryāmy amṛtaḥ bhrhūp yaḥ  divi tiṣṭhan divaḥ  antaraḥ  yam dyauḥ  na veda yasya dyauḥ śarīram yaḥ  divam antaraḥ  yamayati  eṣa ta ātmā antaryāmy amṛtaḥ bhrhūp ya āditye tiṣṭhan   ādityāt  antaraḥ  yam ādityaḥ  na veda yasya ādityaḥ śarīram ya ādityam antaraḥ  yamayati  eṣa ta ātmā antaryāmy amṛtaḥ bhrhūp yaḥ  dikṣu tiṣṭhan digbhyaḥ  antaraḥ  yam diśaḥ  na viduḥ  yasya diśaḥ śarīram yaḥ  diśaḥ  antaraḥ  yamayati  eṣa ta ātmā antaryāmy amṛtaḥ bhrhūp yaḥ  candra tārake tiṣṭhan  candra tārakāt  antaraḥ  yam candra tārakam na veda yasya candra tārakam śarīram yaḥ  candra tārakam antaraḥ  yamayati  eṣa ta ātmā antaryāmy amṛtaḥ bhrhūp ya ākāśe tiṣṭhan   ākāśāt  antaraḥ  yam ākāśaḥ  na veda yasya ākāśaḥ śarīram ya ākāśam antaraḥ  yamayati  eṣa ta ātmā antaryāmy amṛtaḥ bhrhūp yaḥ  tamasi tiṣṭhan   tamasaḥ  antaraḥ  yam tamaḥ  na veda yasya tamaḥ śarīram yaḥ  tamaḥ  antaraḥ  yamayati  eṣa ta ātmā antaryāmy amṛtaḥ bhrhūp yaḥ  tejasi tiṣṭhan   tejasaḥ  antaraḥ  yam tejaḥ  na veda yasya tejaḥ śarīram yaḥ  tejaḥ  antaraḥ  yamayati  eṣa ta ātmā antaryāmy amṛtaḥ bhrhūp samānam anyat  yaḥ  apsu tiṣṭhan agnau antarikṣe vāyau divi āditye yaḥ tamasya āvaraṇa ātmake bāhye tamasi tejasi tad viparīte prakāśa sāmānye iti evam adhidaivatam antaryāmi viṣayam darśanam devatāsu atha adhibhūtam bhūteṣu brahma di stamba paryanteṣu antaryāmi daśanam adhibhūtam atha adhyātmam yaḥ prāṇe prāṇa vāyu sahite ghrāṇe yaḥ  vāci cakṣuṣi śrotre manasi tvaci vijñāne budvau retasi prajanane kasmāt  punar  kāraṇāt  pṛthivī ādi devatā mahābhāgāḥ satyaḥ  manuṣya ādi vadātamani tiṣṭhantam ātmanaḥ  niyantāram antaryāmiṇam na viduḥ ityata āha adṛṣṭena d daṣṭaḥ  na viṣayībhūtaḥ cakṣuḥ darśanasya kasyacid  svayam tu cakṣuṣi sannihita tvāt d daśi svarūpa iti draṣṭā tathā aśrutaḥ śrotra gocara tvam anāpannaḥ kasyacid  svayam tu alupta śravaṇa śaktiḥ sarva śrotreṣu sannihitatva achracotā tathā amataḥ manaḥ saṅkalpa viṣaya tām anāpannaḥ dṛṣṭa śrute eva hi sarvaḥ saṅkalpayati  uddṛṣṭa tvāt akṣuta tvāt eva āmatas  allapta manana śakti tvāt sarva manaḥsu sannihita tvāt ca mantā tathā avijñātaḥ  niścaya gocara tām anāpannaḥ rūpa ādivat  lasukha ādivat vā svayam tu alupta vijñāna śakti tvāt tad sannidhānāt ca vijñātā tatra yam pṛthivī na veda yam sarvāṇi bhūtāni na viduḥ iti ca anye niyantavyā vijñātāraḥ  anyaḥ  niyantā antaryāmi iti prāptam tad anyatva āśaṅkā nivṛtti artham ucyate na anyaḥ  atas  na anyaḥ atas  asmāt antaryāmiṇaḥ  na anyaḥ  asti draṣṭā tathā na anyaḥ  atas  asti mantā na anyaḥ  atas  asti śrotā na anyaḥ  atas  asti mantā na anyaḥ  atas  asti vijñātā yasmāt  paraḥ  na asti draṣṭā śrotā mantā vijñātā yaḥ  adṛṣṭaḥ  draṣṭā aśrutaḥ śrotā amataḥ  mantā avijñātaḥ  vijñātā amṛtaḥ sarva saṃsāra dharma varjitaḥ sarva saṃsāriṇām karma phala vibhāga kartā eṣa te ātma antaryāmī amṛtaḥ asmāt īśvarāt ātmanaḥ  anyat ārtam tatas  hi uddālaka āruṇiḥ upara rāma iti tṛtīyā adhyāye saptamam antaryāmi brāhmaṇam atas  param śanāya ādi vinirmuktam nirupādhikam sākṣāt aparokṣāt  sarva antaram brahma vaktavyam iti ata ārambhaḥ atha ha vācaknavī uvāca sarvam yājñavalkyena niṣiddhā mūrdha pāta bhayāt uparatā satī punar  praṣṭum brāhmaṇa anujñām prārthayate he brāhmaṇā bhagavantaḥ pūjāvantaḥ śṛṇuta mama vacaḥ  hantā aham imam yājñavalkyam punar dvai praśnau prakṣyāmi yadi anumatiḥ bhavatām asti tau praśnau ced yadi vakṣyati kathayiṣyati me kathañcid na vai jātu kadācid  yuṣmākam madhye imam yājñavalkyam kaścid  brahma udyam brahma vadanam prati jetā na vai kaścid  bhavet iti evam uktā brāhmaṇā anujñām pradaduḥ pṛccha gārgi iti labdha anujñā ha yājñavalkyam sā ha uvāca aham vai tvā tvām dvau praśnau prakṣyāmi iti anuṣajyate kau tau  iti jijñāsāyām tayoḥ duruttara tvadyotayitum dṛṣṭānta pūrvakam tau  āha he yājñavalkya yathā loke kāśyaḥ kāśiṣu bhavaḥ kāśyaḥ prasiddham śauryam kāśye vaidehaḥ  vā videhānām vā rājā ugra putraḥ śūra anvaya iti arthaḥ ujjyam avatārita jyākam dhanuḥ punar adhijyam āropitalyākam kṛtvā dvau bāṇavantau bāṇa śabdena śara agre yaḥ  vaṃśa khaṇḍaḥ saṃdhīyate tena vinā api śaraḥ  bhavati iti atas  viśinaṣṭi bāṇavantau  iti dvau bāṇavantau śarau tayoḥ eva viśeṣaṇam sapatna ativyādhinau śatroḥ pīḍā karau  atiśayena haste kṛtvā upottiṣṭhet samīpata ātmānam darśayet  evam eva aham tvā tvām śara sthānīyābhyām praśnābhyām dvābhyām upoda sthām utthitavati asmi tvad samīpe tau me brūhi iti brahma vid ced  āha itaraḥ pṛccha gārgi iti sā ha uvāca yad ūrdhvam upari divaḥaṇḍa kapālāt  yad ca avāgadhaḥ pṛthivyāḥ  adhas  aṇḍa kapālāt  yad ca antarā madhye dyāvāpṛthivī dyāvāpṛthivyoḥ aṇḍa kapālayoḥ ime ca dyāvāpṛthivī yad  bhūtam yad ca atītam bhavat ca vartamānam sva vyāpāra stham bhaviṣyat ca vartamānāt ūrdhva kāla bhā viliṅga gamyam yad  sarvam etad ācakṣate kathayanti āgamataḥ tad  sarvam dvaita jātam yasmin  ekībhavati iti arthaḥ tad  sūtra saṃjñam pūrva uktam kasminnotam ca protam ca pṛthivī dhātuḥ iva apsu sa ha uvāca itaraḥ he gārgi yad  tvayā uktam aūrdhvam divaḥ aityādi tad  sarvam yad  sūtram ācakṣate tad  sūtram ākāśe tadā utam protam ca yad etad  vyākṛtam sūtra ātmakam jagat avyākṛta ākāśe apsu iva pṛthivī dhātuḥ triṣu api kāleṣu vartate utpattau sthitau laye ca punar  sā ha uvāca  namaḥ te astu ityādi praśnasya durvacatva pradarśana artham  yaḥ  me mama etam praśnam vyavocaḥ  viśeṣaṇa apākṛtavān asi  etasya durvaca tve kāraṇam sūtram eva tāvat agamyam itaraiḥ durvācyam kim uta tad  yasmin notam ca protam ca iti atas namaḥ  astu te tubhyam aparasmai dvitīyāya praśnāya dhārayasva dṛḍhīkurva ātmānam iti arthaḥ pṛccha gārgi iti itara āha vyākhyātam anyat sā ha uvāca yadurdhvam yājñavalkya etyādi praśnaḥ prativacanam ca uktasya eva arthasya avadhāraṇa artham punar ucyate na kiñcid apūrvam artha antaram ucyate sarvam yathā uktam gārgyā pratyuccārya tam eva pūrva uktam artham avadhāritavān ākāśa eva iti yājñavalkyaḥ gārgyāha kasmin nu khalu ākāśa otaḥ ca protaḥ ca iti ākāśam eva tāvat  kāla traya atīta tvāt  durvācyam tatas  api kaṣṭataram akṣaram yasmin  ākāśa motam ca protam ca atas  avācyam iti kṛtvā na pratipadyate sā apratipattiḥ nāma nigraha sthānam tārkika samaye atha avācyam api vakṣyati tathā api vipratipattiḥ nāma nigraha sthānam  virudvā pratipattiḥ hi sā yad avācyasya vadanam atas  durvacanam praśnam manyate gārgī tad  doṣa dvayam api parijihīrpan  āha sa ha uvāca yājñavalkyaḥ etad  vai tad  yad  pṛṣṭavatī asi kasmin nu khalu ākāśa otaḥ ca protaḥ ca iti kim tad  akṣaram yad na kṣīyate na kṣarati iti vā akṣaram tad akṣaram he gārgi brāhmaṇā brahma vidaḥ  abhivadanti brahmaṇā abhivadana kathanena na aham avācyam vakṣyāmi na cana pratipadyeyam iti evam dopadrayam pariharati evam apākute praśne punar gārgyāḥ prativacanam draṣṭavyam brūhi kim tad akṣaram yad  brāhmaṇā abhivadanti iti ukta āha prasthūlam tad  sthūlāt anyat  evam tarhi aṇu anaṇu astu tarhi hasvam ahasvam  evam tarhi dīrgham na api dīrgham adīrgham  evam etaiḥ caturbhiḥ parimāṇa pratiṣedhaiḥ dravya dharmaḥ pratiṣidvaḥ na dravyam tad akṣaram iti arthaḥ astu tarhi lohitaḥ  guṇaḥ tatas  api anyat alohitam āgneyaḥ  guṇa u lohitaḥ bhavatu tarhi apyām snehanam na asneha nam astu tarhi  chāyā sarvathā api anirdeśya tvāt chāyāyāḥ  api anyat acchāyam  astu tarhi tamaḥ atamaḥ bhavatu vāyuḥ tarhi avāyuḥ  bhavet tarhi ākāśam anākāśam  bhavatu tarhi saṅga ātmakam jatuvat  asaṅgam arasaḥ  astu tarhi arasam tathā gandhaḥ  astu agandham astu tarhi cakṣuḥ acakṣuṣkam na hi cakṣuḥ asya karaṇam vidyate atas  acakṣuṣkam  paśyati acakṣuḥ iti mantra varṇāt  tathā aśrotram  sa śṛṇoti akarṇaḥ iti bhavatu tarhi vāc avāk tathā manaḥ tathā tejaskam avidyamānam tejaḥ  asya tad atejaskam na hi tejaḥ  agni ādi prakāśavat asya vidyate aprāṇam ādhyātmikaḥ vāyuḥ pratiṣidhyate aprāṇam iti  mukham tarhi dvāram tad amukham amānnam mīyate yena tanmātram amātram mātrā rūpam tad na bhavati na tena kiñcinmīyate aḥ tu tarhi  chidravat  anantaram na asya antaram asti  sambhavet tarhi bahis tasya abāhyam  astu tarhi bhakṣayitṛ tad  na tad aśnāti kñcina  bhavet tarhi bhakṣyam kasyacid  na tad aśnāti kaścana  sarva viśeṣaṇa rahitam iti arthaḥ  ekam eva advitīyam hi tad  kena kim viśiṣyate aneka viśeṣaṇa pratiṣedha prayāsāt astitvam tāvat akṣarasya upagamitam śrutyā  tathā api loka budvim apekṣyā śaṅkyate yatas  atas  astitvāya anumānam pramāṇam upanyasyati vā akṣarasya praśāsane gārgi dadataḥ  manuṣyāḥ praśaṃsanti yajamānam devāḥ darvīm pitaraḥ  anvāyattāḥ etasya vā akṣarasya yad etad adhigatam akṣaram sarva antaram sākṣāt aparokṣāt brahma ya ātmā aśanāya ādi dharma atītaḥ etasya vā akṣarasya praśāsane yathā rājñaḥ praśāsane rājyam asphuṭitam niyatam vartate evam atasya akṣarasya praśāsane he gārgi sūryācandramasaḥ  ahorātrayoḥ loka pradīpau tādarthyena praśāsitrā tābhyām nirvatyamāna loka prayojana vijñānavatā nirmitau ca syātām sādhāraṇa sarva prāṇi prakāśa upakāraka tvāt laukika pradīpavat tasmāt asti tad  yena vidhṛtau  īśvarau svatantrau sastau nirmitau tiṣṭhataḥ  niyata deśa kāla nimitta udaya astamaya vṛddhi kṣayābhyām vartete  tad asti evam etayoḥ praśāsitra kṣaram pradīpa kartṛ vidhārayitṛvat  etasya vā akṣarasya praśāsane gārgī dyāvāpṛthivī ca sāvayava tvāt sphuṭana svabhāve api satyau guru tvāt  patana svabhāve saṃyukta tvāt  viyoga svabhāve cetanāvat abhimāni devatā adhiṣṭhita tvāt svatantre api etasya akṣarasya praśāsane vartete vidhṛte tiṣṭhataḥ etad hi akṣa ram sarva vyavasthā setuḥ sarva maryādā vidharaṇam atas  na asya akṣarasya praśāsanam dyāvāpṛthivyau  atikrāmataḥ tasmāt  siddham asya astitvam akṣarasya avyabhicāri hi tad liṅgam yad  dyāvāpṛthivyau niyate vartete cetanāvantam praśāsitāram asaṃsāriṇam antareṇa na etad  yuktam yena dyauḥ ugrā pṛthivī ca dṛṣṭā iti mantra varṇāt  etasya vā akṣarasya praśāsane gārgi nimeṣā muhūrtā iti ete kāla avayavāḥ sarvasya atīta anāgata vartamānasya janimataḥ kalayitāraḥ yathā loke prabhuṇā niyataḥ  gaṇakaḥ sarva māyam vyayam ca apramattaḥ  gaṇayati tathā prabhu sthānīya eṣām kāla avayavānām niyantā tathā prācayaḥ prāgañcanāḥ pūrva diggamanā nadyaḥ syandante sravanti śvetebhyaḥ  himavat ādibhyaḥ parvatebhyaḥ  giribhyaḥ  gaṅgā ādyā nadyaḥ tāḥ ca yathā pravartitā eva niyatāḥ pravartante anyathā api pravartitum utsahantyaḥ tad etad liṅgam praśāstuḥ pratīcyaḥ  anyāḥ pratīcīm diśam añcanti sindhva ādyā nadyaḥ anyāḥ ca yām yām diśam anupravṛttāḥ tām tām na vyabhicaranti  tad ca siṅgam kiñca dadataḥ  hiraṇya ādīn prayacchata ātma pīḍām kurvataḥ  api pramāṇa jñā api manuṣyāḥ praśaṃsanti  tatra yad ca dīyate ye ca dadati ye ca pratigṛhmanti teṣām iha eva samāgamaḥ  vilayaḥ ca anvakṣaḥ  dṛśyate adṛṣṭaḥ tu paraḥ samāgamaḥ tathā api manuṣyā dadatām dāna phalena saṃyogam paśyantaḥ pramāṇa jña tayā praśaṃsanti  tad ca karma phalena saṃyojayitari kartuḥ karma phala vibhāga jñe praśāstari asati na syāt  dāna kriyāyāḥ pratyakṣa vināśi tvāt tasmāt asti dāna kartṛṇām phalena saṃyojayitā apūrvam iti ced  tad sadbhāve pramāṇa anupapatteḥ praśastuḥ api iti ced  na āgamatātparyasya siddha tvāt ava ucāma dyāgamasya vastu paratvāt kiñca anyat apūrva kalpanāyām ca arthāpatteḥ kṣayaḥ  anyathā eva upapatteḥ sevā phalasya sevyāt  prāpti darśanāt  sevāyāḥ ca kriyā tvāt  tad sāmānyāt ca vāc adānahoma ādīnām sevyād īśvara ādeḥ phala prāptiḥ upapadyate dṛṣṭa kriyā dharma sāmarthyam aparityajya eva phala prāpti kalpanā upapattau dṛṣṭa kriyā dharma sāmarthya parityāgaḥ  na nyāyyaḥ kalpanā ādhikyāt ca īśvaraḥ kalpvaḥ  apūrvā vā tatra kriyāyāḥ ca svabhāvaḥ sevyāt  phala prāptiḥ dṛṣṭā na tu apūrvāt na ca apūrvam dṛṣṭam  tatra apūrvam adṛṣṭam kalpayitavyam tasya ca phala dātṛ tve sāmarthyam sāmarthye ca sati dānam ca abhyadhikam iti iha tu īśvarasya sevyasya sadbhāva mātram kalpyam na tu phala dāna sāmarthyam dātṛ tvam ca sevyāt  phala prāpti darśanāt  anumānam ca darśitam adya avāpṛthivyau vidhṛte tiṣṭhataḥ aityādi tathā ca yajamānam devāḥ  īśvarāḥ santaḥ  jīvana arthe anugatāḥ cara puroḍāśa ādi upajīvana prayojanena anyathā api jīvitum utsahantaḥ kṛpaṇām dīnām vṛttim āśritya sthitāḥ tad ca praśāstuḥ praśāsanāt  syāt  tathā pitaraḥ  api tad artham darvī darvīhomam anvāyattā anugatā iti arthaḥ samānam sarvam anyat itas ca asti tad akṣaram smāt tad ajñāne niyatā saṃsāra upapattiḥ bhavitavyam tu tena yad vijñānāt tad vicchedaḥ nyāya upapatteḥ nanu kriyāta eva tad vicchittiḥ syāt iti ced  na yaḥ  vā etad akṣaram he gārgi aviditvā avijñāya asmin  loke juhoti yajata tapaḥ tapyate yadi api bahūni varṣa sahasrāṇi antavat  eva asya tad  phalam bhavati tad phala upabhoga ante kṣīyanta eva asya karmāṇi api ca yad vijñānāt kārpaṇya atyayaḥ saṃsāra vicchedaḥ yad vijñāna abhāvāt ca karma kṛt  kṛpaṇaḥ kṛta phalasya eva upabhoktā janana maraṇa prabandha ārūḍhaḥ saṃsarati tad asti akṣaram praśāsitṛ tad etad ucyate yaḥ  vā etad akṣaram gārgya viditvā asmāt lokāt  praiti sa kṛpaṇaḥ paṇakrīta iva dāsa ādiḥ atha ya etad akṣaram gārgi viditvā asmāt lokāt  praiti sa brāhmaṇaḥ agneḥ dahana prakāśaka tvāt  svābhāvikasya praśāstṛ tvam acetanasya eva ityata āha tad  vā etad akṣaram gārgi adṛṣṭam na kenacid  dṛṣṭam aviṣaya tvāt  svayam tu draṣṭṛ dṛṣṭi svarūpa tvāt tathā śrutam śrotra aviṣaya tvāt svayam śrotṛ śruti svarūpa tvāt  tathāmatam manasaḥ  aviṣaya tvāt  svayam mantṛmati svarūpa tvāt tathā avijñātam buddheḥ aviṣaya tvāt  svayam vijñātṛ vijñāna svarūpa tvāt kiñca na anyat atas  asmāt akṣarāt asti na asti kiñcid  draṣṭṛ darśana kriyā kartṛ  etad eva akṣaram darśana kriyā kartṛ sarvatra tathā na anyat atas  asti śrotṛ tad eva akṣaram śrotṛ sarvatra na anyat atas  asti mantṛ tad eva akṣaram mantṛ sarvatra sarva manaḥ dvāreṇa na anyat atas  asti vijñātṛ vijñāna kriyā kartṛ  tad eva akṣaram sarva buddhi dvāreṇa vijñāna kriyā kartṛ  na acetanam pradhānam anyat  vā etasmin   u khalu akṣare gārgyākāśa otaḥ ca protaḥ ca iti yad eva sākṣāt aparokṣāt braṅma ya ātmā sarva antaraḥ  aśanāya ādi saṃsāra dharma atītaḥ yasmin  ākāśa otaḥ ca protaḥ ca eṣā parā kāṣṭhā eṣā parā gatiḥ etad  param brahma etad  pṛthivī ādeḥ ākāśa antasya satyasya satyam sā ha uvāca he brāhmaṇā bhagavantaḥ śṛṇuta madīyam vacaḥ  tad eva bahu manyedhvam  kim tad  yad asmāt  yājñavalkyāt namaskāreṇa mucyedhvam asmai namaskāram kṛtvā tad eva bahu manyadhvam iti arthaḥ  jayaḥ tu asya manasā api na āśaṃsanīyaḥ kim uta kāryataḥ  kasmāt  na vai yuṣmākam madhye jātu kadācid api imam yājñavalkyam brahma udyam prati jetā praśnau cena mahyam vakṣyati na jetā bhavitā iti pūrvam eva mayā pratijñātam  adya api mama ayam eva niścayaḥ brahma udyam pratyetat tulyaḥ  na kaścid  vidyata iti tatas  ha vācakna vyupararāma atra antaryāmi brāhmaṇe etad  uktam yam pṛthivī na veda yam sarvāṇi bhūtāni na vidiḥ iti ca yam antaryāmiṇam na vidurye ca na viduḥ yad ca tad akṣaram darśanāt akriyā kartṛ tvena sarveṣām cetana ādi dhātuḥ iti uktam kaḥ tu eṣām viśeṣaḥ kim vā sāmānyam iti tatra kecid ācakṣate parasya mahā samudra sthāna ayasya brahmaṇaḥ  akṣarasya apracalitatva rūpasya īṣat pracalita avasthā antaryāmī atyanta pracalita avasthā kṣetrajñaḥ yaḥ tam na vedāntaryāmiṇam  tathā anyāḥ pañca avasthāḥ parikalpayanti tathā aṣṭa avasthā brahmaṇaḥ  bhavanti iti vadanti anye akṣarasya śaktaya etā iti vadanti ananta śaktimat akṣaram iti ca anye tu akṣarasya vikārā iti vadanti avasthā śaktī tāvat na upapadyeta u akṣarasya aśanāya ādi saṃsāra dharma atītatva śruteḥ na hi aśanāya ādi atīta tvam aśanāya ādi dharmavat avasthāvat tvam ca ekasya yugapad upapadyate  tathā śaktimat tvam ca vikāra avayava tve ca doṣāḥ pradarśitāḥ caturthe tasmāt etā asatyāḥ sarvāḥ kalpanāḥ kaḥ tarhi meda eṣām upādhikṛta iti brūmaḥ na svata eṣām medaḥ  amedaḥ  vā saindhava ghanavat  prajñāna dhana eka rasa svāmāvyāt apūrvam anaparam anantaram abāhyam ayam ātmā brahma iti ca śruteḥ sa vāhya abhyāntaraḥ  hi ajaḥ iti ca ātharvaṇe tasmāt nirūpa adhikasya ātmanaḥ  nirūpa ākhyātvāt nirviśeṣa tvāt eka tvāt ca na iti na iti iti vyapadeśaḥ  bhavati avidyā kāma karma viśiṣṭa kārya karaṇa upādhiḥ ātmā saṃsārī jiva ucyate nitya
