niratiśaya jñāna śakti upādhiḥ ātma antaryām ī īśvara ucyate sa eva nirūpa ādhiḥ kevalaḥ śudvaḥ svena svabhāvena akṣaram para ucyate tathā hiraṇyagarma avyākṛta devatā jāti piṇḍa manuṣya tiryak preta ādi kārya karaṇa upādh ibhiḥ viśiṣṭaḥ tad ākhyaḥ tad arūpaḥ  bhavati tathā tad ejati tad na ejati iti vyākhyātam tathā eṣa ta ātmā eṣa sarva bhūta antarātmā eṣa sarveṣu bhūteṣu gūḍhaḥ tad tavam asi aham eva idam sarvam ātmā eva idam sarvam na anyaḥ  atas  asti draṣṭā ityādi śrutayaḥ  na virudhyante kalpanā antareṣu etāḥ śrutayaḥ na gacchanti tasmāt upādhi medena ela eṣām medaḥ  na anyathā aekam eva advitīyam aiti avadhāraṇāt sarveṣa niṣatsu iti tṛtīyā adhyāyeṣṭamam akṣara brāhmaṇam atha ha enam vidagdhaḥ śākalyaḥ papraccha pṛthivī ādīnām sūkṣma tāratamya krameṇa pūrvasya pūrvasya uttarasmin  uttarasminnota prota bhāvam kathayan sarva antaram brahma prakāśitavān tasya ca brahmaṇaḥ  vyākṛta viṣaye sūtra medeṣu niyantṛ tvam uktam vyākṛta viṣaye vyaktaram liṅgam iti tasya eva brahmaṇaḥ sākṣāt aparokṣa tve niyantavya devatā meda saṃkoca vikā sa dvāreṇa adhigantavye iti tad arya śākalya brāhmaṇam āramyate atha ha enam vidagdha iti nāmataḥ śakalasya apatyam śākalyaḥ papraccha kati saṃkhyākā devāḥ  he yājñavalkya iti sa yājñavalkyaḥ ha kila etayā eva vakṣyamāṇayā nividā pratipede saṃkhyām yām saṃkhyām pṛṣṭavān śākalyaḥ yāvantaḥ  yāvat saṃkhyākā devāḥ  vaiśvadevasya śastrasya nividi nivid nāma devatā saṃkhyā vācakāni mantra padāni kānicid  vaiśvadeve śastre śasyante tāni nivid saṃjñakā ni tasyām nividi yāvantaḥ  devāḥ śrūyante tāvantaḥ  devāḥ  iti kā punar  sā nivid iti tāni nivid padāni pradarśyante trayaḥ ca trī ca śatā trayaḥ ca devāḥ devānām trī ca trīṇi ca śatāni punar api evam trayaḥ ca trī ca sahasrā sahasrāṇ etāvantaḥ  devāḥ  iti śākalyaḥ  api om iti ha uvāca evam eṣām madhyamā saṃkhyā samyaktayā jñātā punar tepām eva devānām saṃkoca viṣayām saṃkhyām pṛcchati kati eva devāḥ  yājñavalkya iti trayaḥ tri śata pada trayaḥ dvau adhyardhaḥ eka iti devatā saṃkoca vikāsa viṣayām saṃkhyām pṛṣṭvā punar  saṃkhyeya svarūpam pṛcchati katame te trayaḥ ca trī ca śatā trayaḥ ca trī ca sahasra iti sa ha uvāca itaraḥ mahimānaḥ  vibhūtayaḥ eṣām trayastriṃśataḥ devānām ete trayaḥ ca trī ca śata ityādayaḥ paramārthataḥ tu trayastriṃśat tvā iva devāḥ  iti katame te trayastriṃśat iti ucyate aṣṭau vasavaḥ ekādaśa rudrāḥ dvādaśa ādityāḥ te ekatriṃśat  indraḥ ca eva prajāpatiḥ ca trayastriṃśau  iti trayastriṃśataḥ pūraṇau katame vasava iti teṣām svarūpam pratyekam pṛchcyate agniḥ ca pṛthivī ca iti agni ādyā nakṣatra antarā ete vasavaḥ prāṇinām karma phala āśraya tvena kārya karaṇa saṃghāta rūpeṇa tad nivāsa tvena ca vipariṇamantaḥ  jagat idam sarvam vāsayanti vasanti ca te yasmāt  vāsanti tasmāt e vasava iti katame rudrā iti daśa ime puruṣe karma buddhīndriyāṇi prāṇāḥ ātmā mana ekādaśaḥ ekādaśānām pūraṇaḥ te ete prāṇā yadā asmāt śarīrāt martyāt  prāṇinām karma phala pabhoga kṣaye utkrāmanti atha tadā rodayanti tad sambandhinaḥ tad tatra yasmāt rodayanti te sambandhinaḥ tasmāt  rudrā iti katama ādityā iti dvādaśa vai māsāḥ saṃvatsarasya kālasya avayavāḥ prasiddhāḥ ete ādityāḥ katham ete hi yasmāt  punar  punar  parivartamānāḥ prāṇinām āyūṃṣi karma phalam ca ādadānā gṛhyanta upādadataḥ  yanti gacchanti te yad  yasmāt evam idam sarvam ādadānā yanti tasmāt ādityā iti katama indraḥ katamaḥ prajāpatiḥ iti stanayiti uḥ eva indraḥ  yajñaḥ prajāpatiḥ iti katamaḥ stanayitnuḥ iti aśaniḥ iti aśaniḥ vajram vīryam balam yad  prāṇinaḥ pramāpayati sa indraḥ indrasya hi tad  karma katamaḥ  yajña iti paśava iti yajñasya hi sādhanāni paśavaḥ  yajñasya arūpa tvāt paśu sādhana āśraya tvāt ca paśavaḥ  yajña iti ucyate katame ṣaṣ iti te  eva agnyādayaḥ  vasu tvena paṭhitāḥ candramasam nakṣatrāṇi ca varjayitvā ṣaṣ  bhavanti ṣaṭa saṃkhyā viśiṣṭāḥ trayastriṃśat ādi yad uktam idam sarvam eta eva ṣaṣ  bhavanti sarvaḥ  hi vasu ādi vistara eteṣu eva ṣaṭasu antarbhavati iti arthaḥ katame te trayaḥ  devāḥ  iti ima eva trayaḥ  lokā iti pṛthivīm agnim ca ekokṛtya ekaḥ devaḥ antarikṣam vāyum ca ekīkṛtya tṛtīyaḥ te eva trayaḥ  devāḥ  iti eṣu hi yasmāt  triṣu deveṣu sarve devāḥ  antarbhavanti tena ta eva devāḥ trayaḥ iti eṣa nairuktānām keṣāñcid  pakṣaḥ katamau tau dvau devau  iti annam ca eva prāṇaḥ ca etau dvau devau anayoḥ sarveṣām uktānām antarbhāvaḥ katamaḥ  adhyargha iti yaḥ  ayam pavate vāyuḥ tad tatra āhuḥ codayanti yad ayam vāyuḥ eka iva eva eka eva pavate  atha katham adhyardha iti yad asmin  idaṃ sarva madhya ardhnot  asmin vāyau sati idam sarva madhya ardhna udadhi ṛddhim prāpnoti tena adhyardha iti katama ekaḥ  deva iti prāṇa iti sa prāṇaḥ  brahma sarva deva ātmaka tvāt mahat  brahma tena sa brahma tyat iti ācakṣate tyat iti tad  brahmācakṣate parokṣa āmidhāyakena śabdena devānām etad eka tvam nānā tvam ca anantānām devānām nivid saṃkhyā viśaṣṭeṣu antarbhāvaḥ teṣām api trayāḥ tri śada ādi pu uttara uttareṣu yāvat ekasmin prāṇe prāṇasya eva ca ekasya sarvaḥ  ananta saṅkhyātaḥ  vistaraḥ evam ekaḥ ca anantaḥ ca avāntara saṃkhyā viśiṣṭaḥ ca prāṇa eva tatra ca devasya ekasya nāma rūpa karna guṇa śakti medaḥ adhikāra medāt  idānīm tasya eva prāṇasya brahmaṇaḥ punar aṣṭadhā meda upadiśyate pṛthivī eva yasya devasya āyatanam āśrayaḥ agniḥ lokaḥ  yasya lokayati anena iti lokaḥ paśyati iti agninā paśyati iti arthaḥ manojyotiḥ manasā jyotiṣā saṃkalpa vikalpa ādi kāryam karoti yaḥ saḥ  ayam manojyotiḥ pṛthivī śarīraḥ  agni darśanaḥ  manasā saṃkalpayitā pṛthivī abhimānī kārya karaṇa saṃghātavān deva iti arthaḥ ya evam viśiṣṭam vai tam puruṣam vidyāt  vijānīyāt  sarvasya ātmana ādhyātmikasya kārya karaṇa saṃghātasya ātmanaḥ paramayanam para āśrayaḥ tam parāyaṇam mātṛ jena tvac māṃsa rudhira rūpeṇa kṣetra sthānīyena bīja sthānīyasya pitṛ jasya asthi majjā śukra rūpasya param ayanam karaṇa ātmanaḥ ca sa vai veditā syāt  ya etad evam vetti sa vai veditā paṇḍitaḥ syāt itya abhiprāyaḥ yājñavalkya tvam tam ajānan  eva paṇḍita abhimāni iti ami prāyaḥ yadi tad vijñāne pāṇḍityam labhyate veda vai aham tam puruṣam sarvasya ātmanaḥ parāyaṇam yam āttha yam kathayasi tam aham veda tatra śākalyasya vacanam draṣṭyam yadi tvam vettha tam puruṣam brūhi kiṃviśeṣaṇaḥ  asau saḥ ya eva ayam śārīraḥ pārdhiva aṃśe śarīre bhavaḥ śārīraḥ  mātṛ jakośa traya rūpa iti arthaḥ sa e devaḥ yaḥ tvayā pṛṣṭaḥ he śākalya kintu asti tatra vaktavyam viśeṣaṇa antaram tad  vada eva pṛcchā eva iti arthaḥ he śākalya sa evam prakṣobhitaḥ  amarpa vaśa ga āha tottrādinta iva gajaḥ tasya devasya śarīrasya kā devatā yasmāt niṣpadyate yaḥ sā tasya devatā iti asmin prakaraṇe vivakṣitaḥ amṛtam iti ha uvāca amṛtam iti yaḥ  bhuktasya annasya rasaḥ  mātṛ jasya lohitasya niṣpatti hetuḥ tasmāt vayan  arasāt lohitam niṣpadyate striyām śritam tatas ca lohita mayam śarīram bīja āśrayam samānam anyat  kāma eva yasya āyatanam strī vyatikāra abhilāṣaḥ kāmaḥ kāma śarīra  iti arthaḥ hradayam lokaḥ hradayena budvayā paśyati ya eva ayam kāma mayaḥ puruṣaḥ  adhyātmam api kāma maya eva tasya kā devatā iti striya iti ha uvāca  strītaḥ  hi kāmasya dīptiḥ jīyate rūpāṇi eva yasya āyatanam rūpāṇi śukla kṛṣṇa ādīni ya eva asau  āditye puruṣaḥ sarveṣām hi rūpāṇām viśiṣṭam kāryam āditye puruṣaḥ tasya kā devatā iti satyām iti ha uvāca satyām iti cakṣuḥ ucyate cakṣuṣaḥ  hi avyātmataḥ ādityasya adhidaivatasya niṣpatti ākāśa eva yasya āyatanam ya eva ayam śrotraḥ  bhavaḥ śrotraḥ tatra api pratiśravaṇa velāyām viśeṣataḥ  bhavati iti prātiśrutkaḥ tasya kādevatā iti diśa iti ha uvāca digbhyaḥ  hi asau  ādhyātmikaḥ niṣpadyate tama eva yasya āyatanam tama iti śārvadi andhakāraḥ parigṛhyate adhyātmam chāyā ām ayaḥ  ajñāna mayaḥ puruṣaḥ tasya kā devatā iti mṛtyuḥ iti ha uvāca mṛtyuḥ apidaivatam tasya niṣpatti kāraṇam rūpāṇi eva yasya āyatanam pūrva sa ādhārāni rūpāṇi uktāni iha tu prakāśakāni viśiṣṭāni rūpāṇi gṛhyante rūpa āyatanasya devasya viśeṣa āyatanam pratibimba ādhāram ādarśa ādi tasya kā devatā iti asuḥ iti ha uvāca tasya pratibimba ākhyasya puruṣasya niṣpattirasoḥ prāṇāt  āpa eva yasya āyatanam sādhāraṇāḥ sarvā āpa āyatanam vāpī kūpa taḍāga ādi āśrayāsu apsu viśeṣa avasthānam tasya kā devatā iti varuṇa iti varuṇāt  saṅghāta karñyodhi ātmam āpa eva vā api ādi apam niṣpatti kāraṇam reta eva yasya āyatanam ya eva ayam putram ayaḥ  viśeṇa āyatanam reta āyatanasya putrasya iti ca asthi mañjā śukāṇi pituḥ jātāni tasya kā devatā iti prajāpatiḥ iti ha uvāca prajñāpatiḥ pitā ucyate pitṛtaḥ  hi putrasya utpattiḥ aṣṭakā deva loka puruṣa bhedena tridhā tridhā ātmānam pravibhajya avasthita ekaikaḥ  devaḥ prāṇa bheda eva upāsana artha vyapadiṣṭaḥ adhunā diś vibhāgena pañcadhā pravibhaktasya ātmānayupasaṃhāra artham āha tūṣṇīmbhūtam śākalyam yājñavalkyaḥ  graheṇa iva āveśayan  āha śākalya iti ha uvāca yājñavalkyaḥ tvām svid iti vitarke ime nūnam brāhmaṇāḥ aṅgārāvakṣaṇam aṅgārā avakṣīyante yasmin sandaṃśa ādau tad aṅgārāvakṣaṇam tadā nūnam tvām akrata kṛtavantaḥ  brāhmaṇāḥ tvam tu tad na budhyase ātmānam mayā dahyamānam iti abhiprāyaḥ yājñavalkya iti ha uvāca śākalyaḥ yad idam kuruṣañcalānām brāhmaṇān atyavādīḥ ati uktavān asi svayam bhītāḥ tvām aṅgārāva kṣayaṇam kṛtavanta iti kim brahma vidvān san  evam adhikṣipasi brāhmaṇān yājñavalkya āha brahma vijñānam tāvat idam mama kim tad  diśaḥ  veda diś viṣayam vijñānam jāne tad ca na kvalam diśa eva sa devā devaiḥ saha diś adhiṣṭhātṛbhiḥ kiñca sa pratiṣṭhitāḥ pratiṣṭhābhiḥ ca saha itara āha yad  yadi diśaḥ  vettha sa devāḥ sa pratiṣṭhā iti saphalam yadi vijñānam tvayā pratijñātam kindevataḥ kā devatā asya tava digbhṛtasya asau hi yājñavalkyaḥ  hṛdayam ātmānam dikṣu pañcadhā vibhaktam diś ātma bhūtam tad dvāreṇa sarvam jagat ātma tvena upagamya aham asmi diś ātmā iti vyavasthitaḥ pūrva abhimukhaḥ sa pratiṣṭhā vacanāt  yathā yājñavalkyasya pratijñā tathā eva pṛcchati kindevataḥ tvam asyām diśi asi iti sarvatra hi vede yām yām devatā dvapāḥ te iha eva tad bhūtaḥ tām tām pratipadyata iti  tathā ca vakṣyati adevaḥ  bhūtvā devān apyeti iti asyām prācyām kā devatā diś ātmanaḥ tava adhiṣṭhātrī kayā devatayā tvam prāpī diś rūpeṇa sampanna iti arthaḥ itara āha āditya devata iti prācyām diśi mama ādityaḥ  devatā saḥ  aham āditya devataḥ sa devā iti etad uktam sa pratiṣṭhā iti tu vaktavyam iti āha sa ādityaḥ kasmin pratiṣṭhita iti cakṣuṣi iti adhyātmataḥ cakṣuṣa ādityaḥ  niṣpanna iti hi mantra brāhmaṇa vādāḥ cakṣoḥ sūryaḥ  ajāyata cakṣuṣa ādityaḥ ityādayaḥ kāryam hi kāraṇe pratiṣṭhitam bhavati kasmin nu cakṣuḥ pratiṣṭhitam iti rūpeṣu iti   rūpa grahaṇāya hi rūpa ātmakam cakṣu rūpeṇa prayuktam  yaiḥ hi rūpaiḥ prayuktam taiḥ ātma grahaṇāya ārabdham cakṣuḥ saha prācyā diśā saha tad sthaiḥ sarvai rūpeṣu pratiṣṭhitam cakṣuṣā saha prācī diś  sarve rūpa bhūtā tāni ca kasmin nu rūpāṇi pratiṣṭhitāni iti hṛdaya iti ha uvāca hṛdaya ārabdhāni rūpāṇi rūpa ākāreṇa hi hṛdayam pariṇatam yasmāt  hṛdayena hi rūpāṇi sarvaḥ  lokaḥ  jānāti hṛdayam iti buddhi manasaḥ  ekīkṛtya nirdeśaḥ tasmāt  hṛdaye hi eva rūpāṇi pratiṣṭhitāni hṛdayena hi smaraṇam bhavati rūpāṇām vāsanā ātmanām tasmāt  hṛdaye rūpāṇi pratiṣṭhitāni iti arthaḥ evam eva etad  yājñavalkya kindevataḥ  asyām dakṣiṇāyām diśi asi iti pūrvavat  dakṣiṇāyām diśi kā devatā tatra yama devata iti yamaḥ  devatā mama dakṣiṇa ādiś bhūtasya sa yamaḥ kasmin pratiṣṭhita iti yajña iti yajñe kāraṇe pratiṣṭhitaḥ  yamaḥ saha diśā katham punar yajñasya kāryam yamaḥ iti ucyate ṛtvigbhiḥ niṣpāditaḥ  yajñaḥ  dakṣiṇayā yajamānaḥ tebhyaḥ  yajñam niṣkrīya tena yajñena dakṣiṇām diśam saha yamena abhijayati tena yajñe yamaḥ kāryatvāt  pratiṣṭhitaḥ saha dakṣiṇayā diśā kasmin nu yajñaḥ pratiṣṭhita iti dakṣiṇāyām iti dakṣiṇayā sa na ṣkrīyate tena dakṣiṇā kāryam yajñaḥ kasmin nu dakṣiṇā pratiṣṭhitā iti śraddhāyām iti śraddhā nāma ditsu tvam āstikya buddhi bhakti sahitā katham tasyām pratiṣṭhitā dakṣiṇā yasmāt  yadā hi eva śraddhatte atha dakṣiṇām dadāti na aśraddadhat  dakṣiṇām dadāti tasmāt śraddhāyām hi eva dakṣiṇā pratiṣṭhitā iti kasmin nu śraddhā pratiṣṭhitā iti hṛdaya iti ha uvāca hṛdayasya hi vṛttiḥ śraddhā yasmāt  hṛdayena hi śraddhām jānāti vṛttiḥ ca vṛttimati pratiṣṭhitā bhavati tasmāt  hṛdaye hi eva śraddhā pratiṣṭhitā bhavati iti evam eva etad  yājñavalkya kinga devataḥ  asyām pratīcyām diśi asi iti tasyām varuṇaḥ  adhidevatā mama sa varuṇaḥ kasmin pratiṣṭhita iti apsu iti apām hi varuṇaḥ kāryam śraddhā vā āpaḥ śraddhātaḥ varuṇam asṛjata iti śruteḥ kasmin  vāpaḥ pratiṣṭhitā iti retasi iti retasaḥ  hi āpaḥ sṛṣṭāḥ iti śruteḥ kasminni retaḥ pratiṣṭhitam iti hṛdaya iti yasmāt  hṛdayasya kāryam retaḥ kāmaḥ  hṛdayasya vṛttiḥ kāminaḥ  hi hṛdayāt retaḥ  adhiskandati tasmāt api pratirūpam anurūpam putram jātam āhuḥ lokikāḥ asya pituḥ hṛdaya ādiva ayam putraḥ suptaḥ  viniḥsṛtaḥ hṛdayāt iva nirmitaḥ  yathā suvarṇena nirmitaḥ kuṇḍalaḥ tasmāt  hṛdaye hi eva retaḥ pratiṣṭhitam bhavati iti evam eva etad  yājñavalkya kindevataḥ  asyām udīcyām diśi asi iti soma devata iti soma iti latām somam devatām ca ekīkṛtya nirdeśaḥ sa somaḥ kasmin pratiṣṭhita iti dīkṣāyām iti dīkṣitaḥ  hi yajamānaḥ somam krīṇāti krītena somena iṣṭvā jñānavān uttarām diśam pratipadyate soma devatā adhiṣṭhitām saumyām kasmin nu dīkṣā pratiṣṭhitā iti satya iti katham yasmāt  satye dīkṣā pratiṣṭhitā tasmāt api dīkṣitam āhuḥ satyam vada iti  kāraṇa bhreṣaḥ  kārya bhreṣaḥ  mā bhūt iti  satye hi eva dīkṣā pratiṣṭhitam iti hṛdaya iti ha uvāca  hṛdayena hi satyam jānāti tasmāt  hṛdaye hi eva satyam pratiṣṭhitam bhavati iti evam eva etad  yājñavalkya kindevataḥ  asyām diśi asi iti meroḥ samantatas  vasatām avyabhicārāt ūrdhvā diś  dhruvā iti ucyate agni devata iti ūrdhvāyām hi prakāśa bhūyaḥ tvam prakāśaḥ ca agniḥ saḥ  agniḥ kasmin pratiṣṭhita iti vāci iti kasminni vāc  pratiṣṭhitā iti hṛdaya iti tatra yājñavalkyaḥ sarvāsu dikṣu vipasṛtena hṛdayena sarvām diśa ātma tvena abhisampannaḥ sa devāḥ sa pratiṣṭhitā diśa ātma bhūtāḥ tasya nāma rūpa karma ātma bhūtasya yājñavalkyasya yad  rūpam tad  prācyā diśā saha hṛdaya bhūtam yājñavalkyasya yad  kevalam karma putra utpādana lakṣaṇam ca yāna sahitam ca sahaphena adhiṣṭhātrībhiḥ ca devatābhiḥ dakṣiṇā pratīci udīcyaḥ karma phala ātmikā hṛdayam eva āpannāḥ tasya dhruvayā diśā saha nāma sarvam vāc dvāreṇa hṛdayam eva āpannam etāvat hi idam sarvam yad uta rūpam vā karma vā nāma vā iti tad  sarvam hṛdayam eva tad  sarva ātmakam hṛdayam pṛcchyate kasmin nu hṛdayam pratiṣṭhitam iti ahallikā iti ha uvāca yājñavalkyaḥ nāma antareṇa sambodhanam kṛtavān yatra yasmin kāle etad  hṛdayam ātmā asya asmad asmad taḥ  vartata iti manyāsai manyase yad hi yadi hi etad  hṛdayam anyatra asmat syāt  bhavet  śvānau vā enat śarīram tadā adyuḥ vayāṃsi vā pakṣiṇaḥ  vā enad vimathnīran viloḍayeyuḥ vikarperan  iti tasmāt mayi śarīre hṛdayam pratiṣṭhitam iti arthaḥ śarīrasya api nāma rūpa karma ātmaka tvāt hṛdaye pratiṣṭhita tvam hṛdaya śarīrasya ūrevam anyenya pratiṣṭhā uktā kārya karaṇayoḥ atas tvām pṛcchāmi kasmin nu tvam ca śarīram ātmā ca tava hṛdayam pratiṣṭhitau stha iti prāṇa iti deha ātmānau prāṇe pratiṣṭhitau syātām prāṇa vṛttau kasmin nu prāṇāḥ pratiṣṭhita iti apāna iti sā api prāṇa vṛttiḥ prāk eva preyāt  apāna vṛttyā ced na nigṛhyeta kasmin  vapānaḥ pratiṣṭhita iti vyāna iti sā api apāna vṛttiḥ adha eva yāyāt  prāṇa vṛttiḥ ca prāk eva madhyasthayā ced vyāna vṛttyā na nigṛhyeta kasmin nu vyānaḥ pratiṣṭhita iti udāna iti sarvāḥ tisraḥ  api vṛttaya udāne kīla sthānīye ced na niruddhā viṣvak eveyuḥ kasminnūdānaḥ pratiṣṭhita iti samāna  iti samāna pratiṣṭhā hi etāḥ sarvā vṛttayaḥ etad uktam bhavati śarīra hṛdaya vāyavaḥ  anyonya pratiṣṭhāḥ saṅghātena niṣatā vartante vijñāna maya artha prayuktā iti sarvam etad  yena niyatam yasmin pratiṣṭhitam ākāśa antamotam ca protam ca tasya nirupādhikasya sākṣāt aparokṣāt  brahmaṇaḥ  nirdeśaḥ katavya iti ayam ārambhaḥ sa eṣaḥ sayaḥ na itinā iti iti nirdiṣṭaḥ  madhu kāṇḍe eṣa saḥ saḥ  ayam ātma agṛhya u na gṛhyaḥ katham yasmāt  sarva kārya dharma atītaḥ tasmāt agṛhyaḥ kutas  yasmāt na hi gṛhyate yad hi karaṇa gocaram vyākṛtam vastu tad  grahaṇa gocaram idam tu tad viparītam ātma tattvam tathā aśīryaḥ yad dhi mūrtam saṃhatam śarīra ādi tad śīryate ayam tu tad viparītaḥ  atas  na hi śīryate tathā āsaṅgaḥ  mūrtaḥ mūrta antareṇa sambadhyamānaḥ sajyate ayam ca tad viparītaḥ  atas  na hi sajyate tathā asitaḥ  abaddhaḥ yad hi mūrta tad  vadhyate ayam tu tad viparīta tvāt abaddha tvāt na vyathate atas  na riṣyati grahaṇa viśaraṇa sambandha kārya dharma rahita tvāt na riṣyati na hiṃsām āpadyate na vinaśyati iti arthaḥ kramam atikramya aupaniṣadasya puruṣasya ākhyāyikātas  apasṛtya śrutyā svena rūpeṇa tvarayā nirdeśaḥ kṛtaḥ tatas  punar ākhyāyikām eva aśriti āha etāni yāni uktāni aṣṭau  āyata nāni apṛthivī eva yasya āyatanam aiti evamādīni aṣṭau lokā agni loka ādayaḥ aṣṭau devāḥ amṛtam iti ha uvāca iti evamādayaḥ aṣṭau puruṣāḥ śarīraḥ puruṣaḥ ityādayaḥ sa yaḥ kaścid  tān puruṣān śārīra prabhṛtīn niruhya niścayena ūhya garmayitvā aṣṭa catuṣka bhedena loka sthitim upapādyaḥ punar  prācī diś ādi dvāreṇa pratyuhya upasaṃhṛtya sva ātmani hṛdaye atyakrāmat atikrāntavān upādhi dharma hṛdaya ādi ātma tvam  svena eva ātmanā vyavasthitaḥ  ya aupaniṣadaḥ puruṣaḥ  aśanāya ādi varjitaḥ upaniṣatsu eva vijñeyaḥ  na anya pramāṇa gamyaḥ tam tvā tvām vidyā abhimāninam puruṣam pṛcchāmi tam ced  yadi me na vivakṣyasi vispaṣṭam na kathayiṣyasi mūrdhā te vipatiṣyati iti āha yājñavalkyaḥ tam tu aupaniṣadam puruṣam śākalyaḥ  na mene ha na vijñātavān kila tasya ha mūrdhā vipapāta vipatitaḥ samāpta ākhyāyakā śrutevacanam tam ha na mena ityādi kim ca api hāsya parimoṣiṇaḥ taskarā asthīni api saṃskāra artha  śiṣyenīyamānāni gṛhān pratyapajahaḥ apahratavantaḥ kinnimittam anyat  dhanam nīyamānam manyamānāḥ pūrva vṛttā hi ākhyāyikā iha sūcitā aṣṭādhyāya kila śākalyena yājñavalkyasya samāna anta eva kila saṃvādaḥ  nivṛttaḥ tatra yājñavalkyena śāpaḥ  dattaḥ pure atithye mariṣyasi na te asthīni ca na gṛhān prāpsyanti iti sa ha tathā eva mamāra tasya hāpi anvaḥ manyamānāḥ parimoṣiṇaḥ  athīnyapajahaḥ  tasmāt na upavādī syāt uta hi evaṃvid  paraḥ  bhavati iti sā epā ākhyāyikā ācāra artha sūcitā vidyā stutaye ca iha yasya na iti na iti iti anya pratiṣedha dvāreṇa brahmaṇaḥ  nirdeśaḥ kṛtaḥ tasya vidhi mukhena katham nirdeśaḥ kartavyaḥ iti punar ākhyāyikām eva āśritya āha mūlam ca jagataḥ  vaktavyam iti ākhyāyikā sambandhaḥ tu avrahya vidaḥ  brāhmaṇān jitvā gaḥ dhanam irtavyam iti nyāyam matvā āha atha ha uvāca atha anantaram tūṣṇīmbhūteṣu brāhmaṇeṣu ha uvāca he brāhemaṇā bhagavanta iti evam sambodhya yaḥ  vaḥ  yuṣmākam madhye kāmayate icchati yājñavalkyam pṛcchāmi iti sa mā mām āgatya pṛcchat  sarve vā mā pṛcchata sarve vā yūyam mā mām pṛcchata yaḥ  vaḥ kāmayate yājñavalkyaḥ  mām pṛcchatu iti tam vaḥ pṛcchami  sarvān vā vaḥ  yuṣmān aham pṛcchāmi te ha brāhmaṇā na dadhṛṣuḥ te brāhmaṇā evam uktā api na pragalbhāḥ saṃvṛttāḥ kiñcid api pratyuttaram vaktum     teṣu apragalbha bhūteṣu brāhmaṇeṣu tān ha etaiḥ vakṣyamāṇaiḥ ślokaiḥ papraccha pṛṣṭavān yathā loke vṛkṣaḥ  vanaspatiḥ vṛkṣasya viśeṣaṇam vanaspatiḥ iti tathā eva puruṣaḥ  amṛpā amṛpā satyam etad  tasya lomā ni tasya puruṣasya lomāni itarasya vanaspateḥ parṇā ni tvagasya utpāṭikā vahiḥ tvac asya puruṣasya itarasya utpāṭikā vanaspateḥ     tvaca eva sakāśāt asya puruṣasya rudhiram prasyandi vanaspateḥ atvaca utpaṭaḥ tvaca eva utsphuṭati yasmāt  evam sarvam samānam eva vanaspateḥ puruṣasya ca tasmāt  ātṛṇṇāt  hisitāt  prati tad  rudhiram nirgacchati vṛkṣa ādivāhatācchinnād rasaḥ     evam māṃsāni asya puruṣasya vanaspatesyāni śakarāṇi śakalāni iti arthaḥ kināṭam vṛkṣasya kināṭam nāma śakalebhyaḥ  abhyantaram valkala rūpam kāṣṭha saṃlagnam tad  snāva puruṣasya tad  sthiram tad ca kināṭam snāvavat  dṛḍham hi tad asthīni puruṣasya snāvnaḥ  antarataḥ asthīni bhavanti  tathā kināṭasya abhyantaratas  dāruṇi kāṣṭhā ni majjā majjā iva vanaspateḥ puruṣasya ca majjopamā kṛtā majjāyāḥ  upamā majja upamā na anyaḥ  viśeṣaḥ  asti iti arthaḥ yathā vanaspateḥ majjā tathā puruṣasya yathā puruṣasya tathā vanaspateḥ     yad  yadi vṛkṣaḥ  vṛkṇaḥ chinnaḥ  rohati punar  punar  prarohati prādurbhavati mūlāt  punarnavataraḥ pūrvasmāt abhinavataraḥ yad etasmāt  viśeṇāt  prāk  vanaspateḥ puruṣasya ca sarvam sāmānyam avagatam  ayam tu vanaspatau viśeṣaḥ  dṛśyate yad chinnasyaprarohaṇam na tu puruṣe mṛtyunā vṛkṇe punar  prarohaṇam dṛśyate  bhavitavyam ca kutaścid prarohaṇena tasmāt vaḥ pṛcchāmi martyaḥ  manuṣyaḥ svid mṛtyunā vṛkṇaḥ kasmāt mūlāt  prarohati mṛtasya puruṣasya kutas  prarohaṇam iti arthaḥ     yadi ced evamvat atha retamaḥ prarohati iti mā vocata mā evam vaṣatum arhatha  kasmāt  yasmāt jīvataḥ puruṣāt tad  retaḥ prajāyate na mṛtāt  api ca dhānāruhaḥ dhānā bījam bījaruhaḥ  pi vṛkṣaḥ  bhavati na kevalam kāṇḍaraha eva  iva śabdaḥ  anarthakaḥ vai vṛkṣaḥ  ajjasā sākṣāt  pretya mṛtvā asambhavaḥ  dhānātaḥ  api pretya sambhavaḥ  bhavet ajjasā punar vanaspateḥ     yad  yadi saha mūlena dhānyā vā āvṛheyuḥ udyat chepa ruyeyuḥ vṛkṣam na punar ā abhavet  punar āgatya na bhavet  tasmāt  vaḥ pṛcchāmi sarvasya eva jagataḥ  mūlam sartyaḥ svid mṛtyunā vṛkṇaḥ kasmāt mūlāt  prarohati     jāta eva iti manyadhvam yadi kim anna praṣṭavyam iti aniṣyamāṇasya hi sambhavaḥ praṣṭavyaḥ na jātasya ayam tu jāta eva āta upasmin viṣaye praśna eva na upa dyata iti ced  na kim tarhi mṛtaḥ punar api jāyata eva anyathā akṛta abhyāgama kṛta nāśa prasaṅga at atas  vaḥ pṛcchāmi kaḥ  nu enam mṛtam punar janayet  tatra vijajñuḥ brāhmaṇāḥ yatas  mṛtaḥ punar  prarohati jagataḥ  mūlam na vijñātam brāhmaṇaiḥ atas brahmiṣṭha tvāt  hratā gāvaḥ yājñavalkyena jitā brāhmaṇāḥ samāptā ākhyāyikā yad jagataḥ  mūlam yena ca śabdena sākṣāt  vyapadiśyate brahma yad  yājñavalkyaḥ  brāhmaṇān pṛṣṭavān  tad  svena rūpeṇa śrutiḥ asi abhyam āha vijñānam vijñaptiḥ vijñānam tad ca ānandam na viṣaya vijñānavat  duḥkha anuvidvam kim tarhi prasannam śivam atulam anāya asaṃnitya tṛptame karasamiti arthaḥ kim tad  brahma umaya viśeṇavat  rātiḥ rāteḥ paṣṭha yatha prathamā dhanasya iti arthaḥ dhanasya dātuḥ karma kṛtaḥ  yajamānasya parāyaṇam parā gatiḥ karma phalasya pradātṛ kiñca vyutthāya eṣaṇābhyasyasmin  eva brahmāṇi tiṣṭhati akarma kṛt tad  brahma vetti iti tad vicca tasya tiṣṭhamānasya ca tad vidaḥ brahma vida iti arthaḥ parāyaṇam iti atra idam vicāryate ānanda śabdaḥ  loke sukha vācī prasidvaḥ atra ca brahmaṇaḥ  viśeṣaṇa tvena ānanda śabdaḥ śrūyate ānandam brahma iti śruti antare ca ānandaḥ  brahma iti vyajānāt  ānandam brahmaṇaḥ  vidvān yad eṣa ākāśa ānandaḥ  na syāta yaḥ  vai bhūmā tad  sukham iti ca  eṣa parama  ānandaḥ iti evamādyāḥ saṃvedye ca sukhe ānanda śabdaḥ prasidvaḥ brahmānandaḥ ca yadi saṃvedyaḥ syāt  yuktā ete brahmaṇi ānanda śabdāḥ nanu ca śruti prāmāṇyāt  saṃvedya ānanda svarūpam eva brahma kim tatra vicāryam iti na virudva śruti vākya darśanāt satyam ānanda śabdaḥ  brahmaṇi śrūyate vijñāna pratiṣedhaḥ ca ekatve yatra tu asya sarvam ātmā eva abhūt tad kena kam paśyet tad kena kam vijānīyāt  yatra na anyat  paśyati na anyat śṛṇoti na anyat vijānāti sa bhūmā prājñena ātmanā sampariṣvaktaḥ  na bāhyam kiñcana veda ityādi virudva śruti vākya darśanāt tena kartavyaḥ  vicāraḥ tasmāt  yuktam veda vāki artha nirṇayāya vicārayitum mokṣa vādi vipratipatteḥ ca sāṃkhyā vaiśeṣikāḥ ca mokṣa vādinaḥ  na asti mokṣe sukham saṃvedyam iti evam vipratipannāḥ anye nigtiśayam sukham sva saṃvadya miti kim tāvat  yuktam ānanda ādi śravaṇāt jakṣata krīḍan ramamāṇaḥ asayāda pitṛ loka kāmaḥ  bhavata yaḥ sarvajñaḥ sarva vid  sarvān kāmān samaśnute ityādi śrutibhyaḥ  mokṣe sukham saṃvedyam iti nanu eka tve kāraka vimāgamāvād vijñāna anupapattiḥ kriyāyāḥ ca ane kakārakrasādhyā tvāt  vijñānasya ca kriyā tvāt  na eṣa doṣaḥ  śabda prāmāṇyāt  bhavet  vijñānam ānanda viṣaye  vijñānam ānandam ityādīni ānanda svarūpasya asaṃvedya tve anupapannāni vacanāni iti avocāma nanu vacanena api agneḥ śaityam udakasya cauṣbhyam na kriyate eva jñāpaka tvāt  vacanānām na ca deśa antare agniḥ śīta iti śakyate jñāpayitum  agamye vā deśa antare uṣṇam udakam iti na pratyak ātmani ānanda vijñāna darśana at na avijñānam ānandam aitvevam ādīnām vacanānām śītaḥ  agniḥ ityādi vākyavat  pratyakṣa ādi virudva artha pratipādaka tvām anubhūyate tu avirudva artha tā  sukhya ham iti sukha ātmakam ātmānam svayam eva vedayate  tasmāt  sutarām pratyakṣā virudvārtha tā  tasmāt ānandam brahma vijñāna ātmakam sat  svayam eva vedayate tathā ānanda pratipādikāḥ śrutayaḥ samañjasāḥ syuḥ ajakṣat krīḍan ramamāṇaḥ iti evamādyāḥ pūrva uktāḥ na kārya karaṇa abhāve anupapatteḥ vijñānasya śarīra viyogaḥ  hi mokṣa ātyantikaḥ  śarīra bhāve ca karaṇa anupapattiḥ āśraya abhāva at tatas ca vijñāna anupattiḥ ākārya karaṇa tvāt deha dyabhāve ca vijñāna utpattau sarveṣām kārya karaṇa upādāna ānarthakya prasaṅgaḥ ekatva virodhāt ca param ced  brahma ānanda ātmakam ātmānam nitya vijñāna tvāt nityam eva vijānīyāt  tad na saṃsāri api saṃsāra vinirmuktaḥ svābhāvyam pratipadyeta  jalāśaya iva udaka añjaliḥ kṣiptaḥ  na pṛthaktvena vyavatiṣṭhate ānanda ātmaka brahma vijñānāya tadā mukta ānanda ātmakam ātmānam vedayate iti etad anarthakam vākyam atha brahma ānandam anyāḥ san muktaḥ  vedayate pratyak ātmānam ca aham asmi ānanda svarūpa iti tadā ekatva virodhaḥ tathā ca sati sarva śruti virodhaḥ tṛtīyā ca kalpanā na upapadyate kiñca anyat brahmaṇaḥ ca nirantara ātma ānanda vijñāne vijñāna avijñāna kalpanā narthakyam  nirantaram ced ātmā ānanda viṣayam brahmaṇaḥ  vijñānam tad eva tasya svabhāva iti ātma ānandam vijānāti iti kalpanā anupapanna tad vijñāna prasaṅge hi kalpanāyāḥ  arthavat tvam yathā ātmānam param ca vetti iti na hi iṣu ādya āsakta manasaḥ  nairantaryeṇa ūṣu jñāna ajñāna kalpanāyā arthavat tvam atha vicchinnam ātma ānandam vijānāti vijñānasya ātma vijñāna  chidre anya viṣayatva prasaṅgaḥ ātma naśya vikriyāvat tvam tatas ca anityatva prasaṅgaḥ tasmāt  vijñānam ānandam iti svarūpa anvākhyāna para eva śrutiḥ na ātma ānanda saṃvedyatva artha ajakṣat  krīḍan aiti ādi śruti virodhaḥ  asaṃvedyatva iti ced   na  sarva ātmā ekatve yathā prāpta anuvādi tvāt muktasya sarva ātma bhāve sati yatra kvacid  yogiṣu deveṣu vā jakṣaṇa ādi prāptam tad  yathāprāptam eva anūdyate tad tasya eva sarva ātma bhāvāt iti sarva ātma bhāva mokṣa stutaye yathā prāpta anuvadi tve duḥkhi tvam api iti ced  yogi ādiṣu yathāprāpta jakṣaṇa ādivat  sthāvara ādiṣu yathāprāpta duḥkhi tvam api iti ced   na nāma rūpa kṛta kārya karaṇa upādhi samparka janita bhrānti adhyāropita tvāt sukhitva duḥkhi tvā ādi viśeṣasya iti parihratam etad  sarvam virudva śrutīnām ca viṣayam avocāma tasmāt  eṣaḥ  asya parama  ānandaḥ itivat  sarvāṣya ānanda vākyāni draṣṭavyāni iti tṛtīyā adhyāye navamam śākalya brāhmaṇam janakaḥ  ha vaideha āsān cakre asya sambandhaḥ śarīra ādyān aṣṭau puruṣān niruhya pratyuhya punar hṛdaye diś bhedanena ca punar  pañcadhā vyāhya hṛdaye pratyūhya hṛdayam śarīram ca punar anyonya pratiṣṭham prāṇa ādi paḍhta vṛtya ātmake samāna ākhye jagat ātmanu sūtra upasaṃhṛtya jagat ātmani sūtra upasaṃhṛtya jagat ātma anaṃśarīra hṛdaya sūtra avastham atikrāntavān ya aupaniṣadaḥ puruṣaḥ  na iti na iti iti vyapadiṣṭaḥ sa sa akṣāñcopādāna kāraṇa svarūpeṇa ca nirdiṣṭaḥ avijñānam ānandam iti tasya eva vāc ādi devatā dvāreṇa punar adhigamaḥ kartavya iti adhigamana upāya antara arthaḥ  ayam ārambhaḥ  brāhmaṇa dvayasya ākhyāyikā tu ācāra pradarśana arthā janakaḥ  ha vaideha āsān cakre āsanam kṛtavān āsthāyikām dattavān iti arthaḥ darśana kāmebhyaḥ  rājñaḥ atha ha tasmin  avasare yājñavalkyaḥ āvavrāja āgatavān ātmanaḥ  yogakṣema artham rājñaḥ  vā vivadiṣām dṛṣṭvā anugraha artham tam āgatam yajñavalkyam yathāvat  pūjām kṛtvā uvāca ha uktavān janakaḥ he yājñavalkya kimartham acārīḥ āgataḥ  asi kim paśūn icchan punar api āhosvit aṇu antān sūkṣma antān sūkṣma vastu nirṇaya antān praśnān mattaḥ śrotum icchan  iti ubhayam eva paśūn praśnān  ca he samrāj  samrāj iti vājapeya yājinaḥ  liṅgam   yaḥ ca ājñayā rājyam praśāsti samrāj    tasyāḥ  mantraṇam he samrāj iti   samastasya vā bhāratasya varṣasya rājā kintu yad te tubhyam kaścid abravīt ācāryaḥ  aneka ācāryaḥ  aneka ācārya sevī hi bhavān  tad śṛṇavāma iti itara āha abravadīt uktavān me mama āacāryaḥ  jitvā nāmataḥ śilinasya apatyam śaili nirvāgvai brahma iti vāgdevatā brahma iti āhetapaḥ  yathā mātṛmān mātā yasya vidyate putrasya samyak anuśāstri anuśāsana kartrī sa mātṛmān ata ūrdhvam pitā yasya anuśāstā sa pitṛmān upanayanāt ūrdhvam ā samāvartanāt ācāryaḥ  yasya anuśāstā sa ācāryavān evam śuddhi traya hetu saṃyuktaḥ sa sādhāda ācāryaḥ svayam na kadācid apu prāmāṇāt vyabhicarati sa yathā brūyāt śiṣyāya tathā asau jitvā śaili niruktavān vāc vai brahma iti avadataḥ  hi kim syāt iti na hi mūkasya iha artham amutra artham vā kiñcana syāt  kintu abravīt uktavāḥ te tubhyam tasya brahmaṇa āyatanam pratiṣṭhām ca āyatanam nāma śarīram pratiṣṭhā triṣu api kāleṣu ya āśrayaḥ āha itaraḥ  na me abravīt iti itara āha yadi evam ekapād vā etad ekaḥ pādaḥ  yasya brahmaṇaḥ tad idam ekapād brahma tribhiḥ pādaiḥ śūnyam upāsyamānam api na phalāya bhavati iti arthaḥ yadi evam sa tvam vidvān sannaḥ asmabhyam brūhi he yājñavalkya iti sa cā aha vāc evā ayatanam vāgdevasya brahmaṇaḥ  vāc eva karaṇam āyatanam śarīram ākāśaḥ  avyākṛta ākhyaḥ pratiṣṭhā utpatti sthiti laya kāleṣu prajñā iti enat upāsīta prajñā itīyam upaniṣad brahmaṇaḥ caturthaḥ pādaḥ prajñā iti kṛtvā enat brahma upāsīta kā prajña tā yājñavalkya ki svayam eva prajñā uta prajñā nimittam yathā ayatana pratiṣṭhe brahmaṇaḥ  vyatirikte tadvat kim na katha tarhi vāc eva samrāj iti ha uvāca vāc eva prajñā iti ha uvāca uktavān na vyatiriktā prajñāti katham punar vāc eva prajñā iti ucyate vācā vai samrāj bandhuḥ prajñāyate asmākam bandhuḥ iti ukte prajñāyakate bandhuḥ tathā rgvaidādi iṣṭam yāga nimitta dharma jātam hutam homa nimittam ca āśitamanna dā ni m ittam pāyitam pāna dāna nimitta mayam ca loka idam ca janma paraḥ ca lokaḥ pratipattavyam ca janma sarvāṇi ca bhūtāni vācā eva samrāj prajñāyante atas  vāc vaisamrāj paramam brahma nānam yathā ukta brahma vidam vāc jahāti sarvāṇi enam bhūtāni abhikṣaranti bali dāna ādibhiḥ iha devaḥ  bhūtvā punar  śarīra pāta uttara kālam devān apyeti apigacchati ya evam vidvān etad upāste vidyā niṣkriya artham hasti tulya ṛṣabhaḥ  hasti ṛṣabhaḥ  yasmin gaḥ sahasretat hastṛṣabham sahasram dadāmi iti ha uvāca janakaḥ  vaidehaḥ sa ha uvāca yājñavalkyaḥ ananuśiṣya śiṣyam kṛtārtham akṛtvā śiṣyāt dhanam na hareta iti me mama pitā amanyata mama api ayam eva abhiprāyaḥ yad eva te kaścid abravīt udaṅkaḥ  nāmataḥ śulbasya apatyam śaulbasya apatyam śaulbāyanaḥ  abravīt prāṇaḥ  vai brahma iti prāṇaḥ  vāyuḥ devatā pūrvavat  prāṇa evā ayanam ākāśaḥ pratiṣṭhā upaniṣad priyam iti enat upāsīta katham punar  priya tvam prāṇasya vai he samrāj kāmāya prāṇasya arthāya aya ājyam yājayati patita ādikam api apratigṛhyasya api ugrādeḥ pratigṛhṇāti api tatra tasyām diśi vadha nimittam āśaṅkam vadha āśaṅkā iti arthaḥ  yām diśam eti taskara ādi ākīrṇām ca tasyām diśi ba dha aśahkā tad ca etad sarvam prāṇasya priya tve bhavati prāṇasya eva samrāj kāmāya tasmāt prāṇaḥ  vai samrāj paramam brahma na enam prāṇaḥ  jahāti samānam anyat  yad eva te kaścid barkuḥ iti nāmataḥ  vṛṣṇasya apatyam vārṣṇaḥ cakṣuḥ vai brahma ityādityaḥ  devatā cakṣuṣi upaniṣad satyam yasmāt śrotreṇa śrutam anṛtam api syāt na tu cakṣuṣā dṛṣṭam tasmāt vai samrāj paśyantam āhuḥ adrākṣīḥ tvam hastinam iti sa ced adrākṣam iti āha tad satyam eva bhavati yaḥ tu anyau brūyat aham aśrauṣam iti tad vyabhicarati yad tu cakṣuṣā dṛṣṭam tad avyabhicāri tvāt satyam eva bhavati yad eva te gardabhī vipīta iti nāmataḥ  bhāradvājaḥ  gotrataḥ śrotram vai brahma iti śrotre diś devatā ananta iti enat upāsīta kā ananta tā śrotrasya diśa eva śrotrasyā anantyam yasmāt tasmāt vai samrāj prācīm udīcām vā yām kāñcid api diśam gacchati na eva asyā antaṅgacchati kañcid apu atas  anantā hi diśaḥ diśaḥ  vai samrāj śrotram tasmāt diś ān antyam eva śrotrasya ṣa anantyam satyakāma iti nāmataḥ  jabālāyāḥ  apatyam jābālaḥ candramā manasi devatā ānanda iti upaniṣati yasmāt mana evā anandaḥ tasmāt manasā vai samrāṭa striyam abhikāmayamānaḥ  abhihāryate prārthayata iti arthaḥ tasmāt yām striyam abhikāmayamānaḥ  abhihāryate tasyām pratirūpaḥ  anurūpaḥ putraḥ  jāyate sa ānanda hetuḥ sa yena manasā nirvartyate tad mana ānandaḥ vidagdhaḥ śākalyaḥ  hṛdayam vai brahma iti hṛdayam vai samrāj sarveṣām bhūtānām āyatanam nāma rūpa karma ātmakāni hi bhūtāni hṛdaya āśrayāṇi iti avocāma śākalya bāhmaṇe hṛdaya pratiṣṭhā anu ca iti tasmāt vadhṛtaye hi eva samrāj sravāṇi bhūtāni pratiṣṭhitāni bhavanti tasmāt hṛdayam sthitiḥ iti upāsīta hṛdaye ca prajāpatiḥ devatā janakaḥ  ha vaidehaḥ yasmāt sa viśeṣaṇāni sarvāṇi brahmāṇi jānāti yājñavalkyaḥ tasmāt ācāryaka tvam hitvā janakaḥ kūrcāt āsana viśeṣāt utthāya upa samīpam avasarpa nyādayoḥ nipatan  iti arthaḥ uvāca uktavān namaḥ te tubhyam astu he yājñavalkya anu mā śādhi anuśādhi mām iti arthaḥ iti śabdaḥ  vākya parisamāpti arthaḥ sa ha uvāca yājñavalkyaḥ  yathā vai loke he samrāj mahāntam dīrgham adhvānam eṣyan gamiṣyan ratham vā sothalena gamiṣyat   āvam vā jalena gamiṣyan samādadīta evam eva etāni brahmāṇi etābhiḥ upaniṣadbhiḥ yuktāni upāsīnaḥ samāhita tmāsi atyantam etābhiḥ upaniṣadbhiḥ saṃyukta ātmā asi na kevalam upaniṣad samāhita evam vṛndārakaḥ pūjyaḥ cā aḍhyaḥ ca īśvaraḥ  na daridra iti arthaḥ adhīta vedaḥ  adhītaḥ  vedaḥ  yena sa tvam adhīta veda uktāḥ ca upaniṣada ācāryaiḥ tubhyam sa tu am ukta upaniṣad ka evam sarva vibhūtati saṃpannaḥ  api sanbhayaya madhyaḥ cha eva paramāt jñānena vinākṛta artha  eva tāvat iti arthaḥ yāvat param brahma na vetsi itas  asmāt deha ādi mucyamāna etābhiḥ toratha sthānīyābhiḥ samāhitaḥ kva kasmin gamiṣyasi kim vastu prāpsyasi iti na aham tad vastu bhagavan pūjā vanveda jāne yatra gamiṣyāmi iti atha yadi evam na jānīṣe yatra gataḥ kṛtārthaḥ syā aham vai tubhyam tad vakṣyāmi yatra gamiṣyasi iti bravītu bhagavān iti yadi prasannaḥ  mām prati śṛṇu indhaḥ ha vai nāma indha iti evaṃnāmā yaḥ cakṣuḥ vai brahma iti purā ukta āditya antara gta puruṣaḥ sa eṣa yaḥ  ayam dakṣiṇe akṣat nakṣaṇi viśeṣeṇa vyavasthitaḥ sa ca satya nāmā tam vā etam puruṣam dīpti guṇa tvāt pratyakṣam nāma asya indha iti tam indham santam indra iti āca kṣateparokṣeṇa yasmāt parokṣa priyā iva hi devāḥ pratyakṣa dviṣaḥ pratyakṣa nāma grahaṇam dviṣanti eṣa tvam vaiśvānaram ātmānam saṃpannaḥ  asi atha etad vāme akṣaṇi puruṣa rūpam eṣa asya patnī yam tvam vaiśvānaram ātmānam saṃpannaḥ  asi tasya asya indrasya bhoktuḥ bhogyā eṣā patnī virāj annam bhogya tvāt eva tad etad annam cāttā ca ekam mithunam svapne kaḥ  asau ya eṣaḥ  antara hṛdaya ākāśaḥ  antar hṛdaye hṛdayasya māṃsa piṇḍasya madhye atha enayoḥ etad vakṣyamāṇam annam bhojyam sthiti hetuḥ kim tad  ya eṣe antar hṛdaye lohita piṇḍaḥ  lohita eva piṇḍa ākāra āpannā lohita piṇḍaḥ annam jagdham dvedhā pariṇamate yad sthūlam tad adhas  gacchati yad anyat tad punarā agninā pacyamānam dvedhā pariṇamate yaḥ  madhyamaḥ  rasaḥ sa lohitāt akrameṇa pāñcabhautikam piṇḍam śarīram upacinoti yaḥ  aṇiṣṭhaḥ  rasaḥ sa eṣa lohita piṇḍa indrasya liṅga ātmanaḥ  hṛdaye mithunībhūtasya yam taijasam ācakṣate sa tayoḥ indra indrāṇi oḥ hṛdaye mithunībhūtayoḥ sūkṣmāsu nāḍīṣu anupraviṣṭaḥ sthiti hetuḥ bhavati tad etad ucyate atha enayoḥ etad annam ityādi kiñca anyat atha enayoḥ etad pravāraṇam bhuktavatoḥ svapatoḥ ca prāvaraṇam bhavati loke tad sāmānyam hi kalpayati śrutiḥ ki tad iha prāvaraṇam yad etad antar hṛdaye jālakam iva aneka nāḍī chidra bahula tvāt jālakam iva atha enayoḥ eṣā sṛtiḥ mārgaḥ saṃcanarataḥ  anayā iti saṃcaraṇī svapnat jāgarita deśa āgamana mārgaḥ kā sā sṛtiḥ yā eṣā hṛdayāt ahṛdaya deśāt ūrdhva abhimukhī sati uccarati nāḍī tasyāḥ parimāṇam idam ucyate yathā loke keśaḥ sahasradhā bhinnaḥ atyanta sūkṣmaḥ  bhavati evam sūkṣmā asya dehasya saṃbandhinyaḥ  hitā nāma hitā iti evam khyātā nāḍyāḥ tāḥ ca antar hṛdaye māsaṃpiṇḍe pritiṣṭhitā bhavanti hṛdayāt viprarūḍhāḥ tāḥ sarvatra kadamba kesa pavat etābhiḥ nāḍobhiḥ atyanta sūkṣmābhiḥ etad annama asravat gacchat āsravati gacchati tad etad devatā śarīram anena annena dāma bhūtena upacīyamānam tiṣṭhati tasmāt yasmāt sthūlena annena upacitaḥ piṇḍa idam tu devatā śarīram liṅgam sūkṣmeṇa annena upacitam tiṣṭhati piṇḍa upacaya karam api annam praviviktam eva mūtra purīṣa ādi sthūlam apekṣya liṅga sthiti karam tu annam tatas  api sākṣmataram atas  pravivikta āhāraḥ piṇḍaḥ tasmāt pravivikta āhārāt api pravivikta āhāratara eṣa liṅga ātmā ivā eva bhavati asmāt śarīrāt śārīram eva śārīram tasmāt śārīrāt  ātmanaḥ  vaiśvānarāt taijasaḥ sūkṣmāt na upacitaḥ  bhavati sa eṣa hṛdaya bhūtaḥ taijasaḥ sūkṣma bhūtena prāṇena vidhriyamāṇaḥ prāṇa eva bhavati tasya asya viduṣaḥ krameṇa vaiśvānarāt taijasam prāptasya hṛdaya ātmānam āpannasya hṛdaya ātmanaḥ ca prāṇa ātmānam āpannasya prācī diś prāñcaḥ prāk gatāḥ prāṇāḥ tathā dakṣiṇā digdakṣiṇe prāṇāḥ sarvā diśaḥ sarve prāṇāḥ evam vidvān kreṇa sarva ātmakam prāṇam ātma tvena upagataḥ  bhavati tam sarva ātmānam pratyak ātmani upasaṃhṛtya draṣṭuḥ hi draṣṭu bhāvam na iti na iti iti ātmānam turīyam pratipadyate yam eṣa vidvān anena krameṇa pratipadyate sa eṣa na iti na iti ātmā ityādi na riṣyati iti antam vyākhyātam etad  abhayam vai janma maraṇa ādi nimitta bhaya śūnyam he janaka prāptaḥ  asi iti ha evam kila uvāca uktavān yājñavalkyaḥ tad etad uktam atha vai te aham tad vakṣyāmi yatra gamiṣyasi iti sa ha uvāca janakaḥ  vaidehaḥ  abhayam eva tvā tvām api gacchatāt gacchatu yaḥ tvam naḥ asmān he yājñavalkya bhagavān pūjau  anna bhayam brahma vedayase jñāpayasi prāpitavān upādhi kṛta ajñāna vyavadhāna apanayanena iti arthaḥ kim anyat aham vidyā niṣkriya artham prayacchāmi sākṣāt ātmānam eva dattavate atas  namaḥ te astu ime videhāḥ tava yatheṣṭam bhujyanta āmayam ca aham asmi dāsa bhāve sthitaḥ  yatheṣṭam mām rājyam ca pracati padyasva iti arthaḥ janakam ha vaideham yājñavalkyaḥ  jagāma iti asya abhisaṃbandhaḥ vijñāna maya ātmā sākṣāt aparokṣāt brahma sarva antaraḥ para eva na anyaḥ  atas  asti draṣṭā na anyat atas  asti draṣṭi tyādi śrutibhyaḥ sa eṣa iha praviṣṭaḥ  vadana ādi liṅgaḥ  asti vyatirikta iti madhu kāṇḍe ajāta śatru saṃvāde prāṇa ādi kartṛtva bhoktṛtva pratyākhyānena adhigataḥ  api sat punar  prāṇana ādi liṅgam upanyasya auṣasta praśne prāṇana ādi liṅgaḥ  yaḥ sāmānyena adhigataḥ prāṇena prāṇiti ityādinā dṛṣṭeḥ draṣṭa iti ādinālupta śakti svabhāvaḥ  adhigataḥ tasya ca para upādhi nimittaḥ saṃsāraḥ  yathā rajjūṣara śuktikā gagana ādiṣu sarpet akaraja malinatva ādi parādhi āropaṇa nimittam eva na svatas tathā nirupādhikaḥ  nirupākhyaḥ  na iti na iti iti vyapadeśyaḥ sākṣāt aparokṣāt sarva antara ātmā brahma akṣaram antaryāmī praśasta aupaniṣadaḥ puruṣaḥ  vijñānam ānandam brahma iti adhigatam tad eva punar indhasajñaḥ pravivikta āhāraḥ tatas  antar hṛdaye liṅga ātmā pravivikta āhārataraḥ tatas  pareṇa jagat ātmā prāṇa upādhiḥ tatas  api pravilāpya jagadātmānam upādhi bhūtam rajju ādau  iva sarpa ādikam vidyayā sa eṣa na iti na iti iti sākṣāt sarva antaram brahma adhigatam evam abhayam pariprāpitaḥ  janakaḥ  yājñavalkyenā agamataḥ saṃkṣepataḥ atra ca jāgrat svapna suṣupta turīyāṇi upani anya prasaṅgena indhaḥ pravivikta āhārataraḥ sarve prāṇāḥ sarve prāṇāḥ sa eṣa na iti na iti iti idānīm jāgrat svapnāt vāreṇa  mahatā tarkeṇa vistarataḥ  adhigamaḥ kartavyaḥ abhayam prāpayitavyam sadbhāvāḥ cā atmanaḥ  vipratipatti āśaṅkā nirākaraṇa dvāreṇa vyatirikta tvam śuddha tvam svayan jyotiṣṭvam alupta śakti svarūpa tvam niratiśaya ānanda svābhāvyam advaita tvam ca adhigantavyam iti idam ārabhyate ākhyāyayikā tu vidyā saṃpradāna grahaṇa vidhi prakāśana arthā vidyā stutaye ca viśeṣataḥ vara dāna ādi sūcanāt  janakam ha vaideham yājñavalkyaḥ  jagāma sa ca gacchan  evam mene cintitavān na vadiṣye kiñcid apu rājñe gamana prayojanam tu yogakṣema artham na vadiṣya iti evaṃsaṃkalpaḥ  api yājñavalkyaḥ  yad yad janakaḥ pṛṣṭavān  tad tad pratipede tatra kaḥ  hetuḥ saṃkalpitasya anyathā karaṇa iti atrā akhyāyikām ācaṣṭe pūrvatra kila janaka yājñavalkyoḥ saṃvāda āsīt agnihotre nimitte tatra janakasya agnihotra viṣayam vijñānam upalabhya parituṣṭaḥ  yājñavalkyaḥ tasmai janakāya ha kila varanda dau sa ca janakaḥ  ha kāma praśnam eva varam vavre vṛtavān  tam ca varam ha asmai dadau yājñavalkyaḥ tena vara pradāna sāmarthyena avyācikhyāsum apidau  iti yājñavalkyam tu uṣṇaim sthitam api samrāj ā iva janakaḥ pūrvam papraccha tatra eva anuktiḥ brahma vidyāyāḥ karmaṇā viruddha tvāt  vidyāyāḥ ca svātantryāt  svatantrā hi brahma vidyā sahakāri sādhana antara nirapekṣā puruṣa artha sādhana iti ca he yājñavalkya iti evam saṃbodhya abhimukhīkaraṇāya kiñjyotiḥ ayam puruṣa iti kim asya puruṣasya jyotiḥ yena jyotiṣā vyavaharati saḥ  ayam kiñjyotiḥ ayam prākṛtaḥ kārya karaṇa saṃghāta rūpaḥ śiraḥ pāṇi ādimān puruṣaḥ pṛcchyate kim ayam sva avayava asaṃghāta bāhyena jyotiḥ antareṇa vyavaharati āhosvit svāvayava saṃghāta madhya pātinā jyotiṣā jyotiṣkārya mayam puruṣaḥ  nirvartayati iti etad abhipretya pṛcchati kiñcātaḥ yadi vyatiriktena yadi vā avyatiriktena jyotiṣā jyotiṣkāryam nirvartayati śṛṇu tatra kāraṇam yadi vyatiriktena eva jyotiṣā jyotiṣkārya nirvartaka tvam asya svabhāvaḥ  nirdhāritaḥ  bhavati tatas  adṛṣṭa jyotiṣkārya viṣaye api anumāsyāmahe vyatirikta jyotiḥ nimittam eva idam kāryam iti atha avyatiriktena eva sva ātmanā jyotiṣā vyavaharati tatas  apratyakṣe api jyotiṣi jyotiṣkārya darśane abyatiriktam eva jyotiḥ anumeyam atha aniyama eva vyatiriktam avyatiriktam vā jyotiḥ puruṣasya vyavahāra hetuḥ tatas  anadhyavasāya eva jyotiḥ viṣaya iti evam manvānaḥ pṛcchati janakaḥ  yājñavalkyam kiñjyotiḥ ayam puruṣa iti nanu evam anumāna kauśale janakasya kim praśnena svayam eva kasmāt na pratipadyata iti satyam etad  tathā api liṅga liṅgi saṃbandha viśeṣāṇām atyanta saukṣmyāt duravabodhyatām manyate bahūnām apu paṇḍitānām kim uta ekasya ata eva hi dharma sūkṣma nirṇaye pariṣad vyāpāra iṣyate puruṣa viśeṣaḥ ca apekṣyate daśa avarā pariṣattrayaḥ  vā ekaḥ  vā iti tasmāt yadi api anumāna kauśalam rājñaḥ tathā api tu yuktaḥ  yājñavalkyaḥ praṣṭum vijñāna kauśala tāratamya upapatteḥ puruṣāṇām athavā śrutiḥ svayam evā akhyāyikā vyājena anumāna mārgam upanyasya asmān bodhayati puruṣa matimanusartī yājñavalkyaḥ  api janaka abhiprāya bhijña tayā vyatiriktam ātma jyotiḥ bodhayiṣyan janakam vyatirikta pratipādakam eva liṅgam pratipede yathā prasiddham āditya jyotiḥ samrāj iti ha uvāca katham ādityena eva sva avayava sa ghāta vyatiriktena cakṣuṣaḥ  anugrāhakeṇa jyotiṣā ayam prākṛtaḥ puruṣa āsta upaviśati palyayate prayeti kṣetram araṇyam vā tatra gatvā karma bāhi aneka jyotiḥ pradarśanam ca liṅgasya avyabhicāritva darśana artham evam eva etad yājñavalkya tathā astam ita āditye yājñavalkya kiñjyotiḥ eva ayam puruṣa iti candramā eva asya jyotiḥ astam iti āditye candramasi astamite agniḥ jyotiḥ śānte agnau vāgjyotiḥ vāc iti śabdaḥ parigṛhyate śabdena viṣayeṇa śrotram indriyam dīpyate śrotra indriye saṃpradīpte manasi viveka upajāyate tena manasā bāhyām ceṣṭām pratipadyate manasā hi ova paśyati manasā śṛṇotī ti brāhmaṇam katham purvāc jyotiḥ iti vācā ujyotiṣṭvam aprasiddham iti ata āha tasmāt vai samrāj ī asmāt vācā jyotiṣā anugṛhītaḥ  ayaṭam puruṣaḥ  vyavaharati tasmāt prasiddham etad vācaḥ  jyotiṣṭvam katham api yatra yasmin kāle prāvṛṣi prāyeṇa medhā andhakāre sarva jyotiḥ pratyasta maye svar  api prāṇiḥ hastaḥ  na vispaṣṭam nirjñāyate atha tasmin kāle sarva ceṣṭā nirodhe prāpte bāhya jyotiṣaḥ  abhāvāt yatra vāc uccarati śvā vā bhaṣati gardabhaḥ  vā rauti upaiva tatra nyeti tena śabdena jyotiṣā śrotra manasoḥ naiḥ antayam bhavati tena jyotiṣkārya tvam vāc pratipadyeta tena vācā jyotiṣā upanyā iti eva upagacchati eva tatra sannihitaḥ  bhavati iti arthaḥ tatra ca karma kurute vipalya iti tatra vāgyotiṣaḥ  grahaṇam gandha ādīnā anupalakṣaṇa artham gandha ādibhiḥ api hi ghrāṇa ādiṣu anugṛhīteṣu pravṛtti nivṛtya ādayaḥ  bhavanti tena taiḥ api anugrahaḥ  bhavati kārya karaṇa saṃghātasya evam eva etad yājñavalkya śāntāyāḥ  punar vāci gandha ādiṣu api ca śānteṣu bāhyeṣu anugrāhakeṣu sarva pravṛtti nirodhaḥ prāptaḥ  asya puruṣasya etad uktam bhavati jāgrat viṣaye bahirmukha anu karaṇāni cakṣuḥ ādīni ādityādi jyotirbhiḥ anugṛhyāmāṇāni yadā tadā sphuṭataraḥ saṃvyavahāraḥ  asya puruṣasyadṛṣṭā tasmāt te vayam manyāmahe sarva bāhya jyotiḥ pratyasta maye api svapna suṣupta kāle jāgarite ca tādṛś avasthāyām sva avayava saṃghāta vyatiriktena eva jyotiṣā jyotiṣkārya siddhiḥ asya iti dṛśyate ca svapne jyotiṣkārya siddhiḥ bandhu saṃgamana viyoga darśanam deśa antra gamana ādi ca suṣuptat ca utthānam sukham aham asva apsam na kiñcid avediṣam iti tasmāt asti vyatiriktam kim api jyotiḥ kim punar tad śāntāyām vāci jyotiḥ bhavati iti ucyate ātmā eva asya jyotiḥ bhavati iti ātmā iti kārya karaṇa sva avayava saṃghāta vyatiriktam kārya karaṇa avabhāsakam ādityādi bāhi jyotiḥvat svayam anyena anavabhāsyamānam abhidhīyate jyotiḥ antar stham ca tad pāriśeṣyāt  kārya karaṇa vyatiriktam tad iti tāvat siddham yad ca kārya karaṇa vyatiriktam kārya karaṇa saṃghāta anugrāhakam ca jyotiḥ tad bāhyaiḥ cakṣuḥ ādi karaṇaiḥ upalabhyamānam dṛṣṭam na tu tathā tad cakṣuḥ ādibhiḥ upalabhyata āditya ādi jyotiḥṣu uparateṣu kāryam tu jyotiṣaḥ  dṛśyote yasmāt tasmāt ātmanā eva ayam jyotiṣā aste palyayate karma kurute vipalya iti iti tasmāt nūnam antaraḥstham jyotiḥ iti avagamyate kiñcā adityādi jyotiḥ vilakṣaṇam tad abhautikam ca sa eva hetuḥ yad cakṣuḥ ādi agrāhyam āditya ādivat  na samāna jātīyena eva ādityādi jyotiṣā kārya karaṇa saṃghātasya bhautikasya bhautikena eva upakāraḥ kriyamāṇaḥ  dṛśyate yathā duṣṭam ca idam anumeyam yadi nāma kārya karaṇāt artha antaram tad upakārakam āt itya ādivat jyotisthā api kārya karaṇa saṃghāta samāna jātīyam eva anumeyam kārya karaṇa sa ghāta upakāraka tvāt ādityādi jyotiḥvat  yad punar antar stha tvāt apratyakṣa tvāt ca vailakṣaṇyam ucyate tad cakṣuḥ ādi jyotirbhiḥ anaikāntikam yatas  apratyakṣāṇi antar sthāni ca cakṣuḥ ādi jyotīṃṣi bhautikāni eva tasmāt tava manoratha mātram vilakṣaṇam ātma jyotiḥ siddham iti kārya karaṇa saṃghāta bhāva bhāvi tvāt ca saṃghāta dharma tvam anumīyate jyotiṣaḥ sāmānyatas  dṛṣṭasya ca anumānasya vyabhicāri tvāt aprāmāṇyam sāmānyatas  dṛṣṭa balena hi bhavān āt itya ādivat vyatiriktam jyotiḥ sādhayati kārya karaṇebhyaḥ na ca pratyakṣam anumānena bādhitum śakyate ayam eva tu kārya karaṇa saṃghātaḥ pratyakṣam paśyati śṛṇoti manute vijānāti ca yadi nāma jyotiḥ antaram asya upakārakam syāt āt ityādivat na tadā atmā syajyotiḥ antaram āditya ādivat eva ya eva tu pratyakṣam darśana kriyām karoti sa evā atmā syāt kārya karaṇa saṃghātaḥ  na anyaḥ pratyakṣa virodhe anumānasya aprāmāṇyāt  nanu ayam eva ced darśana ādi krāya kartā atmā saṃghātaḥ katham avikalasya eva asya darśana ādi kriyā kartṛ tvam kadācid bhavati kadācid na iti na eṣa doṣaḥ  dṛṣṭa tvāt  na hi dṛṣṭe anupapannam nāma na hi khadyote prakāśa aprakāśa tvena dṛśyamāne kāraṇa antaram anumeyam anumeya tve ca kenacid sāmānyāt sarvam sarvatra anumeyam syāt  tad ca aniṣṭam na ca padārtha svabhāvaḥ  na asti na hi agneḥ uṣṇa svābhāvyam anya nimittam udakasya vā śaityam prāṇi dharma adharma ādi apekṣam iti ced  dharma adharma ādeḥ nimitta antara apekṣa svabhāva prasaṅgaḥ astu iti ced na tad anavasthā prasaṅgaḥ sa ca aniṣṭaḥ na svapna smṛtyoḥ dṛṣṭasya eva darśanāt  yad uktam svabhāva vādinā dehasya eva darśana ādi kriyā na vyatiriktasya iti tad na yadi hi dehasya eva darśana ādi kriyā svapne dṛṣṭasya eva darśanam na syāt  andhaḥ svapnam paśyan dṛṣṭa pūrvam eva paśyati na śāka dvīpa ādi gatam adṛṣṭa rūpam tatas cetat siddham bhavati yaḥ svapne paśyati dṛṣṭa pūrvam vastu sa eva pūrvam vidyamāne cakṣuṣi at rākṣīt na deha iti dehaḥ ced draṣṭāsa yena adrākṣīt tasmin  uddhṛte cakṣuṣi svapne tad eva dṛṣṭa pūrvam na paśyet  asti ca loke prasiddhiḥ pūrvam dṛṣṭam mayā himavataḥ śṛṅgam adya aham svapne adrākṣam iti uddhṛta cakṣuṣām andhānām apu tasmāt anuddhṛte api cakṣuṣiḥ yaḥ svapna dṛś sa eva draṣṭā na deha iti avagamyate tathā smṛtau dṛṣṭṛ smartroḥ ekatve sati ya eva draṣṭāsa eva smartā yadā ca evam tadā nimīlita akṣaḥ  api sman dṛṣṭa pūrvam yad rūpam tad dṛṣṭavat eva paśyati iti tasmāt yad nimīlitam tad na draṣṭṛyat nimīlite cakṣuṣi smarat rūpam paśyati tad eva animīlite api cakṣuṣi draṣṭṛ āsīt iti avagamyate mṛte ca dehe avikalasya eva ca rūpa ādi darśana abhāvāt devasya eva draṣṭru tve mṛte api darśana ādi kriyā syāt  tasmādi apāye dehe darśanam na bhavati dbhāve ca bhavati tad darśana ādi kriyā kartṛ na deva iti avagamyate cakṣuḥ ādīni eva darśana ādi kriyā kartṝṇi iti ced  na yad aham adrākṣam tad spṛśāmi iti bhinna kartṛka tve pratisaṃghāna anupapatteḥ manaḥ tarhi iti ced  na manasaḥ  api viṣaya tvāt rūpa ādivat dṛṣṭṛtva ādi anupapatti tasmāt antar stham vyatiriktam āditya ādivat iti siddham yad uktam kārya karaṇa saṃghāta samāna jātīyam eva jyotiḥ antaram anumeyam ādityādibhiḥ tad samāna jātīyaiḥ eva upakriyamāṇa tvāt iti tad asat  upakārya upakāraka bhāvasya aniyama darśanāt katham pārthivaiḥ indhanaiḥ pārthavatu asamāna jātīyaiḥ tṛṇa ulapa ādibhiḥ agneḥ prajvalana upakāraḥ kriyamāṇaḥ  dṛśyate na ca tāvatā tad samāna jātīyaiḥ eva agneḥ prajvana upakāraḥ sarvatra anumeyaḥ syāt  yena udakena api prajvalana upakāraḥ  bhinna jātī yona vaidyutasya agneḥ jāṭharasya ca kriyamāṇaḥ  dṛśyate tasmāt upakārya upakāraka bhāve samāna jātīya asamāna jātīya niyamaḥ  na asti kadācid samāna jātīyā manuṣyā manuṣyaiḥ eva upakriyante kadācid sthāvara paśu ādibhiḥ ca bhinna jātīyaiḥ tasmāt ahetuḥ kārya karaṇa saṃghāta māna jātīyaiḥ evā aditya ādi jyotirbhiḥ upakriyamāṇa tvāt it i yad punar āttha cakṣuḥ ādibhiḥ āditya ādi jyotiḥvat adṛśya tvāt iti ayam hetuḥ jyotiḥ antarasya antar stha tvam vailakṣaṇyam ca na sādhayati cakṣuḥ ādibhiḥ anaikāntika tvāt iti tad asat  cakṣuḥ ādi karaṇebhyaḥ  anya tve sati iti hetoḥ viśeṣaṇatva upapatteḥ kārya karaṇa saṃghāta dharma tvam jyotiṣa iti yad uktam tad na anumāna virodhāt  āditya ādi jyotiḥvat kārya karaṇa saṃghātāt artha antaram jyotiḥ iti hi anumānam uktam tena virudhyata iyam pratijñā kāraya karaṇa saṃghāta dharma tvam jyotiṣa iti tad bhāva bhāvi tvam tu asiddham mṛte dehe jyotiṣaḥ  adarśanāt  sāmānyatas  dṛṣṭasya anumānasya aprāmāṇye sati pāna bhojana ādi sarva vyavahāra lopa prasaṅgaḥ sa ca aniṣṭaḥ pāna bhojana ādiṣu hi kṣudh pipāsā ādi nivṛttim upalabdha vasaḥ tad sāmānyāt pāna bhojana ādi upādānam dṛśyamānam loke na prāpnoti dṛśyante hi upalabdha pāna bhojanāḥ sāmānyatas  punar  pāna bhojana antaraiḥ kṣudh pipāsā ādi nivṛttim anum invantaḥ tādartheyana pravartamānāḥ yad ukta mayam eva tu dehaḥ  darśana ādi kriyā kartā iti tad prathamam eva parihṛtam svapna smṛti oḥ dehāt artha antara bhūtaḥ  draṣṭā iti anena eva jyotiḥ antarasya ātma tvam api pratyuktam yad punar  khadyota ādeḥ kādācid kam prakāśa aprakāśa tvam sat asat pakṣa ādi avayava saṃkoca vikāsa nimititta tvāt prakāśa aprakāśa tvasya yad punaruktam dharma adharmayoḥ avaśyam phala dātṛ tvam svabhāvaḥ  abhyupagantavya iti tad abhyubagame bhavataḥ siddhānta hānāt etena anavasthā doṣaḥ pratyuktaḥ tasmāt asti vyatiriktam ca antar stham jyotiḥ ātmā iti yadi api vyatiriktatva ādi siddham tathā api samāna jātīya anugrāhakatva darśana nimitta bhrāntyā karaṇānām eva anyatamaḥ  vyatiriktaḥ  vā iti avivekataḥ pṛcchati katama iti nyāya sūkṣma tāyāḥ  durvijñeya tvāt upapadyate bhrāntiḥ athavā śarīra vyatirikte siddhe api karaṇa anu sarvāṇi vijñānavantī iva vivekata ātmanaḥ  anupalabdha tvāt  atas  aham pṛcchāmi katama ātmā iti katamaḥ  asau deha indriya prāṇa manaḥsu yaḥ tu ayā ukta ātmā yena jyotiṣā asta iti uktam athavā yaḥ  ayam ātmā tvayā abhipretaḥ  vijñāna mayaḥ sarva ime prāṇā vijñāna mayā iva eṣu prāṇeṣu katamaḥ yathā samuditeṣu brāhmaṇeṣu sarva ime tejasvinaḥ katama eṣu ṣaḍaṅga vid iti pūrvasmin vyākhyāne katama ātmā iti etāvat eva praśna vākyam vijñānam ayaḥ  hṛdi antar jyotiḥ puruṣaḥ katama iti edatantam yaḥ  ayam vijñāna maya iti etasya śabdasya sarvam eva praśna vākyam vijñānam ayaḥ  hṛdi antar jyotiḥ puruṣaḥ katama iti edatantam yaḥ  ayam vijñāna maya iti etasya śabdasya nirdhārita artha viśeṣa viṣaya tvam katama ātmā iti iti śabdasya praśna vākya parisamāpti artha tvam vyavahita saṃbandham antareṇa yuktam iti kṛtvā katama ātmā iti evam antam eva praśna vākyam yaḥ  ayam ityādi param sarvam eva prativacanam iti niścīyate yaḥ  ayam iti ātmanaḥ pratyakṣa tvāt nirdeśaḥ vijñānam ayaḥ  vijñāna prāyaḥ  buddhi vijñāna upādhi saṃprakā vi vekāt vijñāna maya iti ucyate buddhi vijñāna saṃpṛkta eva hi yasmāt upalabhyate rāhuḥ iva candra āditya saṃpṛktaḥ buddhiḥ hi sarva artha karaṇam tamasi iva pradīpaḥ purovasthitaḥ manasā hi eva paśyati manasā śṛṇotī ti hi uktam buddhi vijñāna āloka viśiṣṭam eva hi sarvam viṣaya jātam upalabhyate purovasthita pradīpa āloka viśiṣṭam iva tamasi dvāra mātrāṇi tu anyāni karaṇa anu buddheḥ tasmāt tena eva viśeṣyate vijñāna maya iti yeṣām parama ātma vijñapti vikāra iti vyākhyānam teṣām vijñānam ayaḥ  manaḥ maya iti ādau vijñāna maya śabdasya anya artha darśanāt aśrauta artha tāvasīyate saṃdigdhaḥ ca padārathaḥ  anyatra niścita prayoga darśanāt nirdhārayitum śakyaḥ  vāśya śeṣāt  niścata nyāya balāt vā sa dhīḥ iti ca uttaratra pāṭhāt  hṛdi antar iti vacana āt yuktam vijñāna prāya tvam eva prāṇeṣu iti vyatireka pradarśa arthā saptamī yathā vṛkṣeṣu pāṣāṇa iti sāmīpya lakṣaṇā prāṇeṣu hi vyātiḥ eka avyatireka tā saṃdihyata ātmanaḥ prāṇeṣu prāṇebhyaḥ  vyatirikta iti arthaḥ yaḥ  hi yeṣu bhavati sa tad vyatiriktaḥ  bhavati eva yathā pāṣāṇeṣu vṛkṣaḥ hṛdi tatra atat syāt prāṇeṣu prāṇa jātīya eva buddhiḥ syāt iti ata āha hṛdi antar iti hṛdat śabdena puṇḍarīka ākāraḥ  māṃsa puṇḍaḥ tātthyāt buddhiḥ hṛd tasyā hṛdi buddhau antar iti buddhi vṛtti vyatireka pradarśana artham jyotiḥ avabhāsa ātmaka tvāt ātmā ucyate tena hi avabhāsakenā atmanā jyotiṣā aste palyayate karma kurute cenāvān iva hi ayam kārya karaṇa piṇḍaḥ  yathā aditya prakāśa sthaḥ  ghaṭaḥ  yathā marakata ādiḥ maṇiḥ kṣīra ādi dravye prakṣiptaḥ parīkṣaṇāya ātma  chāyam eva tad kṣīra ādiḥ dvyam karoti tādṛś eda ātmajya iti pabuddheḥ api hṛdayāt sūkṣma tvāt hṛdyantaḥstham api hṛdaya ādikam kārya karaṇa saṃghātam ca ekīkṛtyā atma jyotiḥ chāyam karoti pāramparyeṇa sūkṣma sthīla tāratamyāt sarva antaratama tvā buddhaḥ tāvat svaccha tvāt ānantaryāt cā atma caitanya jyotiḥ praticchāyā bhavati tena hi vivekinām apu tatrā atma abhimāna buddhiḥ prathamā tatas  api ānantaryāt manasi caitanya avabhāsa tā buddhi saṃparkāt  tatas  indriyeṣu manaḥ saṃyogāt  tatas  anantaram śarīre indriya saṃparkāt  pāramparyeṇa kṛtsnam kārya karaṇa saṃghātam ātmā caitanya svarūpa jyotiṣā avabhāsayati tena hi sarvasya lokasya kārya karaṇa saṃghāte tad vṛttiṣu ca aniyatā atma abhimāna buddhiḥ yathā vivekam jāyate tathā ca bhagavatā uktam gītāsu yathā prakāśayati ekaḥ kṛtsnam lokam imam raviḥ kṣetram kṣetrī tathā kṛtsnam prakāśayati bhārati yad ā āditya gatam tejaḥ ityādi ca nityaḥ  anityānām cenaḥ cetanānām iti ca kāṭhake tam eva bhāntam anubhāti sarvam tasya bhāsā sarvam idam vibhāti iti ca yena sūryaḥ tapati tejasā uddhaḥ iti ca mantarvarṇaḥ tena ayam hṛdi antar jyotiḥ puruṣa ākāśavat sarvaga tvāt pūrṇa iti puruṣaḥ niratiśayam ca asya svayan jyotiṣṭvam sarva avabhāsaka tvāt svayam anya anava bhāsya tvāt ca sa eṣa puruṣaḥ svayam eva jyotiḥ svabhāvaḥ  yam tvam pṛcchasi katama ātmā iti bāhyānām jyotiṣām sarva karaṇa anugrāhakāṇām pratyasta maye antaḥkaraṇa dvāreṇa hṛdi antar jyotiḥ puruṣa ātmā anugrāhakaḥ karaṇānām iti uktam yadā api bāhya karaṇa anugrāhakāṇām ādityādi jyotiṣām bhāvaḥ tadā api ādityādi jyotiṣām para artha tvāt kārya karaṇa saṃghātasya ācaitanye sva artha anupapatteḥ sva artha jyotiṣa ātmanaḥ  anugraha abhāve ayam kārya karaṇa saṃghātaḥ  na vyavahārāya kalpate ātma jyotiḥ anugraheṇa eva hi sarvadā sarvaḥ saṃvyavahāraḥ yad etad hṛdayam manaḥ caittasaṃjñānam ityādi śruti antarāt sa abhimānaḥ  hi sarva prāṇi saṃvyavahāpaḥ abhimāna hetum ca marakata maṇi dṛṣṭāntena avocāma yadi api evam etad tattha api jāgrat viṣaye sarva karaṇa agocara tvāt ātma jyotiṣaḥ  buddhi ādi bāhya abhyantara kārya karaṇa vvahāra sannipāta vyākula tvāt na śakyate tad jyotiḥ ātma ākhyam muñja iṣīkāvat niṣkṛṣya darśayitum iti atas  svapne didarśayiṣuḥ prakramate sa samānaḥ san  ubhau lokau  anusaṃcarati yaḥ puruṣaḥ svayam eva jyotiḥ ātmā sa samānaḥ sadṛśaḥ san kena prakṛta tvāt sannihita tvāt ca hṛdayena hṛdi iti ca hṛd śabda vācyā buddhaḥ prakṛtā sannihitā ca tasmāt tayā eva sāmānyam kim punar  sāmānyam aśva mahiṣavat vivekataḥ  anupalabdhiḥ avabhāsyā buddhiḥ abhāsakam tad ā ātma jyotiḥ ālokavat avabhāsya avabhāsakayoḥ vivekataḥ anupalabdhiḥ prasiddhā viśuddha tvāt hi ālokaḥ  avabhāsyena sadṛśaḥ  bhavati yathā raktam avabhāsayan rakta sadṛśaḥ  rakta ākāraḥ  bhavati yathā haritam nīlam lohitam ca avabhāsayan  ālokaḥ tad samānaḥ  bhavati tathā buddhim avabhāsayan buddha dvāreṇa kṛtsamam kṣetram avabhāsayati iti uktam marakata maṇi nidarśanena tena sarveṇa samānaḥ  buddhi sāmānya dvāreṇa sarva maya iti cāta eva vakṣyati tena asau kutaścid pravabhajya muñja iṣīkā vatsvena jyotīrūpeṇa darśayitum na śakyata iti sarva vyāpāram tatra adhyāropya nāma rūpa gatam jyotirdharmam ca nāma rūpayoḥ nāma rūpe cā atma jyotiṣi sarvaḥ  lokaḥ  momugyate ayam ātmā na ayamāmtaivandharmā na eva dharmā kartā akartā śuddhaḥ  aśuddhaḥ  baddhaḥ  muktaḥ sthitaḥ  gata āgataḥ  asti na asti ityādi vikalpaiḥ atas  samānaḥ mannubhau lokau pratipanna pratipattavyauviha loka para lokau  upātta deha indriya ādi saṅghāta tyāga anya upādāna āstān aprabandha śata sannipātaiḥ anukrameṇa sañcarati dhī sādṛśyam eva ubhaya loka saṃcaraṇa hetuḥ na svata iti tatra nāma rūpa upādhi sādṛśyam bhrānti nimittam yad tad eva hetuḥ na svata iti etad ucyate yasmāt sa samānaḥ san  ubhau lokau  anukrameṇa sañcarati tad etad pratyakṣam iti etad darśayati yatas  dhyāyati iva dhyāna vyāpāram karoti iva cintayati iva dhyāna vyāpavatīm buddhim sa tad sthena cit svabhāva jyota rūpeṇa avabhāsayan  tad sadṛśaḥ tad samānaḥ sandhyātīva ālokavat eva atas  bhavati cintayati iti bhrāntiḥ lokasya na tu paramārtha taḥ  dhyāyati tathā lelāyati iva atyartham calati iva teṣu eva karameṣu buddhi ādiṣu vāyuṣu ca calatsu tad avabhāsaka tvāt tad sadṛśam tad iti lelāyati iva na tu paramārthataḥ calana dharmakam tad ā ātma jyotiḥ katham punar etad avagamyate tad samānatva bhrāntiḥ eva ubhaya loka saṃcaraṇa ādiḥ hetu tvam svata iti asya arthasya pradarśanāya hetar upadiśyate sa ātmā hi yasmāt svapnaḥ  bhūtvā sa yayā dhiyā samānaḥ sā dhīḥ yadyat bhavati tad tad asau  apu bhavati iva tasmāt yadā asau svapnaḥ  bhavati svāpa vṛttim pratipadyate dhīḥ tadā saḥ  api svapna vṛttim pratipadyate dā dhīḥ jajāgariṣati tadā asau  api ata āha svapnaḥ  bhūtvā svapna vṛttim avabhāsayan dhiyaḥ svāpa vṛtya ākāraḥ  bhūtvā ima lokam jāgarita vyavahāra lakṣaṇam kārya karaṇa saṅghāta ātmakam laukika śāstrīya vyavahāra āspadam atikrāmati atīti krāmati viviktena svenā atma jyotiṣā svapna ātmikā dhī vṛttam avabhāyan  avatiṣṭhate yasmāt tasmāt svayan jyotar svabhāva eva asau viśuddhaḥ sa kartṛ kriyā kāraka phala śūnyaḥ paramārtha taḥ  dhī sādṛśyam eva tu ubhaya loka saṃcāra ādi saṃvyavahāra bhrānti hetuḥ mṛtyaḥ rūpā ṇi mṛtyuḥ karma avidyā ādiḥ na tasya anyat rūpam svatas  kārya karaṇāni eva asya rūpāṇi atas tānu mṛtyaḥ rūpāṇi atikrāmati kriyā phala āśrayāṇi nanu na asti eva dhiyā samānam anyat hiyaḥ avabhāsakam ātma jyotiḥ pratyakṣeṇa vā anumānena palambhāt  yathā anyā tad kāla eva dvitīyā dhīḥ yadtva avabhāsya avabhāsakayoḥ anya tve api viveka anupalambhāt sādṛśyam iti ghaṭa ādi ālokayoḥ tatra bhavatu anyatu enā alokasya upambhāt ghaṭā ādeḥ saṃśliṣṭayoḥ sādṛśyam bhinnayoḥ eva na ca tathā iha ghaṭa ādeḥ iva dhiyoṣa avabhāsakam jyotiḥ intaram pratyakṣeṇa vā anumānena vā upalabhāmahe dhīḥ eva hi cit svarūpa avabhāsaka tvena su ākārā viṣaya ākārā ca tasmāt na anumānataḥ  na api pratyakṣataḥ dhiyaḥ  avabhāsakam jyotiḥ śakyate pratipādayitum vyatiriktam yad api dṛṣṭānta rūpam abhihitam avabhāsya avaśāsakayoḥ bhinnayoḥ eva ghaṭa ādi ālokayoḥ saṃyuktāyoḥ sādṛśyam iti tatra abhyupagama mātram asmābhiḥ uktam na tatra ghaṭa ādi avabhāsya avabhāsakau bhinnau parama arthaḥ tu ghaṭa ādiḥ eva avabhāsa ātmakaḥ sa ālokaḥ anyaḥ  anyaḥ  hi ghaṭa ādiḥ utpadyate vijñāna mātram eva sa āloka ghaṭa ādi viṣaya ākāram avabhāsate yad evam tadā na bāhyaḥ  dṛṣṭāntaḥ  asti vijñāna lakṣaṇa mātra tvāt sarvasya em tasyava vijñāna s grāhyā grāhaka ākāra tām alam pakari kalpya tasya eva punar viśuddham parikalpayanti tad grāhaka vinirmuktam vijñānam svacchībhūtam kṣaṇikam vyavatiṣṭhata iti kecid  tasya apu śāntim kecid icchanti tad api vijñānam saṃvṛtam grāhya grāhaka aṃśa vinirumuktam śūnyam eva ghaṭa ādi bāhya vastuvat iti apare mādhyamikā ācakṣate sarvā etāḥ kalpanā buddha vijñāna avabhāsakasya vyatiriktasyā atma jyotiṣaḥ  apahna vādasya śreyaḥ mārgasya pratipakṣa bhūtā vaidikasya tatra yeṣām bāhyor athaḥ asti tān pratyucyate tāvat  na sva ātma avabhāsaka tvam ghaṭa ādeḥ tamasi avasthitaḥ  ghaṭa ādiḥ tāvat na kadācid apu sva ātmanā avabhāsyate pradīpa ādi āloka saṃyogena tu niyamena eva avabhāsyamānaḥ  dṛṣṭaḥ sa ālokaḥ  ghaṭa iti saṃśliṣṭayoḥ apu ghaṭa ālokayoḥ anya tvam eva punar  punar  saṃśleṣe viśleṣe ca viśeṣa darśanāt rajju ghaṭayoḥ iva anya tve ca vyatirikta avabhāsaka tvam na sva ātmanā eva svam ātmānam avabhāsayati nanu pradīpaḥ sva ātmānam eva avabhāsayanta dṛṣṭa iti na hi ghaṭa ādivat pradīpa darśanāya pkāśa antaram upādadate laukikāḥ tasmāt pradīpaḥ sva ātmānam prakāśayati na avabhāsyatva aviśeṣāt yadi api pradīpaḥ  anyasya avabhāsakaḥ svayam avabhāsāt ka tvāt tathā pu vyatirikta caitanya avabhāsya tvam na vyabhicarati ghaṭa ādivat eva yadā ca evam tadā vyatirikta avabhāsya tvam tāvat avaśyaṃbhāvi nanu yathā ghaṭaḥ caitanya avabhāsya tve api san  ātmānam ghaṭam ca avabhāsayati na svatas  paratas  vā viśeṣa abhāvāt yathā caitanya avabhāsya tvam ghaṭasya tathā pradīpasya api caitanya avabhāsya tvam aviśiṣṭam yad tu ucyate pradīpa ātmānam ghaṭam ca avabhāsayati iti tad asat  kasmāt  yadā atmānam na avabhāsayati tadā kīdṛśaḥ syāt  na hi tadā pradīpasya svatas  vā paratas  vā viśeṣaḥ kaścid upalabhyate sa hi avabhāsyaḥ  bhavati yasya avabhāsaka saṃnidhau  asaṃnidhau ca viśeṣa ātmānam pradīpaḥ prakāśayati iti mṛṣā eva acya ut caitanya grāhya tvam tu ghaṭa ādibhiḥ aviśiṣṭam pradīpasya tasmāt vijñanasyā atma grāhaka tve na pradīpaḥ  dṛṣṭāntaḥ caitanya grāhya tvam ca vijñānasya bāhya viṣayaiḥ aviśiṣṭam caitanya grāhya tve ca vijñānasya kim grāhya vijñāna grāhya tā eva kiṃvā grāhaka vijñāna grāhyatā iti tatrasaṃdihyamāne vastuni yaḥ  anyatra dṛṣṭaḥ  nyāyaḥ sa kalpayitum yuktaḥ  na tu dṛṣṭa viparītaḥ tathā ca sati yathā vyitiriktena eva grāhakeṇa bāhyānām pradīpānām grāhya tvam dṛṣṭam tathā vijñānasya api caitanya grāhya tvāt pkāśaka tve satyā api pradīpavat vyatirikta caitanya grāhya tvam yuktam kalpayitum na tu ananya grāhya tvam yaśva anyaḥ  vijñānasya grahītā sa ātmā jyotiḥ antaram vijñānāt  tadā anavasthā iti ced  naḥ grāhyatva mātra hi tad grāhakasya vastu antara tve liṅgam uktam nyāyataḥ na tu ekāntatas  grāhaka tve tad grāhaka antara astitve vā kadācid api liṅgam saṃbhavati tasmāt na tad anavasthā prasaṅgaḥ vijñānasya vyakti rikta grāhya tve karaṇa antara apekṣāyām anavasthā iti ced  na niyama abhāvāt  na hi sarvatra ayam niyamaḥ  bhavati yatra vastu antareṇa gṛhyate vastu antaram tatra grāhya grāhaka vyatiriktam karaṇa antaram syāt iti na ekāntena niyantum śakyate vaicitrya darśanāt  katham ghaṭaḥ tāvat sva ātma vyatiriktenā atmanā gṛhyate tad pa pradīpa ādiḥ ālokaḥ  grāhya grāhaka vyatiriktam karaṇam na hi pradīpa ādi ālokaḥ  ghaṭa aṃśaḥ cakṣuḥ aṃśaḥ  vā ghaṭavat cakṣuḥ grāhya tve api pradīpasya cakṣuḥ pradīpa vyatirekeṇa na bāhyam āloka sthānīyam kiñcid karaṇa antaram apekṣate tasmāt na eva niyantum śakyate yatra yatra vyatirikta grāhaka grāhya tvam tatra tatra karaṇa antaram syāt eva iti tasmāt vijñānasya vyakti rikta grāhaka grāhya tve na karaṇa dvāra anavasthā na api grāhaka tvadvārā kadācid api upapādayitum śakyate tasmāt siddham vijñāna vyatiriktam ātma jyotiḥ antaram iti nanu na asti eva bāhyor athaḥ ghaṭa ādiḥ pradīpaḥ  vā vijñāna vyatiriktaḥ yad hi yad vyatirekeṇa na upalamyate tad tāvat mātram vastu dṛṣṭam yathā svapna vijñāna grāhyam ghaṭa paṭa ādi vastu svapna vijñāna vyatirekeṇa anupalambhāt svapna ghaṭa pradīpa ādeḥ svapna vijñāna mātra tā avagamyate tathā jāgarite api ghaṭa pradīpa ādeḥ jāgarite api ghaṭa pradīpa ādeḥ jāgra dvijñāna mātram eva tu sarvam tatra yad uktam vijñānasya vyatirikta avabhāsya tvāt vijñāna vyatiriktam asti jyotiḥ antaram gaṭa ādeḥ iva iti tad mithyā sarvasya vijñāna mātra tve dṛṣṭānta abhāvāt na yāvat tāvat abhyupagamāt  na tu bāhyor athaḥ bhavatā ekāntena eva na abhyupagamyate nanu mayā na abhyupagamyata eva na vijñānam ghaṭaḥ pradīpa iti ca śabda artha pṛthaktvāt yāvattāvajat api bāhyam artha antaram avaśyam abhyupagantavyam vijñānāt artha antaram vastu na ced abhyupagamyate vijñānam ghaṭaḥ paṭa iti evamādīnām bhabdānām ekārtha tve paryāya śabda tvam prāpnoti tathā sādhanānām phalasya ca eka tve sādhya sādhana bheda upadśa śāstra anartha prasaṅgaḥ tad kartuḥ ajñāna prasaṅgaḥ  vā kiñca anyat vijñāna vyatirekeṇa vādi prativāda vāda doṣa bhyupagamāt na hi ātma vijñāna mātram eva vādi prativādi vādaḥ tad doṣaḥ  vā abhyugamyate nirākartavya tvāt prativādya ādīnām na hi ātmīyam vijñāna nirākartavyam abhyupagamyate svayam vā atmā kasyacid  tathā ca sati sarva saṃvyavahāra lopa prasaṅgaḥ na ca pravādya ādayaḥ sva ātmanā eva gṛhyanta iti abhyupagamaḥ vyatirikta grāhyā hi te abhyupagamyante tasmāt tadvat sarvam eva vyatirikta grāhyam vastu jāgrat viṣaya tvāt jāgrat vastu pratipādya ādivat iti sa lābhau dṛṣṭāntaḥ saṃtati antaravat vijñāna antaravat ca iti tasmāt vijñāna vādinā api na śakyam vijñāna vyatiriktam jyotiḥ antaram nirākartum svapne vijñāna vyatireka abhāvāt ayuktam iti ced  na abhāvāt api bhāvasya vastu antaratva upapatteḥ bhavatā eva viṣayaḥ  ghaṭa ādiḥ yadi abhāvaḥ  yadi vā bhāvaḥ syāt ubhayathā api ghaṭa ādi vijñānasya bhāva bhūta tvam abhyupagatam eva na tu tad nivartayitum śakyate tad nivartaka nyāya abhāvāta etena sarvasya śūnyatā pratyuktā pratyagātmā agrāhyatā cā atmanaḥ  aham iti mīmāṃsaka pakṣaḥ pratyuktaḥ yad tu uktam sa ālokaḥ  anyaḥ ca anyaḥ ca ghaṭaḥ  jāyata iti tad asat  kṣaṇa antare api sa eva ayam ghaṭa iti pratyabhijñānāt  sādṛśyāt pratyaya bhijñānam kṛtta utthita keśa nakha ādiṣu eva iti ced  na tatra api kṣaṇika tvasya asiddha tvāt jāti eka tvāt ca kṛtteṣu punar utthiteṣu ca keśa nakha ādiṣu keśa nakhatva ajāteḥ eka īśa nakhatva pratyayaḥ tad nimittaḥ  abhrānta  e na hi dṛśyamāna lūna utthita keśa nakha ādiṣu vyakti nimittaḥ sa eva iti pratyayaḥ bhavati kasyacid dīrkha kāla vyavahita dṛṣṭeṣu sa eva iti pratyayaḥ tasmāt na samaḥ  dṛṣṭāntaḥ pratyakṣeṇa hi pratyabhijñāyamāne vastuni tad eva iti na ca anya tvam anumātum yuktam pratyakṣa virodhe liṅgasya āabhāsatva upapatteḥ sādṛśya pratyaya anupapatteḥ ca jñānasya kṣaṇika tvāt  ekasya hi vastu darśinaḥ vastu antara darśane sādṛśya pratyayaḥ syāt  na tu vastu darśī ekaḥ  vastu antara darśanāya kṣaṇa antaram avatiṣṭhate vijñānasya kṣaṇika tvāt sakṛt vastu darśanena eva kṣaya upapatteḥ tena idam sadṛśam iti hi sādṛśya pratyayaḥ bhavati tena iti dṛṣṭa smaraṇam im iti vartamāna pratyayaḥ tena iti dṛṣṭam smṛtvā yāvat idim iti vartamāna kṣaṇa kālam avatiṣṭheta tatas  kṣaṇika vāda hāniḥ atha tena iti ava upakṣīṇaḥ smārtaḥ pratyaya idam iti ca anya eva vārtamānikaḥ pratyayaḥ kṣīyate tatas  sādṛśya pratyata anupapattiḥ tena idam sadṛśam iti aneka darśina ekasya abhāvāt  vyapadeśa anupapattiḥ ca draṣṭavya darśanena eva upakṣayāt vijñānasya idam paśyāmi ada u adrākṣam iti vyapadeśa anupapaccardṛṣṭavataḥ  vyapadeśa kṣaṇān avasthānāt atha avatiṣṭeta kṣaṇika vāda hāniḥ atha adṛṣṭavataḥ  vyapadeṣaḥ sādṛśya pratyayaḥ ca tadā anūm jāti andhasya iva rūpa viśeṣa vyapadeśaḥ tad sādṛśya pratyayaḥ ca sarvam andha paramparā iti prasajyeta sarvajña śāstra praṇaya na ādi na ca etad iṣyate akṛta abhyāgama kṛta vipraṇāśa doṣau tu prasiddhatarau kṣaṇa vāde dṛṣṭa vyapadeśa hetuḥ pūrvettara sahita eka eva hi śṛṅgalāvat pratyayaḥ jāyata iti ced  tena idam sadṛśam iti ca na varmānātītayoḥ bhinna kāla tvāt tatra vartamāna pratyaya ekaḥ śṛṅgala avayava sthānīyaḥ  atītaḥ ca aparaḥ tau pratyayau bhinna kālau tad ubhaya pratyaya viṣaya spṛkcet śṛṅkhalā pratyayaḥ tatas  kṣaṇa dvaya avyāpi tvāt ekasya vijñānasya punar  kṣaṇa vāda hāniḥ mamatavata ādi viśeṣa anupapatteḥ ca sarva saṃvyavahārala uprasaṅgaḥ sarvasya ca sva saṃvedya vijñāna mātra tve vijñānasya ca su accha avabodha ābhāsa mātra svābhāvya abhyupagamāt tad darśinaḥ ca anyasya abhāve anitya duḥkha śūnya anātmatva ādi aneka kalpanā anupattiḥ na ca dāḍima ādeḥ iva viruddha an eka aṃśava tvam vijñānasya svaccha avabhāsa svābhāvyāt dvi jñānasya anitya duḥkha ādīnām vijñāna aṃśa tve ca sati anubhīyamāna tvāt vyatirikta viṣayatva prasaṅgaḥ atha anitya duḥkha ādi ātmā eka tvam eva vijñānasya tadā tad viyogāt viśuddhi kalpanā anupapattiḥ saṃyogi mala vigāddhi viśuddhaḥ bhavati yathā adarśa prabhṛtīnām na tusvābhāvikena raktatva ādīnām dravya antara yogena viyojanam dṛśyate tatra api saṃyoga pūrva tvam anumīyate bīja bhāvanayā puṣpa phala ādīnām guṇa antara utpatti darśanāt atas  vijñānasya viśuddhi kalpanā anupapattiḥ atas  vijñānasya viśuddhi kalna anupattiḥ viṣaya viṣayya abhāsa tvam ca yad malam parikalpyate vijñānasya tad api anya saṃsarga abhāvādān upapannam na hi avidyamānena vidyamānasya saṃsargaḥ syāt  asati ca anya saṃsargeyaḥ  dharmaḥ  yasya dṛṣṭaḥ sa tad svabhātvān na tena viyogam arhati yathā agneḥ auṣṇyam savituḥ vā prabhā tasmāt anitya saṃsargeṇa malina tvam tad viśuddhiḥ ca vijñānasya iti iyam kalpanā andha paramparā eva pramāṇa śūnyā iti avagamyate yad api tasya vijñānasya nirvāṇam puruṣa artham kalpayanti tatra api phala āśraya anupapattiḥ kaṇṭaka viddhasya hi kaṇṭaka vedha janita duḥkha nivṛttiḥ phalam na tu kaṇṭaka viddha maraṇe tad duḥkha nivṛtta phalasyā aśraya upapadyate tadvat sarva nirvāṇe asati ca phala āśraye puruṣa artha kalpanā vyarthā eva yasya hi puruṣa śabda vācyasya satvasya ātmanaḥ  vijñānasya ca arthaḥ parikalpyate tasya punar  puruṣasya nirvāṇe kasya arthaḥ puruṣa artha iti syāt  yasya punar asti aneka artha daśīm vijñāna vyatirikta ātmā tasya dṛṣṭa smaraṇa dukha saṃyoga viyoga ādi sarvam eva upapannam anya saṃyoga nimittam kāluṣyam tad viyoga nimittā ca viśuddhiḥ iti śūnya vādi pakṣaḥ tu sarva pramāṇa vipratiṣiddha iti tad nirākaraṇāya nā adaraḥ kriyate yathā eva iha ekasmin dehe svapnaḥ  bhūtvā mṛtyaḥ rūpāṇi kārya karaṇāni atikramya svapne sva  ātmajyetiṣyāḥ ta evam sa vai prakṛtaḥ puruṣaḥ  ajāyamānaḥ katham jāyamāna iti ucyate śarīram deha indriya saṃghātam abhisaṃpadyamānaḥ śarīra ātma bhāvam āpadyamāna iti arthaḥ pāpmabhiḥ pāpma samavāyibhiḥ dharma adharma āśrayaiḥ kārya karaṇaiḥ iti arthaḥ saṃsṛjyate saṃyujyate sa eva utkrāman śarīra antara mūrdhaṃva krāman gacchat mriyamāṇa  iti etasya vyākhyānam utkrāman  iti tān eva saṃśliṣyān pāpma rūpa kārya karaṇa upādāna parityāga abhyām anavaracam saṃcarati dhiyā samānaḥ san tathā saḥ  ayam puruṣa ubhau  iha loka parokau janma maraṇābhyām kārya karaṇa upādāna parityāga  anavaratam pratipadyamāna ā saṃsāra mokṣāt saṃcarati tasmāt siddham asyā atma yajyotiṣaḥ anya tvam kārya karaṇa rūpebhyaḥ pāpmabhyaḥ saṃyoga viyogābhyām na hi tad dharma tve sati taiḥ eva saṃyogaḥ  viyogaḥ  vā yuktaḥ nanu na syaḥ asya ubhau lokau yau janma maraṇābhyām anukrameṇa saṃcarati svapna jāgarite iva svapna jāgarite tu pratyakṣam avagamyete na tu ihaloka para lokau kenacid pramaṇena tasmāt ete eva svapna jāgagarite ihaloka para lokau  iti ucyate tasya etasya puruṣasya vai dve e sthāne bhavataḥ  na tṛta cīyam caturtham vā ke te idam ca tpratipannam vartamānam janma śarīra inja driya viṣaya vedanā viśiṣṭam sthānam pratyakṣataḥ anubhūyamānam para loke  eva sthānam para loka sthānam tad ca śarīra ādi viviyoga uttara kāla anubhāvyam nanu svapnaḥ  api para loka sthā ca sati dve eva iti avadhāraṇam ayuktam na katham tarhi saṃdhyam tad  ihaloka para lokayoḥ yaḥ saṃdhiḥ tasmin bhavam saṃdhyam yad tṛtīyam tad svapna sthānam tena sthāna dvitva avadhāraṇam na hi grāmayoḥ saṃdhaḥ tau  eva grāmau  apekṣya tṛtīyatva parigaṇanam arhati katham punar tasya para loka sthā asya astitvam avagamyate yad apekṣya svapna sthānam saṃdhyam bhavet  yatas tasmin saṃdhye svapna sthāne tiṣṭan bhavan vartamāna ete ubhe sthāne paśyati ke te ubhe idañca para loka sthānam ca tasmāt stas  svapna jāgarita vyatirekeṇa ubhau lokau yaḥ  dhiyā samānaḥ san  anusaṃcarati janma maraṇa saṃtāna prabandhena katham punar  svapne sthitaḥ lokau paśyati kim āśrayaḥ kena vidhinā iti ucyete atha katham paśyati iti śṛṇu yathākrama akrāmati anena iti ākrama āśrayaḥ  avaṣṭambha iti arthaḥ yādṛśa ākmayaḥ  asya saḥ  ayam yathākramaḥ ayam puruṣaḥ para loka sthāne pratipattavye nimitte yathākramaḥ  bhavati yādṛśena para loka pratipatti sādhanena vidyā karma pūrva prajñāna lakṣaṇena yuktaḥ  bhavati iti arthaḥ tam ākramam para loka sthānāya unmukhībhūtam prāpta aṅkurībhāvam iva bījam tam ākramyauvaṣṭabhyā aśrityaḥ bhayān paśyati bahuvacanam dharma adharma phaloneka tvāt ubhaya prakārān iti arthaḥ kān  tān pāpmanaḥ pāpa phalāni na tu punar  sākṣāt eva pāpmanām darśanam saṃbhavati tasmāt pāpa phalāni duḥkhāni iti arthaḥ ānandān  ca dharma phalāni sukhāni iti etad  tān ubhayān pāpmana ānandān  ca paśyati janma antara dṛṣṭa vāsanā āmayāt yāni ca pratipattavyajanma viṣayāṇi kṣudra dharma adharma phalāni dharma adharma prayuktaḥ  devatā anugrahāt vā apaśyati tad katham avagamyate para loka sthāna saṃbandhi pāpmānān da darśanam svapna iti ucyate yasmāt iha janmani ananubhāvyam api paśyati bahu na ca svapnaḥ  nāma apūrvam darśanam pūrva dṛṣṭa smṛtiḥ hi svapnaḥ prāyeṇa tena svapnjā garita sthāna vyatirekeṇa sta ubhau lokau yad āditya ādi bāhya jyotiṣām abhāve ayam kārya kāraṇa saṃgātaḥ puruṣaḥ  yena vyatiriktenā atmanā jyotiṣā vyavaharati iti uktam tad eva na asti yadā adityādi jyoti ṣāma bhāva gamanam yatra idam viviktam svayan jyotiḥ upalabhya uta yena sarva dā eva ayaṅkārya karaṇa saṃghātaḥ saṃsṛṣṭa eva upalabhyeta tasmāt asat samaḥ asan  eva vā svena vivikta svabhāvena jyotīrūpeṇā atmā iti atha kvacid viviktaḥ svena jyotīrūpeṇa upalabhyeta bāhya ādhyātmika bhūta bhautika saṃsarga śūnyaḥ tatas  yathā uktam sarvam bhaviṣyati iti et artham āha sa yaḥ prakṛta ātmā yatra yasmin kāle prasvapiti prakarṣeṇa svāpam anubhavati tadā kim upādānaḥ kena vidhinā svapiti saṃdhyam sthānam pratipadyata iti acyate asya dṛṣṭasya lokasya jāgarita lakṣaṇasya sarvāvataḥ sarvam avati iti sarva  ānayam lokaḥ kārya karaṇa saṃghātaḥ  viṣaya vedanā saṃyuktaḥ sarvāvatvam asya vyākhyātam anna traya prakaraṇe athaḥ ayam vā ātmā ityādinā sarvā vā bhūta bhautika mātrā asya saṃsarga kāṇabhūtā vidyanta iti sarvavān sarvān eva sarvāvān  tasya sarvāvataḥ mātrām eka deśam avayavam apādāya apacchidyā adāya gṛhītvā dṛṣṭa janma vāsanā vāsitaḥ san  iti arthaḥ svayam ātmanā eva vihatya deham pātayitvā niḥsaṃbodham āpādya jāgarite hi oditi ādīnām cakṣuḥ ādiṣu anugrahaḥ  deha vyavavahāra arthaḥ deha vyavahāraḥ cā atmanaḥ  dharma adharma phala upabhoga prayuktaḥ tad dharma adharma phala upabhoga uparamaṇam asmin deha ātma karma uparam kṛtam iti ātmā asya vihantā iti ucyate svayam nirmāya nirmāṇam kṛtvā vāsanā mayam svapna deham māyā mayam iva nirmāṇam api tad karma apekṣa tvāt svayaṅkartṛkam ucyate svenā atmīyena bhāsā mātrā upādāna lakṣaṇena bhāsā dīptyā prakāśena sarva vāsanā ātmakena antaḥkaraṇa vṛkki prakāśena iti arthaḥ sā hi tatra viṣaya bhūtāḥ  sarva vāsanā mayī prakāśate sā tatra svayam bhā ucyate tena svena bhāsā viṣaya bhūtena svena ca jyotiṣā tad viṣayiṇā vivikta rūpeṇa alupta dṛś svabhāvena tad bhāva rūpam vāsanā ātmakam viṣayīkurvan prasvapiti yad evam vartanam tad prasvapiti iti ucyate atra etasyām avasthāyām etasmin kāle ayam puruṣa ātmā svayam eva vivakta jyotiḥ bhavati bāhya ādhyātmika bhūta bhautika saṃsarga rahitam jyotiḥ bhavati nanu asya lokasya mātra upādānam kṛtam katham tasmin satyatrāyam puraṣaḥ svayan jyotiḥ bhavati iti ucyate na eṣa doṣaḥ viṣaya bhūtam eva hi tad  tena eva ca atra ayam puruṣaḥ svayam jyotiḥ darśayitum śakyaḥ na tu anyathā asati viṣaye kasmiṃścid suṣupta kāla iva yadā punar  sā bhā vāsanā ātmikā viṣaya bhūta upalabhyamānā bhavati tadā asiḥ kośāt iva niṣkṛṣṭaḥ sarva saṃsarga rahitam cakṣuḥ ādi kārya karaṇa vyāvṛtta svarūpam alupta dṛś ātma jyotiḥ svena rūpeṇa avabhāsayat gṛhyate tena atra ayam puruśaḥ svayan jyotiḥ bhavati iti siddham nanu atra katham puruṣaḥ svayan jyotiḥ yena jāgarata iva grāhya grāhaka ādi lakṣaṇaḥ sarve vyavahāraḥ  dṛśyate cakṣuḥ ādi anugrāhakāḥ cā aditya ādyā lokāḥ tathā eva dṛśyante yathā jāgarite tatra katham viśeṣa avadhāraṇam kriyate atra ayam puruṣaḥ svayam jyotiḥ bhavati iti ucyate vailakṣaṇyāt svapna darśanasya jāgaritam hi indriya buddha mana āloka ādi vyāpāra saṃkīrṇam ātma jyotiḥ iha tu svapn indriya abhāvāt tad anugrāhakāt ityādi āloka abhāvāt ca viviktam kevalam bhavati tasmāt vilakṣaṇam nanu tathā eva viṣayā upalabhyante svapne api yathā jāgarite tatra katham indrāya abhāvāt vailakṣamyam ucyate iti śṛṇu na tatra liṣayāḥ svapne ratha ādi lakṣaṇāḥ tathā na ratha yogā ratheṣu yujyanta iti ratha yogā aśva ādayaḥ tatra na vidyante na ca panthānaḥ  ratha mārgā bhavanti atha rathān ratha yogān pathaḥ ca sṛjate svayam katham punar  sṛjate ratha ādi sādhanānām vṛkṣa ādīnāṃma bhāve ucyete nanu uktam asya lokasya sarvāvataḥ mātrām apādāya svayam vihatya svayam nirmāya iti antaḥkaraṇa vṛttiḥ asya lokasya vyavatiṣṭhate tad ucyate svayam nirmāya iti tad evā aha ratha ādīn sṛjata iti na tu tatra karaṇam vā karaṇa anugrāga kāṇi vā aditi ādi jyotīṃṣi tad avabhāsyā vā rathāt ayaḥ  viṣayā vidyante tad vāsanā mātram tu kevalam tad upalabdhi karma nimitta codita udbhūta antaḥkaraṇa vṛtyā āśrayam dṛśyate tad yasya jyotiṣaḥ  dṛśyate alupta dṛśaḥ tad ātma jyotiḥ atra kevalam asiḥ iva kośāt vivivaktam tathā na tatrā anandāḥ sukha viśeṣā mudaḥ  harṣā putra ādi lābha nimittāḥ pramudaḥ ta eva prakorṣa upetāḥ atha cā ananda ādīn sṛjate tathā na tatra veśa antāḥ palvalāḥ puṣkariṇyaḥ taḍāgāḥ sravanti aḥ  nadyaḥ  bhavanti atha veśānta ādīn sṛjate vāsanā mātra rūpān yasmāt sa hi kartā tdava āsana aśracitta vṛti udbhava nimitta karma hetu tvena iti avocāma tasya kartṛ tvam na tu sākṣāt eva tatra kriyā saṃbhavati sādhana abhāvāt  na hi kārakam antareṇa kriyā saṃbhavati na ca tatra hasta pāda ādīni kriyā kārakāṇi saṃbhavanti yad ka tu tāni vidyante jāgarite tatrā atma jyotiḥ ava bhāsitaiḥ kārya karaṇaiḥ  ratha ādi vāsanā āśraya antaḥkaraṇa vṛti udbhava nimittam karma nivartyate tena ucyate sa hi kartā iti tad uktam ātmanā eva ayam jyotiṣā aste palyayate karma kuruta iti tatra api na paramārthataḥ svatas  kartṛ tvam caitanya jyotiṣaḥ  avabhāsakatva vyatirekeṇa yad caitanya ātma jyotiṣā antaḥkaraṇa dvāreṇa annādyam iti ādi vāsanā nirmitam ākrīḍana rūpam na te paśyati tam na paśyati kaścana kaṣṭam bhaḥ vartate atyanta viviktam dṛṣṭi gocara āpannam api ahaḥ bhāgya hīna tā lokasya yad śakya darśanam api jyotiṣaḥ  vyatirikta tve kāsau tam ātmānam suptam āyatam sahasā bhṛśam na bodhayet iti āhuḥ evam kathayanti cikatsakādayaḥ  janā loke nūnam te paśyanti jāgrat dehāt indriya dvārataḥ  apasṛtya kevalaḥ  bahis vartata iti yata āhuḥ tam nā ayatam bodhayet iti tatra ca doṣam paśyanti bhṛśam hi asau bodhyamānaḥ tāni indriya dvārāṇi sahasā pratibodhyamānaḥ  na pratipadyata iti tad etad āha durbhiṣajyam ha ratha yogā ityādi tasmāt atra ayam puraṣaḥ svayan jyotiḥ bhavati eva svayan jyotiḥ ātmā asti iti svapna nidarśena pradarśitam atikrāmati mṛtyaḥ rūpāṇi iti ca krameṇa saṃcarat niga loka para loka ādīn iha loka para loka ādi vyatiriktaḥ tathā jāgrat svapna kulāyābhyām vyatiriktaḥ tatra ca kāma saṃcārāt nityaḥ ca iti etad pratipad ā āditam yājñavalkyena atas  vidyā niṣkriya artham sahasram dadāmi iti āha janakaḥ saḥ  aham evam bodhitaḥ tvayā abhagavate tubhyam sahasram dadāmi vimokṣaḥ ca kāma praśnaḥ mayā abhipretaḥ tad upayogyayam tadārthyāt tad eka deśa eva itas tvām niyokṣyāmi samasta kāma praśna nirṇaya śravaṇena vimokṣa āyāta ūrdhvam brūhi iti yena saṃsārāt vipramucyeyam tvad prasādāt  vimokṣa padārtha eka deśa nirṇaya hetoḥ sahasra dānam yad prastutam ātmanā eva ayam jyotiṣā asta iti tad pratyakṣataḥ pratipāditam atra ayam puruṣaḥ svayan jyotiḥ bhavati iti svapne yad tu uktam svpanaḥ  bhūtvā imam lokam atikrāmati mṛtyaḥ rūpāṇi iti tatra etad āśaṅkayte mṛtyaḥ rūpāṇi eva atikrāmati na mṛtyum pratyakṣam hi etad svapne kārya rakaraṇa vyāvṛttasya apu moda trāsa ādi darśanam tasmāt nūnam na eva ayam mṛtyum atikrāmati karmaṇaḥ  hi mṛtyoḥ kāryam modatra āsa ādi dṛśyate yadi ca mṛtyunā svayan jyotiḥ puruṣaḥ eṣa yaḥ svapne pradarśita etasmin saṃprasāde samyak prasīdati asmin  iti saṃprasādaḥ jāgarite deha indriya vyāpāra śata saṃnipāta jam hitvā kāluṣyam tebhyaḥ  vipramukta īṣat śramam upalabhya iti arthaḥ dṛṣṭvā eva na kṛtvā iti arthaḥ puṇyam ca puṇya phalam pāpam ca pāpa phalam na tu puṇya pāpayoḥ sākṣāt dadarśanam asti iti avocāma tasmāt na puṇya pāpābhyām anu baddhaḥ yaḥ
