ātma svabhāvatva āśaṅkā mṛtyuḥ ced svabhāvaḥ  astha  svapne api kuryāt  na tu karoti svabhāvaḥ ced kriyā syāt anirmokṣa tā eva syāva na tu svabhāvaḥ svapne abhāvāt  atas  vimokṣaḥ  asya upapadyate na svābhāvikatva śaṅkā nirmokṣa tā vā tatra caritvā iti caraṇa phalam śramam upalabhya iti arthaḥ tatas  saṃprasāda anuvabha uttara kālam punar  pratinyāyam yathānyāyam yathāgatam niścita āyaḥ nyāyaḥ svapna antam ca buddha antam ca dṛṣṭānta pradarśana phalam tu mṛtyu rūpaḥ kārya karaṇa saṃghātaḥ saha tad prayojakābhyām kāma karmabhyām anātma dharma uyam cā atmā etasmāt vilakṣaṇa iti vistarataḥ  vyākhyātam atra ca sthāna traya anusaṃtāreṇa svayan jyotiṣa ātmanaḥ kārya karaṇa saṃghāta vyatiriktasya kāma karmabhyām vivakta tā uktā svatas  na ayam saṃsāra dharma vān upādhi nimittam eva tu asya saṃsāri tvam avidyā adhyāropitam iti eṣa samudāya artha uktaḥ tatra ca jāgrat svapna suṣupta sthānānām trayāṇām viprakīrṇa rūpa uktaḥ  na puñjīkṛtya ekatra darśitaḥ yasmāt jāgarite sa saṅgaḥ sa mṛtyuḥ sa kārya karaṇa saṃghāta upalakṣyate avidyayā svapne tu kāma saṃyuktaḥ  mṛtyu rūpa vinirmukta upalabhyate suṣupte punar buddha antam āgataḥ  buddha antāt ca suṣupte saṃprasannaḥ  asaṅgaḥ  bhavati iti asaṃgatā api dṛśyate eka vākyatayā tu upasaṃhrayamāṇam phalam nitya mukta buddha śuddha svabhāva tā asya na ekatra puñjīkṛtya pradarśitā iti tad pradarśanāya kaṇḍikā arabhyate suṣupte hi evaṃrūpa tā asya vakṣyamāṇā tad vā asya etad aticchandā apahata pāpmā abhayam rūpāmi ti yasmāt evaṃrūpam vilakṣaṇam suṣuptam pravivikṣati tad katham iti āha dṛṣṭāntena asya arthasya prakaṭībhāvaḥ  bhavati iti tatra dṛṣṭānta upādīyate tad yathā asmin  ākāśe bhautike śyenaḥ  vā suparṇaḥ  vā su praṇa śabdena kṣipraḥ śyena ucyate yathā akāśe asmin vihṛtya viparipatya śrāntaḥ  nānā paripatana lakṣaṇena karmaṇā parikhinnaḥ saṃhṛtya pakṣau saṃgamayya pakṣau samyak līyate asmin  iti saṃlayaḥ  nīḍaḥ  nīḍāya eva dhriyate sva ātmanā eva dhrāyate svayam eva yathā ayam dṛṣṭānta evam eva ayam puruṣa etasyāḥ  etasmai antāya dhāvati anta śabda vācyasya viśeṣaṇam yatra yasmin  ante suptaḥ  na kañcana na kañcid api kāmam kāmayate tathā ca na kañcana svapnam paśyati na kañcana kām iti svapn buddha antayoḥ aviśeṣeṇa sarvaḥ kāmaḥ pratiṣidhyate kañcana iti avaśeṣita abhidhānāt tathā na kañcana svapnam iti jāgarite api yad darśanam tad api svapnam manyate śrutirata āha na kañcana svapnam paśyati iti tathā ca śruti antaram tasya traya āvasathāḥ trayaḥ svapnāḥ iti yathā dṛṣṭānte pakṣiṇaḥ paripatana ja śrama apanupattaye sva nīḍa aupasarpaṇam evam jāgrat svapnayoḥ kārya karaṇa saṃyoga ja kriyā phalaiḥ saṃyujyamānasya pakṣiṇaḥ paripatana ja iva śramaḥ  bhavaci tad śmāpa nuttaye sva ātmanaḥ  nīḍām āyatanam sarva saṃsāra dharma vilakṣaṇam sarva kriyā kāraka phala āyāsa śūnyam svam ātmānam praviśati yadi asya ayam svabhāvaḥ sarva saṃsāra dharma śūnyatā para upādhi nimittam ca asya saṃsāra dharmi tvam yad nimittam ca asya para upādhikṛtam saṃsāra dharmi tvam sā ca avidyā tasyāḥ  avidyāyāḥ  kim svābhāvika tvam āhosvid kāma karma ādivat āgantuka tvam yadi cā agantuka tvam tatas  vimokṣa upapadyate tasyāḥ cā agantuka tve kopa pattiḥ katham vā nā atma dharmaḥ  avidyā iti sarva anartha bīja bhūtāyāḥ  avidyāyāḥ satatva avadhāraṇa artham parā kaṇḍikā arabhyate tā vā asya śiraḥ pāṇi ādi lakṣaṇasya puruṣasya etā hitā nāma nāḍyaḥ  yathā keśaḥ sahasradhā bhinnaḥ tāvatā tāvat parimāṇena aṇimnā aṇu tvena tiṣṭhanti tāśṭa śuklasya rasasya nīlasya piṅgalasya haritasya lohitasya pūrṇā etaiḥ śuklatva ādibhī rasa viśeṣaiḥ pūrṇā iti arthaḥ ethe ca rasānām varṇa viśeṣā vāta pitta śleṣmaṇām itaretara saṃyoga vaiṣamya viśeṣāt vicitrā bahavaḥ ca bhavanti tāsu evavidhāsu nāḍīṣu sūkṣmāsu bāla agra sahasra bheda parimāṇāsu śukla ādi rasa pūrṇāsu sarala deha vyāpinīṣu saptadaśakam liṅgam vartate tad āśritāḥ sarvā vāsanā uccāvaca saṃsāra dharma anubhava janitāḥ tad liṅgam vāsanā āśrayam sūkṣma tvāt su accham sphaṭika maṇi kalpam nāḍī gata rasa upādhi saṃsarga vaśāt dharma adharma prerita udbhūta vṛtti viśeṣam strī ratha hasti ādi ākāra viśeṣaiḥ vāsanābhiḥ pratyavabhāsate atha evam sati yatra yasmin kāle kecana śatravaḥ  anye vā taskarā mām āgatya ghnanti iti mṛṣā eva vāsanā nimittaḥ pratyayaḥ avidyā ākhyaḥ  jāyate tad etad ucyata enam svapna dṛśaṅghnanti iva iti tathā hastī iva enam vicchāyayati vicchādayati vidrāvayati dhāvayati iva iti arthaḥ gartam iva patati gartam jīrṇa kūpa ādikam iva patantam ātmānam upalakṣayati tādṛśī hi asya mṛṣā vāsanā udbhavati atyanta nikṛṣṭa adharma udbhāsita antaḥkaraṇa vṛtya āśrayā duḥkha svarūpa vṛtyā āśrayā duḥkha svarūpa tvāt kiṃbahunā yad eva jāgrat bhayam hasti ādi lakṣaṇam tad eva bhaya rūpam atra asmin svapne vinā eva hasti ādi rūpam bhayam avidyā vāsanayā mṛṣā eva udbhūtayā manyate atha punar yatra avidyā apakṛṣyamāṇā vidyā ca utkṛṣyamāṇā kiṃviṣayā kiṃlakṣaṇā ca iti ucyate atha punar yatra yasmin kāle deva iva svayam bhavati devatā viṣayā vidyā yadā udbhūtā jāgarita kāle tadā udbhūtayā vāsanayā devam ivā atmānam manyate svapne api tad ucyate deva iva rājā iva rājya sthaḥ  abhiṣiktaḥ svapne api rājā aham iti manyate rāja vāsanā vāsitaḥ evam atyanta prakṣīyamāṇā vidyā udbhūtā ca vidyā sarva ātma viṣayā yadā yadā svapne api tad bhāvitaḥ  aham eva idam sarvaḥ  asmi iti manyate sa yaḥ sarva ātma bhāvaḥ saḥ  asyāḥ atmanaḥ paramaḥ  lokaḥ parama  ātma bhāvaḥ svābhāvakaḥ yad tu sarva ātma bhāvāt arvāc bāla agra mātram api anya tvena dṛśyate na aham asmi iti tad avasthā vidyī tayā avidyayā ye pratyupasthāpitā anātma bhāvā lokāḥ te aparamāḥ sthāvara antāḥ tān saṃvyavahāra viṣayān  lokān apekṣma ayam sarva ātma bhāvaḥ samastaḥ  anantaraḥ  abāhyaḥ saḥ  asya paramaḥ  lokaḥ tasmāt apakṛṣyamāṇāyām avidyāyām vidyāyām ca kāṣṭām gatāyām sarva ātma bhāvaḥ  mokṣaḥ yathā svayan jyotiṣṭvam svapne pratyakṣata eva upalabhyate atha yatra enam ghnanti iva jinanti iva iti te ete vidyā avidyā kārye sarva ātma bhāvaḥ paricchinna ātma bhāvaḥ ca vidyayā śuddhayā sarva ātmā bhavati avidyayā ca asarvaḥ  bhavati anyatas  kutas cad pravibhaktaḥ  bhavati yatas  pravabhaktaḥ  bhavati tena virudhyate viruddha tvāt hanyate jīyate vicchādyate ca asarva viṣaya tve ca bhinna tvāt etad bhavati samastaḥ tu sankutaḥ bhidyate yena virudhyetaviroda abhāve kena hanyate jīyate vicchādyate ca ata idam avidyāyāḥ sattvam uktam bhavati sarva ātmānam santam asarva ātma tvena grāhayati ātmanaḥ  anyadhaḥ tvaram avidyamānam pratyupasthāpayati ātmānam asarvam āpādayati tatas tad viṣayaḥ kāmaḥ  bhavati yatas  bhidyate kāmataḥ kriyām upādatte tatas  phalam tad etad uktam vakṣyamāṇam ca yatra hi dvaitam iva bhavati tad itara itaram paśyati ityādi idam avidyāyāḥ sata tvam saha kāryeṇa pradarśitam vidyāyāḥ ca kāryam sarvam ātma bhāvaḥ pradarśitaḥ  avidyāyāḥ  viparyeṇa sā ca avidyā nā atmanaḥ svābhāvikaḥ  dharmaḥ  yasmāt vidyāyām utkṛṣyamāṇāyām svayam apacīyamānā satī kāṣṭhām gatāyām vidyāya aṃpari niṣṭhite sarva ātma bhāve sarva ātmanā nivartate rajjvām iva sarpa jñānam rajju niścaye tad ca uktam yatra tu asya sarvam ātmā eva abhūt tad kena kam paśyet ityādi tasmāt nā atma dharmaḥ  avidyā na hi svābhāvikasya ucchittiḥ kadācid api upadyate savituḥ iva uṣṇya prakāśayoḥ tasmāt tasyāḥ  mokṣa aupapadyate idānīm yaḥ  asau sarva ātma bhāvaḥ  mokṣaḥ  vidyā phalam kriyā kāraka phala śūnyam sa pratyakṣataḥ nirdiśyate yatra avidyā kāma karmāṇi na santi tad etad prastutam yatra suptaḥ  na kañcana kāmam kāmayate na kañcana svapnam paśyāti iti tad etad vā asya rūpam yaḥ sarva ātma bhāvaḥ asaḥ  asya paramaḥ  lokaḥ aiti uktaḥ tad aticchandā aticchandam iti arthaḥ rūpa paratvāt chandaḥ kāmaḥ atigataḥ candaḥ  yasmāt  rūpāt  tad aticchandam rūpam  anyaḥ  asau sāntar chandaḥ śabdaḥ  gāyatrī ādi chanda uvācī  ayam tu kāma vacanaḥ atas  svara anta eva  tathā api aticchandā iti pāṭhaḥ svādhyāya dharmaḥ  draṣṭavyaḥ asti ca loke kāma vacana prayuttkaḥ chanda śabdaḥ asvacchandaḥ aparacchandaḥ iti ādau  atas  aaticchandam iti evam upaneyam kāma varjitam etad  rūpam iti asmin  arthe tathā apahata pāpma pāpma ṣabdena dharma adharmau  ucyete pāpmabhiḥ saṃsṛjyate pāpmanaḥ  vijahāti iti uttka tvāt  apahata pāpma dharma adharma varjitam iti etad  kiñca abhayam bhayam hi nāma avidyā kāryam aavidyayā bhayam manyate iti hi uttkam tad kārya dvāreṇa kāraṇa pratiṣedhaḥ  ayam  abhayam rūpam iti āvidyā varjitam iti etad  tad etad  vidyā phalam sarvatma bhāvaḥ tad etad itad chanda apahata pāpma abhayam rūpam sarva saṃsāra dharma varjitam ate abhayam rūpam etad  idam ca pūrvam eva upanyasyam atīta anantara brahmaṇa samāptau abhayam vai janaka prāptaḥ  asi iti āgamataḥ iha tu tarkataḥ prapañcitam darśita āgama artha pratyaya dārḍhyāya ayam ātmā svayam caitanya jyotiḥ svabhāvaḥ sarvam svena caitanya jyotiṣā avabhāsayati sa yad tatra kiñcid  paśyati ramatecarati jānāti ca iti uttkam sthitam ca etad nyāyataḥ  nityam svarūpam caitanya jyotiṣṭvam ātmanaḥ sa yad yātma atra avinaṣṭaḥ svena eva rūpeṇa vartate kasmāt ayam aham asmi iti ātmānam vā bahis vā imāni bhūtāni iti jāgrat svapnayoḥ iva na jānāti iti atra ucyate  śṛṇvātra ajñāna hetum eka tvam eva ajñāna hetuḥ  tad  katham iti ucyate dṛṣṭāntena hi pratyakṣībhavati vivakṣitor atha iti āha tad tatra yathā loke priyayā iṣṭāyāḥ  striyā sampariṣvattakaḥ samyak  pariṣvattkaḥ kāmayantyā kāmukaḥ san na bāhyam ātmanaḥ kiñcana kiñcid api veda mattaḥ  anyat  vastu iti na ca antaram ayam aham ā asmi sukhī duḥkhī vā iti  apariṣvatt kastu tathā pravibhatt kaḥ jānāti sarva bheva brāhyam ābhyantaram ca  pariṣvaṅga uttara kālantu ekatva āpatteḥ na jānāti evam eva yathā dṛṣṭāntaḥ  ayam puruṣaḥ kṣetrajñaḥ  bhūta mātra asaṃsargataḥ saindhava khilyavat  pravibhattkaḥ jala ādau candra ādi pratibimbavat kārya karaṇa iha praviṣṭaḥ saḥ  ayam puruṣaḥ prajñena parama arthena svābhāvikena svena ātmanā pareṇa jyotiṣā sampariṣvattkaḥ samyak pariṣvakta ekībhūtaḥ  nirantaraḥ sarva ātmā na bāhyam kiñcana vastu antaram na api āntaram ātmani ayam aham asmi sukhī duḥkhī vā iti veda tatra caitanya jyotiḥ svabhāva tve kasmāt iha na jānāti iti yad aprākṣīḥ tatra ayam hetuḥ mayā uttka eka tvam yathā strīpuṃsayoḥ sampariṣvattkayoḥ tatra arthān nānā tvam viśeṣa vijñāna hetuḥ iti uttkam bhavati  nānātve ca kāraṇ ātmanaḥ  vastavantarasya pratyupasthāpikā avidyā iti uktam tatra ca avidyāyā yadā praviviktaḥ  bhavati tadā sarveṇa eka tvam eva asya bhavati tatas ca jñāna jñeya ādi kāraka vibhāge asati kutaḥ viśeṣa vijñāna prādurbhāvaḥ kāmaḥ  vā sambhavati svābhāvike svarūpstha ātma jyotiṣi yasmāt evam sarva eka tvam eva asya rūpam atas tad vā asyāḥ atmanaḥ svayan jyotiḥ sva bhavasya etad rūpam āpta kāmam yasma ātmaḥ tam etad tasmāt āptāḥ kāmā asmin rūpe tad idam āpta kāmam sya hi anya tvena pravibhaktaḥ kāmaḥ tad anāpta kāmam bhavati yathā jāgarita avasthāyām devadatta ādi rūpam na tu idam tathā kutaścid pravibhajyate atas tad āpta kāmam bhavati kim anyasmāt vastu antarāt na pravibhajyata āhosvit ātmā eva tad vastu antaramata āha na anyat asti ātmanaḥ katham yata ātma kāmam ātmā eva kāmā yasmin rūpe anyatra pravibhaktā iva anya tvena kāmyamānā yathā yathā jāgrat svapnayoḥ tasyā atmā eva anyatva pratyupasthāpaka hetoḥ avidyāyāḥ  abhāvāt ātma kāmam ata eva akāmam etad rūpam kāmya viṣaya abhāvāt śoka antaram śāka  chidram śoka śūnyam iti etad śoka madhyam iti vā sarvathā api aśokam etad rūpam śoka varjitam iti arthaḥ prakṛtaḥ svayan jyotiḥ ātma avidyā kāma karma vinirmukta iti uktam asaṅga tvāt ātmanaḥ  āgantuka tvāt ca teṣām tatra evam āśaṅkā jāyate caitanya svabhāva tve sati api ekībhāvāt na jānāti strīpuṃsayoḥ iva saṃpariṣvaktayoḥ iti uktam tatra prāsaṅgikam etad uktam kāma krama ādivat svayan jyotiṣṭvam api asyā atmanaḥ  na svabhāvaḥ yasmāt saṃprasāde na upalabhyata iti āśaṅkāyām prāptāyām tad nirākaraṇāya strīpuṃsayoḥ dṛṣṭānta upādānena vidyamānasya eva svayan jyotiṣṭvasya suṣupte agrahaṇam ekībhāvāt hetoḥ na tu kāma karma ādivat āgantukam iti etad prāsaṅgikam abhidhāya yad prakṛtam tad eva anupravartayati atra ca etad prakṛtam avidyā kāma karma vinirmuktam eva tad rūpam yad suṣupta ātmanaḥ  gṛhyate pratyakṣata iti tad etad yathābhūtam eva abhihitam sarva saṃbandha atītam etad rūpam iti yasmāt atra etasmin suṣupta sthāne atichchanda apahata pāpmā abhayam etad rūpam tasmāt atra pitā janakaḥ tasya ca janayitṛ tvāt yad pitṛ tvam putram prati tad karma nimittam tena ca karmaṇā ayam asaṃbaddhaḥ  asmin kāle tasmāt pitā putra saṃbandha nimittāt karmaṇaḥ  vinirmukta tvāt pitā api apitā bhavati tathā putraḥ  api pituḥ aputra ubhavati iti sāmarthyāt gamyate ubhayoḥ hi saṃbandha nimittam karma tamayatikrāntaḥ  vartate apahata pāpmā iti hi uktam tathā amātā mātā lokāḥ karmaṇā jetavyā jitāḥ ca tad karma saṃbandha abhāvāt lokā alokāḥ tathā devāḥ karma aṅga bhūtāḥ tad karma saṃbandha atyayāt devā adevāḥ tathā vedāḥ sādhya sādhana saṃbandha abhidhāyakā mantra lakṣaṇāḥ ca abhidhāka tvena karma aṅga bhūtā adhītā adhyetavyāḥ ca karma nimittam eva saṃbadhyante puruṣeṇa tad karma atikramaṇāt etasmin kāle vedā api avedāḥ saṃpadyante na kevalam śubha karma saṃbandha atītaḥ kim tarhi aśubhaiḥ api atyanta ghoraiḥ karmabhiḥ asaṃbaddha eva ayam vartata iti atam arthām āha atra stenaḥ  brāhmaṇa suvarṇa hartā bhrūṇa ghnā saha pāṭhāt avagamyate sa tena ghoroṇa karmaṇā etasmin kāle vinirmuktaḥ  bhavati yena ayam karmaṇā mahāpātakī stena ucyate tathā bhrūṇa hā abhrūṇa hā tathā cāṇḍālaḥ  na kevalam pratyutpannena eva karmaṇā vinirmuktaḥ kim tarhi sahajena api atyanta nikṛṣṭa jāti prāpakeṇa api vinirmukta eva ayam cāṇḍālaḥ  nāma śūdreṇa brāhmaṇyām utpannaḥ caṇḍāla eva cāṇḍālaḥ sa jāti nimittena karmaṇā saṃbaddha tvāt acāṇḍālaḥ  bhavati paulkasaḥ pulkasa eva paulkasaḥ śūdreṇa eva kṣatriyāyām utpannaḥ saḥ  api apulkasaḥ  bhavati tathā aśrama lakṣaṇaiḥ ca karmabhiḥ asaṃbagaddhaḥ  bhavati iti ucyate śramaṇaḥ parivrāḍyat karma nimittaḥ  bhavati sa tena vinirmukta tvāt aśramaṇaḥ tathā pāpasaḥ  vānaprasthaḥ  atāpasaḥ sarveṣām varṇa āśrama ādīnām upalakṣaṇa artham ubhayoḥ grahaṇam kim bahunā anvāgatam na anvāgatam ananva āgatam asaṃbandham iti etad puṇyena śāstra vihitena karmaṇā tathā pāpena vihita akaraṇa pratiṣiddha kriyā lakṣaṇena rūpa para tvāt napuṃsaka liṅgam abhayam rūpiti hi anuvartate kim punar asaṃbaddha tve kāraṇam iti tad hetuḥ ucyate tīrṇaḥ  atikrāntaḥ  hi yasmāt evaṃrūpaḥ tadā tasmin kāle sarvān śokān śokāḥ kāmāḥ iṣṭa viṣaya prārthanā hi tad viṣaya viyoge śoka tvam āpadyate iṣṭam hi viṣayaṃma prāptam viyuktam ca uddiśya cintayānaḥ tad guṇān saṃtapyate puruṣaḥ  atas  śokaḥ  ratiḥ kāma iti paryāyāḥ yasmāt sarava kāma atītaḥ  hi atra ayam bhavati na kañcana kāmam kāmayate aticchandā iti hi uktam tad prakriyā āpatatas  ayam śoka śahdaḥ kāma vacana eva bhavitum arhati kāmaḥ ca karma hetuḥ vakṣyati hi sa yathākāmaḥ  bhavati tad krayuḥ bhavati yad kratuḥ bhavati tad karma kurute iti atas  sarva kāma atitīrṇa tvāt yuktam ānan vāgatam puṇyena ityādi hṛdayasya hṛdayam iti puṇḍarīka ākāraḥ  māṃsa piṇḍaḥ tad stham antaḥkaraṇam buddharhṛdayam iti ucyate tāt sthān mañcakrośanavat  hṛdayasya buddheḥ ye śokāḥ buddhi saṃśrayā hi te akāmaḥ saṃkalpaḥ  vicikitsā ityādi sarvam mana eva ati ukta tvāt  vakṣyati ca kāmā ye asya hṛdi śritāḥ iti ātma saṃśraya bhrānti apanodāya hi idam vacanam hṛdi śritā hṛdayasya śokā iti ca hṛdaya karaṇa saṃbandha atītaḥ ca ayam asmin kāle atikrāmati mṛtyaḥ rūpāṇi iti hi uktam hṛdaya karaṇa sahandhā atīta tvāt tad saṃśraya kāma saṃbandha atītaḥ  bhavati iti yuktataram vacanam ye tu vādinaḥ  hṛdi śritāḥ kāmā vāsanāḥ ca hṛdaya saṃbandhinam ātmanam upasṛpya upaśliṣyanti hṛdaya viyoge api cā atmani avatiṣṭhante puṭa tailasya iva puṣpa ādi gandha iti ācakṣate teṣām kāmaḥ saṃkalpaḥ  hṛdaye haryova rūpāṇi hṛdayasya śokā ityādīnām vacanānām ānarthakyam eva hṛdaya karaṇa utpādya tvāt iti ced  na hṛdi śritā iti viśeṣaṇāt  na hi hṛdayasya karaṇa mātra tve hṛdi śritā iti vacanam samañjasam hṛdaye hi eva rūpāṇi pratiṣṭhitāni iti ca ātma viśaddeḥ ca vivakṣita tvāt hṛt śrayaṇa vacanam yathārtham eva yuktam dhyāyati iva lelāyati iva iti ca śrureḥ anyā artha asaṃbhavāt  kāmā ye asya hṛdi śritā iti viśeṣaṇāt ātma āśrayā api santi iti ced  na anāśrita apekṣa tvāt na atrā aśraya antaram apekṣya ye hṛdi iti viśeṣaṇam kim tarhi ye hṛdi anāśritāḥ kāmāḥ tān apekṣya viśeṣaṇam ye tu aprarūñā bhaviṣyā bhūtāḥ ca pratipakṣataḥ  nivṛttāḥ te na eva hṛdi śritāḥ saṃbhāvyante ca te atas  yuktam tān apekṣya viśeṣaṇam ye prarūḍhā vartamānā viṣaye te sarve pramucyanta iti tathā api viśeṣaṇa ānarthakyam iti ced  na teṣu yatat mādhikyāt heya artha tvāt itaratha aśrutam aniṣṭam cakalpitam syāt ātma āśraya tvam kāmānām na kañcana kāmam kāmayata iti prāpta pratiṣedhāt ātma āśraya tvam kāmānām śrutam eva iti ced  na sadhīḥ svapnaḥ  bhūtvā iti para nimitta tvāt kāma āśrayatva prāpteḥ asaṅga vacanāt ca na hi kāma āśraya tve asaṅga vacanam upapadyate saṅgaḥ ca kāma iti avocāma ātma kāma iti śruteḥ ātma viṣayaḥ  asya kāmaḥ  bhavati iti ced  na vyatirikta kāma abhāva artha tvāt tasyāḥ vaiśeṣika ādi tantra nyāya upapannam ātmanaḥ kāma ādi āśraya tvam iti ced  na hṛdi śritā ityādi viśeṣa śruti virodha anapekṣyāḥ tā veśeṣikā ādi tantra upapattayaḥ śruti virodhe nyāya bhāsatva upagamāt svayan jyotiṣṭva bādhanāt ca kāma ādīnām ca svapne kevala dṛśi mātra viṣaya tvāt svayan jyotiṣṭvam siddham sthitam ca bādhyeta ātma samavāyi tve dṛśyatva anupapatteḥ cakṣuḥ gata viśeṣavat  draṣṭuḥ hi dṛśyam artha antara bhūtam iti draṣṭuḥ svayan jyotiṣṭvam siddham tad bādhitam syāt yadi kāma ādi āśraya tvam parikalpyet  sarva śāstra artha vipratiṣedhāt ca parasya eka deśa kalpanāyām kāma ādi āśraya tve ca sarva śāstra artha jātam kupyeta etad ca vistareṇa caturthe avocāma mahatā hi prayatnena kāma ādi āśrayatva kalapnājha pratiṣeddhavyā ātmānaḥ pareṇa ekatva śāstra artha siddhayeḥ tad kalpanāyām punar  kriyamāṇāyām śāstra artham eva bādhitaḥ syāt  yathecca adhīnām ātma dharma tvam kalpayantaḥ  vaiśeṣikā naiyāyikāḥ ca upaniṣad śāstra artha bādhanāt nā adaraṇīyā strī puṃsayoḥ iva eka tvāt na paśyati iti uktam svayan jyotiḥ iti ca svayan jyotiḥ iti ca svan jyotiṣṭvam nāma caitanya ātma svabhāva tā yadi hi agni uṣṇatva ādivat caitanya ātma svabhāva ātmā sa katham ekatve api hi svabhāvam jahyāt na jānīyāt  atha na jahāti katham iha suṣupte na paśyati vipratiṣiddham etad caitanyam ātma svabhāvaḥ  na jānāti ca iti na vipratiṣiddham ubhayam api etad upapadyata eva katham yad vai suṣupte tad na paśyati paśyan vai tad tatra paśyan  eva na paśyati yad tatra suṣupte na paśyati iti jānīṣe tad na tathā gṛhṇīyāḥ kasmāt  paśyan vai bhavati tatra nanu ānam na paśyati iti suṣupte jānīme yatas  na cakṣuḥ vā manaḥ  vā darśane karaṇam vyāpṛtam asti vyāpṛteṣu hi darśana śravaṇa ādiṣu paśyati iti vyavahāraḥ  bhavati śṛṇoti iti vā na ca vyāpṛtāni karaṇāni paśyāmaḥ tasmāt na paśyati eva ayam na hi kim tarhi paśyan  eva bhavati katham na hi yasmāt draṣṭuḥ dṛṣṭa kartuḥ yā dṛṣṭiḥ tasyāḥ  dṛṣṭeḥ viparilopaḥ  vināśaḥ sa na vidyate yathā agneḥ auṣṇyam hi sā nanu vipratiṣiddham idam abhidhīyate draṣṭuḥ sā dṛṣṭiḥ na viparilupyata ita ca aśakyam vaktum nanu na viparilupyata iti vacanāt avināśinī syāt  na vanacasya jñāpaka tvāt  na hi nyāya prāptaḥ  vināśaḥ kṛtakasya vacana śatena api vārayitum śakyate vacanasya jñāpaka tvāt  na hi nyāya prāptaḥ  vināśaḥ kṛtakasya vacana śatena apu vārayitum śakyate vacanasya yathāprāpta artha jñāpaka tvāt na eṣa doṣaḥ āditya ādi prakāśaka tvavat darśana upapatteḥ yathā adityādayaḥ  nitya prakāśa svabhāvā eva santaḥ svābhāvikena nityena eva prakāśena prakāśayanti na hi aprakāśa ātmānaḥ santaḥ prakāśam kurvantaḥ prakāśayanti iti ucyante kim tarhi svabhāvena eva nityena prakāśena tathā ayam api ātmā viparilupta svabhāvayā dṛṣṭyā nityayā draṣṭā iti ucyante gauṇam tarhi draṣṭu tvam na evam eva mukhyatva upapatteḥ yadi hi anyathā api ātmanaḥ  draṣṭu tvam dṛṣṭam tadā asya draṣṭu tvasya gauṇa tvam na tu ātmanaḥ  anyaḥ  darśana prakāraḥ  asti tad evam eva mukhyam draṣṭu tvam upapadyate na anyathā yathā adityādīnām prakāśayitṛ tvam nityena eva sva bhāvikena akriyamāṇena prakāśakena tad eva ca prakāśayitṛ tvam mukhyam prakāśayitṛtva antara anupapatteḥ tasmāt na draṣṭuḥ dṛṣṭiḥ viparilupyata ita na vipratiṣedha gandhaḥ  api asti nanu anitya kriyā kartṛ viṣaya eva tṛd pratyaya antasya śabdasya prayogaḥ  dṛṣṭaḥ  yathā chettā bhettā gantā iti tathā draṣṭā iti atra api iti ced  na prakāśayitā iti dṛṣṭa tvāt  bhavatu prakāśakeṣu anyathā saṃbhavān na tu ātmani iti ced  na dṛṣṭi aviparilopa śruteḥ paśyāmi na paśyāmi iti anubhava darśanāt na iti ced  na karaṇa vyāpāra viśeṣa apekṣa tvāt uddhṛta cakṣuṣām ca svapn ātma dṛṣṭeḥ aviparulopadarśanāt  tasmāt avipulupta svabhāva evā atmanaḥ  dṛṣṭaḥ atasya avipariluptayā dṛṣṭyā svayan jyotiḥ svabhāvayā paśyan  eva bhavati suṣupte katham tarhi na paśyati iti ucyate na tu tad asti kim tad  dvitīyam viṣaya bhūtam kiṃvaśiṣṭam tatas  draṣciḥ anyat anya tvena vibhaktam yad paśyet yad upalabheta yad hi tad viśeṣa darśana kāraṇam antaḥkaraṇam cakṣū rūpam ca tad avidyayā anyatvena pratyupasthāpitam āsīt  tad etasmin kāla ekībhutam ātmanaḥ pareṇa pariṣvaṅgāt  draṣṭuḥ hi paricchinnasya viśeṣa darśanāya karaṇam anya tvena vyatiṣṭhate ayam tu svena sarva ātmanā saṃpiṣvaktaḥ svena pareṇa prājñenā atmanā priyayā iva puruṣaḥ tena na pṛthaktvena vyavasthitāni karaṇāni viṣayāḥ ca tad abhāvāt viśeṣa darśanam na asti karaṇa ādi kṛtam hi tad nā atma kṛtam ātma kṛtam iva pratyavabhāsate tasmāt ta kṛtā iyam bhrāntiḥ ātmanaḥ  dṛṣṭiḥ parilupyataca iti samānam anyat  yad vai tad na jighrati yad vai tad na rasayate yad vai tad na vadati yad vai tad na śṛṇoti yad vai tatra manute yad vai tad na spṛśati yad vai tad na spṛśati yad vai tad na vijānāti iti manana vijñānayoḥ dṛṣṭi ādi sahakāri tve api sati cakṣuḥ ādi nirapekṣe bhūta bhaviṣyat vartamāna viṣaya vyāpāraḥ  vidyata iti pṛthak grahaṇam kim punar dṛṣṭi ādīnām agneḥ auṣṇya prakāśana jvalana ādivat dharma bheda āhosvit abhinnasya eva dharmasya para upādhi nimittam dharma anyatvam iti atra kecid vyācakṣate ātma vastunaḥ svata eva eka tvam nānā tvam ca yathā goḥ godravya tayā eka tvam nānā tvam ca anumeyam sarvatra avyabhicāra darśanāt ātmanaḥ  api tadvat eva dṛṣṭi ādīnām parasparam nānā tvam ātmanā ca eka tvam iti na anya paratvāt na hi dṛṣṭi ādi dharma bheda pradarśa param idam vākyam yad vai tad ityādi kim tarhi yadi caitanya ātma jyotiḥ katham na jānāti suṣupte nūnam atas  na caitanya ātmajyotiḥ iti evam āśaṅkā prāptau tad nirākaraṇayā etad ārabdham yad vai tad ityādi yad asya jāgrat svapnayoḥ cakṣuḥ ādi aneka upādhi dvāram caitanya ātma jyotiḥ svābhāvyam upalakṣitam dṛṣṭi ādi abhidheya vyavahāra āpannam suṣuptam upādhi bheda vyāpāra nivṛttau  anudbhāsyamāna tvāt anupalakṣyamāṇa svabhāvam api upādhi bhedena bhinnam iva yathā prāpta anuvādena eva vidyam āntavam ucyate tatra dṛṣṭi ādi dharma bheda kalpanā vivakṣita artha anabhijña tayā saindhava ghanavat prajñāna eka rasa ghana śruti virodhāt ca vijñānam anandam satyam jñānam prajñānam brahma ityādi śrutibhyaḥ ca śabda pravṛteḥ ca laukikaḥ  ca śabda pravṛttaḥ cakṣuṣā rūpam vijānāti śrotreṇa śabdam vijānāti rasanena annasya rasam vijānāti iti ca sarvatra eva ca dṛṣṭi ādi śabda abhidheyānām vijñāna śabda vācyatām eva darśayati śabda pravṛttiḥ ca pramāṇam dṛṣṭānta upapatteḥ ca yathā hi loke svaccha svābhāvya yuktaḥ sphacikaḥ tad nimittam eva kevalam harita nīla lohita ādi upādhi bheda saḥ yāgāt tad ākāra tvam śakyante tathā cakṣuḥ ādi upādhi bheda saṃyogat prajñāna ghana svabhāvasya evā atma jyotiṣaḥ  dṛṣṭi ādi śakti bheda upalakṣyate prajñāna ghanasya svaccha svābhāvyāt sphaṭika svaccha svābhāvyavat svayan jyotiṣṭvāt ca yathā śakti bheda upalakṣyate yathā cā aditya jyotiravabhāsya bhedaiḥ saṃyujyamānam harita nīla pīta lohita ādi bhedaiḥ avibhāgyam tad ākāra abhāvam bhavati tathā ca kṛtsnañjagat avabhāsayat cakṣuḥ ādīni ca tad ākāram bhavati tathā ca uktam ātmanā eva ayam jyotiṣā asta ityādi na ca nivayaveṣu aneka ātma tā śakyate kalpayitum dṛṣṭānta abhāvāt yad api ākāśasya sarva gatatva ādi dharma bhedaḥ parikalpyate paramāṇu ādīnām ca gandha rasa ādi aneka guṇa tvam tad api nirīpyamāṇam para upādhi nimittam eva bhavati ākāśasyatāvat sarvaga tvam nāma na svatas  dharmaḥ  asti sarva upādhi saṃśrayāt hi sarvatra svena rūpeṇa sattvam apekṣya sarvagatva vyavahāraḥ  na tu ākāśaḥ kvacid gataḥ  vāgataḥ  vā svatas  gamanam hi nāma deśa antara sthasya deśa antareṇa saṃyoga kāraṇam sā ca kriyā na eva aviśeṣe saṃbhavati eva dharma bhedā na eva santi ākāśe tathā paramāṇu ādau  api paramāṇuḥ nāma pṛthivyāḥ  gandha ghanāyāḥ parama sūkṣmaḥ  avayavaḥ  gandha ātmaka eva na tasya purgandhavattva nāma śakyate kalpayitum atha tasya eva rasa ādima tvam syāt iti ced na tatra api abādi saṃsa sarga nimitta tvāt tasmāt na niravayavasya aneka dharmavat tve dṛṣṭāntaḥ  sti etena dṛś ādi śakti bhedānām pṛthak cakṣu rūpa ādi bhedena pariṇāma bheda kalpanā parama ātmani prayuktā jāgrat svapnayoḥ iva yad vijānīyāt tad dvitīyam pravibhaktam anya tvena na asti iti uktam atas  suṣupte na vijānāti viśeṣamṣa nanu yadi asya ayam eva svabhāvaḥ kiṃnimittam asya viśeṣa vijñānam svabhāva parityāgena atha viśeṣa vijñānam eva asya svabhāvaḥ kasmāt eṣa viśeṣam na vijānāti iti ucyate śṛṇu yatra yasmiḍh jāgarite svapne vā anyat ivā atmanaḥ  vastu antaram iva avidyayā pratyupasthāpitam bhavati tatra tasmāt avidyā pratyupasthāpitāt anyaḥ  anyam ivā atmānam manyamānaḥ  asati ātmanaḥ pravibhakte vastu antare asati ca ātmani tatas  pravibhakte anyaḥ  anyat paśyet upalabheta tad ca darśitam svapne pratyakṣataḥ ghnanti iva jinanti iva iti tathā anyaḥ  anyat jighret rasayet vadet śṛṇuyāt manvāti spṛśet vijānīyāt iti yatra punar  sā avidyā suṣupte vastu antara pratyupasthāpikā śāntā tena anya tvena avidyā pravibhaktasya vastunaḥ  abhāvāt kena kam paśyet jighret vijānīyāt vā atas  svena eva hi prājñena aatmanā sva yan jyotiḥ svabhāvena saṃpariṣvaktaḥ samastaḥ saṃprasanna āpta kāma  ātma kāmaḥ salilavaḥ tvad śībhūtaḥ salila iva ekaḥ  dvitīyasya abhāvāt  avidyāyāḥ  hi dvitīyasya abhāvāt  etad amṛtam abhayam eṣa bhma lokaḥ  brahmā eva lokaḥ  brahma lokaḥ para eva ayam asmin kāle vyāvṛtta kārya karaṇa upādhi bhedaḥ sva ātma jyotiṣi śānta sarva saṃbandhaḥ  vartate he samrāj iti ha evam ha enam janakam anuśaśāsa anuṣṭavān yājñavalkya iti śruti vacanam etad  katham vā anuśaśāsa eṣā asya vijñāna mayasya paramā gatiḥ yāḥ tu anyā deha graha lakṣaṇā brahma ādi stamba paryantā avidyā kalpitāḥ tā gatayaḥ atas  aparamā avidyā viṣaya tvāt iyam tu devatva ādi gatīnām karma vidyā sādhyānām parama uttamā yaḥ samasta ātma bhāvaḥ  yatra na anyat paśyati na anyat śṛṇoti na anya dvijānāti iti eṣā eva ca paramā saṃpad sarva āsām saṃpadām vibhūtīnām iyam paramā svābhāvika tvāt asyāḥ kṛtakā hi anyāḥ saṃpadaḥ tathā eṣaḥ asya paramaḥ  lokaḥ ye anye karma phala āśrayā lokāḥ te asmāt aparamāḥ ayam tu na kenacana karmaṇā mīyate svābhāvika tvāt eṣosya paramaḥ  lokaḥ tathā eṣaḥ asi aparama  ānandaḥ yāni anyāni viṣaya indriya saṃbandha janitāni ānanda jātāni tāni apekṣya eṣaḥ  asya parama  ānandaḥ  nitya tvāt  yaḥ  vai bhūmā tad sukham iti śruti antarāt yatra anyat paśyanyat vijānāti tāni apekṣya eṣaḥ  asya parama  ānanda unitya tvāt yaḥ  vai bhūmā tad sukham iti śruti antarāt yatra anyat paśyat vijānāti tad alpam martyam amukhyam kṣukham idam tu tad viparītam eta eṣaḥ  asya parama  ānandaḥ etasya evai aanandasya mātrām kalām avidyā pratyupasthāpitām viṣaya indriya saṃbandha kāla vibhāvyām anyāni bhūtāni upajīvanti kāni tāni tatas  evā anandāt avidyathā pravibhajyamāna svarūpāṇi anya tvena tāni brahmaṇaḥ parikalpyamānāni anyāni santi upajīvanti bhūtāni viṣaya indriya saṃparka dvāreṇa vibhāvyamānām yasya paramān dasya mātrā avayavā brahma ādibhiḥ manuṣya paryantaiḥ bhūtaiḥ upajīvyante tad ānanda mātrāt vāreṇa mātriṇam parama ānandam adhijigami yiṣan  āha saindhava lavaṇa śakalaiḥ iva lavaṇaśailam sa yaḥ kasmin manuṣyāṇām madhye rāddhaḥ saṃsiddhaḥ  avikalaḥ samagra avayava iti arthaḥ samṛddha upabhoga upakaraṇa saṃpannaḥ  bhavati kiñca anyeṣām samāna jātīyānām adhipatiḥ svatantra patiḥ na māṇḍalikaḥ sarvaiḥ samastaiḥ mānuṣyakaiḥ iti divya bhoga upakaraṇa nivṛti artham manuṣyāṇām eva yāni bhoga upakaraṇāni taiḥ saṃpannānām api atiṣayena saṃpannaḥ saṃpannatamaḥ sa manuṣyāṇām parama  ānandaḥ tatrā ananda andita uḥ abheda nirdeśāt na artha antara bhūta tvam iti etad parama ānandarasya eva iyam viṣaya aviṣayyākareṇa mātrā prasṛtā iti hayuktam yatra vā anyat iva syāt ityādi vākyena tasmāt yuktaḥ  ayam parama  ānanda iti abheda nirdeśaḥ yudhiṣṭhira ādi tulyaḥ  rājātra udāharaṇam dṛṣṭam manuṣya ānandaram ādim kṛtvā śataguṇa uttara krameṇa unnīya parama ānandam yatra bhedaḥ  nivartate tam adhigamayati atra ayam ānandaḥ śataguṇa uttarottara krameṇa vardhamānaḥ  yatra vṛddhi kāṣṭām anubhavati yatra gaṇita bhedaḥ  nivartate anya darśana śravaṇa mananā bhāvāttam parama ānandam vivakṣan  āha atha ye manuṣyāṇām evaṃprakārāḥ śatam ānanda bhedāḥ sa ekaḥ pitṝṇām teṣām viśeṣaṇam jita lokānām iti śrāddha ādi karmabhiḥ pitṝn  toṣayitvā tena karmaṇā jitaḥ  lokaḥ  yeṣām te jita lokāḥ pitaraḥ teṣām pitṛṇām jita lokānām manuṣya ānanda śata guṇīkṛta parimāṇa  eka ānandaḥ  bhavati saḥ  api śata guṇīkṛtaḥ  gandharva loke  eka ānandaḥ  bhavati sa ca śata guṇīkṛtaḥ karma devānām eka ānandaḥ agnihotra ādi śrauta karmaṇā ye deva tvam prāpnuvanti te karma devaiḥ tathā evai aajāna devānām eka ānandaḥ ājānata eva utpattita eva ye devāḥ te  ājāna devāḥ yaḥ ca śrotriyaḥ  adhīta vedaḥ  avaḍa jinaḥ  vṛjinam pāpam tad rahitaḥ  yathā ukta kāriti arthaḥ akāma hataḥ  vīta tṛṣṇa ājāna devaḥ  abhyor avāgyāvantaḥ  viṣayāḥ teṣu tasya ca evaṃbhūtasyā ajāna devaiḥ samāna  ānanda iti etad anvākṛṣyate ca śabdāt tad śata guṇīkṛta parimāṇaḥ prajāpati loke  eka ānandaḥ  virāj śarīre tathā tad vijñānavān śrotriyaḥ  adhīta vedaḥ ca āvṛjina ityādi pūrvavat  tad śata guṇīkṛta parimāṇa  eka ānandaḥ  brahma loke hiraṇyagarbha ātmani yaḥ ca ityādi pūrvavat eva atas  param gaṇita nivṛttaḥ eṣa parama  ānanda prayuktaḥ yasya ca parama ānanda jasya brahma loka ādyānandā mātrā udadheḥ iva vipruṣaḥ evam śataguṇa uttara uttara vṛddhi upetā ānandā yatra ekatā yānti yaḥ ca śrotriya pratyakṣaḥ  atha eṣa eva saṃprasāda lakṣaṇaḥ parama  ānandaḥ tatra hi na anyat paśyati na anyat śṛṇoti athaḥ bhūmā bhūma tvāt amṛtaḥ itare tad viparītāḥ atra ca śrotrayitvādvṛjina tve tulye akāma hatatva kṛtaḥ  viśeṣa ānanda śataguṇa vṛddhi hetuḥ atra etāni sādhanāni śrotriyatva āvṛjinatva akāma hata tvāni tasya tasyāḥ anandasya prāptau  artha ādi bhihita anu yathā karmāṇgnihotra ādīni devānām devatva prāptau tatra ca śrotriyatva āvṛjinatva lakṣaṇe karmaṇī adhara bhūmiṣu api samāne iti na uttara ānanda prāpti sādhane abhyupeyete akāma hata tvam tu vairāgya tāratamya upapatteḥ uttarottara bhūmi ānanda prāpti sādhanam iti avagamyate sa eṣa parama  ānandaḥ  vitṛṣṇa śrotriya pratyakṣaḥ  adhigataḥ tathā ca vedavyāsaḥ yad ca kāma sukham loke yad ca divyam mahat sukham tṛṣṇā kṣaya sukhasya ete na arhataḥ ṣoḍaśīm kalām iti eṣa brahma lokaḥ  he samrāj iti ha uvāca yājñavalkyaḥ saḥ  aham evanuśiṣṭaḥ  bhagavate tubhyam sahasram dadāmi gavām ata ūdhvam vimokṣāya eva brūhi iti vyākhyātam etad  atra ha vimokṣāya iti asmin vākye yājñavalkyaḥ  bibhayāñcakāra bhītavān yājñavalkyasya bhaya kāraṇam āha śrutiḥ na yājñavalkyaḥ  vaktṛtva sāmarthya abhāvāt bhīta vān ajñānāt vā kim tarhi medhāvī rājā sarvebhyaḥ  mā mām antebhyaḥ praśna nirṇayavasānebhya udarautsīdāvṛṇot avarodham kṛtavān iti arthaḥ yadyāt mayā nirṇītam praśna rūpam vimokṣa artham tad tad eka deśa tvena eva kāma praśnasya gṛhītvā punar  punar mām paryanuyuṅktta eva medhāvi tvāt iti etad bhaya kāraṇam sarvam madīyam vijñānam kāma praśna vyājena upāditsati iti atra vijñāna mayaḥ svayan jyotiḥ ātmā svapne pradarśitaḥ svapna antabudvānta saṃcāreṇa kārya karaṇa vyatirittka tā kāma karma pravivekaḥ ca asaṅga tayā mahā matsya dṛṣṭāntena pradarśitaḥ punar ca avidyā kāryam svapna eva dhnanta uva ityādinā pradarśitam arthāt avidyāyāḥ sa tattvaṃnirdhīritam atat varma adhyāropaṇa rūpa tvam anātma dharma tvam ca tathā vidyāyāḥ ca kāryam pradarśitam sarvatma bhāvaḥ svapna eva pratyakṣataḥ sarvaḥ  asmi iti manyate saḥ  asya paramaḥ  loka iti tatra ca sarva ātma bhāvaḥ svabhāvaḥ  asya evam avidyā kāma karma ādi sarva saṃsāra dharma saṃbandha atītam rūpam asya sākṣāt suṣupte gṛhyata iti ena t vijñāpitam svayan jyotiḥ ātmā eṣa parama  ānandaḥ eṣa vidyāyā viṣayaḥ sa eṣa paramaḥ saṃprasādaḥ sukhasya ca parā kāṣṭhā iti etad evam antena granthena vyākhyātam tad caid sarvam vimokṣa padārtha sarvam vimokṣa padārthasya dṛṣṭānta bhūtam bandhanasya ca te ca ete mokṣa bandhane sa hetuke sa prapañce nirdiṣṭe vidyā avidyā kārye tad sarvam dṛṣṭānta bhūtam eva iti tad dārṣṭa antika sthānīye mokṣa handhane sa hetuke kāma praśna artha bhūte tvayā vatt kavye iti punar  parthanuyuṅttke janakaḥ  ata ūrdhvam vimokṣāya eva brūhi iti tatra mahā matsya vatsu abuddha antauvasaṅgaḥ saṃcarati eka ātmā svayan jyotiḥ iti uktam yathā ca asau kārya karaṇa anu mṛtyu rūpāṇi parityajan  upāda dānaḥ ca mahā matsyavat svapna buddha antau  anusaṃcarati tathā jāyamānaḥ  mriyamāṇaḥ ca taiḥ eva mṛtyu rūpaiḥ saṃyujyate viyujyate ca ubhau loka anusaṃcarati iti saṃcaraṇam svapna buddhanta anusaṃcārasya dārṣṭa antika tvena sūcitam tad iha vistareṇa sa nimittam saṃcaraṇam varṇayitavyam iti tad arthaḥ  ayam ārambhaḥ tatra ca buddha antāt svapna antam ayam ātma anupraveśitaḥ tasmāt saṃprāsāda sthānam mokṣa dṛṣṭanā anta bhūtam tatas  pracyāvya buddha ante saṃsāra vyavahāraḥ pradariśyitavya iti tena asya saṃbandhaḥ sa vai buddha antāt spna anta krameṇa saṃprasanna eṣa etasmin saṃprasāde sthitvā tatas  punar īṣat pracyutaḥ svapna ante ratvā caritvā ityādi pūrvavat bundāya evā adravati ita ārabhya asya saṃsāraḥ  varṇyate yathā ayam ātmā svapna antāt buddha antam āgata evam ayam asmāt dehat deha antaram pratipatsyata iti āha atra dṛṣṭāntam tad tatra yathā loke anaḥ śakaṭam su samāhitam suṣṭhu bhṛśam vā samāhitam bhāṇḍa upaskaraṇena ulūkhala musala śūrpa piṭhara ādinā annādyena ca saṃpannam saṃbhāreṇā akrana antam iti arthaḥ tathā bhāra ākrāntam sat utsarjat śabdam kurvat yathā yayāt gacchet śā kaṭikena adhiṣṭhitam sat  evam eva yathā uktaḥ  dṛṣṭāntaḥ  ayam śarīraḥ śārīre bhavaḥ kaḥ  asau ātmā liṅga upādhiḥ yaḥ svapna buddha anta āvivi janma maraṇābhyām pāpma saṃsarga viyoga lakṣaṇābhyām iha loka para lokau  anusaṃcarati yasya utkramaṇam anu prāṇa ādi utkramaṇam sa prājñena pareṇā atmanā sva yan jyotiḥ svabhāvena anvārūṭhaḥ  adhiṣṭhitaḥ  avabhāsyamānaḥ tathā ca uktam āttam anaiva ayam jyotiṣā aste palyayata iti utsarjan yāti tatra caitanya ātma jyotiṣā bhāsye liṅge prāṇa pradhāne gacchati tad upādhiḥ api ātmā gacchati iva tathā śruti antaram kasmin  vaham ityādi dhyāyati iva iti ca ata eva uktam prājñenā atmanā anvārūṭha iti anyathā prājñena ekībhūtaḥ śakaṭavat katham utsarjan yāti tena liṅga upādhiḥ ātma utsarjan marmasu nikṛtyamāneṣu duḥkha vedanayār aatas  śabdam kurvan yāti gacchati tad kasmin kāla iti ucyate yatra etad bhavati etad iti kriyā viśeṣaṇam ūrdhva ucchvāsī yatra ūrdhva ucchāsita tvam asya bhavati iti arthaḥ dṛśyamānasya api anuvadanam vairāgya ga hetoḥ īdṛśaḥ kaṣṭaḥ khalu ayam saṃsāraḥ yena utkrānti kāle marmasu utkṛtyamāneṣu smṛti lopaḥ  duḥkha vedanā ārtasya puruṣa artha sādhana pratipattau ca asāmarthyam para vaśīkṛta cittasya tasmāt yāvat iyam avasthā nā agamiṣyati tāvat eva puruṣa artha sādhana karvyatāyām apramattaḥ  bhavet iti āha kāruṇyāt śrutiḥ tad asya ūrdhva ucchvāsi tvam kasmin kāle kiṃnimittam katham kimartham vā syāt iti etad ucyate saḥ  ayam prākṛtaḥ śiraḥ pāṇi ādimān piṇḍaḥ  yatra yasmin kāle ayamaṇi mānam aṇoḥ bhāvam aṇu tvam kārśyam iti arthaḥ nyeti nigacchati kiṃnimittam jarayā vā svayam eva kāla pakva phalavat jīrṇaḥ kārśyam gacchati upatapati iti upatapan jvara ādi rogaḥ tena upatapatā vā upatapyamānaḥ  hirogeṇa viṣama agnitayā annam bhuktam na jarayati tatas  anna rasena anupacīyamānaḥ piṇḍaḥ kārśyam āpapadyate tad ucyata upatapatā vā iti aṇimānam nigacchati yadā atyanta kārśyam pratipannaḥ  jarā ādi nimittaiḥ tadā ūrdhva uccha vāsī bhavati yadā ūrdhva ucchvāsī tadā bhṛśa āhita saṃbhāra śakaṭavat utsarjan yāti jaribhā abhavaḥ  roga ādi pīḍanam kārśyāpattiḥ ca śarīravataḥ  avaśyaṃbhāvina ete anarthā iti vairāgyāya idam ucyate yadā asau  utsarjanyāti tadā katham śarīram vimuñcati iti dṛṣṭānta ucyate tad tatra yatāmram vā phalam udumbaram vā pippalam vāphalam viṣama aneka dṛṣṭānta upādānam maraṇasya aniyata nimittatva khyāpana artham aniyatāni hi maraṇasya nimittāni asaṃkhyātāni ca etad api vairāgya artham eva yasmāt ayam aneka maraṇa nimittavān  tasmāt sarvadā mṛtyoḥ āsye vartata iti bandhanāt badhyate yena vṛntena saha sa bandhana kāraṇaḥ  rasaḥ  yasmin vā badhyata iti vṛntam eva ucyate bandhana tasmāt rasāt vṛntāt vā bandhanāt pramucyate vāta ādi aneka nimitam evam eva ayam puruṣaḥ  liṅga ātmā liṅga upādhirebhyaḥ  aṅgebhyaḥ cakṣuḥ ādi deha avayavebhyaḥ saṃpramucya samyak nirlepena pramucya na suṣupta gamana kāla iva prāṇena rakṣan kim tarhi saha vāyunā upasaṃhṛtya punar  pratinyāyam punar śabandāt pūrvam api ayam dedāt deha antaram asakṛt gatavān yathā svapna buddha antau punar  purgacchati tathā punar  pratinyāyam pratigamanam yathāgatam iti arthaḥ pratiyoni yonim yoni prati karma śruta ādi vaśādādravati kimartham prāṇāya eva prāṇa vyūhāya eva iti arthaḥ sa prāṇa  eva hi gacchati tatas  prāṇayā eva iti viśeṣaṇam anarthakam prāṇa vyūhāya hi gamanam dehāt deha antaram prati tena hi asya karma phala upabhoga artha siddhiḥ na prāṇa sattā mātreṇa tasmāt tādarthāyartham yuktam viśeṣaṇam prāṇa vyūhāya iti tatra asya idam śarīram parityajya gacchataḥ  na anyasya deha antarasya upādāne sāmarthyam asti deha indriya viyogāt  na ca anye asya bhṛtya sthānīyā gṛham iva rājñe śarīra antaram kṛtvā pratīkṣamāṇā vidyante atha evam sati katham asya śarīra antara upādānam iti ucyate sarvam hi asya jagatsva karma phala upabhoga sādhana tvāya upāttam sva karma phala upabhogāya ca ayam pravṛttaḥ  dehāt deha antaram pratipitsuḥ tasmāt sarvam eva jagatsva karmaṇā prayuktam tad karma phala upabhoga ayogyam sādhanam kṛtvā pratīkṣata eva kṛtam lokam puruṣaḥ  abhijāyate iti śruteḥ yathā svapnāt jāgaritam pratipitsoḥ tad katham iti loka prasiddhaḥ  dṛṣṭānta ucyate tad tatra yathā rājānam rājya abhiṣiktam āyāntam sva rāṣṭra ugrā jāti viśeṣāḥ krūra karmaṇaḥ  vā pratyenasaḥ prati pratenasi pāpa karmaṇi niyuktāḥ pratyenasaḥ taskara ādi daṇḍanādau niyuktāḥ sūtāḥ ca grāmaṇyaḥ  grāma netāraḥ te pūrvam eva rājña āgamanam buddhvā annaiḥ bhojya bhakṣya ādi prakāraiḥ pānaiḥ madirā ādibhiḥ āvasathaiḥ ca prāsāda ādibhiḥ pratikalpante niṣpannaiḥ eva pritīkṣante ayam rājā ayāti ayam āgacchati iti evam vadantaḥ yathā ayam dṛṣṭānta evam ha evaṃvidam karma phalasya veditāram saṃsāriṇam iti arthaḥ karma phalam hi prastutam tad evaṃśabdena parāmṛśyate sarvāṇi bhūtāni śarīra kartṝṇi karaṇa anugrahītṝṇi cā adityādīni tad karma prayuktāni kṛtaiḥ eva karma phalaḥ babhoga sādhanaiḥ pratīkṣante idam brahma bhoktṛ kartṛ ca asmākam āyāti tathā idam āgacchati iti evam eva ca kṛtvā pratīkṣanta iti arthaḥ tam eva jigamiṣum ke saha gacchante ye vā gacchanti te kim tad kriyā praṇunnā āhosvit tad karma vaśāt svayam eva gacchanti para loka śarīra kartṝṇi ca bhūtāni iti atra ucyate dṛṣṭāntaḥ tatat yathā rājānam prayiyāsantam prakarṣeṇa yātum icchantam ugrāḥ pratyenasaḥ sūta grāmaṇyaḥ tam yathā abhisamāyanti ābhumikhyena samāyanti ekībhāvena tam abhimukhā āyanti anājñaptā eva rājñā kevalam tad jigamiṣa abhijñāḥ evam eva imam ātmānam bhoktāram antakāle maraṇa kāle sarve prāṇā vāc ādayaḥ  abhisamāyanti yatra ātat ūrdhva ucchvāsī bhavati iti vyākhyātam sa yatra ayamam ātmā saṃsāra upavarṇanam prastutam tatra ayam puruṣa ebhyaḥ  aṅgebhyaḥ saṃpramucya iti uktam tad saṃpramokṣaṇam kasmin kāle kathe vā iti sa vistaram saṃsaraṇam varṇayitavyam iti āpabhyate saḥ  ayam ātmā prastutaḥ  yatra yasmin kāle abalyam abala bhāvam ni etya gatvā yad dehasya daurbalyam tad ātmana eva daurbalyam iti uparyate abalyam nyetya iti na hi asau svatas  amūrta tvāt abala bhāvam gacchati tathā saṃmoham iva saṃmūṭha tā saṃmohaḥ  viveka abhāvaḥ saṃmūḍha tām iva nyeti nigacchati na ca asya svatas  saṃmohaḥ  asaṃmohaḥ  vā asti nitya caitanya jyotiḥ svabhāva tvāt tena iva śabdaḥ saṃmoham iva nyeti iti utkrānti kālam hi karaṇa upasaṃhāra nimittaḥ  vyākulībhāva ātmana iva lakṣyate laikikaiḥ tathā ca vaktāraḥ  bhavanti saṃmūḍhaḥ saṃmūḍhaḥ  ayam iti atha vā ubhayatreva śabda prayogaḥ  yojyaḥ abalyam iva nyet  saṃmoham iva nyeti iti ubhayaḥ  para upādhi nimittatva aviśeṣāt  samāna kartṛka nirdeśāt ca atha asmin kāla ete prāṇā vāc ādaya enam ātmanam abhisamāyanti tadā asya śārīrasyā atmanaḥ  aṅgebhyaḥ saṃpramoṇam katham punar  saṃpramokṣaṇam kena vā prakāreṇā atmānam abhisamāyanti iti ucyate sa ātmā etāḥ tejaḥ mātrāḥ tejasā u mātrāḥ tejaḥ mātrāḥ tejaḥ vayavā rūpa ādi prakāśaka tvāt cakṣuḥ ādīni karaṇāni iti arthaḥ tā etāḥ samabhyāda dānaḥ samyak nirlepena abhyādadāna ābhimukhyena ña adadānaḥ saṃharamāṇaḥ tad svapna apekṣayā viśeṣaṇam samiti na tu svapne nirlepena samyāga ādānam asti tu ādāna mātram agṛhītā vāc gṛhītam cakṣuḥ aasya lokasya sarvāvataḥ mātrām apādāya aśukram ādāye atyādi vākyebhyaḥ hṛdayam eva puṇḍarīka ākāram anvakrāmati anvāgacchati hṛdaye abhivyakta vijñānaḥ  bhavati iti arthaḥ buddhi ādi vikṣepa upasaṃhāpe sati na hi tasya svatas calanam vikṣepa upasaṃhāra ādi vikriyā vā dhyāyati iva lelāyati iva iti uktvāt buddhi ādi upādhi dvārā eva hi sarva vikriyā adhyāropyatetasmin kadā punar tasya tejaḥ mātra abhyādām iti ucte sa yatra eṣa cakṣuṣi bhavaḥ cākṣuṣa puruṣa jāditya aṃśaḥ  bhoktuḥ karmaṇā prayuktaḥ  yādavat deha dhāraṇam tāvat cakṣuṣaḥ  anugraham kurvan vartate maraṇa kāle tu asya cakṣuḥ anugraham parityajati svam āditi ātmānam pratipadyate tad etad uktam yatra asya puruṣasya mṛtasya agnim vāc apyeti vātam prāṇaḥ cakṣuḥ ādityāmi tyādi punar deha grahaṇa kāle saṃśrayiṣyanti tathā svapsyataḥ prabudhyataḥ ca tad etad āhi cākṣuṣaḥ puruṣaḥ  yatra yasmin kāle parāṅparyāvartate parisamantāt parāṅvyāvartata iti atha atra asmin kāle arūpajñaḥ  bhavati mumūrṣū rūpam na jānāti tadā ayam ātmā cakṣuḥ ādi tejaḥ mātrāḥ samabhyāda dānaḥ  bhavati svapnkāla iva ekībhavati karaṇa jātam svena liṅga ātmanā tadā evana pārśva sthā āhuḥ na paśyati iti tathā ghrāṇa devatā nivṛttau ghrāṇam ekībhavati liṅga ātmanā tadā na jighrati iti āhuḥ samānam anyat  jihvāyām somaḥ  varuṇaḥ  vā devatā tad nivṛti apekṣayā na rasayata iti āhuḥ tathā na vadati na śṛṇoti na manute na spṛśati na vijānāti iti āhuḥ tadā upalakṣyate devatā nivṛttiḥ karaṇānām ca hṛdaya ekībhāvaḥ tatra hṛdaya upasaṃhṛteṣu karaṇeṣu yaḥ  antarvāya pāraḥ sa kathyate tasya ha etasya prakṛtasya hṛdayasya hṛdaya  chidrasya iti etad  agram nāḍī mukham nirgama dvāram pradyotate svapna kāla iva svena bhāsā tejaḥ mātra ādāna kṛtena svonāva jyotiṣā atmanā eva ca tenā atma jyotiṣā pradyotena hṛdaya agreṇa eṣa ātmā vijñānam ayaḥ  liṅga upādhiḥ nigracchati niṣkramāti tathā atharvaṇe kasmin  vaham utkrānta utkrāntaḥ  bhaviṣyāmi kasmin vā pratiṣṭhate pratiṣṭhāsyāmi iti sa prāṇam asṛjata iti tatra cā atma caitanya jyotiḥ sarvadā abhivyaktataram tad upādhi dvārā hi ātmani janma maraṇa gamana āgamana ādi sarva vikriyā lakṣaṇaḥ saṃvyavahāraḥ tad ātmakam hi dvādaśavidham karaṇam buddhi ādi tad sūtram tad jīvanam saḥ  antarātmā jagataḥ tasthuṣaḥ ca tena pradyotena hṛdaya agra prakāśena niṣkramamāṇaḥ kena mārgeṇa niṣkrāmati iti ucyate cakṣuṣṭaḥ  vā āditya loka prāpti nimittam jñānam karma vā yadi syāt  mūrdhnaḥ vā brahma loka prāpti nimittam ced  anyebhyaḥ  vā śarīra deśebhyaḥ śarīra avayavebhyaḥ  yathākarma yathāśrutam tam vijñāna ātmānam utkrāmantam para lokasya prasthitam para lokāya udbhūta ākūtam iti artha prāṇaḥ sarva adhikāri sthānīyaḥ rājña iva anūtkrāmati tam ca prāṇam anūtkrāmantam vāc ādayaḥ sarve prāṇām anūtkrāmanti yathā pradhānān vāci khyāseyam na tu krameṇa sārthavat gmanam iha vivakṣitam tadā eṣa ātmā sa vijñānaḥ  bhavati svapn iva viśeṣa vijñānavān bhavati karma vaśāt n svatantraḥ svātantryeṇa hi sa vijñāna tve sarvaḥ kṛtakṛtyaḥ syāt  na eva tu tad labhyate ata evā aha vyāsaḥ sadā tad bhāva bhāvitaḥ iti karmaṇā tu udbhāvyamānena antaḥkaraṇa vṛtti viśeṣa āśrita vāsanā ātmaka viśeṣa vijñānena sarvaḥ  loka etasmin kāle sa vijñānaḥ  bhavati sa vijñānam eva ca gantavyam anvavakrām atyagacchati viśeṣa vijñāna udbhāsitam eva iti arthaḥ tasmāt tad kāle svātantrya artham yoga dharma anusevanam parisaṃkhyāna abhyāsaḥ ca viśiṣṭa puṇya upayaḥ ca śraddhadhānaiḥ para loka arthibhiḥ apramattaiḥ kartavya iti sarva śāstrāṇām yatnataḥ  vidheyor athaḥ duścaritāt ca uparamaṇam na hi tad kāle śakyate kiñcid sampādayitum karmaṇā nīyamānasya svātantrya abhāvāt apuṇyaḥ  vai puṇyena karmaṇā bhavati pāpaḥ pāpena atyuktam etasya hi anarthasya upaśama upāya vidhānāyā sarva śākhā upaniṣadaḥ pravṛttāḥ na hi tad vihita upāya anusevanam muktvā atyanti kaḥ  asya anarthasya upaśama upāyaḥ  asti tasmāt atra eva upaniṣad vihita upāye yatna paraiḥ bhavitavyam iti eṣa prakaraṇa arthaḥ śakaṭa vaḥ taṃbhṛ saṃbhāram utsarjanyāti iti uktam kim punar tasya para lokāya pravṛttasya pathdanam śākaṭika saṃbhāra sthānīyam gatvā vā para lokam yad bhuṅkte śarīra ādi ārambhakam ca yad tad kim iti ucyate tam para lokāya gacchantam ātmānam vidyā karmaṇī vidyā ca karma ca vidyā karmaṇī vidyā srava prakārā vihitā pratiṣiddhā ca avihita apratiṣiddhā ca tathā karma vihitam pratiṣiddham ca avihita pratiṣiddham ca samanvārabhete samyak anvārabhete anvālabhete anugacchataḥ pūrva prajñā ca pūrva anubhūta viṣayā prajñā pūrva prajñā atīta karma phala anubhava vāsanā iti arthaḥ sā ca vāsanā pūrva karma rambhe karma vipāke ca aṅgam bhavati tena asau  api anvāpabhate na hi tayā vāsanayā vinā karma kartum phalam ca upabhoktum śakyate na hi anabhyaste viṣaye kauśalam indrayāṇām bhavati pūrva anubhava vāsanā pravṛttānām tu indriyāṇām iha abhyāsam anantareṇa kauśalam upapadyate dṛśyate ca keṣāñcid kāsu cid kriyāsu citrakarma ādi lakṣaṇāsu vinā eva iha abhyāsena janmata eva kauśalam kāsucid atyanta saukarya yuktāsu api akauśalam koṣāñcid  tathā pūrva prajñayā vinā karmaṇi vā phala upabhoge vā na kasyacid pravṛttiḥ upapadyate tasmāt etad trayam śākaṭika sambhāra sthānīyam para loka pathya dana vidyā karma pūrvaprajñā ākhyam yasmāt vidyā kramaṇī pūrvapjñā ca deha antara pratipati upabhoga sādhanam tasmat vidyā karma ādi śubham eva samātaret yathā iṣṭa deha sambhoga upabhogau syātām iti prakaraṇa arthaḥ evam vidyā ādi sambāra samphṛtaḥ  deha antaram pratipadyamānaḥ  muktvā pūrvam deham pakṣī iva vṛkṣa antaram deha antaram pratipadyate athavā ativāhikena śarīra antareṇa karma phala janma deśam nīyate kiñca atrasthasya eva sarva gatānām karaṇānām vṛtti lābhaḥ  bhavati āhosvit śarīraḥsya saṃkucitāni karaṇāni mṛtasya bhinna ghaṭa pradīpa prakāśavat sarvatas  vyapya punar deha antara ārambhe saṅkocam upagacchanti kiñca manaḥ mātram vaiśeṣika samaya iva deha antara ārambha deśam prati gacchati kiṃvā kalpanānā antaram eva vedānta samaya iti ucyate ta ete sarva eva samāḥ sarve anantāḥ iti śruteḥ sarva ātmakāni tāvat karaṇāni sarva ātmaka prāṇa saṃśrayāt ca teṣām ādhyāmika ādhibhautika paricchedaḥ prāṇi karma jñāna bhāvanā nimittaḥ atas tad vaśāt svabhāvataḥ sargatānām anantānām api prāṇānām karjñāna vāsanā anurūpeṇa eva dehān nara ārambha vaśāt prāṇānām vṛttiḥ saṃkucati vikasati ca tathā ca uktam samaḥ pluṣiṇā samaḥ  maśakena samaḥ  nāgena sama ebhiḥ tribhiḥ lokaiḥ samaḥ  anena sarveṇa iti tathā ca idam vacanam anukūlam sa yaḥ  ha etān ananta anupāste ityādi tam yathā yathā upāsate iti ca tatra vāsanā pūrva prajñā ākhyā vidyā karma tantrā jalūkavat saṃtatā eva svapna kāla iva karma kṛtam dehāt deha antaram ārabhate hṛdayasya eva punar deha antara ārambhe deha antaram pūrva āśrayam vimuñcati iti etasmin  arthe dṛṣṭānta upādīyate tad tatra deha antara sañcāra idam nidarśanam yathā yena prakāreṇa tṛṇajalāyukā tṛṇajalūkā tṛṇasya antam avasānam gatvā prāpya anyam tṛṇa antaram ākramam ākramyata iti ākramaḥ tamākramam ākramyā aścityā atmānam ātmanaḥ pūrvavayavam upasaṃharati antya avayava sthāne evam eva ayam ātmā yaḥ prakṛtaḥ saṃsāri idam śarīram pūrva upāttam nihatya svapnam pratipitsuḥ iva pātayitvā avidyām gamayitvā acetanam kṛtvā sva ātmosaṃhāreṇa anyam ākramam tṛṇa antaram iva tṛṇajalūkā śarīra antaram gṛhītvā prasārityā vāsanayā amānam upasaṃharati tatrā atma bhāvam ārabhate yathā svapne deha antaram ārabhate svapna deha antarasya śarīra ambha deśa ārabhyamāṇe dehe jaṅgame sthāvare vā tatra ca karma vaśāt karaṇāni labdha vṛttīni saṃhanyante bāhyam ca kuśa mṛttikā sthānīyam śarīram ārabhyate tatra ca karaṇa vyūham apekṣya vāc ādi anugrahāya agni ādi devatāḥ saṃścayante eṣa deha antara ārambha vidhiḥ tatra deha antara ārambhe nittha upāttam eva upādānam upamṛdya upamṛdya deha antaram ārabhata āha usti dapūrvam eva punar  punar ādatta iti atra ucyate dṛṣṭāntaḥ tad tatra itasmin  arthe yathā peśaskārī peśaḥ suvarṇa tad  karoti iti peśaskārī suvarṇakāraḥ peśasaḥ suvarṇasya mātrām apādāya apicchidya gṛhītvā anyat  pūrvasmāt  racanā viśeṣāt navataram abhinavataram kalyāṇāt  kalyāṇataram rūpam tanute nirminoti evam eva ayam ātmā ityādi pūrvavat  nitya upāttāni eva pṛthivī ādīni ākāśa antāni pañca bhūtāni yāni adve vāva brahmaṇaḥ  rūpe iti caturthe vyākhyātāni peśaḥ sthāna āyānitāni eva upamṛdya upamṛdya anyat anyat ca deha antaram navataram kalyāṇataram rūpam saṃsthāna veśeṣam vā pitṛbhyaḥ  hitam pitṛ loka upabhoga yogyam iti arthaḥ gāndharvam gandharvāṇām upabhoga yogyam tathā devānām daivam prajāpateḥ prajāpatyam brahmaṇa idam brāhmam vā  yathākarma yathāśrutam anyeṣa aṃvā bhūtānām sambandhi śarīra antaram kuruta iti abhisambanyate yaḥ  asya bandhana saṃjñakā upādhi bhūtāḥ yaiḥ saṃyuttkaḥ tad maye ayam iti vibhāvyate te padārthāḥ puñjīkṛtya iha ekatra pratinirdiśyante sa vā ayam ya evam saṃsarati ātmā brahmā eva para eva yaḥ  aśanāya ādi atītaḥ  vijñānam ayaḥ  vijñānam budviḥ tena upalaṅyamāṇaḥ tad mayaḥ katama ātmā iti yaḥ  ayam vijñāna mayaḥ prāṇeṣu iti hayuktam vijñānam ayaḥ  vījñāna prāyaḥ  yasmāt tad varma tvam asya vibhāvyate dhyāyati iva lelāyati iva iti tathā manaḥ mayaḥ  manaḥ saṃnikarṣāt manaḥ mayaḥ tathā prāṇa mayaḥ prāṇaḥ pañca vṛttiḥ tad mayaḥ  yena cetanaḥ calati iva lakṣyate tathā cakṣuḥ mayaḥ  rūpa darśana kāle evam śrotra mayaḥ śabda śravaṇa kāle evam tasya tasya indriyasya vyāpāra udbhave tad tad mayaḥ  bhavati evam budvi prāṇa dvāreṇa cakṣuḥ ādi karaṇa mayaḥ san śarīra ārambhaka pṛthivī ādi bhūtam ayaḥ  bhavati tatra pārthiva śarīra ārambhe pṛthivīmayaḥ  bhavati tathā varuṇa ādi lokeṣu āpi aśarīra ārambha āpaḥ mayaḥ  bhavati tathā vāyavya śarīra ārambhe vāyu mayaḥ  bhavati tathā akāśa śarīra ārambha ākāśam ayaḥ  bhavati evam etāni taijasāni deva śarīrāṇi teṣu ārabhyamāṇeṣu tad mayaḥ tejaḥ mayaḥ  bhavati atas  vyatiriktāni paśu ādi śarīrāṇi naraka preta ādi śarīrāṇi ca atejaḥ mayāni tāni apekṣyā aha atejaḥ maya iti evam kārya karaṇa saṃghāta mayaḥ san  ātmā prāptavyam vastu antaram paśyan  idam mayā prāpta madaḥ  mayā prāptavyam iti evam viparīta pratyayaḥ tad abhilāṣaḥ kāmam ayaḥ  bhavati tasmin kāme doṣam paśyataḥ tad viṣaya abhilāṣa praśāme citam prasannam akaluṣam śāntam bhavati tad mayaḥ  akāma mayaḥ evam tasmin vihate kām ekena acid sa kāmaḥ krodha tvena pariṇamate tena tad mayaḥ  bhavan krodha mayaḥ sa krodhaḥ kenacid upāyena nivartitaḥ  yadā bhavati tadā prasannam anākulam citam sat akrodha ucyate tena tad mayaḥ evam kāma krodha abhyāma kāma akrodhābhyām ca tad mayaḥ  bhūtvā dharmam ayaḥ  adharma mayaḥ ca bhavati na hi kāma krodha ādibhiḥ vinā dharma ādi pravṛtti rūpapadyate yad yad vi kurute karma tad tad kāmasya ceṣṭitam iti smaraṇāt  dharmam ayaḥ  adharmayaḥ ca bhūtvā sarvam ayaḥ  bhavati samastam dharma adharmayoḥ kāryam yāvartki cit vyākṛtam tad sarvam dharma adharmayoḥ phalam tad pratipadyāmānaḥ tad mayaḥ  bhavati kim bahunā tad etad sidvam asya yad ayam idaṃmayaḥ  gṛhyamāṇa viṣayādi daṃmayaḥ tasmāt ayam adaḥ mayaḥ ada iti parokṣam kāryeṇa gṛhyamāṇena nirdiśyate anantā hi antaḥkaraṇe bhāvanā viśeṣāḥ na eva te viśeṣataḥ  nirdeṣṭum śakyante tasmiḥ tasmin kṣaṇe kāryataḥ  avagamyanta idam asya hradi vartate adosyate tena gṛhyamāṇa kāryeṇa idaṃmaya tayā nirdiśyate parokṣaḥ  antar sthaḥ  vyavahāraḥ  ayam idānīm adaḥ maya iti saṃkṣepataḥ tu yathā kartum yathā vā caritum śīlam asya saḥ  ayam yathākārī yathā cārī sa tathā bhavati karaṇam nāma niyatā kriyā vidhi pratiṣedha ādi gamyā caraṇam nāma aniyatam iti viśeṣaḥ sādhu kārī sādhuḥ bhavati iti yathākārīti asya viśeṣaṇam pāpa kārī pāpaḥ  bhavati iti ca yathācārī iti asya tāt śīlya pratyaya upādānāt atyanta tātparyatā eva tad maya tvam na tu tad karma mātreṇa uti āśaṅkayā aha puṇyaḥ puṇyena karmaṇā bhavati pāpaḥ pāpena iti puṇya pāpa karma mātreṇa eva tad maya tā syāt na tu tāt śīlyam apekṣate tāt śīlye tu tad mayatva atiśaya iti ayam viśeṣaḥ tatra kāma krodha ādi pūrvaka puṇya kāritā sarva maya tve hetuḥ saṃsārasya kāraṇam dehāt deha antara saṃcārasya ca etad prayuktaḥ  hi anyat anyat deha antaram upādatte tasmāt puṇya apuṇye saṃsārasya kāraṇam etad viṣayau hi vidhi pratiṣedhau atra śāstrasya sāphalyam iti athaḥ api anye bandha mokṣa kuśalāḥ khalu āhuḥ satyam kāma ādi pūrvake puṇya apuṇye śarīra grahaṇa kāraṇam tathā api kāma prayuktaḥ  hi puruṣaḥ puṇya puṇye karmaṇī upacinoti kāma prahāṇe tu karma vidyā mānam api puṇya puṇyepa caya karam na bhavati upacite api puṇya puṇye karmaṇī kāma śūnye phala ārambhake na bhavataḥ tasmāt kāma eva saṃsārasya mūlam tathā cektam ātharvaṇe kāmānyaḥ kāmayate manyamānaḥ sa kāmabhiḥ jāyate tatra tatra iti tasmāt kāma maya eva ayam puruṣaḥ  yad anya maya tvam tad akāraṇam vidyānam api iti aptaḥ  avadhārayati kāma maya eva iti yasmāt sa ca kāma mayaḥ sanyādṛśena kāmena yathākāmaḥ  bhavati tad kratuḥ bavati sa kāma īṣat abhilāṣa mātreṇa abhivyaktaḥ  yasmin viṣaye bhavati saḥ  avihanyamānaḥ sphuṭībhavan kratu tvām āpadyate kratuḥ na adhyavasāyaḥ  niścayaḥ  yad anantarā kriyā pravartate yad kratuḥ bhavati yādṛś kāma kāryeṇa kratunā yathārūpaḥ kratuḥ asya saḥ  ayam yad kratuḥ bhavati tad karma kuruteya t viṣayaḥ kratuḥ tad phala nirvṛttaye yad yogyam karma tad kurute nirvartayati yad karma kurute tad abhisaṃpadyate tadīyam phalam abhisaṃpadyate tasmāt sarva maya tve asya saṃsāri tve ca kāma hetuḥ iti tad tasmin  artha eṣa ślokaḥ  mantra upi bhavati tad eva eti tad eva gacchati sakta āsaktaḥ tatra udbhūta abhilāṣaḥ san  iti arthaḥ katham eti saha karmaṇā yad karma phala āsaktaḥ sannakara uttena karmaṇā saha eva tadā iti tad phalam eti kim tad liṅga manaḥ manaḥ pradhāna tvān liṅgasya manaḥ  liṅgam iti ucyate athavā liṅgayate avagamyate avagacchati yena tad liṅgam tad manaḥ  yatra yasmin niṣaktam niścayena saktam udbhūta abhilāṣam asya saṃsāriṇaḥ tad abhilāṣaḥ  hi tad karma kṛtavān tasmāt tad manaḥ  abhiṣaṅga vaśāt eva asya tena karmaṇā tad phala prāptiḥ tena etasi dvam bhavati kāmaḥ  mūlam saṃsārasya iti ata ucchinna kāmasya vidyamānāni api karmāṇi brahma vidaḥ  vandhya prasavāni bhavanti paryāpta kāma saya kṛtātmanaḥ ca iha eva sarve pravilītanti kāmāḥ iti śruteḥ kiñca prāpya antam karmaṇaḥ prāpya bhuktvā antam avasānam tasya karmaṇaḥ phalam bhuktvā antam prāpya tasmāt lokāt punar aiti āgacchati asmai lokāya karmaṇe ayam hi lokaḥ karma pradhānaḥ tenā aha karmaṇa iti punar  karma karaṇāya punar  karma kṛtvā phala āsaṅga vaśāt punar amum lokam yāti iti evam iti nu evam nu kāmayamānaḥ saṃsarati ya māt kāmayamāna eva evam saṃsarati atha tasmāt akāmayamānaḥ  na kvacid saṃsarati phala āsaktasya hi gatiḥ uktā akāmasya hi kriyā anupapatteḥ akāmayamānaḥ  mucyata eva katham punakāmaya mānaḥ  bhavati yaḥ  akāmaḥ  bhavati asau  akāmayamānaḥ katham akāma tā iti ucyate yaḥ  niṣṭakāmaḥ  yasmāt nirgatāḥ kāmāḥ saḥ  ayam niṣkāmaḥ katham kāmā nirgacchanti ya āpta kāmaḥ  bhavati āptāḥ kāmā yena sa āpta kāmaḥ katham āpyante kāmā ātma kāma tvena yasyā ama eva na anyaḥ kāmayitavyaḥ  vastu antara bhūtaḥ padārthaḥ  bhavati ātmā eva anantaraḥ  abāhyaḥ kṛtsnaḥ prajñāna ghana ekarasaḥ  na ūrdhva na tiryak na adha ātmanaḥ  anyat kāmayitavyam vastu antaram yasya sarvam ātmā eva abhūt tad kena kam paśyet śṛṇuyāt manvīta vijānīyāt vaivam vijānan kam kāmayeta jñāyamānaḥ  hi anya tvena padārthaḥ kāmayitavyaḥ  bhavati na ca asau  anyaḥ  brahma vida āpta kāmasya asti ya evā atmakāma tayā apta kāmaḥ sa niṣkāmaḥ  akāmaḥ  akāmayamānaḥ ca iti mucyate na hi yasyā atmā eva sarvam bhavati tasya anātmā kāmayitavyaḥ  asti anātmā ca anyaḥ kāmayitavyaḥ sarvam cā atmā eva abhūt iti vipra tiṣidvam sarva ātma darśinaḥ kāmayitavya abhāvāt karma anupapattiḥ ye tu pratyavāya parihāra artham karma kalpayanti brahma vidaḥ  api teṣām sarva bhavati pratyavāyasya jihāsita vyasyā atmanaḥ  anyasya abhipreta tvāt  yena ca aśanāya ādi atītaḥ  nityam pratyavāya saṃbadvaḥ  vidita ātmā tam vayam brahma vidam brūmaḥ nityam eva aśanāya ādi atītam ātmanam paśyati yasmāt ca jihāsita vyam anyam upādeyam vā yaḥ  na paśyati tasya karma na śakyata eva saṃbaddhu m yaḥ tu abrahma vitasya bhavati eva pratyavāya parihāra artham karma iti na virodhaḥ atas  kāma abhāvāt akāmayamānaḥ  na jāyate mucyata eva tasya evam akāmayamānasya karma abhāve gamana kāraṇa abhāvāt prāṇā vāc ādayaḥ  na utkrāmanti na ūrdhva krāmanti dehāt  sa ca vidvān āpta kāma  ātma kāma tayā iha eva brahma bhūtaḥ sarva ātmanaḥ  hi brahmaṇaḥ  dṛṣṭānta tvena pradarśitam etad rūpam tad vā asya etad āpta kāmam ātma kāmam akāmam rūpam iti tasya hi dārṣṭa antika bhūtaḥ  ayam artha upasaṃhriyate atha akāmayamāna ityādinā sa katham evaṃbhūtaḥ  mucyata iti ucyate yaḥ  hi suṣupta avastham iva nirviśeṣam advaitam alupta cit rūpa jyotiḥ svabhāvam ātmānam paśyati tasya eva akāmayamānasya karma bhāve gamana kāraṇa bhāvat prāṇā vāc ādayaḥ  na utkrāmanti kintu vidvān saiha eva brahma yadi api dehāvān iva lakṣyate sa brahmā eva san brahmā apyeti yasmāt na hi tasya abrahmatva pariccheda hetavaḥ kāmāḥ santi tasmāt iha eva brahmā eva san brahmā apyeti na śarīra pātettara kālam na hi viduṣaḥ  mṛtasya bhāva antara āpattiḥ jīvataḥ  anya bhāvaḥ  deha antara pratisaṃdhāna abhāva mātreṇa uva tu brahmā api eti iti ucyate bhāva antarārāpattau hi mokṣasya sarva upaniṣa nid vivakṣitor atha ātmā ekatva ākhyaḥ sa bādhitaḥ  bhavet  karma hetukaḥ ca mokṣaḥ prāpnoti na jñāna nimitta iti sa ca aniṣṭaḥ  anitya tvam ca mokṣasya prāpnoti na hi kriyā nirvṛttor athaḥ nityaḥ  dṛṣṭaḥ nityaḥ ca mokṣaḥ  abhyupagamyate eṣa nityaḥ  mahimā iti mantra varṇāt  na ca svābhāvikāt svabhāvāt anyat nityam kalpayitum śakyam svābhāvikaḥ ced agni udātmanaḥ svabhāvaḥ sa na śakyate puruṣa vyāpāra anubhāvī iti vaktum na hi agneḥ auṣṇyam prakāśaḥ  vā agnu vyāpāra anantara anubhāvī agni vyāpāra anubhāvī svābhāvikaḥ ca iti vipratiṣiddham jvalana vyāpāna anubhāvi tvam uṣṇa prākāśa guṇābhyām abhivyajyate tad na agni epa īkṣayā kim tarhi anya dṛṣṭeḥ agneḥ auṣṇya prakāśau dharmau vyavahitai kasyacid dṛṣṭyā tu asaṃbadhyamānau jvalana apekṣayā vyadhāna apagame dṛṣṭeḥ abhivyajyete tad apekṣayā bhrāntiḥ upajāyate jvalana pūrvakau  etauviṣṇa prākāśau dharmau jātau  iti yadi uṣṇa prakāśayoḥ api svābhāvika tvam na syāt  yaḥ svābhāvaki agneḥ dharmaḥ tam udāhariṣyāmaḥ na ca svābhāvikaḥ  dharma eva na asti padārthānām iti śakyam vaktum na ca nigaḍa bhaṅga iva abhāva bhūtaḥ  mokṣaḥ  bandhana nivṛttiḥ upapadyate paramātmā ekatva abhyupagamāt aekam eva advitīyam aiti śruteḥ na ca anyaḥ  baddhaḥ  asti yasya nigaḍa nivṛttivat bandhana nivṛttarmokṣaḥ syāt  parama ātma vyatirekeṇa anyasya abhāvam vistareṇa avādiṣma tasmāt avidyā nivṛtti mātre mokṣa vyavahāra iti ca avocāma yathā rajju ādau sarpa ādya jñāna nivṛttau sarpa ādi nivṛttiḥ ye api ācakṣate mokṣe vijñāna antaram ānanda antaram ca abhivyajyata iti sairvaktavyaḥ  abhivyakti śabda arthaḥ yadi tāvat laukikikī ā iva upalabdhi viṣaya vyāptiḥ abhivyakti śabda arthaḥ tatas  vaktavyam kim vidyamānam abhivyajyate avidyamānam iti vā vidyamānam ced yasya muktasya tad abhivyajyate tasyā atma bhūtam eva tad iti upalabdhi vyavadhāna anupapatteḥ nitya abhivyakta tvāt muktasya abhivyajyata iti viśeṣa vacanam arthakam atha kadācid eva abhivyajyata upalabdhi vyavadhānāt anātma bhūtam tad iti anyatas  abhivyakti prasaṅgaḥ tathā ca abhivyakti sādhana apekṣayā upalabdhi samāna āśraya tve tu vyavadhāna kalpanā anupapatteḥ sarvadā abhivyakti prasaṅgaḥ tathā ca abhivyakti sādhana apekṣa tā upalabdhi samāna āśraya tve tu vyavadhāna kalpanā anupapatteḥ sarvadā abhivyaktiḥ anabhivyaktiḥ vā na tu antarāla kalpanāyā pramāṇam asti na ca samāna āśrayaṇām ekasyā atma bhūtānām dharmāṇām itaretara viṣaya viṣayi tvam saṃbhavati vijñāna sukha yoṣca prāc abhivyakteḥ saṃsāri tvam abhivyakti uttara kālam ca mukta tvaṃsya saḥ  anyaḥ parasmāt nitya abhivyakta jñāna svarūpāt atyanta vailakṣaṇyāt śaityam iva auṣṇyāt  paramātma bheda kalpanāyāñca vaidikaḥ kṛtāntaḥ parityaktaḥ syāt  mokṣasya idānīm iva nirviśeṣa tve tad artha adhika yatna anupapattiḥ śāstra vaiyarthyam ca prāpnoti iti ced na na avidyā bhrama apoha āptha tvāt na hi vastu tas  muktā muktatva aviśeṣaḥ  asti ātmanaḥ  nityāka rūpa tvāt kintu tad viṣaya avidyā apohyate śāstra upadeśa janita vijñānena prāk tad upadeśa prāpteḥ tad arthaḥ ca prayatna upapadyata eva avidyāvataḥ  avidyā nivṛtya nivṛtti kṛtaḥ  veśeṣa ātmanaḥ syāt iti ced  avidyā kalpanā viṣayatva abhyupagamāt rajjūṣara śuktakāgaganānām sarva udaka rajata malinatva ādivat adoṣa  iti avocāma timira atimitara dṛṣṭivat avidyā kartṛtva akatṛ tvā akṛta ātmanaḥ  viśeṣaḥ syāt iti ced  na dhyāti iva lelāyati iva iti svatas  avidyā kartṛtva sva pratiṣiddha tvā aneka vyāpāra sannipāta janita tvāt ca avidyā bhramasya viṣatva upapatteṣca yasya ca avidyā bhramaḥ  ghaṭa ādivat viviktaḥ  gṛhyate sa na avidyā bhramavān aham na jāne mugdhe asmi iti pratyata darśanāt avidyā bhramava tvam eva iti ced na tasya api viveka grahaṇāt  na hi yaḥ  yasya vivekena grahītā sa tasmin bhrānta iti ucyate tasya ca viveka grahaṇam tasmin  eva ca bhrama iti vipratiṣiddham na jāne mugdhaḥ  asmi iti dṛśyata iti bravīṣi tad darśinaḥ ca ajñānam mugdha rūpa tā dṛśyata iti ca tad darśanasya viṣayaḥ  bhavati karma tām āpadyata iti tad katham karma bhūtam sat kartṛ svarūpa dṛśi viśeṣaṇa jñānam ugdhate syātām atha dṛśi viśeṣaṇa tvam tayoḥ katham karma syātām dṛśinā vyāpyete karma hi kartṛ kriyayā vyāpyamānam bhavati anyat ca vyāpyam anyat vyāpakam na tena eva tad vyāpyate vada katham evam satya jñānam ugdhate dṛśi viśeṣaṇe syātām na ca ajñāna aviveka darśī ajñānam ātmanaḥ karma bhūtam upalabhamāna upalabdhṛ dharma tvena gṛhmāti śarīre kārśya rūpa dādavat tathā sukha duḥkha icchā prayatna ādīn sarvaḥ  lokaḥ  gṛhṇāti iti ced  tathā api grahītuḥ lokasya vivaktatā eva abhyupagatā syāt  na jāne aham tvad uktam mugdha eva iti ced  bhavatu ajñaḥ  mugdhaḥ  yaḥ tu evandarśū tam jñam amugdham pratijānīmahe vayam tathā vyosena uktam icchā ādi kṛtsnam kṣetram kṣetrī prakāśayati iti samam sarveṣu bhūteṣu tiṣṭhantam parameśvaram vinaśyat su vinaśyantam ityādi śataśa uktam tasmāt nā atmanaḥ svatas  baddha mukta jñāna kṛtaḥ  viśeṣaḥ  asti sarvadā sama eka rasa svābhāvya abhyupagamāt ye tvataḥ anyathā atma vastu parikalpya bandha mokṣa ādiśāstriṃ ca artha vādam āpādayanti ta utsahante khe api śākunam padam draṣṭum kham vā muṣṭinā akraṣṭum carmavat veṣṭitum vayam tu tad kartum aśaktāḥ sarvādā samaikaram asat vaitam avikriyam ajam ajaram amaram amṛtam abhayam ātma tattvam brahmā eva sma iti eṣa sarva vedānta niścitor atha iti evam pratipadyāmahe tasmāt brahma apyeti iti upacāra mātram etad vipīratagrahavat deha saṃtateḥ vi ccheda mātram vijñāna phalam apekṣya svapna buddha anta gamana dṛṣṭāntasya dārṣṭa antikaḥ saṃsāraḥ  varṇitaḥ saṃsāra hetuḥ ca vidyā karma pūrva prajñā varṇitā yaiḥ ca upādhi bhūtaiḥ kārya karaṇa lakṣaṇa bhūtaiḥ pariveṣṭitaḥ saṃsāri tvam anubhavati tāni ca uktāni teṣām sākṣāt prayojakau dharma adharvau  iti pūrva pakṣam kṛtvā kāma eva iti avadhāritam yathā ca brahmaṇena ayam arthaḥ  ayavadhārita evam mantreṇa api iti bandham bandha kāraṇam ca uktvā upasaṃhṛtam prakaraṇam iti na kāmayamāna iti atha akāyamāna iti ārabhya suṣupta dṛṣṭanātasya dārṣṭa antika bhūtaḥ sarva ātma bhāvaḥ  mokṣa uktaḥ mokṣa kāraṇam cā atma kāma tayā yad āpta kāma tvam uktam tad ca sāmartha āyadana ātma jñānam antareṇā atmaka āmaya tayā apta kāma tvam iti sāmarthyāt brahma vidyā eva mokṣa kāraṇam iti uktam atas  yadi api kāmaḥ  mūlam iti uktam tathā api mokṣa kāraṇa viparyayeṇa bandha kāraṇam avidyā ityet api uktam eva bhavati atra api mokṣaḥ  mokṣa sādhanam ca brāhmaṇena uktam tasya eva dṛḍhīkaraṇāya mantra udāhriyate śloka śabda vācyaḥ tad tasmin  eva artha eṣa ślokaḥ  mantraḥ  bhavati yadā yasmin kāle sarve samastāḥ kāmāḥ tṛṣṇā prabhedāḥ pramucyante ātma kāmya brahma vidaḥ sa mūlataḥ  viśīryante ye prasiddhā loka iha amutra arthāḥ putra vitta loka eṣaṇā lakṣaṇā asya prasiddhasya puruṣasya hṛdi buddhau śritā āśritāḥ atha tadā martyaḥ  maraṇa dharmā san kāma viyogāt sa mūlataḥ amṛtaḥ  bhavati atra asmin  eva śarīre vartamānaḥ  brahma samaśnute brahma bhāvam mokṣam pratipadyata iti arthaḥ atas  mokṣaḥ  na deśa antara gamana ādi apekṣate tasmāt viduṣaḥ  na utkrāmanti prāṇā yā avasthitā eva sva kāraṇe puruṣe samavanīyante nāma mātram hi avaśiṣyata iti uktam katham punar  samanavīteṣu prāṇeṣu dehe ca sva kāraṇe pralīne vidvān muktaḥ  atra eva sarva ātmā sanvartamānaḥ punar  pūrvavat dehi tvam saṃsāritva lakṣaṇam na pratipadyata iti atra ucyate tad tatra ayam dṛṣṭāntaḥ  yathā loke ahiḥ sarpaḥ tasya nirlvayanī nirmekaḥ sa ahi nirlvayanī valmīke sarpa āśraye valmīka ādau  iti arthaḥ mṛtā pratyastā prakṣiptān ātma bhāvena sarpeṇa parityaktā śayīta varte evam eva yathā ayam dṛṣṭānta idam śarīram sarpa sthānīyena muktena anātma bhāvena parityaktam mṛtam iva śete atha itaraḥ sarpa sthānīyaḥ  muktaḥ sarmātama bhūtaḥ sarpavat tatra eva vartamānaḥ  api aśarīra eva na pūrvavtupanaḥ sa śarīraḥ  bhavati kāma karma prayukta śarīra ātma bhāvena hi pūrvam śarīraḥ  martyaḥ ca tad viyogāt atha idānīm aśarīraḥ  ata eva ca amṛtaḥ prāṇaḥ prāṇiti iti prāṇaḥ prāṇasya prāṇam iti hi vakṣyamāṇe śloke prāṇa bandhanam hi somya manaḥ iti ca śruti antare prakaraṇa vākya sama arthāt ca para evā atmā atra prāṇa śabda vācyaḥ brahmā eva paramātmā eva kim punar tad teja eva vijñānam jyotiḥ yenā atma jyotiṣā jagat avabhāsyamānam prajñā netram vijñāna jyotiṣmad sat avibraṃśadvartate yaḥ kāma praśnaḥ vimokṣa arthaḥ  yājñavalkyena varaḥ  dattaḥ  janakāya sa hetukaḥ  bandha mokṣa artha lakṣaṇaḥ  dṛṣṭāntika bhūtaḥ sa eṣa nirṇītaḥ sa vistaraḥ  janaka yājñavalkya ākhyāyikā rūpa dhāriṇyā śrutyā saṃsāra vimokṣa upāya uktaḥ prāṇibhyaḥ idānīm śrutiḥ svayam evā aha vidyā niṣkriya artham janakena evam uktam iti katham saḥ  aham ovam vimokṣitaḥ tvayā bhagavate tubhyam vidyā niṣkriya artham sahasram dadāmi iti ha eva kila uvācā uktavān janakaḥ  vaidehaḥ atra kasmdā vimokṣa padārthe nirṇīte videha rājyam ātmānam eva ca na nivedayati eka deśa uktau  iva sahasram eva dadāti tatra kaḥ  abhiprāya iti atra kecid varṇayanti adhyātma vidyā rasikaḥ  janakaḥ śrutam api artam punar mantraiḥ śuśrūṣati atas  na sarvam eva nivedayati śrutvā abhipretam yājñavalkyāt punar ante nivedayiṣyāmi iti hi manyate yadi ca atra eva sarva nivedayāmi nivṛtta abhilāṣaḥ  ayam śravaṇāt iti matvā ślokān navakṣyati iti ca bhayāt sahasra dānam śuśrūṣā liṅga jñāpanāya iti sarvam api etad asat  puruṣasya iva pramāṇa bhūtāyāḥ śruteḥ vyāja anupapatteḥ artha śeṣa upapatteḥ ca vimokṣa padārtha ukte api ātma jñāna sādhana ātma jñāna śeṣa bhūtaḥ sarveṣaṇā parityāgaḥ saṃnyāsa ākhyaḥ  vaktavyor atha śeṣaḥ  vidyate tasmāt śloka mātra śuśrūṣā kalpanā anṛjvaḥ agatikā hi gatiḥ puvarukta artha kalpanā sā ca ayuktā satyām gatau na ca tad stuti mātram iti avocāma nanu evam satyata ūrdhvam vimokṣāya eva iti vaktavyam na eṣa dauṣaḥ ātma jñānavat aprayojakaḥ saṃnyāsaḥ pakṣe pratipatti karmavat iti hi manyate saṃnyāsena tanum tyajet  iti smṛteḥ sādhutva āpakṣe api na ata ūrdhvam vimokṣāya eva iti praśnam arhati mokṣa sādhana bhūtātma jñāna paripāka artha tvāt ātma kāmasya brahma vidaḥ  mokṣa iti etasmin  arthe mantra brahmaṇā ukte vistara pratipādakā ete ślokā bhavanāti aṇuḥ sūkṣmaḥ panthā durvijñeya tvāt vitatas  vistīrṇaḥ  vispaṣṭa taraṇa hetu tvāt vā vitara iti pāṭhā antarāt mokṣa sādhanaḥ  jñāna mārgaḥ purāṇaḥ cirantanaḥ  nitya śruti prakāśita tvāt na tārkika buddhi prabhava kudṛṣṭi mārgavadarvāk kālikaḥ  mā spṛṣṭaḥ  mayā labdha iti arthaḥ yaḥ  hi yena labhyate sa tam spṛśati iva saṃbadhyate tena ayaḥ brahma vidyā lakṣaṇaḥ  mokṣa mārgaḥ  mayā labdha tvāt mā spṛṣṭa iti ucyate na kevalam mayā labdhaḥ kintu anuvittaḥ  mayā eva anuvedanam nāma vidyāyāḥ paripāka apekṣayā phala avasāna tā niṣṭhā prāptiḥ bhujeḥ iva tṛpti avasāna tā pūrvam tu jñāna prāpti saṃbandha mātram eva iti viśeṣaḥ kim asā  ena mantra dṛś ekaḥ  brahma vidyā phalam prāptaḥ  na anyaḥ prāptavān yena anuvittaḥ  mayāva iti avadhārayati na eṣa doṣaḥ asyāḥ phalam ātma sākṣikam anuttamam iti brahma vidyāyāḥ stuti paratvāt  evam hi kṛtārtha ātma abhimāna karam ātma pratyaya sākṣikam ātma jñānam kim atas  param anyatsyāt iti brahma vidyā stauti na tu puranyaḥ brahma vid tad phalam na prāpnoti iti tad yaḥ yaḥ  devānām iti sarva artha śruteḥ tad evā aha tena brahma vidyā mārgeṇa dhīrāḥ prajñāvantaḥ  anye api brahma vida iti arthaḥ apiyantpigacchanti brahma vidyā phalam mokṣam svargam lokam svarga loka śabda viṣṭapa vācyam api san  iha prakaraṇāt mokṣa abhidhāyakaḥ itas  asmāt śarīra pātāt ūrdhvam jīvanta eva vimuktāḥ santaḥ tasmin mokṣa sādhana mārge vipratipattiḥ mumukṣūṇām katham tasmin śuklam śuddham vimalam āhuḥ kecid mumukṣavaḥ  nīlam anye piṅgalam anye haritam lohitam ca yathādarśanam na āḍhyaḥ tu etāḥ suṣumna ādyāḥ śleṣma ādiḥ asaṃsaṃpūrṇāḥ śuklasya nīlasya piṅgalasya ityādi ukta tvāt  ādityam vā mokṣa mārgam evaṃvidham manyante eṣa śukla eṣa nīlaḥ iti ādi śruti antārāt  darśana mārgasya śukla ādi varṇa asaṃbhavāt sarvathā api tu prakṛtāt brahma vidyā mārgāt anya ete śukla ādayaḥ nanu śuklaḥ śuddhaḥ  adhvataiya mārgaḥ naḥ nīla pūta ādi śabdaiḥ varṇa vācakaiḥ saha anudravaṇāt  yān śukla ādīn yoginaḥ  mokṣa pathān āhuḥ na te mokṣa mārgāḥ saṃsāra viṣayā ve hi te cakṣuṣaḥ  vā mūrdhnaḥ vā anyebhyaḥ  vā śarīra deśebhya iti śarīdeśāt niḥsaraṇa saṃbandhāt  brahma ādi loka prāpakāhi te tasmāt ayam eva mokṣa mārgaḥ  ya ātkāma tvenā aptakāma tayā sarvakāmakṣe gamana anupapattau pradīpa nirvāṇavat cakṣuḥ ādīnām kārya karaṇānām atra eva samavanaya iti eṣa jñāna mārgaḥ panthā brahmaṇā paramātma svarūpeṇa eva brāhmaṇena tyakta sarvaiśaṇenana anuvittaḥ tena brahma vidyā mārgeṇa brahma vid anyaḥ  apyeti kīdṛśaḥ  brahma vittena eti iti ucyate pūrvam puṇya kṛt bhūtvā punar tyaktu putra ādi eṣaṇaḥ parātma tejasi ātmānam saṃyojya tasmin  abhinirvṛttaḥ taijam asaḥ cā atma bhūta iha eva iti arthaḥ īdṛśaḥ  brahma vittena mārgeṇa eti na punar  puṇya ādi samuccaya kāriṇaḥ  grahaṇam virodhāt iti avocāma apuṇya puṇya uparame yam punarbhava nirbhāḥ śāntāḥ saṃnyāsinaḥ  yānti tasmai mokṣa ātmane namaḥ iti ca smṛteḥ tyaja dharmam adhramam ca ityādi puṇyā puṇya tyāga upadeśāt nirāśiṣam anārambham nirnamaskāram astutum akṣoṇam kṣīṇa karmāṇam tam devāḥ  brāhmaṇam viduḥ na etādṛśam brāhmaṇasya asti vittam yathā ekatā sama tā satyatā ca śīlam sthitiḥ daṇḍa nidhānam ārjavam tatas tatas ta uparamaḥ kriyābhyaḥ ityādi smṛtibhyaḥ ca upadekṣyati ca iha api tu eṣa nityaḥ  mahimā brahmaṇasya na vardhate karmaṇā naḥ kanīyān iti karma prayojana abhāve hetum uktavā tasmāt eva vid śāntaḥ  dānta ityādinā sarva kriyā uparamam tasmāt yathāvyākhyātam eva puṇya kṛtvam athavā yaḥ  brahma vittena eti sa puṇya kṛta ejasaḥ ca iti brahma vid sutiḥ eṣā puṇya kṛti taijase ca yogini mahābhāgyam prasiddham loke tābhyām atas  brahma vid satūyate prakhyāta mahābhāgya tvāt loke andham adarśana ātmakam tamaḥ saṃsāra niyāmakam praviśanti pratipadyante ke ye avidyām vidyātaḥ  anyām sādhya sādhana lakṣaṇam upāsate karma anuvartanta iti arthaḥ tatas tasmāt api bhūya iva bahutaram iva tamaḥ praviśanti ke ya u vidyāyām avidyā vastu pratipādikāyām karma arthāyām trayyām eva vidyāyām ratā abhiratāḥ vidhi pratiṣedha para eva vedaḥ  na anyaḥ  asti iti upaniṣad artha anapekṣiṇa iti arthaḥ yadi te adarśana lakṣaṇam tamaḥ pravisanti kaḥ  doṣa iti ucyate anandā anānandā asukhā nāma te lokāḥ tena andhena adarśana lakṣaṇena tamasā avṛtā vyāptāḥ te tasya ajñāna tamasaḥ  gocarāḥ tān  te pretya mṛtvā abhigacchanti abhiyānti ke ye avidvāṃsaḥ kim sāmānyena avidvattā mātreṇa na iti ucyate abudhaḥ budheḥ avagamana arthasya dhātoḥ kvippratyaya antasya rūpam ātma avagama varjitā iti arthaḥ janāḥ prakṛtā eva janana dharmiṇaḥ  vā iti etad  ātmānam svam param rūpam sarva prāṇimanīṣita jñam hṛd stham aśanāya ādi dharma atītam ca udyadi vijānīyāt sahasreṣu kaścid  ced iti ātma vidyāyā durlabha tvam darśayati katham ayam para ātmā sarva prāṇi pratyaya sākṣī yaḥ  na iti na iti ityāt yuktaḥ  yasmāt na anyaḥ  asti draṣṭā śrotā mantā vijñātā samaḥ sarva bhūta sthaḥ  nitya śuddha buddha mukta svabhāvaḥ  asmi bhavāmi iti pūruṣaḥ puruṣaḥ sa kim icchan  tad sava rūpa vyatiriktam anya t astu phala bhūtam kimicchankasya vānyasyā atmanaḥ  vyatiriktasya kāmāya prayojanāya na hi tasyā atmana eṣṭavyam phalam na ca ātmanaḥ  anyosti yasya kāmāya icchati sarvasya ātma bhūta tvāt atas  kimicchankasya kāmāya śarīram anusaṃjvaret bhraṃśet  śarīra upādhi kṛta duḥkham anuduḥkhī syāt  śarīra tāpam anutapyeta anātma darśinaḥ hi tad vyatirikta vastavantara īpsoḥ mama idam syāt putrasya idam bhāryāyāḥ  idam iti evam īhamānaḥ punar  punar janana maraṇa prabandha rūḍhaḥ śarīra rogam anu rujyate sarva ātma darśinaḥ tu tad asaṃbhava iti etad āha kiñca yasya brāhmaṇasya anuvittaḥ  anulabdhaḥ pratibuddhaḥ sākṣātkṛtaḥ katham aham asmi param brahma iti evam pratyagātma tvena avagata ātmā asmin saṃdahye saṃdehe aneka anartha saṃkaṭa upacaye gahane viṣame aneka śata sahasra viveka vijñāna pratipakṣe viṣame praviṣṭaḥ sa yasya brāhmaṇasya anuvittaḥ pratibodhena iti arthaḥ sa viśva kṛt viśvasya kartā katham viśvakṛttavam tasya kim viśvakṛt iti nāma iti āśaṅkyā aha sa hi yasmāt sarvasya kartā na nāma mātram na kevalam viśvakṛt para prayuktaḥ san kim tarhi tasya lokaḥ sarvaḥ kim anyā lokaḥ  anyaḥ  asau  iti ucyate sa u loka eva loka śabdenā atmā ucyate tasya sarva ātmā sa ca sarvasya ña atmā iti arthaḥ ya eṣa brāhmaṇena pratyagātmā pratibuddhatayā anuvitta ātma anartha saṃkaṭe gahane praviṣṭaḥ sa na saṃsārī kintu para eva yasmāt viśvasya kartā sarvasyā atmā tasya ca sarva ātmā eka eva advitīyaḥ para eva asmi iti anusaṃdhātavya iti śloka arthaḥ kiñca iha eva āleka artha saṃkule santaḥ  bhavantaḥ jñāna dīrgha nidrā mohitāḥ santaḥ kathañcid iva brahma tattvam ātma tvena atha vidmaḥ  vijānīmaḥ tad etad brahma prakṛta mahaḥ vayam kṛtārthā iti abhiprāyaḥ yad etad brahma vijānīmaḥ tad na ced viditavantaḥ  vayam vedanam vedaḥ  vedaḥ  asya asti iti vedī vedyā iva vediḥ na vedira vediḥ tatas  aham avediḥ syām yadi avediḥ syām kaḥ  doṣaḥ syāt mahati ananta parimāṇā janma maraṇa ādi lakṣaṇā vinaṣṭiḥ vinaśanam ahaḥ vayam asmāt mahataḥ  vinaśanāt nirmuktā yad advayam brahma viditavanta iti arthaḥ yathā ca vayam brahma viditvā asmāt vinaśanāt vipramuktā evaṃye tad viduḥ amṛtāḥ te bhavanti ye punar na eva brahma viduḥ ta itare brahma vidbhyaḥ  anye abrahma vida iti arthaḥ duḥkham eva janma maraṇa ādi lakṣaṇam eva apiyanti pratipadyante na kadācid api aviduṣām tatas  vinivṛttiḥ iti arthaḥ duḥkham eva hi ta ātma tvena upagacchanti yadā punar etam ātmānam kathañcid parama kāruṇikam kañcid ācāryam prāpya tatas  labdha prayādaḥ san  anu paścāt paśyati sākṣātkaroti svam ātmānam devam dyotanavantam dātāram vā sarva prāṇi karma phalānām yathā karma anurūpam añjasā sākṣāt īśānam sāvāminam bhūta bhavyasya kāla trayasya iti etad  na tatas tasmāt īśānāt devāt ātmānam viśeṣeṇa jugupsate gopāyitum icchati sarvaḥ  hi leka īśvarāt guptam icchati bhedeḥ śī ayam tu ekatvadarśī na bibheti kutaścana atas  na tadā vijugupsate yadā īśānam devam añjasā atma tvena paśyati na tadā nindati vā kiñcid  sarvam ātmānam hi paśyati sa evaṃpaśyan kamasau nindyāt  kiñca yasmāt īśānāt arvāgi asmāt anya viṣaya eva iti arthaḥ saṃvatsaraḥ kāla ātmā sarvasya janimataḥ paricchettā yama paricchindan  arvāk eva vartate ahobhiḥ sva avayavaiḥ ahorātraiḥ iti arthaḥ tad jyotiṣām jyotiḥ ādityādi jyotiṣām api avabhāsaka tvāt āyuḥ iti upāsane tasmāt āyuṣmantaḥ te tasmāt āyuṣkāmenā ayuḥ guṇena upāsyam brahma iti arthaḥ kiñca yasmin yatra brahmaṇi pañca pañcajanā gandharva ādayaḥ pañca eva saṃkhyātā gandharvāḥ pitaraḥ  devāḥ  asurā rakṣāṃsi niṣāda pañcamā vā varṇā ākāśaḥ ca avyākṛta ākhyaḥ  yasmin sūtram imotam ca protam ca yasmin pratiṣṭhita etasmin   u khalu akṣare gārgyākāśa iti uktam tam evā atmānam amṛtam brahma manye aham na ca aham ātmānam tatas  anya tvena jāne kim tarhi amṛtaḥ  aham brahma vidvān sanna jñāna mātreṇa tu martyaḥ  aham āsam tad apagamāt vidvān aham amṛta eva kiñca tena hi caitanya ātma jyotiṣā avabhāsyamānaḥ prāṇa ātma bhūtena prāṇi iti tena prāṇasya api prāṇaḥ sa tam prāṇasya prāṇam tathā cakṣuṣaḥ  api cakṣuḥ uta śrautrasya api śrotram brahmam aśaktyodhiṣṭhitānām hi cakṣuḥ ādīnām darśana ādi sāmarthyam svatas  kāṣṭha loṣṭa samāni hi tāni caitanya ātma jyotiḥ śūnyāni manasaḥ  api mana iti ye viduḥ cakṣuḥ adāvyāpāra anumitāstivam pratyāga ātmānam na viṣaya bhūtam ye viduḥ te nicikyuḥ niścayena jñātavantaḥ  brahma purāṇam cirantanam agryam agre bhavam tad yad ātma vidaḥ  viduḥ iti hi ātharvaṇe yasmāt evam tasmāt edhā eva ekena eva prakāreṇa vijñāna ghana eka rasa prakāreṇā akāśavat nirantareṇa anudraṣṭavyam yasmāt etad brahma aprameyam sarva eka tvāt  anyena hi anyat pramīyata idam tu ekam eva atas  aprameyam dhruvam nityam kūṭastham avicālī iti arthaḥ nanu viruddham idam ucyate aprameyam jñāyata iti ca jñāyata iti pramāṇaiḥ mīyata iti arthaḥ  aprameyam iti ca tad pratiṣedhaḥ na eṣa doṣaḥ anyat avastuvat anāgama pramāṇa prameyatva pratiṣedha artha tvāt yathā anyāni vastūni āgama nirapekṣaiḥ pramāṇaiḥ viṣayīkriyante na tathā etad ātmata tvam pramāṇa antareṇa viṣayīkartum śakyate sarvasya āamatve kena kam paśyet vijīnāyat iti pramātṛ pramāṇa ādi vyāpāra pratiṣedhena evā agamaḥ  api vijñāpayati na tu abhidhāna abhidhelakṣaṇa vākya dharma aṅgīkaraṇena tasmāt nā agamanā api svarga meru ādivat tad pratipādyate pratipādayitra ātma bhūtam hi tad  pratipādayituḥ pratipādanasya pratipādya viṣaya tvāt bhede hi sati tad bhavati jñānam ca tasmin parātbhāva nivṛttiḥ eva na tasmin sākṣāt ātma bhāvaḥ kartavye vidyamānvāda ātma bhavasya nityaḥ  hi ātma bhāvaḥ sarvasya ātat viṣaya iva pratyavabhasate tasmāt atad viṣaya avabhāsa nivṛtta vyatirekeṇa na tasmin  ātma bhāvaḥ  vidhīyate anyātbhāva nivṛttau  ātma bhāvaḥ sva ātmani svābhāvikaḥ  yaḥ sa kevalaḥ  bhavati iti ātmā jñāyata iti ucyate svatas ca aprameyaḥ pramāṇa antareṇa na viṣayīkriyata iti uccayate svatas ca aprameyaḥ pramāṇa antareṇa na viṣayīkriyata iti ubhayam api aviruddham eva virajaḥ  vigata rajaḥ  rajaḥ  nāma dharma adharma ādi malam tad rahita iti etad  paraḥ paraḥ  vyatiriktaḥ sūkṣmaḥ  vyāpī vā akāśāt api avyākṛta ākhyāt ajaḥ na jāyate janma pratiṣedhāt uttare api bhāva vikārāḥ pratiṣiddhāḥ sarveṣām janma ādi tvāt  ātmā mahān parimāṇataḥ  mahatatraḥ sarvasmāt  dhruvaḥ  avināśī tam īdṛśam ātmānam eva dhīraḥ  dhāmān vijñāya upadeśataḥ śāstrataḥ ca prajñām śāstra ācārya upadiṣṭa viṣayām jijñāsā pari samāpti karīm kurvīta brāhmaṇaḥ evam prajñā karaṇa sādhanāni saṃnyāsa śama dama uparama titikṣā samādhānāni kuryīt iti arthaḥ na anudhyāyāt na anucintayet bahūn prabhūtān śabdān tatra bahutva pratiṣedhāt kevala ātmakatva pratipādakāḥ su alpāḥ śabdā anujñāyante om iti evam dhyāyatha ātmānam anyā vācaḥ  vimiñcatha iti cā atharvaṇe vācaḥ  viglāpanam viśeṣeṇa glāni karam śrama karam hi yasmāt tad bahu śabda abhidhyānam iti sa hetukau bandha mokṣau  abhihitau mantra brāhmaṇabhyām ślokaiḥ ca punar mokṣa svarūpam vistareṇa pratipāditam evam etasmin  ātma viṣaye sarvaḥ  vedaḥ  yathā upayuktaḥ  bhavati tad tathā vaktavyam iti tad artheyam kaṇḍikā arabhyate tad ca tathā asmin prapāṭhake abhihitam sa prayojanam anūdyātra eva upayogaḥ kṛtsnasya vedasya kāmya rāśi varjitasya iti evam artham ukta artha anuvādaḥ sa vā eṣa ityādiḥ sa iti ukta parāmarśa arthaḥ kaḥ  asau  uktaḥ parāmṛśyate tam prati nirdiśati ya eṣa vijñāna maya iti atīntara vākya ukta saṃpratyayaḥ  mā bhūt iti ya eṣaḥ katama eṣa iti ucyate vijñāna mayaḥ prāṇeṣu iti uttara vākya ulliṅganam saṃśaya nivṛti artham uktam hi pūrvam janaka praśna ārambhe katam ātmā iti yaḥ  ayam vijñāna mayaḥ prāṇeṣu ityādi etad uktam bhavati yaḥ  ayam vijñāna mayaḥ prāṇeṣu ityādinā vākyena pratipāditaḥ svayan jyotiḥ ātmā sa eṣa kāma karma avidyānām anātma dharmatva pratidāpādana dvāreṇa mokṣitaḥ paramātma bhāvam āpāditaḥ para eva ayam na anya iti eṣa sa sākṣāt mahān aja ātmā iti uktaḥ yaḥ  ayam vijñāna mayaḥ prāṇeṣu iti yathāvyākhyāta artha eva ya eṣaḥ  antar hṛdaye hṛdayepuṇḍarīka madhye hṛdaya puṇḍarīka madhye ya eṣa ākāśaḥ para evā atmā nirupādhikaḥ  vijñāna mayasya sva svabhāḥ tasmin sva svabhāve parama ātmani ākāśa ākhye sete caturtham etad vyākhyātam
