kva eṣa tadā abhūt iti asya prativacana tvena sa ca sarvasya brahma indrāt eḥ vaśī sarvaḥ  hi asya vaśe vartate uktam ca etasya vā akṣarasya praśāsana iti na kevalam vaśī sarvasya īśāna īśitā ca brhama indra prabhṛtīnām īśitṛ tvam ca kadācid jāti kṛtam yathā rāja kumārasya balavattarān api bhṛtyān prati tadvat mā bhūt iti āha sarvasya adhipatiḥ adhiṣṭhāya pālayitā svatantra iti arthaḥ na rāja putravat amātya ādi bhṛtya tantraḥ trayam api etad vaśitva ādi hetu hetumat rūpam yasmāt sarvasya adhipatiḥ tatas  asau sarvasya īśānaḥ yaḥ  hi yam adhiṣṭāya pālayati sa tam pratīṣṭa eva iti prasiddham yasmāt ca sarvasya īśānaḥ tasmāt sarvasya vaśī iti kica anyat sa evaṃbhūtaḥ  hṛdi antar jyotiḥ puruṣaḥ  vijñānam ayaḥ  na sādhunā śāstra vihitena karmaṇā bhūyān bhavati na vardhate pūrva avasthātaḥ kenacid dharmeṇa naḥ eva śāstra priṣiddhena asādhunā karmaṇā kanīyān alpa taraḥ  bhavati pūrva avasthātaḥ  na hīyata iti arthaḥ kiñca sarvaḥ  hi adhiṣṭhāna pālana ādi kurvan para anugraha pīḍā kṛtena dharma adharma ākhyona yujyate asya eva tu katham tad abhāva iti ucyate yasmāt eṣa sarva īśvaraḥ san karmaṇaḥ  api īśitum bhavati eva śīlam asya tasmāt na karmaṇā saṃbandhyate kiñcāṣa bhūta adhipatiḥ brahma ādi stambha paryantānām bhūtānām adhipatiḥ iti ukta artham padam eṣa bhūtānām teṣām eva pālayitā rakṣitā eṣa setuḥ kiṃviśiṣṭa iti āha vidharaṇaḥ  varṇa āśrama ādi vyavasthāyāḥ  vidhārayitā tad āha eṣām bhūḥ ādīnā brahma loka antānām lokānām asaṃbhedāya asaṃbhinna maryādāyai parameśvareṇa setuvat avidhāryamāṇā lokāḥ saṃbhinna maryādāḥ syuḥ atas  lokānām asaṃbhedāya setu bhūtaḥ  ayam parameśvaraḥ  yaḥ svayan jyoḥ ātmā eva evaṃvid sarvasya vaśī ityādi brahma vidyāyāḥ phalam etad nirddiṣmaṭam kijyetiḥ iyaṃpuruṣa iti evamādi ṣaṣṭha prapāṭhaka vihitāyām etasyām brahma vidyāyām evaṃphalāyām kāmya eka deśa varjitam kṛtsnam karma kāṇḍam tādarthyena vaniyujyate tad katham iti ucyate tam etam eva bhūtam aupaniṣadam puruṣam veda anuvacanena mantra brāhmaṇa adhyayanena nitya svādhyāya lakṣaṇena vividiṣanti veditum icchanti ke brāhmaṇāḥ brāhmaṇa grahaṇam upalakṣaṇa artham aviśiṣṭaḥ  hi adhikāraḥ trayāṇām varṇānām athavā karma kāṇḍena mantra ha brāhmaṇena veda anuvacanena vivijiṣanti katham vividiṣantī iti ucyate yajñena ityādi ya punar mantra brāhmaṇa lakṣaṇena veda anuvacanena prakāśyamānam vividaṣanti iti vyācakṣate teṣām āraṇyaka mātram eva veda anuvacanam syāt  na hi karmakāṇena para ātmā prakāśyate taḥ tvaipaniṣadam iti viśeṣa śruteḥ veda anuvacanena iti ca aviśeṣita tvāt samasta grāhi dam vacanam na ca tad eka deśa utsarhe yuktaḥ nanu tvad pakṣe api upaniṣad varjam iti eka deśa tvam syāt  nā adya vyākhyāne avirodhāt asmat pakṣe na eṣa doṣaḥ  bhavati yadā veda anuvacana śabdena nityaḥ svādhyāyaḥ  vidhīyate tadā upaniṣada pu gṛhītā eva iti veda anuvacana śabda artha eka deśaḥ  na parityaktaḥ  bhavati yajña ādi saha pāṭhāt ca yajña ādīni karmāṇi eva anukramiṣyan veda anuvacana śabdam prayuṅkte tasmāt krama eva veda anuvacana śabdena ucyata iti gamyate karma hi nitya svādhyāyaḥ katham punar nitya svādhyāya ādibhiḥ karmabhiḥ ātmānam vividaṣanti na eva hi tāni ātmānam prakāśanayanta yathā upaniṣadaḥ na eṣa dodhaḥ karmaṇām viśuddhi hetu tvāt  karmabhiḥ saṃskṛtā hi viśuddha ātmānaḥ śaknuvanti ātmānam upaniṣad prakāśitam apratibandhena veditum tathā hi ātharvaṇe viśuddha sattvaḥ tatas tu tam paśyate niṣkalam dhyāyamānaḥ iti smṛtiḥ ca jñānam utpadyate puṃsām kṣayāt pāpasya karmaṇaḥ ityādiḥ katham punar nityāni karmāṇi saṃskāra arthāni iti avagamyate sa ha vā ātma yājī yaḥ  veda idam me anena aṅgam saṃskriyata idam me anena aṅgam upadhīyate ityādi śruteḥ sarveṣu ca smṛti śāstreṣu karmāṇi saṃskāra arthāni evā acakṣate aṣṭācatvāriṃśat saṃskārā ityādiṣu gītāsu ca yajñaḥ  daina tapaḥ ca eva pāvanāni manīṣiṇām sarve api ete yajña vidaḥ  yajña kṣapita kalmaṣāḥ iti yajñena iti dravya yajñā jñāna yajñāḥ ca saṃskāra arthāḥ saṃskṛtasya ca viśuddha satvasya jñāna utpattiḥ apratibandhena bhaviṣyati atas  yajñena vividiṣṭi dānena dānam api pāpa kṣaya hetu tvāt dharma vṛddhi hetu tvāt ca tapasā tapa iti aviśeṣeṇa kṛcchra cāndrāyaṇa ādi prāptau viśeṣaṇam anāśakena iti kāmān aśanam anāśakam na tu bhojana nivṛttiḥ bhojana nivṛttau mriyata eva nā atma vedanam veda anuvacana yajña dāna tapaḥ śabdena sarvam eva nityam karma upalakṣyate evam kāmya varjitam nityam karma jātam sarvam ātma jñāna utpatti dvāreṇa mokṣa sādhana tvam pritapadyate evam karma kāṇḍena asya eka vākya tauvagatiḥ evam yathā uktena nyāyena etam evā atmānam viditvā yathā prakāśitam muniḥ bhavati mananāt muniḥ yogī bhavati iti artha etam eva viditvā muniḥ bhavati na anyam nanu anya vedane api muni tvam syāt katham avadhāryata etam eva iti bāḍham anya vedane api muniḥ bhavet  kitu anya vedane na muniḥ eva syāt kim tarhi karmi api bhavet saḥ etam tu aupaniṣadam puruṣam viditvā muniḥ eva syāt na tu karmī atas  asādhāraṇam muni tvam vivakṣitam asya iti avadhārayati etam eva iti etasmin hi vidite kena kam paśyet iti evam kriyā sambhavāt mananam eva syāt  kiñca ecamevā atmānam svam lokam icchantaḥ prārthayantaḥ pravrājinaḥ pravrajana śīlāḥ pravraḍanti prakarṣeṇa vrajanti sarvāṇi karmāṇi saṃnyasyanti iti arthaḥ etam eva lokam icchanta iti avadhāraṇāt na bāhya lokatraya īpsūnām pārivrājya udhikāra iti gamyate na hi gaṅgādvāram pratipitsuḥ kāśī deśa nivāsī pūrva abhimukhaḥ praiti tasmāt bāhya loka traya arthinām putra karma apara brahma vidyāḥ sādhanam putreṇa ayam lokaḥ  jayyaḥ na anyena karmaṇā ityādi śruteḥ athaḥ tad arthibhiḥ putra ādi sādhanam pratyākhyāya na pārivrājyam pratipattum yuktam atad sādhana tvāt pārivrājyasya tasmāt etam eva lokam icchantaḥ pravrajanti iti yuktam avadhāraṇam ātma loka prāptiḥ hi avidyā nivṛttau sva ātmani avasthānam eva tasmāt ātmānam ced lokam icchaci yaḥ tasya sarva kriyā uparama evā atma valoka sādhanam mukhyam antaraṅgam yathā putra ādiḥ eva bāhya loka trayasya putra ādi karmaṇaḥ ātma lokam pratyasādhana tvāt  asambhavena viruddha tvam avocāma tasmāt ātmānam lokam icchantaḥ prvrajanti eva sarva kriyā abhyaḥ  nivarterannā iva iti arthaḥ yathā ca bāhya loka traya arthinaḥ pratiniyatāni putra ādīni sādhanāni vihatāni evam ātma loka arthanaḥ sarva eṣaṇā nivṛttiḥ pārivrājyam brahma vidaḥ  vidhīyata eva kutas  punar ta ātma loka arthanaḥ pravraḍanti eva iti ucyate tatra artha vāda vākya rūpeṇa hotum darśayatu etad ha sma vai tad  tad etad pārivrājye kāraṇam ucyate ha sma vai kila pūrva itikrānta kālīnā vidvāṃsa ātma jñāḥ prajām karma apara brahma vidyā ca prajā upalabhitam hi trayam etad bāhya loka traya sādhanam nirdiśyate prajām iti prajām kim na kāmayante putra ādi loka traya sādhanam na anutiṣṭhanti iti arthaḥ nanu apara brahma darśam anutiṣṭhanti eva tad balāt hi vyutthānam na apavādāt  brahma tam parāda āt yaḥ  anyatrā atmanaḥ  brahma veda sarvam tam parāda āditya para brahma darśam api apavadati eva apara brahmaṇaḥ  api sarva madhya antararbhāvāt  yatra na anyat paśyati iti ca pūrva apara bāhya antara darśana pratiṣedhāt ca apūrvam anaparam anantaram abāhyam iti tad kena kam paśyet vijīnāyīt iti ca tasmāt nā atma darśana vyatirekeṇa anyat vyutthāna kāraṇam apekṣate kaḥ punar teṣām abhiprāya iti ucyate kim prayojanam phalam sādhyam kariṣyāmaḥ prajayā sādhanena prajā hi bāhya loka sādhanam nirjñātā sa ca bāhya lokaḥ  na asti asmākam ātma vyatiriktaḥ sarvam hi asmākam ātma bhūtam eva sarvasya ca vayam ātma bhūtāḥ ātmā ca nā atma tvāt eva na kenacid sādhanena utpādya āpyaḥ  vikāryaḥ saṃskāryaḥ  vā yad api ātma yājinaḥ saṃskāra artham karma iti tad api kārya karaṇa ātma darśana viṣayam eva idam me anena aṅgam saṃskriyata iti aṅga aṅgitva ādi śravaṇāt na hi vijñāna ghana eka rasa nairantarya darśinaḥ aṅga aṅgi saṃskāra upadhāna darśanam sambhavati tasmāt na kiñcid praḍādi sādhanaiḥ kariṣyāmaḥ aviduṣām hi tad pradāji sādhanaiḥ karvyam phalam na hi mṛgatṛṣṇikāyām udaka pānām tad udaka darśī pravṛtta iti tatra uṣara mātram udaka abhāvam paśyeta u api pravṛttiḥ yuktā evam asmākam api parama artha ātma loka darśinām prajā ādi sādhana sādhye mṛgatṛṣṇikā ādi same avidvat darśana viṣaye na pravṛttiḥ yuktā iti abhiprāyaḥ tad etad ucyate yeṣām asmākam parama artha darśinām naḥ ayam ātma aśanāya ādi vinirmuktaḥ sādhu asādhu byāma vikāryaḥ  ayam lokaḥ phalam abhipratam na cā asyāḥ atmanaḥ sādhya sādhana ādi sarva saṃsāra dharma vinirmuktasya sādhanam kiñcid eṣitavyam sādhyasya hi sādhana anveṣaṇā kriyate asādhyasya sādhana anveṣaṇāyām hi jala buddhyā sthala iva taraṇam kṛtam syāt  khe vā śākuna pada anveṣaṇam tasmāt etam ātmānam viditvā prvjeyuḥ eva brāhmaṇā na karmā arabheran  iti arthaḥ yasmāt pūrve brāhnā evam vidvāṃsaḥ prajām akāmayamānāḥ ta evam sādhya sādhana saṃvyavahāram nindantaḥ  avidvat viṣayaḥ  ayam iti kṛtvā kim kṛtavanta iti ucyate te ha sma kila putra aṣaṇāyāḥ ca vista eṣaṇāyāḥ ca lokāṣaṇāyāḥ ca vyutthāya atha bhikṣā caryam canaranti ityādi vyākhyātam tasmāt ātmānam lokam icchantaḥ pravrajanti pravrajeyuḥ iti eṣa vidhiḥ artha vādena saṃgacchate hi sārtha vādasya asya lokaḥ tutya abhimukhyam upapadyate pravrajanti iti asya arthavāda rūpaḥ  hi etad ha sma ityādiḥ uttaraḥ  granthaḥ arthavādaḥ ced na arthavāda antaram apekṣeta apekṣate tu etad ha sma ityādi artha vādam pravrajanti iti etad  yasmāt pūrve vidvāṃsaḥ prajā ādi karmabhyaḥ  nivṛttāḥ pravjitavanta ava tasmāt adhunātanā api pravrajanti pravjeyuḥ iti evam sambadhyamānam na lokastiti abhimukham bhavitum arhati vijñāna samāna kartṛkatva upadeśa ādityānauvocāma veda anuvacana ādi sahapāṭhāt ca yathā atma vedana sādhana tvena vihitānām veda anuvacana ādīnām yathārtha tvam eva na arthavāda tvam tathā taiḥ eva saha paṭhitasya pārivrājyasyā atma loka prāpti sādhana tvena arthavāda tvam ayuktam phala vibhāga upadeśāt ca etam eva ātmānam lokam viditvā iti anyasmāt bāhyāt lokāt ātmānam phala antara tvena pravibhajati yathā putra eṇa eva ayam lokaḥ  ḍayyaḥ  na anyena karmaṇā karmaṇā pitṛ loke  iti na ca pravrajanti iti etad pārpatat loka stuti param pradhānavat ca artha vāda apekṣam sakṛt śrutam syāt  tasmāt abhrāntiḥ eva eṣā loka stiti param iti na ca anuṣṭheyena pārivrājyena stutuḥ upapadyate di pārivrājyam anuṣṭheyam api sat anya stuti artham syāt darśa pūrṇamāsa ādīnām api anuṣṭhāyānām stuti artha tā syāt  na ca anyatra kartavyatā etasmāt viṣaya ārjñātā yata iha stuti arthaḥ  bhavet  yadi punar  kvacid vidhiḥ parikalpyeta pārivrājyasya sa iha eva mukhyaḥ  na anyatra sambhavati yad api anadhikṛta viṣaye pārivrājyam parikalpyate tatra vṛkṣa ādi ārohaṇa ādya pu pārivrājyat kalpyeta kartavya tvena anirjñātatva aviśeṣāt tasmāt stutitva gandhaḥ  aapi atra na śakyaḥ kalpayitum yadyayātmā loka iṣyate kimartham tad prāpti sādhana tvena karmāṇi eva nā abheran kim pārivrājyena iti atra ucyate asyāḥ atma lokasya karmabhiḥ asaṃbandhāt  yam ātmānam icchantaḥ pravrajeyuḥ sa ātmā sādhana tvena phala tvena ca utpādyatva ādi prakārāṇām anyatamatvena apu karmabhiḥ na saṃbadhyate tasmāt sa eṣa na iti na iti ātma agṛhya u na hi gṛhyata ityādi lakṣaṇaḥ yasmāt eva lakṣaṇa ātmā karma phala sādhana asaṃbandhī sarva saṃsāra dharma vilakṣaṇaḥ  aśanāya ādi atītaḥ  asthūla ādi dharmavān ajaḥ  ajaraḥ  amaraḥ  amṛtaḥ  abhayaḥ saindhava ghanavat vijñāna eka rasa svabhāvaḥ svayan jyotiḥ eka eva advayaḥ apūrvaḥ  anaparaḥ  anantaraḥ  abāhya iti atad āgamataḥ tarkataḥ ca sthāpitam viśeṣataḥ ca iha janaka yājñavalkya saṃvāde asmin  tasmāt evaṃlakṣaṇa ātmani vidita ātma tvena na eva karma ārambha upapadyate tasmāt ātmā nirviśeṣaḥ na hi cakṣuṣmān pathi pravṛttaḥ  ahini kūpe kaṇke vā patati kṛtsnasya ca karma phalasya vidyā phale antarbhāvāt  na ca āyatna prāpye vastuni vidvān yatnam ātiṣṭhati aṅke ced madhu vindeta kimartham parvatam vrajet  iṣṭasya arthasya saṃprāptau kaḥ  vidvān yatnam ācaret  sarvam karma akhilam pārtham jñāne para samāpyate iti gītām u iha api ca etasya eva parama ānandasya brahma vid prāpyasya anyāni bhūtāni mātrām upajīvanti iti uktam atas  brahma vidā na karma ārambhaḥ yasmāt sarva eṣaṇā vinivṛttaḥ sa eva na iti na iti ātmānam ātma tvena upagamya tad rūpeṇa eva vartate tasmāt etam eva vidam na iti na iti ātma bhūta m u ha eva ete vakṣyamāṇe na tarataḥ  na prāpnuta iti yuktam eva iti vākya śeṣaḥ ke te iti ucyate atas  asmān nimittāt śarīra dhāraṇa ādi hetoḥ pāpam apuṇyam karma akaram kṛtavān asmi kaṣṭam khalu mama vṛttam anena pāpena karmaṇā aham narakam pratipatsya iti yaḥ  ayam paścāt pāpam karma kṛtavataḥ paritāmapaḥ sa enam na iti na iti ātma bhūtam na tarati yathā atas  kalyāṇam phala viṣaya kāmāt nimittāt yajña dāna ādi lakṣaṇam puṇyam śobhanam karma kṛtavān asmi jataḥ  aham asya phalaṃsukham upabhokṣya deha antara iti eṣaḥ api harṣaḥ tam na tarati ubhe u ha eva eṣa brahma vid ete karmaṇī tarati puṇya pāpa lakṣaṇe evam brahma vidaḥ saṃnyāsina ubhe api karmaṇaḥ  kṣīyate pūrva janmani kṛte ye te ca apūrve ca nā arabhyete kiñca na enam kṛta akṛte kṛtam nitya anuṣṭhānam akṛtam tasya eva akriyā te api kṛta akṛte enam na tapataḥ anātma jñam hi kṛtam phala dānena akṛtam pratyavāya utpādanena tapataḥ ayam tu brahma vid ā ātma vidyā agninā sarvāṇi karmāṇi bhasmīkaroti yathedhāṃsi samidvaḥ  agniḥ ityādi smṛteḥ śarīra ārambhakayoḥ tu upabhogena eva kṣayaḥ atas  brahma vida karma saṃbandhī tad etad vastu brāc maṇena uktam ṛcā mantreṇa abhyuktam prakāśitam eṣa na iti na ityādi lakṣaṇaḥ  nityaḥ  mahimā anye tu mahimānaḥ karma kṛtā iti anityāḥ ayam tu tad vilakṣaṇaḥ  mahimā svābhāvika tvāt nityaḥ  brahma vidaḥ  brāhmaṇasya tyakta sarveṣaṇasya kutaḥ asya nitya tvam iti hetum āha karmaṇā na vardhate śubha lakṣaṇena kṛtena vṛdvilakṣaṇām vikriyām na prāpna iti aśubhena karmaṇā naḥ kanīyān na api apakṣaya lakṣaṇām vikriyām prāpnoti upacaya apacaya hetu bhūtā eva hi sarvā vikriyā iti etābhyām pratiṣidhyante atas  avikriya tvāt nitya eṣa mahimā tasmāt tasya eva mahimnaḥ syāt bhavet pada vid padasya vettā padyate gamyate jñāyata iti mahimnaḥ svarūpam eva padam tasya padasya veditā kim tad pada vedanena syāt iti ucyate tam viditvā mahimānam na lipyate na saṃbadhyate karmaṇā pāpakena dharma adharma lakṣaṇena ubhayam api pāpakam eva viduṣaḥ tasmāt evam akarma saṃbandhi eṣa brāhmaṇasya mahimā na iti na ityādi lakṣaṇaḥ tasmāt evaṃvid śāntaḥ  bāhya indriya vyāpārata upaśāntaḥ tathā dāntaḥ  antar  karaṇa tṛṣṇā atas  nivṛtta uparataḥ sarva eṣaṇā vinirmuktaḥ saṃnyāsī titikṣuḥ dvandva sahiṣṇuḥ samāhita indriya antaḥ karaṇa acalana rūpāt vyāvṛtya ekāgrya rūpeṇa samāhitaḥ  bhūtvā tad etad uktam purastāt bālyam ca pāṇḍityam ca nirvidya iti ātmani eva sve kārya karaṇa saṃghāta ātmānam pratyak cetayitāram paśyati tatra kim tāvat mānnam paricchinam na iti ucyatesarvam samastam ātmānam eva paśyati na anyat ātma vyatiriktam vāla agra mānnam api asti iti evam paśyati mananāt muniḥ bhavati jāgrat svapna suṣupta ākhyam sthānan  ayam hitvā evam paśyantam brāhmaṇam na enam pāpmā puṇya pāpa lakṣaṇaḥ tarati na prāpna iti ayam tu brahma vid sarvam pāpmānam tarati ātma bhāvena eva vyāpnoti atikrāmati na enam pāpmā kṛta akṛta lakṣaṇaḥ tapati iṣṭa phala pratyavāya utpādanābhyām sarvam pāpmāna m ayam tapati brahma vid sarvatma darśana vahrinā bhasmīkaroti sa eṣa evaṃvidvipāyaḥ  vigata dharma adharmaḥ  birajaḥ  vigata rajaḥ  rajaḥ kāmaḥ  vigata kāmaḥ  avicikitsaḥ chinna saṃśayaḥ  aham asmi sarva ātmā param brahma iti niścita matiḥ brāhmaṇaḥ  bhavati ayam tu evaṃbhūta atasyām avasthāyām mukhyaḥ  brāhmaṇaḥ prāk etasmāt brahma svarūpa avasthānāt gauṇam asya brāhmaṇyam eṣa brahma lokaḥ  brahmā eva lokaḥ  brahma lokaḥ  mukhyaḥ  nirupacaritaḥ sarva ātma bhāva lakṣaṇaḥ  he smāraṭ  enam brahma lokam pariprāpitaḥ  asi abhayam na iti na ityādi lakṣaṇam iti ha uvāca yājñavalkyaḥ evam brahma bhūtaḥ  janakaḥ  yājñavalkyena brahma bhāvam āpāditaḥ pratyāha saḥ  aham tvayā brahma bhāvam āpāditaḥ san bhagavate tubhyam videhān deśāt mama rājya samastam dadāmi mām ca saha kartavyatākā parisamāptaḥ parama puruṣa arthaḥ etāvat puruṣeṇa kartavyam eṣā niṣṭhā eṣā parā gatiḥ etad niḥśreyasam etad prāpya kṛtakṛtyaḥ  brāhmaṇaḥ  bhavati etad sarva veda anuśāsanam iti yaḥ  ayam janaka yājñavalkya ākhyāyikāyām vyākhyāta ātmā sa vā eṣa mahān aja ātma anna ādaḥ sarva bhūta sthaḥ sarvān na anāmattā vasudānaḥ  vasu dhanam sarva prāṇi karma phalam tasya dātā prāṇinām yathākarma phalena yojayitā iti arthaḥ tam ekam ajam annādam vasu dānam ātmānam annāda vasu dāna guṇābhyām yuktam yaḥ  veda sa sarva bhūteṣu ātma bhūtaḥ  annamatti vindate ca vasu sarvam karma phala jātam labhate sarva ātma tvāt ena ya evam yathā uktam veda athavā dṛṣṭa phala arthibhiḥ api evaṅguṇa upāsyaḥ tena anna ādaḥ  vasoḥ ca labdhā dṛṣṭena eva phalena annātṛ tvena goḥ ca ādinā ca asya yogaḥ  bhavati iti arthaḥ idānīm samastasya evā araṇyarakasya yor atha uktaḥ sa samuccityā asyā kaṇḍikāyām nirdiśyata etāvān samasta āraṇyaka artha iti sa vā eṣa mahān aja ātma ajaraḥ  na jīryata iti na vipariṇamata iti arthaḥ amaraḥ  yasmāt ca ajaraḥ tasmāt amaraḥ  na mriyata iti amaraḥ yaḥ  hi jāyate jīryate ca sa vinaśyati mriyate vā ayam tu aja tvāt ajara tvāt ca avināśī yatas  ata eva amṛtaḥ yasmāt jani prabhṛtiḥ tribhiḥ bhāva viripaiḥ varjitaḥ tasmāt itaraiḥ api bhāva vikāraiḥ tribhiḥ tad kṛtaiḥ ca kāma karma moha ādibhiḥ mṛtyu rūpaiḥ vījata iti etad  abhayaḥ  ata eva yasmāt ca evam pūrva ukta viśeṣaṇaḥ tasmasmāt bhaya varjitaḥ bhayam ca hi nāma avidyā kāryam tad kārya priti ṣedhena bhāva vikāra pratiṣedhena ca avidyāyāḥ pratiṣedhaḥ siddhaḥ  veditavyaḥ abhaya ātmā evaṅguṇa viśiṣṭaḥ kim asau brahma parivṛḍham niratiśayam mahat iti arthaḥ abhayam vai brahma prasiddham etad loke abhayam brahma iti tasmāt yuktam evaṅguṇa viśiṣṭa ātmā brahma iti ya evam yathoktam ātmānam abhayam brahma veda saḥ  abhayam hi vai brahma bhavati eṣa sarvasya upaniṣadaḥ saṃkṣiptor atha uktaḥ etasya eva artha s samyak prabodhāya utpatti sthiti pralaya ādi kalpanā kriyā kāraka phala adhyāropaṇā cā atmani kṛtā tad apohena ca na iti na iti iti adhi āropita aviśeṣa apanaya dvāreṇa punar tatvam āveditam yathā eka prabhṛti ā apara ardha saṃkhyā svarūpa parijñānāyāḥ  rekhā adhyāropaṇam kṛtvā ekeyam rekhā daśeyam śateyam sahasreyam iti grāhayati avagamayati saṃkhyā svarūpam kevalam na tu saṃkhyāyāḥ  rekhā ātma tvam eva yathā ca ākāra ādīni akṣarāṇi grāhayati tathā ca iha utpati ādi aneka upāyam āsthāya ekam brahma tattvam āveditam punar tad kalpita upāya janita viśeṣa pariśodhana artham na iti na iti iti tattva upasaṃhāraḥ kṛtaḥ tad upasaṃhṛtam punar  pariśuddham kevalam eva saphalam jñānam ante asya kaṇḍikāyām iti iti caturtham brāhmaṇam āgama pradhānena madhuka aṇḍena brahma tattvam nirdhāritam punar tasya eva upatti pradhānena yājñavalkīyena kāṇḍena pakṣa pratipakṣa parigraham kṛtvā vigṛhya vādena vicāritam śaiṣya ācārya saṃbandhena ca ṣaṣṭhe praśna prativacana nyāyena sa vistaram vicārya upasaṃhṛtam atha idānīm nigamana sthānīyam maitreyī brāhmaṇam ārabhyete ayam ca nyāyaḥ  vākya kovidaiḥ parigṛhītaḥ  hetu apadeśāt pratijñāyāḥ punarvacanam nigamanam iti athavā agama pradhānena madhuka aṇḍena yad amṛtatva sādhanam sa saṃnyāsa bha ātma jñānam abhihitam tad eva tarkeṇa api amṛtatva sādhanam sa saṃnyāsam ātma jñānam adhigamyate tarka pradhānaṃhi yājñavalkīyam kāṇḍam tasmāt śāstra tarkābhyām niścitam etad yad etad ātma jñānam sa saṃnyāsam amṛtatva sādhanam iti tasmāt śāstra śraddhāvadbhiḥ amṛtatva pratipitsubhiḥ etad pratipattavyam iti āgama upapattibhyām hi niścitor athaḥ śraddheyaḥ  bhavati avyabhicārāt iti akṣarāṇām tu caturthe yathā vyākhyātor athaḥ tathā pratipattavyaḥ  atra api yāni akṣarāṇi avyākhyātāni tāni vyākhyāsyāmaḥ atha iti hetu upadeśa anantarya pradarśana arthaḥ hetu pradhānāni hi vākyāni atītāni tad anantaram āgama pradhānena pratijñātor athaḥ nigamyate maitreyī brāhmaṇena ha śabdaḥ  vṛttāvadyotakaḥ yājñavalkyasya ṛṣeḥ kila dve bhārye patnyau babhūvatuḥ āstām maitreyī ca nāmata ekā aparā kātyāyanī nāmataḥ tayoḥ bhāryayoḥ maitreyī iha kila brahma vādinī brahma vadana śīlā babhūvā asīt strī prajñā striyām yocitā sā strī prajñā sā eva yasyāḥ prajñā gṛha prayojana anveṣaṇā lakṣaṇā sā strī prajñā eva tarhi tasmin kāla āsīt kātyāyanī atha evam sati ha kila yājñavalkyaḥ  anyat pūrvasmāt gārhasthya lakṣaṇāt vṛttāt pārivrājya lakṣaṇam vṛttam upākariṣyan  upācikīrṣuḥ san he maitreyī iti jyeṣṭhām bhāryām āmantrayāmāsa āmanñya ca uvāca ha pravrajiṣyan pāni vrājyam kariṣyan vā are maitreyī asmāt sthānāt gārhasthyāt aham asmi bhavāmi maitreyī anujānīhi mām hanta icchasi yadi te anayā kātyāyanyā antam karavāṇotyādi vyākhyātam sā evam uktā uvāca maitreyī sarvā iyam pṛthivī vittena pūrṇā syāt nu kim syām kim aham vitta sādhyena karmaṇā amṛtā ahaḥ na syām iti na iti ha uvāca yājñavalkya ityādi samānam anyat  sa ha uvāca priyā eva pūrvam khalu naḥ asmabhyam bhavatī bhavanti sataḥ  priyam eva avṛdha dvardhitavatī nirdhāritavatī asi atas tuṣṭaḥ  aham hanta icchasi ced amṛtatva sādhanam jñātum he bhavati te tubhyam tad mṛtatva sādhanam vyākhyāsyāmi ātmani khalvare maitreyī dṛṣṭe katham dṛṣṭa ātmani iti ucyate pūrvam ācārya āgamābhyām śrute punar tarkeṇa upapattayā mate vicārite śravaṇam tu āgama mātreṇa mata upapattyā paścāt vijñāna evam etad na anyathā iti nirdhārite kim bhavati iti ucyata idam viditam bhavati idam sarvam iti yadā ātmanaḥ  anyat  ātma vyatirekeṇa abhāvāt  tam ayatha artha darśitam parādāt parākuryāt kaivalyā saṃbandhinam kuryāt ayam anātma svarūpeṇa mām paśyati iti aparādhāt iti bhāvaḥ caturthe śabda niḥśvāsena iva loka ādi artha niḥśvāsaḥ sāmarthyāt iktaḥ  bhavati iti pṛthak na uktaḥ iha tu sarva śāstra upa saṃhāram iti kṛtvār atha prāptaḥ  api arthaḥ spaṣṭīkartavya iti pṛthak ucyate sarva kārya pralaye vidyā nimitte saindhava ghanavat anantaraḥ  avāhyaḥ kṛtsnaḥ prajñāna dhana eka ātmā avatiṣṭhate pūrvam tu bhūta mānna asaṃsarga viśeṣat labdha viśeṣa vijñānaḥ san tasmin pravilāpite vidyayā viśeṣa vijñāne tad nimitte ca bhūta saṃsarge na pretya saṃjñā asti iti evam yājñavalkyena uktā sā ha uvāca atra eva mā bhagavān etasmin  eva vastuni prajñāna ghana eva na pretya saṃjñā asti iti moha antam moha madhyama apī pidāpī pada dava gamitavān asi saṃsohitavān asi iti arthaḥ atas  na vā aham imam ātmānam ukta lakṣaṇam vijānāmi vivekata iti sa ha uvāca na aham moham bravīmi avināśī vā are ayam ātmā yatas  vinaṣṭum śīlam asya iti vināśī na vināśya vināśī vinā śabdena vikriyā vināśī iti avikriya ātmā iti arthaḥ are maitreyī ayam ātmā prakṛtaḥ  anucchitti dharmā ucchittiḥ uccheda ucchedaḥ  antaḥ vināśa ucchittiḥ dharmaḥ  asya iti ucchittiḥ ardharmā na ucchitti dharmānucchitti dharmā na api vikriyā lakṣaṇaḥ  na api apaccheda lakṣaṇaḥ  vīnāśaḥ  asya vidyata iti arthaḥ caturṣu api prapāṭhakeṣu eka ātmā tulyaḥ  nirdhāritaḥ param brahma upāya viśeṣaḥ tu tasya adhigame anyaḥ ca anyaḥ ca upeyaḥ tu sa evā atmā yaḥ caturthe atha ata ādeśaḥ  na iti na iti iti nirdiṣṭaḥ sa eva pañcame prāṇa paṇa upanyāsena śākalya yājñavalkya saṃvāde nirdhāritaḥ punar  pañcama samāptau punar janaka yājñavalkya saṃvāde punar iha upaniṣad samāptau caturṇām api prapāṭhakānām etad ātma niṣṭhatā na anyaḥ  antarāle kaścid api vivakṣiter atha iti etad pradarśana āya anta upasaṃhāraḥ sa eṣa na iti na ityādiḥ yasmāt prakāra śatena api nirūpyamāṇe tad tave na iti na iti ātmā eva niṣṭhā na anya upalabhyate tarkeṇa vā agamena vā tasmāt etad eva amṛtatva sādhanam yad etad na iti na iti ātma parijñānam sarva saṃnyāsaḥ ca iti etam artham upasaṃjihīrṣan  āha etāvat etāvat mātram yad etad na iti na iti advaita ātma darśanam idam ca anya sahakāri kāraṇa nirapekṣam eva are maitreyī amṛtatva sādhanam yad pṛṣṭatī asi yad eva bhagavān veda tad eva me brūhi amṛtatva sādhanam iti tad etāvat evetu vijñeyam tvayā iti ha evam kila amṛtatva sādhanam ātma jñānam priyāyai bhāryāyāḥ  uktvā saṃnyāsa paryavasānā etāvān upadeśa etad veda anuśāsanam eṣā parama niṣṭhā eṣa puruṣa artha karta vyatānta iti idānīm vicāryate śāstra artha viveka pratipattaye yata ākulāni hi vākyāni dṛśyante yāvajjīvam agni hotram juhuyāt  yāvat jīvam darśa pūrṇamāsābhyām yajeta kurvan  eva iha karmāṇi jijīviṣet śatam samāḥ etad vai jarā maryam sarvam yad agnihotram ityādīnyā eka āśrami ājñāpakānyāni cā aśrama antara pratipādakāni vākyāni viditvā vyutthāya pravrajanti brahmacaryam samāpya gṛhī bhavet grahāt vanī bhūtvā pravrajet  yadi vetarathā brahmacaryāt eva pravrajet gṛhāt vā vanāt vā iti na karmaṇā na prajayā dhanena tyāgena ekemṛtatva mānaśuḥ ityādīni tathā smṛtayaḥ ca brahmacaryavān pravrajati aviśīrṇa brahmacaryaḥ  yam icchat tamāvasā iti tasyāḥ aśramam avikalpam ekebruvate tathā vaidānanadhītya brahmacaryeṇa putra pautrān icchet pāvana artham pitṛṇām agnīn ādhāya vidhivat ceṣṭa yajñaḥ  vanam praviśya atha muniḥ bubhūṣet  prājāpatyām nirupya iṣṭim sarva vesa dakṣiṇām ātmani agnīn samāropya brāhmaṇaḥ pravrajet gṛhāt  ityādyāḥ evam vyutthāna vikalpa kramayata iṣṭa āśrama pratipatti pratāpādakāni hi śruti smṛti vākyāni śataśa upalaṃbhyanta itaretara viruddhāni ācāraḥ ca tad vidām vipratipattiḥ ca śāstra artha pratapat tṝṇām bahu vidām api atas  na śakyate śāstra arthaḥ  manda buddhibhiḥ vivekena pratipattum pariniṣṭhata śāstra nyāya buddhibhiḥ eva hi oṣām vākyānām viṣaya vibhāgaḥ śakyate avadhārayitum tasmāt eṣām viṣaya vibhāga jñāpanāya yathā buddhi sāmarthaṃya vicārayiṣyāmaḥ yāvat jīva śruti ādi vākyānām anya artha asaṃbhavāt kriyā vasāna ava veda artha  tam yajña pātraiḥ dahanti iti antya karma śravaṇāt jarā marya śravaṇāt ca liṅgāt ca bhasma antam śarīram iti na hi pārivrājya pakṣe bhasma anta tā śarīrasya syāt  smṛtiḥ ca niṣeka ādi śmaśāna antaḥ  mantraiḥ yasya uditaḥ  vidhiḥ tasyāḥ  śāstre adhikāraḥ  asmin jñeyaḥ  na anyasya kasyacid  iti sa mantrakam hi yad karma vedena iha vidhīyate tasya śmaśāna anta tām darśayati smṛtiḥ adhikāra abhāva pradarśanāt ca atyantam eva śruti adhikāra abhāvaḥ  akarmiṇaḥ  gamyate agni udvāsanā apavādāt ca avīra hā vā eṣa devānām yaḥ  agnim udvāsayate iti nanu vyutthāna ādi vijhadhānāt vaikalpikam kriyā avasāna tvam veda arthasya na anya artha tvāt vyutthāna ādi śrutīnām ayāvat jīvam at nihotram juhoti yāt jīvam darśa pūrṇamāsābhyām yajeta iti evamādīnām śrutīnām jīvana mātra nimitta tvāt yadā na śakyate anya artha tā kalpayitum tadā vyutthāna ādi vākyānām karma anadhikṛta viṣayatva saṃbhavāt kurvan  eva iha karmāṇi jijīvaṣet śatam samāḥ iti ca mantra varṇāt jarayā vā hi eva asmān mucyate mṛtyunā vā iti ca jarā mṛtyubhyām anyatra karma viyogāt chidrā saṃbhavāt karmiṇām śmaśāna anta tvam na vaikalpikam kāṇa kubja ādayaḥ  api karmaṇi anadhikṛtā anugrāhyā eva śrutyā iti vyutthāna ādi āśrama antara vidhānam na anupapannam pārivrājya ākrama vidhānasya anavakāśa tvam iti ced  na viśva jit sarvamedhayoḥ yāvat jīva vidhi apavāda tvāt yāvat jīva agnihotra ādi vidheḥ viśva jit sarvamedhayoḥ eva apavādaḥ tatra ca krama pratipatti saṃbhavaḥ  brahmacaryam samāpya gṛhī bhavet gṛhāt vanī bhutvā pravrajet i ti virodha anupapatteḥ na hi evaṃviṣaya tve pārivrājya kama vidhāna vākyasya kaścid virodhaḥ krama pratipatteḥ anya viṣaya parikalpanāyām kaścid bādhaḥ nā atma jñānasya amṛtatva hetutva abhyupagamāt yad tāvat ātmā iti eva upāsīta iti ārabhya sa eṣa na iti na iti etad antena granthena yad upasaṃhṛtam ātma jñānam tad amṛtatva sādhanam iti abhyupagatam bhavatā tatra etāvat eva amṛtatva sādhanam anya nirapekṣam iti etad na mṛṣyate tatra bhavantam pṛcchāmi kimartham ātma jñānam marṣayati bhavān iti śṛṇu tatra kāraṇam yathāsvarga kāmasya svarga prāpti upāyam ajānataḥ  agnihotra ādi svarga sādhanam abhyupagamyate tathā iha api ātma jñānam yathā jñāpyate tatā bhūtam eva amṛtatva sādhanam ātma jñānam abhyupagantum yuktam tulya prāmāṇyāt ubhaya tra yadi evam kim syāt  sarva karma hetu upamardaka tvāt ātma jñānasya vidyā udbhave karma nivṛttiḥ syāt  dāra agni saṃbaddhānām tāvat agni hotra ādi karmaṇām bheda buddhi viṣaya saṃpradāna kāraka sādhya tvam anya buddhi para  chedyām hi agni ādi devatām saṃpradāna kāraka bhūta amantreṇa na hi tad karma nirvartyate yayā hi saṃpradāna kāraka buddhyā saṃpradāna kārakam karma sādhana tvena upadiśyate sā iha vidyayā nivartyate anyaḥ  asau  anyaḥ  aham asmi iti na sa veda devāḥ tam parāduḥ yaḥ  anyatrā atmanaḥ  devān veda mṛtyaḥ sa mṛtyum āpnoti ya iha na anā iva paśyati ekadhā eva anudraṣṭavyam sarvam ātmānam paśyati ityādi śrutibhyaḥ na ca deśa kāla nimitta dyapekṣa tvam vyavasthita ātma vastu viṣaya tvāt ātma jñānasya kriyāyāḥ tu puruṣa tantra tvāt syāt deśa kāla nimitta ādi epekṣa tvam jñānam tu vastu tantra tvāt na deśa kāla nimitta ādi apekṣate yathā agniḥ uṣṇa ākāśaḥ  amūrta iti tathā atma vijñānam apu nanu evam sati prāmāṇa bhūtasya karvidheḥ nirodhaḥ syāt  na ca tulya pramāṇayoḥ itaretara nirodhaḥ  yuktaḥ na svābhāvika bheda buddhi mātra nirodhaka tvāt  na hi vidhi antara nirodhakam ātma jñānam svābhāvika bheda buddhi mātram niruṇaddhi tathā api hetu apahārāt karma anupapatteḥ vidhainirodha eva syāt iti ced  na kāma pratiṣedhāt kāmya pravṛtti nirodhavat adoṣāt  yathā svarga kāmaḥ  yajeta iti svarga sādhane yāge pravṛttasya kāma pratiṣevidheḥ kāme vihate kāmya yāga anuṣṭhāna pravṛttiḥ nirudhyate na ca etāvatā kāmya vidhiḥ niruddhaḥ  bhavati kāma pratiṣedha vidhinā kāmya vidheḥ anarkatva jñānāt pravṛti anupapattiḥ iti ced  ananuṣṭheya tve anuṣṭha ātuḥ abhāvāt anuṣṭhāna vidhyā narthakyāt aprāmāṇyam eva karma vidhīnām iti ced  na prāc ātma jñānāt pravṛti upapatteḥ svābhāvikasya kriyā kāraka phala bheda vijñānasya prāc ātma jñānāt karma hetu tvam upapadyata eva yathā kāma viṣaye doṣa vijñāna utpatteḥ prāk kāmya karma pravṛtti hetu tvam syāt eva svarga ādi icchāyāḥ svābhāvikyāḥ tadvāt tathā sati anartha arthaḥ  veda iti ced  na artha anarthayoḥ abhiprāta tantra tvāt mokṣam ekam varjayitvā anyasya avidyā viṣaya tvāta puruṣa abhiprāya tantrau hi ārtha anarthau maraṇa ādi kāmya iṣṭa darśanāt tasmāt yāvat ātma jñāna vidheḥ ābhimukhyam tāvat eva karma vidhaya tasmāt nā atma jñāna sahabhāvi tvam karmaṇām iti atas  siddham ātma jñānam eva amṛtatva sādhanam etāvat are khalu amṛta tvam iti karma nirapekṣa tvāt jñānasya atas  viduṣaḥ tāvat pārivrājyam siddham saṃpradāna ādi karma kāraka jāti ādi śūnya avikriya brahma ātma dṛḍha pratipatti mātreṇa vacanam antareṇa api ukta nyāyataḥ tathā ca vyākhyātam etad  yeṣām naḥ ayam ātmāyam loka iti hotu vacanena pūrve vidvāsaḥ prajām akāmayamānā vyuttiṣṭhanti iti pārivrājyam viduṣām ātma loka avabodhāt eva tathā ca vividiṣā uḥ apu siddham pārivrājyam etam evā atmānam lokam icchantaḥ pravrajanti iti vacanāt  karmaṇām ca avidvat viṣaya tvam avocāma avidyā viṣaye ca utpatya āpti vikāra saṃskārthāni karmāṇi iti atas  ātma saṃskāra dvaireṇā atma jñāna sādhana tvam api karmaṇām avocāma yajña ādibhiḥ vividaṣanti iti atha eta satya vid viṣayāṇām āśrama karmaṇām bala abala vicāraṇāyām ātma jñāna utpādanam prati yama pradhāna anām amānitva ādīnām mānasānām ca dhyāna jñāna vairāgya ādīnām sannipatya upakāra tvam hiṃsā rāga dveṣa ādi bāhulyāt bahu kliṣṭa karma vimiśritā itara iti atas  pārivrājyam mumukṣūṇām praśaṃsanti tyāga eva hi sarveṣām uktānām api karmaṇām vairāgyam punar etasya mokṣasya paramaḥ  avadhiḥ kim te dhanena kim u bandhubhiḥ te kim te dāraiḥ brāhmaṇa yaḥ  mariṣyasi ātmānam anviccha guhā praviṣṭam pitāmahāḥ te kva gatāḥ pitā ca evam sa ākhya yoga śāstreṣu ca saṃnyāsaḥ  jñānam prati pratyāsanna ucyate kāma pravṛtti abhāvāt ca kāma pravṛtteḥ hi jñāna pratikūla tā sarva śāstreṣu prasiddhā tasmāt viraktasya mumukṣoḥ vinā api jñānena brahmacaryāt eva pravrajet iti ādyu upapannam nanu sa avakāśa tvāt anadhikṛta viṣayam etad iti uktam yāvat jīva śruti uparodhāt na eṣa doṣaḥ nitarām sa avakāśa tvāt yāvat jīva śrutīnām avadvid kāmi kartavya tā hi avocāma sarva karmaṇām na tu nirapekṣam eva jīvana nimittam eva kartavyam karma prāyeṇa hi puruṣāḥ kāma bahulāḥ kāmaḥ ca aneka viṣayaḥ  aneka karma sādhana sādhyaḥ ca aneka phala sādhanāni ca vaidikāni karmāṇi dāra agni saṃbandha puruṣa kartavyā anu punar  punar ca anuṣṭhīyamāna anu bahu phala anu kṛṣi ādivat varṣa śata samāptīni ca gārhasthye vā araṇye vātaḥ tad apekṣayā yāvat jīva śrutayaḥ akurvan  eva iha karmāṇi iti ca mantra varṇaḥ tasmin  ca pakṣe viśva jit sarvamedhayoḥ karma parityāgaḥ yasmin  ca pakṣe yāvat jīva anuṣṭhānam tadā śmaśāna anta tvam bhasma anta tā ca śarīrasya itara varṇa apekṣayā vā yāvat jīva śrutiḥ na hi kṣattriya vaiśyayaḥ pārivrājya pratipattiḥ asti tathā amantraiḥ yasya uditaḥ  vidhiḥ aaika āśramyam tu ācāryā iti evamādīnām kṣatriya vaiśya apekṣa tvam tasmāt puru śasām arthaya jñāna vairāgya kāma ādi apekṣayā vyutthāna vikalpa krama pārivrājya pripatta prakārā na virudhyante anadhikṛtānām ca pṛthak vidhānāt pārivrājya s asnāta kaḥ  vāsnātakaḥ  vā utsanna agniḥ anagni kaḥ  ve atyādinā tasmāt siddha āśrama antarāṇi adhikṛtānām eva iti pañcamam brāhmaṇam atha anantaram yājñavalkīyasya kāṇḍasya vaṃśa ārabhyate yathā madhuka aṇḍasya vaṃśaḥ vyākhyānam tu pūrvavat  brahma svayaṃbhu brahmaṇe nama om iti om atha pañcamaḥ  adhyāyaḥatha pañcama adhyāyasya prathamam brāhmaṇam pūrṇamadaḥ pūrṇam na kutaścid  vyāvṛttam vyāpi iti etad  niṣṭhā ca kartari draṣṭavyā ada iti parokṣa abhidhāyi sarvanāma tad param brahma iti arthaḥ tad  sampūrṇam ākāśavat  vyāpi nirantaram nirupādhikam ca tad eva idam sa upādhikam nāma rūpa sthaṃ vyavahāra āpannam pūrṇam svena rūpeṇa parama ātmanā vyāpi iva na upādhi paricchinnena viśeṣa ātmanā tad idam viśeṣa āpannam kārya ātmakam brahma pūrṇāt  kāraṇa ātmana udacyata udricyata udgacchati iti etad  yadi api kārya ātmanā udricyate tathā api yad  svarūpam pūrṇa tvam paramātma bhāvam tad na jāhāti pūrṇam eva udricyate pūrṇasya kārya ātmanaḥ  brahmaṇaḥ pūrṇa pūrṇa tvam ādāya gṛhītvā ātma sva rūpa eka rasa tvam āpadya vidyayā avidyā kṛtam bhūtamātra upādhi saṃsarga jamanyatva avabhāsam tiraskṛtya pūrṇam eva anantaram avāhyam prajñāna ghana eka rasa svabhāvam kevalam brahmā avaśiṣyate yad uktam brahma vā idam agra āsīt tad ātmānam eva avet tasmāt tad sarvam abhavat iti eṣaḥ  asya mantrasya arthaḥ tatra brahma iti asya arthaḥ pūrṇamada iti idam pūrṇam iti brahma vā idam agra āsīt iti asya arthaḥ tathā ca śruti antaram yad eva iha tad amutrayat amutra tad anu iha iti atas  adaḥ śabda vācyam pūrṇam brahma tad eva idam pūrṇam kārya stham nāma rūpa upādhi saṃyuktam avidyayā udriktam tasmāt eva parama artha svarūpāt anyat iva pratyavabhāsamānam tad yad ātmānam eva param pūrṇam brahma viditvā ahamadaḥ pūrṇam brahma asmi iti evam pūrṇam ādāya tiraskṛtya āpūrṇa svarūpa tām avidyā kṛtām nāma rūpa upādhi saṃparka jām etayā brahma vidyayā pūrṇam eva kevalam avaśiṣyate tathā ca uktam tasmāt tad sarvam abhavat iti yaḥ sarva upaniṣad arthaḥ  brahma sa eṣaḥ  anena mantreṇa anūdyata uttara sambandha artham brahma vidyā sādhana tvena hi vakṣyamāṇāni sādhanāni uṅkāra dama dāna dayā ākhyāni vidhitsitāni khila prakaraṇa sambandhāt sarva upāsana aṅga bhūtāni ca atra eke varṇayanti pūrṇāt kāraṇāt pūrṇam kāryam udricyate udriktam kāryam vartamāna kāle api pūrṇam eva parama artha vastu bhūtam dvaita rūpeṇa punar  pralaya kāle pūrṇasya kāryasya pūrṇa tām ādāyā atmani dhitvā pūrṇam eva avaśiṣyate kāraṇa rūpam evam utpatti sthiti pralayeṣu triṣu api kāleṣu kārya kāraṇayoḥ pūrṇa tā eva sā ca ekā eva pūrṇa tā kārya kāraṇayoḥ bhedena vyapadiśyate evam ca dvaitādvaita ātmakam ekam brahma yathā kila samudraḥ  jala taraṅga phena budbuda ādi ātmaka eva yathā ca jalam satyam tad udbhavāḥ ca taraṅga phela budbuda ādayaḥ samudra ātma bhūtā evā avirbhāva tirobhāva dharmiṇaḥ parama artha satyā eva evam sarvam idam dvaitam parama artha satyam eva jala taraṅga ādi sthānīyam samudra jala sthānīyam tu param brahma evam ca kila dvaitasya satya tve karma kāṇḍasya prāmāṇyam yadā punar dvaitam dvaitam iva avidyā kṛtam mṛgatṛṣṇikāvat anṛtam advaitam eva paramārthataḥ tadā kila karma kāṇḍam viṣaya abhāvāt apramāṇam bhavati tathā ca virodha eva syāt  veda eka deśa bhūta upaniṣad pramāṇam parama artha advaita vastu pratipādaka tvāt apramāṇam karma kāṇḍam asat dvaita viṣaya tvāt tad virodha parijihīrṣayā śrutyā etad uktam kārya kāraṇayoḥ satya tvam samudravat pūrṇa mada ityādinā iti tad asat  viśiṣṭa viṣaya apavāda vikalpayoḥ asambhavāt na hi iyam su vivakṣitā kalpanā kasmāt  yathā kriyā viṣaya utsarga prāptasya eka deśe apavādaḥ kriyate yathā ahiṃsan sarva bhūtāni anyatra tīrthebhya iti hiṃsā sarva bhūta viṣaya utsargeṇa nivāritā tīrthe viśiṣṭa viṣaye jyotiṣṭoma ādau  anujñāyate na ca tathā vastu viṣaya iha advaitam brahma utsargeṇa pratipādya punar tad eka deśe apavaditum śakyate brahmaṇaḥ  advaita tvāt eva eka deśa anupapatteḥ tathā vikalpa anupapatteḥ ca yathā atirātre ṣoḍaśinam gṛhṇāti na atirātre ṣoḍaśinam gṛhṇāti iti grahaṇa agrahaṇayoḥ puruṣa adhīna tvāt vikalpaḥ  bhavati na tu iha tathā vastu viṣaye dvaitam vā syāt advaitam vā iti vikalpaḥ sambhavati apuruṣa tantra tvāt ātma vastunaḥ virodhāt ca dvaita advaita tvayoḥ ekasya tasmāt na su vivakṣitā iyam kalpanā śruti nyāya virodhāt ca saindhava ghanavat prajñāna eka rasa ghanam nirantaram pūrva apara bāhya abhyantara bheda vivarjitam sa bāhya abhyantaram ajam na iti na iti asthūla manaṇva jam ajaram abhayam amṛtam iti evamādyāḥ śrutayaḥ niścita arthāḥ saṃśaya viparyāsa āśaṅkā rahitāḥ sarvāḥ samudre prakṣiptāḥ syuḥ akiñcitkara tvāt  tathā nyāya virodhaḥ  api sāvayavasya aneka ātmakasya kriyāvataḥ  nityatva anupapatteḥ nitya tvam cā atmanaḥ smṛti ādi darśanāt anumīyate tad virodhaḥ ca prāpnoti anitya tve bhavat kalpanā narthakyam ca sphuṭam eva ca asmin pakṣe karma kāṇḍa ānarthakyam akṛta abhyāgama kṛta vipraṇāśa prasaṅgāt  nanu brahmaṇaḥ  dvaitādvaita ātmaka tve samudra ādi dṛṣṭāntā vidyante katham ucyate bhavatā ekasya dvaitādvaita tvam viruddham iti na anya viṣaya tvāt  nitya aniravayava vastu viṣayam hi viruddha tvam avocāma dvaita advaita tvasya na kārya viṣaye sa avayave tasmāt śruti smati nyāya virodhāt anupapanneyam kalpanā asyāḥ kalpanāyāḥ  varam upaniṣad parityāga eva adhyeya tvāt ca na sa astra artheyam kalpanā na hi janana maraṇa ādi anartha śata sahasra bheda samākulam samudra vana ādivat sāvayavam aneka rasam brahma dhyeya tvena vijñeya tvena vā śrutyā upadiśyate prajñāna ghana tām ca upadiśati ekadhā eva anudraṣṭavyam iti ca anekadhā darśana apavādāt ca mṛtyoḥ sa mṛtyum āpnoti ya iha na anā iva paśyati iti yad ca śrutyā ninditam tad na kartavyam yad ca na kriyate na sa śāsra arthaḥ brahmaṇaḥ  aneka rasa tvam anekadhātvam ca dvaita rūpam nindita tvāt na draṣṭavyam atas  na śāsra arthaḥ yad tu eka rasa tvam brahmaṇaḥ tad draṣṭavya tvāt praśastam praśasta tvāt ca śāstra arthaḥ  bhavitum arhati yad tu uktam veda eka deśasya aprāmāṇyam karma viṣaye dvaita abhāvāt advaite ca prāmāṇyam iti tad na yathā prāpta upadeśa artha tvāt na hi dvaitam advaitam vā vastu jāta mātram eva puruṣam jñāpayitvā paścāt karma vā brahma vidyām vā upadiśati śāsram na ca upadeśa arham dvaitam jāta mātra prāṇi buddhi gamya tvāt na ca dvaitasya anṛtatva buddhiḥ prathamam eva kasya acid syāt  yena dvaitasya satya tvam upadiśya paścāt ātmanaḥ prāmāṇyam pratipādayet śāsram na api pāṣaṇḍibhiḥ api prasthāpitāḥ śāsrasya prāmāṇyam na gṛhṇīyuḥ tasmāt yathāprāptam eva dvaitam avidyā kṛtam svābhāvikam upādāya svābhāvikyā eva avidyayā yuktāya rāga dveṣa ādi doṣavate yathā abhimata puruṣa artha sādhanam karma upadiśati agre paścāt prasiddha kriyā kāraka phala svarūpa doṣa darśanavate tad biparīta audāsīnya svarūpa avasthāna phala arthine tad upāya bhūtām ātmā ekatva darśana ātmikām brahma vidyām upadiśati atha evam sati tad audāsīni svarūpa avasthāne phale prāpte śāsrasya prāmāṇyam pratyarthi tvam nivartate tad abhāvāt śāsrasya api śāsra tvam tam prati nivartata eva tathā prati puruṣam parisamāptam śāsram iti na śāsra virodha gandhaḥ  api asti advaita jñāna avasāna tvāt śāsra śiṣya śāsana ādi dvaita bhedasya anyatama avasthāne hi virodhaḥ syāt avasthitasya itara itara apekṣa tvāt tu śāsra śiṣya śāsanānām na anyatamaḥ  api avatiṣṭhate sarva samāptau tu kasya viredha āśaṅkyeta advaite kevale śive siddhe na api avirodha tāta eva atha api abhyupagamya brūmaḥ dvaitādvaita ātmaka tve api śāsra virodhasya tulya tvāt  yadā api samudra ādivat dvaita ātmakam ekam eva brahma na anyat asti iti virudhyate yasmin dvaita viṣaye anyonya upadeśaḥ saḥ  anyaḥ  dvaitam ca anyat eva iti samudra dṛṣṭāntaḥ  viruddhaḥ na ca samudra udaka ekatvavat vijñāna eka tve brahmaṇaḥ  anyatra upadeśa grahaṇa ādi kalpanā sambhavati na hi hasta ādi dvaitādvaita ātmake devadatte vākkarṇayoḥ devadatta eka deśa bhūtayoḥ vāc upadeṣṭrī karṇaḥ kevala upadeśasya grahītā devadattaḥ tu na upadeṣṭā na api upadeśasya grahīta iti kalpayitum śakyate samudra eka udaka ātma tvavat eka vijñānava tvāt devadattasya tasmāt śrati nyāya virodhaḥ ca abhipreta artha asiddhiḥ ca evaṅkalpanāyām syāt  tasmāt yathāvyākhyāta eva asmābhiḥ pūrṇamada iti asya mantrasya arthaḥ om kham brahma iti mantraḥ  ayam ca anyatra aviniyukta iha brāhmaṇena dhyāna karmaṇi viniyujyate atra ca brahma iti viśeṣya abhidhānam kham iti viśeṣaṇam viśeṣaṇa viśeṣyayoḥ ca sāmānādhikaraṇyena nirdeśaḥ  nīlotpalavat  kham brahma iti brahma śabdaḥ  bṛhat vastu mātra āspadaḥ  aviśeṣitaḥ  atas  viśeṣyate kham brahma iti yad tad kham brahma tadā uṃśabda vācyamoṃ śabda svarūpam evavā ubha yathā api sāmānādhikaraṇyam aviruddham iha ca brahma upāsana sādhanatva artha m oṃ śabdaḥ prayuktaḥ tathā ca śruti antarāt etad ālambanam śreṣṭham etad ālambanam param om iti ātmānam yuñjīta om iti etena eva akṣareṇa param puruṣam abhidhyāyīta om iti evam dhyāyatha ātmānam iti ādeḥ anya artha asaṃbhavāt ca upadeśasya yathā anyatrom iti śaṃsati om iti udgāyati iti evamādau svādhyāya ārambha apavargayoḥ ca uṅkāra prayogaḥ  viniyogāt avagamyate na ca tathār atha antaram iha avagamyate tasmāt dhyāna sādhana tvena eva iha uṅkāra śabdasya upadeśaḥ yadi api brahma ātma ādi śabdā brahmaṇaḥ  vācakāḥ tathā api śruti prāmāṇyāt brahmaṇaḥ  nediṣṭham abhidhānam oṅkāraḥ ata eva brahma pratipattau  idam param sādhanam tad ca dvi prakāreṇa pratīka tvena abhidhāna tvena ca pratīka tvena yathā viṣṇu ādi pratimā abhedena evam oṅkāraḥ  brahma iti pratipattavyaḥ tathā hi oṅkāra ālambanasya brahma prasīdati etad ālambanam śreṣṭham etad ālambanam param etad ālambanam jñātvā brahma loke mahīyate iti śruteḥ tatra kham iti bhautike khe pratītiḥ mā bhūt iti āha kham purāṇam ciratanam kham parama ātma ākāśam iti arthaḥ yad tad paramātma ākāśam purāṇam kham tad cakṣuḥ ādya viṣaya tvāt nirālambanam aśakyam grahītum iti śraddhā bhaktibhyām bhāva viśeṣeṇa ca uṅkāra āveśayati yathā viṣṇu aṅga aṅkitāyām śilā ādi pratimāyām viṣṇum loka evam vāyuḥ am kham vāyuḥ asmin vidyata iti vāyuḥ am kham kha mātram kham iti ucyate na purāṇam kham iti evam āha sma kaḥ  asau kauravyāyaṇī putraḥ vāyure hi khe mukhyaḥ sva śabda vyavahāraḥ tasmāt mukhe saṃpratyayaḥ  yukta iti manyate tatra yadi purāṇam kham brahma nirūpa adhi svarūpam yadi vā vāyuḥ am kham sa upādhikam brahma sarvathā api oṅkāraḥ pratīka tvena eva pratimāvat sādhana tvam pratipadyate etad vai satyakāma param ca aparam ca brahma yadā uṅkāraḥ iti śruti antarāt kevalam sva śabda arthe vipratipattiḥ vedaḥ  ayam oṅkāraḥ  veda vijānāti anena yad veditavyam tasmāt veda oṅkāraḥ  vācakaḥ  abhidhānam tena abhidhānena yad veditavyam brahma prakāśyamānam abhidhīyamānam veda sādhakaḥ  vijānāti upalabhate tasmāt vedaḥ  ayam iti brāhmaṇā viduḥ tasmāt brāhyaṇānām abhidhāna tvena sādhana tvam abhipretam oṅkārasya athavā vedaḥ  ayam iti ādi artha vādaḥ katham oṅkāraḥ  brahmaṇaḥ pratīka tvena vihitaḥ om kham brahma iti sāmāna adhikaraṇyāt tasya stutiḥ idānīm veda tvena sarvaḥ  hi ayam veda oṅkāra eva etad prabhava etad ātmakaḥ sarvam ṛc yajuḥ sāma ādi bheda bhinna eva oṅkāraḥ tad yathā śaṅkunā sarvāṇi parṇāni ityādi śruti antarāt itas ca ayam veda oṅkāraḥ  yad veditavyam tad sarvam veditavyam oṅkāraḥ  vedaḥ itarasya api vedasya veda tvam ata eva tasmāt viśiṣṭaḥ  ayam oṅkāraḥ sādhana tvena pratipattavya iti athavā vedaḥ saḥ kaḥ  asau yam brāhmaṇā viduroṅkārāt  brāhmaṇānām hi asau praṇava udgotha ādi vikalpaiḥ vijñeyaḥ tasmin hi prayujyamāne sādhana tvena sarvaḥ  vedaḥ prayuktaḥ  bhavati iti iti adhunā dama ādi sādhana traya vidhāna arthoṃ ayam ārambhaḥ trayāḥ tri saṃkhyākāḥ prajāpatyāḥ prajāpateḥ apatyāni prājāpatyāḥ te kim prajāpattau pitari brahmacaryam śiṣyatva vṛtteḥ brahmacaryasya prādhānyāt śiṣyāḥ santaḥ  brahmacaryam ūṣuḥ uṣitavanta iti arthaḥ ke te viśeṣataḥ  devāḥ  manuṣyā asurāḥ ca te ca uṣitvā brahmacaryam kim akurvan  iti ucyate teṣām devāḥ  ūcuḥ pitaram prajāpatim kim iti bravītu kathayatu naḥ asmabhyam yad anuśāsanam bhavān iti tebhya evam arthibhyaḥ  ha etad akṣaram varṇa mātram uvāca da iti uktvā ca tān papraccha pitā kim vyajñāsiṣṭa aiti mayā upadeśa artham abhihitasya akṣarasya artham vijñātavanta āhosvit na iti devāḥ  ūcuḥ vyajñāsiṣma iti vijñātavantaḥ  vayam yadi evam ucyatām kim mayā uktam iti devāḥ  ūcuḥ da abhyata adāntā yūyam svabhāvataḥ  atas  dāntā bhavatā iti naḥ asmān āttha kathayati itara āhomiti samyak vyajñāsiṣṭa iti samānam anyat  svabhāvataḥ  lubdhā yūyamatas  yathāśakti saṃvibhajata datta iti naḥ asmān āttha kim anyat brūyāt na u hitam iti manuṣyāḥ tathā asurā dayadhvam iti krūrā yūyam hiṃsā ādi parā atas  dayadhvam prāṇiṣu dayām kuruta iti tad etad prajāpateḥ anuśāsanam adya api anuvartata eva yaḥ pūrvam prajāpatiḥ deva ādīn anuśaśāsa saḥ  adya api anuśāsti eva daivyā stanayitnu lakṣaṇayā vācā katham eṣā śrūyate daivaḥ  vāc  kāsau stanayitnuḥ da da da iti dāmyata datta dayadhvam iti eṣām vākyānām upalakṣaṇāya tris dakāra uccāryate anukṛtiḥ na tu stanayitnu śabdaḥ tris eva saṃkhyā niyamasya lokaḥ  aprasiddha tvāt  yasmāt adya api prajāpatiḥ dāmyata datta dayadhvam iti anuśāsti eva tasmāt kāraṇāt etad trayam kim tad  trayam iti ucyate damam dānam dayām iti śikṣet upādadyāt prajāpateḥ anuśāsanam asmābhiḥ kartavyam iti evam kartavyam iti evam matim kuryāt  tathā ca smṛtiḥ trividham narakasya idam dvāram na aśatam ātmanaḥ kāmaḥ krodhaḥ tathā lobhaḥ tasmāt etad  trayam tyajet  iti asya hi vidheḥ śeṣaḥ pūrvaḥ tathā api deva ādīn uddiśya kimartham dakāra trayam uccāritavān prajāpatiḥ pṛthak anuśāsana arthibhyaḥ te vā katham vivekena pratipannāḥ prajāpateḥ manogatam samānena eva dakāra varṇa mātreṇa iti para abhiprāya jñā vikalpayanti atra eka āhuḥ adāntatva ādānātu ādayāsu tvaiḥ aparādhi tvam ātmanaḥ  manyamānāḥ śaṅkitā eva prajāpatau  ūṣuḥ kim naḥ vakṣyati iti teṣām ca dakāra śravaṇa mātrāt evā atma āśaṅkā vaśena tad artha pratipattiḥ abhūt  loke api hi prasiddham putrāḥ śiṣyāḥ ca anuśāsyāḥ santaḥ  doṣān nivartayitavyā iti atas  yuktam prajāpateḥ dakāra mātra uccāraṇam dama ādi traye ca dakāra anvayāt ātmanaḥ  doṣa ānurūpyeṇa deva ādīnām vivekena pratipattum ca iti phalam tu etad ātma doṣa jñāne sati doṣān nivartayitum śakyate alpena api upadeśena dakāra mātreṇa iti nanu etad  trayāṇām deva ādīnām anuśāsanam deva ādibhiḥ api ekaikam eva upādeya madya tve api na tu trayam manuṣyaiḥ śikṣitavyam iti atra ucyate pūrvaiḥ daiva ādibhiḥ api ekaikam eva upādeya madya tve api na tu trayam manuṣyaiḥ śikṣitavyam iti athavā na devāḥ  asurā vā anye kecana vidyante manuṣyebhyaḥ manuṣyāṇām eva ādāntā ye anyaiḥ uttamaiḥ guṇaiḥ saṃpannāḥ te devāḥ  lobha pradhānā manuṣyāḥ tathā hiṃsā parāḥ krūrā asurāḥ ta eva manuṣyā adāntatva ādi doṣa kṣa trayam apekṣya deva ādi viśabda bhājaḥ  bhavanti itarān  ca guṇān sattva rajaḥ tamāṃsi apekṣya atas  manuṣyaiḥ eva śikṣitavyam etad  trayam iti tad apekṣayā eva prajāpatinā upadiṣṭa tvāt  tathā hi manuṣyaḥ adāntā lubdhāḥ krūrāḥ ca dṛśyante tathā ca smṛtiḥ kāmaḥ krodhaḥ tathā lobhaḥ tasmāt etad  trayam tyajet  iti dama ādi sādhana trayam sarva upāsana śeṣam vihitam dāntaḥ  alubdha u dayāluḥ san sarva upāsaneṣu adhikriyate tatra nirupādhikasya brahmaṇaḥ  darśanam atikrāntam atha adhunā sa upādhikasya tasya eva abhyudaya phalāni vaktavyāni iti evam arthaḥ  ayam ārambhaḥ eṣa prajāpatiḥ yad hṛśyam prajāpatiḥ anuśāsti iti anantaram eva abhihitam kaḥ punar asau  anuśāstā prajāpatiḥ iti ucyate eṣa prajāpatiḥ kaḥ  asau yathṛdayam hṛdayam iti hṛdaya sthā buddhiḥ ucyate yasmin śākalya brāhmaṇa ante nāma rūpa karmaṇām upasaṃhāra uktaḥ  diś vibhāga dvāreṇa tad etad sarva bhūta pratiṣṭham sarva bhūta ātma bhūtam hṛdayam prajāpatiḥ prajānām sraṣṭā etad brahma bṛhat tvāt sarva ātma tvāt ca brahma etad  sarvam uktam pañcama adhyāye hṛdayasya sarva tvam tad sarvam yasmāt tasmāt upāsyam hṛdayam brahma tatra hṛdaya nāma akṣara viṣayam eva tāvat upāsanam ucyate tad etad hṛdayam iti nāma tri akṣaram trīṇi akṣarāṇi asya iti tri akṣaram kāni punar tāni trīṇi akṣarāṇi ucyante hṛ iti ekam akṣaram abhiharanti hṛteḥ āhṛti karmaṇaḥ  hṛ iti etad rūpam iti yaḥ  veda yasmāt hṛdayāya brahmaṇe svāḥ ca indriyāṇi anye ca viṣayāḥ śabda ādayaḥ svam svam kāryam abhiharanti hṛdayam ca bhoktṛ artham abhiharati atas  hṛdaya nāmnaḥ  hṛ iti etad akṣaram iti yaḥ  veda asmai viduṣe abhiharanti svāḥ ca jñātayaḥ anye ca asaṃbaddhāḥ balim iti vākya śeṣaḥ vijñāna ānurūpyeṇa etad phalam tathā da iti etad api ekākṣaram etad api dāna arthasya dadāteḥ da iti etad rūpam hṛdaya nāma akṣara tvena nibaddham atra api hṛdayāya brahmaṇaḥ  svāḥ ca karaṇāni anye ca viṣayāḥ svam svam vīryam dadati hṛdayam ca bhoktre dadāti svam vīryam atas  dakāra iti evam yaḥ  veda asmai dadati svāḥ ca anye ca tathā yam iti etad api ekam akṣaram iṇaḥ  gati arthasya yam iti etad rūpam asmin nāmni nibaddham iti yaḥ  veda sa svargam lokam eti evam nāma akṣarāt api īdṛśam viśiṣṭam phalam prāpnoti kim u vaktavyam hṛdaya svarūpaḥ  pāsanāt iti hṛdaya stutaye nāma akṣara upanyāsaḥ tasya eva hṛdaya ākhyasya brahmaṇaḥ satyam iti upāsanam vidhitsan  āha tad tad iti hṛdayam brahma parāmṛṣṭam vā iti smaraṇa artham tad yad hṛdayam brahma smaryata iti ekaḥ tad śabdaḥ tad etad ucyate prakāra antarema iti dvitīyaḥ tad śabdaḥ kim punar tad prakāra antaram etad eva tad iti etad śabdena saṃbadhyate tṛtīyaḥ tad śabdaḥ etad iti vakṣyamāṇam buddhau saṃnidhīkṛtyā aha āsa babhūva kim punar etad evā asa yad uktam hṛdayam brahma iti tad iti tṛtīyaḥ tad śabdaḥ  viniyuktaḥ kim tad iti viśeṣataḥ  nirdiśati satyam eva sat ca tyat ca mūrtam cāmūrtam ca satyam brahma pañcabhūta ātmakam iti etad  sa yaḥ kaścid satya ātmānam etam mahat mahattva ādi akṣam pūjyam prathama jam prathama jātam sarvasmāt saṃsāriṇa etad eva agre jātam brahmātaḥ prathama jam veda vijānāti satyam brahma iti tasya idam phalam ucyate yathā satyena brahmaṇā ime lokā ātmasāt kṛtā jitā evam satya ātmānam brahma mahat yakṣam prathama jam veda sa jayati imān lokān kiñca jitaḥ  vaśīkṛta innvittham yathā brahmaṇā asau śatruḥ iti vākya śeṣaḥ asat ca asat bhavet asau śatruḥ jitaḥ  bhavet iti arthaḥ kasya etad phalam iti punar nigamayati ya evam etad mahat yakṣam prathama jam veda satyam brahma iti atas  vidyā anurūpam phalam yuktam satyam hi eva yasmāt brahma satyasya brahmaṇaḥ stuti artham idam āha mahat yakṣam prathama jam iti uktam tad katham prathama ja tvam iti ucyate āpa eva idam agra āsuḥ āpa iti karma samavāyinyaḥ  agnihotra ādi āhutayaḥ agnihotra ādyāhiteḥ drava ātmaka tvāt ap tvam tāḥ cā apaḥ  agni hotrādi karma apavarga uttara kālam kenacid dṛṣṭena sūkṣmeṇā atmanā karma samavāyi tvam aparityajanti itara bhūta sahitā eva na kevalāḥ karma samavāyi tvāt tu prādhānyam apām iti sarvāṇi eva bhūtāni prāk utpatteḥ avyākṛta avasthāni kartṛ sahitāni nirdiśyanta āpa iti tā āpaḥ  bīja bhūtā jagataḥ  avyākṛta ātmanā avasthitāḥ tā eva idam sarvam nāma rūpa vikṛtam jagat agre  āsuḥ na anyat kiñcit vikāra jātam āsīt  tāḥ punar āpaḥ satyam asṛjanta tasmāt satyam brahma prathama jam tad etad hiraṇyagarbhasya sūtra ātmanaḥ  janma yad avyākṛtasya jagataḥ  vyākaraṇam tad satyam brahma kutas  mahat tvāt  katham mahat tvam iti āha yasmāt sarvasya sraṣṭṭa katham yad satyam brahma tad  prajāpatim prajānām patim virājam sūrya ādi karaṇam asṛjatā iti anuṣaṅgaḥ prajāpatiḥ devān sa virāj prajāpatiḥ deva nasṛjata yasmāt sarvam evam krameṇa satyāt brahmaṇaḥ  jātam tasmāt mahat satyam brahma katham punar yakṣam iti ucyate ta evam sṛṣṭā devāḥ pitaram api virājam atītya tad eva satyam brahma upāmate ata etad prathama jam mahat yakṣam tasmāt sarva ātmanā upāsyam tad tasya api satyasya brahmaṇaḥ  nāma satyam iti tad etad tri akṣaram kāni tāni akṣarāṇi iti āha sa iti ekam akṣaram ti iti ekam akṣaram tītīkāra anubandhaḥ nirdeśa arthaḥ yam iti ekam akṣaram tatra teṣām prathama uttame akṣare sa kāraya kārau satyam mṛtyu rūpa abhāvāt madhyataḥ  madhye anṛtam anṛtam hi mṛtyuḥ mṛtyvanṛtayoḥ takāra sāmānyāt tad etad anṛtam takāra akṣaram mṛtyu rūpam ubhayatas  satyena sa kārayakāra lakṣaṇena parigṛhotaṃvi āptam antar bhāvitam satya rūpābhyām atas  akiñcitkaram tad satya bhūyam eva satya bāhulyam eva bhavati evam satya bāhulyam sarvasya mṛtyoḥ anṛtasya akiñcitkara tvam ca yaḥ  vidvān  tam evam vidvāṃsam anṛtam kadācid pramāda uktam na hinasti asya adhunā satyasya brahmaṇaḥ saṃsthāna viśeṣa upāsanam ucyate tad yad  kim tad satyam brahma prathama jam kim asau saḥ kaḥ  asau  ādityaḥ kaḥ punar asau  ādityaḥ  ya eṣa ka eṣa ya etasmin  āditya maṇḍale puruṣaḥ  abhimānī saḥ  asau satyam brahma yaḥ ca ayam adhyātmam yaḥ  ayam dakṣiṇe akṣat nakṣaṇi puruṣaḥ caśabdāt sa ca satyam brahma iti saṃbandhaḥ tau  etau  āditya akṣi sthau puruṣau  ekasya satyasya brahmaṇaḥ saṃsthāna viśeṣau yasmāt tasmāt anyonyasmin  itaretarasmin  ādityaḥ cākṣuṣe cākṣuṣaḥ cā aditye pratiṣṭhitau adhyātma adhidaivatayoḥ anyonya upakārya upakāraka tvāt katham pratiṣṭhitau  iti ucyate raśmibhiḥ prakāśena anugraham kurvan  eṣa ādityaḥ  asmin  cākṣuṣe adhyātme pratiṣṭhitaḥ ayam ca cākṣuṣaḥ prāṇaiḥ ādityam anugṛhṇan  amuṣmin  āditye adhidaive pratiṣṭhitaḥ saḥ  asmin śarīre vijñānam ayaḥ  bhoktā yadā yasmin kāla utkramiṣyan bhavati tadā asau cākṣuṣa āditya puruṣaḥ  raśmīn upasaṃhṛtya kevalena audāsīnyena rūpeṇa vyavatiṣṭhate tadā ayam vijñāna mayaḥ paśyati śuddham eva kevalam viraśmi etad maṇḍalam candra maṇḍalam iva tad etad ariṣṭa darśanam prāsahgikam pradarśayate katham nāma puruṣaḥ karaṇīye yatnavān syāt iti na enam cākṣuṣam puruṣa murarīkṛtya tam pratyanugrahāya ete raśmayaḥ svāmi kartavya vaśāt pūrvam āgacchantaḥ  api punar tad karma kṣayam anurudhyamānā iva na upayanti na pratyāgacchanti enam atas  avagamyate paraspara upakārya upakāraka bhāvāt satyasya eva ekasyā atmanaḥ ṃ aśā vetau  iti tatra yaḥ  asau kaḥ  ya eṣa etasmin maṇḍale puruṣaḥ satya nāmā tasya vyāhṛtayaḥ avayavāḥ katham bhūḥ iti yā iyam vyāhṛtiḥ sā tasya śiraḥ prāthamyāt  tatra sāmānyam svayam eva āha śruti ekam eka saṃkhyāyiktam śiraḥ tathā etad akṣaram ekam bhūḥ iti bhuva iti bāhū dvitva sāmānyāt dvau bāhū dve ete akṣare tathā svar iti pratiṣṭhā dve pratiṣṭhe dve ete akṣare pratiṣṭhe pādau pratitiṣṭhati ābhyām iti tasya asya vyāhṛtyavayavasya satyasya brahmaṇa upaniṣad rahasyam abhidhānam yena abhidhānena abhidhīyamānam tad brahma abhimukhaḥ  bhavati lokavat  kā asau  iti āha ahar iti ahar iti ca etad rūpam hanteḥ jahāteḥ ca iti yaḥ  veda sa hanti jahāti ca pāpmānam ya evam veda evam yaḥ  ayam dakṣiṇe akṣan puruṣaḥ tasya bhūḥ iti śira ityādi sarvam samānam tasya upaniṣad aham iti pratyagātma bhūta tvāt  pūrvavat dhānteḥ jahāteḥ ca iti upādhīnām aneka tvāt aneka viśeṣaṇa tvāt ca tasya eva prakṛtasya brahmaṇaḥ  manaupādhi viśiṣṭasya upāsanam vidhitsanna aham anaḥ mayaḥ  manaḥ prāyaḥ manasi upalabhyamāna tvāt  manasā ca upalabhata iti manaḥ mayaḥ  ayam puruṣaḥ  bhās  satyaḥ  bhā eva satyam sadbhāvaḥ svarūpam yasya saḥ  ayam bhās  satyaḥ  bhāsvara iti etad  manasaḥ sarva artha avabhāsamatvāt manaḥ maya tvāt ca asya bhāsvara tvāt  tasmin  antar hṛdaye hṛdayasya antar tasmin  iti etad yathā vrīhiḥ vā yavaḥ  vā pariṇamata evam parimāṇaḥ tasmin  antar hṛdaye yogibhiḥ dṛśyata iti arthaḥ sa eṣa sarvasya īśānaḥ sarvasya sva bheda jātasya īśānaḥ svāmī svāmi tve api sati kaścid amātya ādi tantraḥ  ayam tu na tathā kim tarhi adhipatiḥ adhiṣṭhāya pālayitā sarvam idam praśāsti yad idam kiñca yad kiñccit sarvam jagat tad sarvam praśāsti em manaḥ mayasya upāsanāt tathārūpa āpattiḥ eva phalam tam tathā yathepāsate tad eva bhavati iti brāhmaṇam tathā eva upāsana antaram satyasya brahmaṇaḥ  viśiṣṭa phalam ārabhyate vidyut brahma iti āhuḥ vidyutaḥ  brahmaṇaḥ  nirvacanam ucyate vidānāt avakhaṇḍanāt tamasaḥ  medha andhakāram vidārya hi avabhāsate atas  vidyut  evam guṇam vidyut brahma iti yaḥ  vedāsai vidyati avakhaṇḍayati vināśayati pāpmana enam ātmānam prati pratikūla bhūtāḥ pāpmānaḥ  ye tān sarvān pāpmanaḥ  akhaṇḍayati iti arthaḥ ya evam veda vidyut brahma iti tasya anurūpam phalam vidyut hi yasmāt brahma punar upāsana antaram tasya eva brahmaṇaḥ  vāc vai brahma iti vāc iti śabda srayī tām vācam dhenum dhenuḥ iva dhenuḥ yathā dhenuḥ caturbhiḥ stanaiḥ stanyam payaḥ kṣarati vatsāya evam vāgdhenuḥ vakṣyamāṇaiḥ stanaiḥ paya iva annam kṣarati deva ādibhyaḥ ke punar te stanā ye vā te yebhyaḥ kṣarati tasyāḥ  etasyāḥ  vācaḥ  dhenvā dvau stanau devāḥ  upajīvanti vatsa sthānīyāḥ kau tau svāhākāram ca vaṣaṭkāram ca ābhyām hi haviḥ dīyate devebhyaḥ hantakāram manuṣyāḥ hanta iti manuṣyebhyaḥ  annam prayacchanti svadhākāram ca vaṣaṭkāram ca ābhyām hi haviḥ dīyate devebhyaḥ hantakāram manuṣyāḥ hanta iti manuṣyebhyaḥ  annam prayacchanti svadhākāram ca vaṣaṭkāram ca ābhyām hi haviḥ dīyate devebhyaḥ hantakāram manuṣyāḥ hanta iti manuṣyebhyaḥ  annam prayacchanti svadhākāram pitaraḥ svadhākāreṇa hi pitṛbhyaḥ svadhām prayacchanti tasyāḥ  dhenvā vācaḥ prāṇa ṛṣabhaḥ prāṇena hi vāc prasūyate manaḥ  vatsaḥ manasā hi prasrāvyate manasā hi ālocite viṣaye vāc pravartate tasmāt manaḥ  vatsa sthānīyam evam vāgdhenu upāsakaḥ tād bhāvyam eva pratipadyate ayam agniḥ vaiśvāna naraḥ pūrvavat upāsana antara m ayam agniḥ vaiśvānaraḥ kaḥ  ayam agniḥ iti āha yaḥ  ayam antaḥpuruṣe kim śarīra ārambhakaḥ  na iti ucyate yena agninā vaiśvānara ākhyena idam annam pacyate kim tad annam yad idam adyate bhujyate annam prajā abhijaṭhiraḥ  agniḥ iti arthaḥ tasya sākṣāt upalakṣaṇa artham idam āha tasya agneḥ annam pacataḥ  jāṭharasya eṣa ghoṣaḥ  bhavati kaḥ  asau yam ghoṣam etad iti kriyā viśeṣaṇam karṇau  apidhāya aṅgulībhyām apidhānam kṛtvā śṛṇoti tam prajāpatim upāsīta vaiśvānaram agnim atra api tādbhāvyam phalam tatra prāsaṅgikam idam ariṣṭa lakṣaṇam ucyate saḥ  atra śarīre bhoktā yadā utkramiṣyan bhavati na enam ghoṣam śṛṇoti sarveṣām asmin prakaraṇa upāsanānām gatiḥ iyam phalam ca ucyate yadā vai puruṣaḥ  vidvān asmāt lokāt praiti śarīram parityajati sa tadā vāyum āgacchati antarikṣe tiryak bhūtaḥ  vāyuḥ stimitaḥ  abhedyaḥ tiṣṭhati sa vāyuḥ tatra sva ātmani tasmai samprāptāya vijihote sva ātma avayavān vigamayati cchidrīkaroti ātmānam iti arthaḥ kiṃparimāmam chidram iti ucyate yathā ratha vakrasya kham chidram prasiddha parimāṇam tena chidreṇa sa vidvān ūrdhva ākramata ūrdhvaḥ sangacchati sa ādityam āgacchati ādityaḥ  brahma lokam jigamiṣoḥ mārga nirodham kṛtvā sthitaḥ saḥ  api evaṃvida upāsakāya dvāram prayacchati tasmai sa tatra vijihote yathā lambarasya kham vāditra viśeṣasya cchidra parimāmam tena sa ūrdhva  ākramate sa candramasam āgacchati saḥ  api tasmai tatra vijihīte yathā dundubheḥ kham prasiddham tena sa ūrdhva  ākramate sa lokam prajāpati lokam āgacchati kiṃviśiṣṭam aśokam mānasena duḥkhena vivarjitam iti etad  ahimam hima varjitam śārīra duḥkha varjitam iti arthaḥ tam prāpya tasmin vasati śāśvatīḥ nityāḥ samāḥ saṃvatsarān iti arthaḥ brahmaṇaḥ  bahūn kalpān vasati iti etad  etad vai paramam tapaḥ kim tad  yadi āhitaḥ  vyādhitaḥ  jvara ādi parigṛhītaḥ sanyat tapyate tad etad paramam tapa iti evam cintayet  duḥkha sāmānyāt  tasya evam cintayataḥ  viduṣaḥ karma kṣaya hetuḥ tad eva tapaḥ  bhavati anindataḥ  aviṣīdataḥ sa eva ca tena vijñāna tapasā dagdha kilbaṣaḥ paramam ha eva lokam jayati ya evam veda tathā etad vai paramam tapaḥ  yam pretam agnau  abhyādadhati agnipraveśa sāmānyāt  paramam ha eva lokam jayati ya evam veda annam brahma iti tathā etad upāsana antaram vidhitsan  āha annam brahmān namadyate yad tad brahma iti eka ācāryā āhuḥ tad na tathā grahītavyam annam brahma iti anye cā ahuḥ prāṇaḥ  brahma iti tad ca tathā na grahītavyam kimartham punar annam brahma iti na grāhyam yasmāt pūyati klidyate pūtibhāvam āpadyata ṛte prāṇāt tad katham brahma bhavitum arhati brahma hi nāma tad yad avināśi astu tarhi prāṇaḥ  brahma na eva yasmāt śuṣyati vai prāṇa ṛte annāt  attā hi prāṇaḥ atas  annenā adyena vinā na śaknoti ātmānam dhārayitum tasmāt śruṣyati vai prāṇa ṛte annāt  ata ekaikasya brahma tā na upapadyate yasmāt tasmāt ete ha tu eva anna prāṇa devate ekadhābhūyam ekadhā bāvam bhūtvā gatvā parama tām parama tvam gacchataḥ  brahma tvam prāpnutaḥ tad etad eva madhyavasya ha smā aha sma prātṛ daḥ  nāma pitarātmanaḥ kiṃsviditisvid iti vitarke yathā mayā brahma parikalpitam evam viduṣe kiṃsvid sādhu kuryām sādhu śobhanam pūjām kām tu asmai kuryām iti abhiprāyaḥ kinā iva asmai viduṣe asādhu kuryām kṛtakṛtyaḥ  asau  iti abhiprāyaḥ anna prāṇau saha bhūtaḥ  brahma iti vidvān nāsau  asādhu karamena khaṇḍitaḥ  bhavati na api sādhu karaṇena mahīkṛtaḥ tad evaṃvādinam sa pitā ha smā aha pāṇinā hastena nivārayat mā prātṛda mā evam vocaḥ kaḥ tu enayoḥ anna prāṇayoḥ eka dhā bhūyam bhūtvā parama tām kaḥ tu gacchati na kaścid api vidvān anena brahma darśanena parama tām gacchati tasmāt na evam vaktum arhasi kṛtakṛtyaḥ  asau  iti yadi evam bravītu bhavān katham parama tām gacchati iti tasmā u ha etad vakṣyamāṇam vaca uvāca kim tad  vi iti kim tad vi iti ucyate annam vai vi anne hi yasmāt imāni sarvāṇi bhūtāni viṣṭāni āśrita anyatas  annam vī iti ucyate kiñca ram iti ram iti ca uktavān pitā kim punar tad ram prāṇaḥ  vai ram kuta iti āha prāṇe hi kaścid anāyatanaḥ nirāśrayaḥ  ramate na api sati api āyatane aprāṇaḥ  durbalaḥ  ramate yadā tvāyatanavān prāṇī balavān  ca tadā kṛtārtham ātmānam manyamānaḥ  ramate lokaḥ yuvā syāt sādhu yuva adhyāyakaḥ ityādi śruteḥ idānīm evaṃvidaḥ phalam āha sarvāṇi ha vā asmin bhūtāni viśanti anna guṇa jñānāt sarvāṇi bhūtāni ramante prāṇa guṇa jñāna at ya evam veda uktham tathā upāsana antaram uktham śasram tad hi pradhānam mahāvrate kratau kim punar tad uktham prāṇaḥ  vā uktham prāṇaḥ ca pradhāna indriyāṇām uktham ca śasrāṇām ata uktham iti upāsīta katham prāṇa uktham iti āha prāṇaḥ  hi yasmāt idam sarvam utthāpayati utthāpanāt uktha prāṇaḥ na hi aprāṇaḥ kaścid uttiṣṭhati tad upāsana phalam āha uddhā asmāt evaṃvida uktha vid prāṇa vid vīraḥ putra uttiṣṭhati ha dṛṣṭam etad phalam adṛṣṭam tu ukthasya sāyujyam salokatām jayati ya evam veda yajuḥ iti ca upāsīta prāṇam prāṇau vai yajuḥ katham yujaḥ prāṇaḥ prāṇe hi yasmāt sarvāṇi bhūtāni yujyante na hi asati prāṇe kenacid kasyacid yoga sāmarthyam atas  yunakti iti prāṇaḥ  yajuḥ evaṃvidaḥ phalam āha yujyanta udyacchanta iti arthaḥ ha asmā evaṃvide sarvāṇi bhūtāni śraiṣṭhyam śreṣṭha bhāvaḥ tasmai śraiṣṭhyāya śreṣṭha bhāvāya naḥ śreṣṭhaḥ  bhavet iti yajuṣaḥ prāṇasya sāyujyam ityādi sarva samānam sāma iti ca upāsīta prāṇam prāṇaḥ  vai sāma katham prāṇaḥ sāma prāṇe hi yasmāt sarvāṇi bhūtāni samyañci saṃgacchante saṃgamanāt sāmya āpatti hetutvāt sāma prāṇaḥ samyañci saṃgacchante ha asmai sarvāṇi bhūtāni na kevalam saṃgacchanta eva śreṣṭha bhāvāya ca asmai kalpante samarthyante sāmnaḥ sāyujyam ityādi purvavat  tam prāṇam kṣattram iti upāsīta prāṇau vai kṣattram prasiddham etad prāṇaḥ  hi vai kṣattram katham prasiddham etad prāṇaḥ  hi vai kṣattram katham prasiddha tā iti āha trāyate pālayati enam piṇḍam deham prāṇaḥ kṣaṇitoḥ śasra ādi hiṃsitāt punar māṃsenā apūrayati yasmāt tasmāt kṣata trāṇāt prasiddham kṣattra tvam prāṇasya vidvat phalam āha pra kṣattram atram na trāyate anyena kenacid iti atram kṣattram prāṇam prāpnoti iti arthaḥ śākhā antare vā pāṭhāt kṣattra mātram prāṇaḥ  bhavati iti arthaḥ kṣattrasya sāyujyam salokatām jayati ya evam veda brahmaṇaḥ  hṛdaya ādi aneka upādhi viśiṣṭasya upāsanam uktam atha idānīm gāyatrī upādhi viśiṣṭasya upāsanam vaktavyam iti ārabhyate sarva  chandasām hi gāyatri icchandaḥ pradhāna bhūtam tad prayoktṛ gaya trāṇāt gāyatrī iti vakṣyati na ca anyeṣām chandasām prayoktṛ prāṇa trāṇa sāmarthyam prāṇa ātma bhūtā ca sā sarva  chandasām cā atmā prāṇaḥ prāṇaḥ ca kṣata trāṇāt kṣattram iti uktam prāṇaḥ ca gāyatrī tasmāt tad upāsanam eva vidhitsyate dvijottama janma hetu tvāt ca gāyatryā brāhmaṇam asṛjata triṣṭubhā rājanyam jagatyā vaiśyamati dvijottamasya dvitīyam janma gāyatrī nimittam tasmāt pradhānā gāyatrī brāhmaṇā vyutthāya brāhmaṇā abhivadanti sa brāhmaṇaḥ  vipāpaḥ  virajaḥ  avicikitsaḥ brāhmaṇaḥ  bhavati iti uttama puruṣa artha saṃbandham brāhmaṇasya darśayati tad ca brāhmaṇa tvam gāyatrī janma mūlam atas  vaktavyam gāyatryāḥ sa tattvam gāyatryā hi yaḥ sṛṣṭaḥ  dvijottamaḥ  niraṅkuśa eva uttama puruṣa artha sādhane adhikriyate atas tad mūlaḥ parama puruṣa artha saṃbandhaḥ tasmāt tad upāsana vidhānāyāḥ aha bhūmiḥ antarikṣam dyauḥ iti etāni aṣṭau  akṣarāṇi aṣṭa akṣaram aṣṭau  akṣarāṇi yasya tad idam aṣṭa akṣaram ha vai prasiddha avadyotakau ekam prathamam gāyatryai gāyatryāḥ padam yakāreṇa eva aṣṭatva pūraṇam etad u ha eva etad eva asyā gāyatryāḥ padam pādaḥ prathamaḥ  bhūmi ādi lakṣaṇa srailokya ātmā aṣṭa akṣaratva sāmānyāt  evam etad trailokya ātmakam gāyatryāḥ prathamam padam yaḥ  vedatasya etad phalam sa vidvān yāvat kiñci deṣu triṣu jetavyam tāvat sarvam ha jayati yaḥ  asyāḥ  etad evam padam veda tad arcaḥ  yajūṃsi sāmāni iti trayī vidyā nāma akṣarāṇi etāni api aṣṭau  eva tathā eva aṣṭa akṣaram ha vā ekam gāyatryai padam dvitīyam etad u ha eva asyā etad ṛgyajuḥ sāma lakṣaṇam aṣṭa akṣaratva sāmānyāt eva sa yāvatī iyam trayī vidyā trayyā vidyayā yāvat phala jātam āpyate tāvat ha jayati yaḥ  asyāḥ  etad gāyatryāsraividya lakṣaṇam padam veda tathā prāṇaḥ  apānaḥ  vyāna etāni api prāṇa ādi abhidhāna akṣarāṇi aṣṭau tad ca gāyatryāstṛtīyam padam yāvat idam prāṇi jātam tāvat ha jayati yaḥ  asyāḥ  etad evam gāyatryāstṛtīyam padam veda atha anantaram gāyatryā asripadāyāḥ śabda ātmikāyāḥ turīyam padam ucyate abhidheya bhūtam asyāḥ prakṛtāyāḥ  gāyatryā etad eva vakṣyam āmam turīyam darśatam padam parorajā ya eṣa tapati turīyam ityādi vākya padārtham svam eva vyācaṣṭe śrutiḥ yad vai caturtham prasiddham loke tad idam turīya śabdena abhidhīyate darśatam padam iti asya kor atha iti ucyate dadṛśa iva dṛśyata iva hi eṣa maṇḍala sthaḥ puruṣaḥ  rajaḥ  rajaḥ jātam samastam lokam iti arthaḥ upari upari ādhipatya bhāvena sarvam lokam rajaḥ jātam tapati upari upari iti vīpsā sarva loka ādhipatya khyāpana arthā nanu sarva śabdena eva siddha tvāt vīpsā narthikā na eṣa doṣaḥ yeṣām upariṣṭāt savitā dṛśyate tad viṣaya eva sarva śabdaḥ syāt iti āśaṅkā nivṛtti arthā vīpsā ye ca amuṣmāt parāñcaḥ  lokāḥ teṣām ceṣṭe devakānām ca iti śruti anrāt  tasmāt sarva avarodha arthā vīpsā yathā asau savitā sarva ādhipatya lakṣaṇayā śriyā yaśasā ca khyātyā tapati evam ha eva śriyā yaśasā ca tapati yaḥ  asyāḥ  etad evam turīyam darśatam padam veda sā eṣā tripadā uktā yā trailokya traividya prāṇa lakṣaṇā gāyatrī etasmin  caturthe turīye darśate pade parorajasi pratiṣṭhitā mūrta amūrta rasa tvāt ādityasya rasa apāye hi vastu nīra sama pratiṣṭhitam bhavati yathā kāṣṭha ādi dagdha sāram tadvat  tathā mūrta amūrta rasa tvāt ādityasya rasa apāye hi vastu nīra sama pratiṣṭhitam bhavati yathā kāṣṭha ādi dagdha sāram tadvat  tathā mūrta amūrta ātmakam jagattripadā gāyatrī āditye pratiṣṭhitā tad rasa tvāt saha tribhiḥ pādaiḥ tad vai turīyam padam satye pratiṣṭhitam kim punar tad satyam iti ucyate cakṣuḥ vai satyam katham cakṣuḥ satyam iti āha prasiddham etad cakṣuḥ hi vai satyam katham prasiddha tā iti āha tasmāt yad idānīm eva dvau vivadamānau viruddham vadamāna āveyā tām āgaccheyātām aham adarśam dṛṣṭavān anasmi iti anya āha aham aśrauṣam tvayā dṛṣṭam na tathā tad vastu iti tayoḥ ya evam brūyāt aham adrākṣam iti tasmā eva śraddadhyāma napunar yaḥ  brūyāt aham aśrauṣam iti śrotuḥ mṛṣā śravaṇam api saṃbhavati na tu cakṣuṣaḥ  mṛṣā darśanam tasmāt na aśrauṣam iti uktavate śraddadhyāma tasmāt satya pratipatti hetu tvāt satyam cakṣuḥ tasmin satye cakṣuṣi saha tribhiḥ itaraiḥ pādaiḥ turīyam padam pratiṣṭhitam iti arthaḥ uktam ca sa ādityaḥ kasmin pratiṣṭhita iti cakṣuṣi iti tad vai turīya pada āśrayam satyam bale pratiṣṭhitam kim punar tad balam iti āha prāṇaḥ  vai balam tasmin prāṇe bale pratiṣṭhitam satyam tathā ca uktam sūtre tadā utam ca protam ca iti yasmāt bale satyam pratiṣṭhitam tasmāt āhuḥ balam satyāt ogīya ojīya ojastaram iti arthaḥ loke api yasmin hi yad āśritam bhavati tasmāt āśritāt āśrayasya balavattara tvam prasiddham na hi durbalam balavataḥ kvacid āśraya bhūtam dṛṣṭam evam ukta nyāyena u eṣā gāyatrī adhyātmam adhyātme prāṇe pratiṣṭhitā sā eṣā gāyatrī prāṇaḥ atas  gāyatryām jagat pratiṣṭhitam yasmin prāṇe sarve devāḥ  ekam bhavanti sarvam vedāḥ karmāṇi phalam ca sā evam gāyatrī prāṇa rūpā satī jagata ātmā sā ha eṣā gayān  tatre trātavatī ke punar gayāḥ prāṇā vāc ādayaḥ  vai gayāḥ śabda karamāt  tān  tatre sā eṣā gāyatrī tad tatra yadi asmāt gayān  tatre tasmāt gāyatrī nāma gāyatrāṇāt gāyatrī iti prathitā sa ācārya upanīya māṇavakam aṣṭa varṣam yām eva amūm gāyatrīm sāvitrīm savitṛ devatākām anvāha pacchos dharcaśaḥ samastām ca eṣā eva sā sākṣāt prāṇaḥ  jagata ātmā māṇavakāya samarpita iha idānīm vyākhyātā na anyā sa ācāryaḥ  yasmai māṇavakāya anvāha anuvakti tasya māṇavakasya gayān prāṇāṃsrāyate naraka ādi patanāt tām etām sāvitrīm ha eke śākhinaḥ  anuṣṭubh chandaskām anvāhuḥ upanītāya tad abhiprāyam āha vāc anuṣṭubh  vāc ca śarīre sarasvatī tām eva hi vācam sarasvatīm māṇavakāya anubrūma iti etad vadantaḥ na tathā kuryāt na tathā vidyāt yatta āhuḥ mṛṣā eva tad  kim tarhi gāyatrīm eva sāvitrīm anubrūyāt  kasmāt  yasmāt prāṇaḥ  gāyatrī iti uktam prāṇa ukte vāc ca sarasvatī ca anye ta prāṇāḥ sarvam māṇavakāya samarpitam bhavati kiñca idam prāsaṅgikamuktvā gāyatrī vidam stauti yadi ha vā api evaṃvid bahu iva na hi tasya sarva ātmanaḥ  bahu nāma asti kicit sarva ātmaka tvāt viduṣaḥ pratigṛhṇāti na ha eva tad pratigraha jātam gāyatryā ekañcana ekam api padam prati paryāptam sa ya imānsrīn sa yaḥ  gāyatrī vidimān bhūḥ ādīṃ srīn gaḥ  aśva ādi dhana pūrṇān  lokān pratigṛhṇīyāt sa pratigrahaḥ  asyāḥ  gāyatryā etad prathamam padam yad vyākhyātam āpnuyāt prathama pada vijñāna phalam tena bhuktam syāt na tu adhika doṣa utpādakaḥ sa pratigrahaḥ atha punar yāvatī iyam trayī vidyā yaḥ tāvat pratigṛhṇīyāt saḥ  asyāḥ  etad tṛtīyam padam āpnuyāt  tena tṛtīya pada vijñāna phalam bhuktam syāt  kalpayitvā idam icyate pāda traya samam api yadi kaścid pratigṛhṇīyāt tad pāda traya vijñāna phalasya eva kṣaya kāraṇam na tu anyasya doṣasya kartṛ tve kṣamam na ca evam dātā pratigrahītā vā gāyatrī vijñāna stutaye kalpyate dātā pratigrahītā ca yadi api evam saṃbhāvyate na asau pratigrahaḥ  aparādha kṣamaḥ kasmāt yatas  abhyadhikam api puruṣa artha vijñānam avaśiṣṭam eva caturtha pāda viṣayam gāyatryāḥ tad darśayati atha asya etad eva turīyam darśatam padam parorajā ya eṣa tapati yad ca etad na eva kenacana kenacid api pratigraheṇā api am na eva prāpyam iti arthaḥ yathā pūrva uktāni trīṇi padāni etāni api na evā apyāni kenacid kalpayitvā evam uktam paramārthataḥ kuta u etāvat pratigṛhṇoyāt trailokya ādi samam tasmāt gāyatrī evaṃprakāra upāsya iti arthaḥ tasyāḥ  upasthānam tasyāḥ  gāyatryā upasthānam upetya sthānam namaskaraṇam anena mantreṇa kau asau mantra iti āha he gāyatrī asi bhavasi trailokya pādena ekapadī trayī vidyā rūpeṇa dvitīyena dvipadī prāṇa ādinā tṛtīyena tripadyasi caturthena turīyeṇa catuṣpadyasi evam caturbhiḥ pādaiḥ upāsakaiḥ padyase jñāyase atas  param pareṇa nirupādhikena svenā atmanā āpadasi avidyamānam padam yasyāḥ tava yena padyase sā tvam apadasi yasmāt na hi padyase na iti na iti ātma tvāt  atas  vyavahāra viṣayāya namabhte turīyāya darśatāya padāya poradase asau śatruḥ pāpmā tvad prāpti vighna karaḥ adaḥ tad ātmanaḥ kāryam yad tvad prāpti vighna kartṛ tvam mā prāpanmā eva prāpnotu iti śabdaḥ  mantra parisamāpti arthaḥ yam dviṣya ādyam prati dveṣam kuryāt svayam vidvān  tam pratyanena upasthānam asau śatruḥ amuka nāma iti nāma gṛhṇīyāt asmai yajñadattāya abhipretaḥ kāmaḥ  mā samṛddhi samṛddhim mā prāpnotu iti vā upatiṣṭhate na ha eva asmai devadattāya sa kāmaḥ samṛdhyate kasmai yasmā evam upatiṣṭhate aham adaḥ  devadatta abhipretam prāpam iti vā upatiṣṭhate asauvadaḥ  mā prāpat iti ādi trayāṇām mantra padānām yathākāmam vikalpaḥ gāyatryā mukha vidhānāya arthavāda ucyate etad ha kila vai smaryate tad tatra gāyatrī vijñāna viṣaye janakaḥ  vaidehaḥ  buḍilaḥ nāmataḥ  aśvatarāśvasya apatyam āśvatarāśviḥ tam kila uktavān yad nu iti vitarke haḥ ahaḥ iti etad tad yad tvam gāyatrī vid brūthā gāyatrī vidasmi iti yad abrūthāḥ kim idam tasya vacasaḥ  ananurūpam atha katham yadi gāyatrī vid pratigraha doṣeṇa hastaḥ bhūtaḥ  vahasi iti sa pratyāha rājñā smāritaḥ  mukham gāyatryā hi yasmāt asya he samrāṇna vidāñcakāra na vijñātavān asmi iti ha uvāca eka āhga vikala tvāt gāyatrī vijñānam mama aphalam jātam śṛṇu tarhi tasyāḥ  gāyatryā agniḥ eva mukham yadi ha vā api bahu iva indhanam agnau  abhyādadhati laukikāḥ sarvam eva tad saṃdahati eva indhanam agniḥ evam ha eva evaṃvid gāyatryā agniḥ mukham iti evam vetti iti evaṃvitsyāt svayam gāyatrī ātma agnimukhaḥ san yadi api bahu iva pāpam kurute pratigraha ādi doṣam tad sarvam pāpa jātam saṃpsāya bhakṣayitvā śuddhaḥ  agnivat pūtaḥ ca tasmāt pratigraha doṣāt gāyatrī ātma ajaraḥ  amṛtaḥ ca saṃbhavati yaḥ  jñāna karma samuccaya kārī saḥ  anta kāla ādityam prārthayati asti ca prasaṅgaḥ  gāyatryāḥ turīyaḥ pādaḥ  hi saḥ tad upasthānam prakṛtam atas  sa eva prārthyate hiraṇya mayena jyotiḥ mayena pātreṇa yathā pātreṇa iṣṭam vastu apidhīyata evam idam satya ākhyam brahma jyotiḥ mayena maṇḍalena apihitam iva asamāhita cetasām adṛśya tvāt tad ucyate satyasya apihitam mukham mukhyam svarūpam tad apidhānam pātram apidhānam iva darśana pratibandha kāraṇam tattvam he pūṣañjagataḥ poṣaṇat pūṣā savitāpā  ṛṇvapāvṛtam kuru darśana pratibandha kāraṇam apanayā iti arthaḥ satya dharmāya satyam dharmaḥ  asya mama saḥ  aham satya dharmā tasmai tvad ātma bhūtāya iti arthaḥ dṛṣṭaye darśanāya pūṣan  ityādīni nāmānya āmantraṇa arthani savituḥ ekarṣa ekaḥ ca asau  ṛṣiḥ ca eka ṛṣiḥ darśanāt ṛṣiḥ sa hi sarvasya jagata ātmā cakṣuḥ ca san sarvam paśyati ekaḥ  vā gacchati iti eka ṛṣiḥ sūrya ekākī carati iti mantra varṇāt  yama sarvam hi jagataḥ saṃyamanam tvad kṛtam sūrya suṣṭhu vīrayate rasān raśmīn prāṇān dhiyaḥ vā jagata iti prājāpatya prajāpateḥ īśvarasya apatyam hiraṇyagarbhasya vā he prājāpatya vyūha vigamaya raśmīn samūha saṃkṣipā atmanaḥ tejaḥ  yena aham śaknuyām tvad svarūpam añjasā draṣṭam vidyotana iva rūpāṇām ata upasaṃhara tejaḥ yad te tava rūpam sarva kalyāṇānām atiśayena kalyāṇam kalyāṇatamam tad te paśyāmi paśyāmaḥ  vayam vacana vyatyayena yaḥ  asau bhūrbhuvaḥ svar vyāhṛtya vayavaḥ puruṣaḥ puruṣa ākṛti tvāt puruṣaḥ saḥ  aham asmi bhavāmi aharam iti ca upaniṣada ukta tvāt āditya cākṣuṣayoḥ tad eva idam parāmṛśyate saḥ  aham asmi amṛtam iti saṃbandhaḥ mama amṛtasya satyasya śarīra pāte śarīra sthaḥ  yaḥ prāṇaḥ  vāyuḥ saḥ  anilam bāhyam vāyum eva pratigacchatu tathā anyā devatāḥ svām svām prakṛtim gacchantu atha idam api bhasma antam sat pṛthivīm yātu śarīram atha idānīm ātmanaḥ saṃkalpa bhūtām manasi vyavasthitām agni devatām prārthayate om krataḥ oṃm iti krataḥ iti ca saṃbodhana artha veva oṅkāra pratīka tvāt om manaḥ maya tvāt ca kratuḥ he om he krataḥ smara smartavyam antakāle hi tvad smaraṇa vaśa ādiṣṭā gatiḥ prāpyate atas  prārthyate yad mayā kṛtam tad smara punaruktiḥ ādara arthā kiñca he agne naya prāpaya su pathā śobhanena mārgeṇa rāye dhanāya karma phala prāptaya iti arthaḥ na dakṣiṇena kṛṣṇena punarāvṛtti yuktena kim tarhi śuklena eva su pathā asmān viśvāni sarvāṇi he deva vayunāni prajñānāni sarva prāṇinām vidvān kiñca yuyodhi apanaya viyojaya asmad asmad taḥ  juhurāṇam kuṭilam enaḥ pāpam pāpa jātam sarvam tena pāpena viyuktā vayam eṣyām uttareṇa pathā tvad prasādāt  kintu vayam tubhyam paricaryām kartum na śaknumaḥ  bhūyiṣṭhām bahutamām te tubhyam namauktim namaskāra vacanam vidhema namaskāra uktyā paricarema iti arthaḥ anyat kartum aśaktāḥ santa iti om prāṇaḥ  gāyatrī iti uktam kasmāt punar  kāraṇāt prāṇa bhāvaḥ  gāyatryā na punar vāc ādi bhāva iti yasmāt jyeṣṭhaḥ ca śreṣṭhaḥ ca prāṇaḥ  na vāc ādayaḥ  jyaiṣṭhya śraiṣṭhya bhājaḥ katham jyeṣṭha tvam śreṣṭha tvam ca prāṇasya uti tad nirdidhārayiṣayā idam ārabhyate athavā uktha yajuḥ sāmakṣattra ādi bhāvaiḥ prāṇasya eva upāsanam abhihitam satsu api anyeṣu cakṣuḥ ādiṣu tatra hetu mātram ihā anantaryeṇa saṃbadhyate na punar  pūrva śeṣa tā vivakṣitam tu khila tvāt asya kāṇḍasya pūrvatra yad anuktam viśiṣṭa phalam prāṇa viṣayam upāsanam tad vaktavyam iti yaḥ kaścid ha vā iti āvadhāraṇaṛchai yaḥ  jyeṣṭha śreṣṭha guṇam vakṣyamāṇam yaḥ  veda asau bhavati eva jyeṣṭhaḥ ca śreṣṭhaḥ ca evam phalena pralobhitaḥ san praśnāya amukhībhūtaḥ tasmai cā aha prāṇaḥ  vai jyeṣṭhaḥ ca śreṣṭhaḥ ca iti katham punar avagamyate prāṇaḥ  jyeṣṭhaḥ ca śreṣṭhaḥ ca iti yasmāt niṣeka kāla eva śukra śoṇita saṃmbandhaḥ prāṇa ādi kalāpasya aviśiṣṭaḥ tathā api na aprāṇam śukram virohati iti prathamaḥ  vṛtti lābhaḥ prāṇasya cakṣuḥ ādibhyaḥ atas  jyeṣṭhaḥ  vayasā prāṇaḥ niṣeka kāla dārabhya garbham puṣyati prāṇaḥ prāṇe hi labdha vṛttau paścāt cakṣuḥ ādīnām vṛtti lābhaḥ atas yuktam prāṇasya jyeṣṭha tvam cakṣuḥ ādiṣu bhavati tu kaścid kule jyeṣṭhaḥ  guṇa hīna tvāt tu na śreṣṭhaḥ madhyamaḥ kaniṣṭhaḥ  vā guṇāḍhya tvāt bhavet śreṣṭhaḥ  na jyeṣṭhaḥ na tu tathā iha iti āha prāṇa eva tu jyeṣṭhaḥ ca śreṣṭhaḥ ca katham punar  śraiṣṭhyam avagamyate prāṇasya tad iha saṃvādena darśayiṣyāmaḥ sarvathā api tu prāṇam jyeṣṭha śreṣṭha guṇam yaḥ  veda upāste sa svānām jñātīnām jyeṣṭhaḥ ca śreṣṭhaḥ ca bhavati jyeṣṭha śreṣṭha guṇa upāsana sāmarthyāt su vyatirekeṇa api ca yeṣām madhye jyeṣṭhaḥ ca śreṣṭhaḥ ca bhaviṣyāmi iti bubhūṣati bhavitum icchati teṣām api jyeṣṭha śreṣṭha prāṇa darśī jyeṣṭhaḥ ca śreṣṭhaḥ ca bhavati nanu vayenimittam jyeṣṭha tvam tad icchātaḥ katham bhavati iti ucyate na eṣa doṣaḥ prāṇavat vṛtti lābhasya eva jyeṣṭha tvasya vivakṣita tvāt  yaḥ  ha vai vasiṣṭhām veda vasiṣṭhaḥ svānām bhavati tad darśana anurūpeṇa phalam yeṣām ca jñāti vyatirekeṇa vasiṣṭhaḥ  bhavitum icchati teṣām ca vasiṣṭhaḥ  bhavati ucyatām tarhi kāsau vasiṣṭha iti vāc vai vasiṣṭhā vāsayati atiśayena vaḥ te vā iti vasiṣṭhā vāggminaḥ  hi dhanavantaḥ  vasanti atiśayena ācchādana arthasya vā vaseḥ vasiṣṭhā abhibhavanti hi vācā vāggminaḥ  anyān tena vasiṣṭha guṇavat parijñānāt vasiṣṭha guṇa u bhavati iti darśana anurūpam phalam yaḥ  ha vai pratiṣṭhām veda pratitiṣṭhati anayā iti pratiṣṭhā tām pratiṣṭhām pratiṣṭhā guṇavatīm yaḥ  veda tasya etad phalam pratitiṣṭhati same deśe kāle ca tathā durge viṣame ca durgamane ca deśe durbhikṣa ādau vā kāle viṣame yadi evam ucyatām kāsau pratiṣṭhā cakṣuḥ vai pratiṣṭhā katham cakṣuṣaḥ pratiṣṭhātvam iti āha cakṣuṣā hi same ca durge dṛṣṭavā pratitiṣṭhati atas  anurūpam phalam pratitiṣṭhati same pratitiṣṭhati durge ya evam veda iti yaḥ  ha vai sampadam veda sampad guṇa yuktam yaḥ  veda tasya etad phalam asmai viduṣe saṃpadyate ha kim yam kāmam kāmayate sa kāmaḥ kim punar  saṃpad guṇakam śrotram vai saṃpad  katham punar  śrotrasya saṃpad guṇa tvam iti ucyate śrotre sati hi yasmāt sarve vedā abhisampannāḥ śrotra indriyavataḥ  adhyeya tvāt  veda vihita karma āyattāḥ ca kāmāḥ tasmāt śrotram saṃpad  atas  vijñāna anurūpam phalam saṃ ha asmai padyate yam kāmam kāmayate ya evam veda yaḥ  ha vā āyatanam veda āyatanam āśrayaḥ tad ya u vedā ayatanam svānām bhavati āyatanam janānām anyeṣām api kim punar tad āyatanam iti ucyate manaḥ  vā āyatanam āśraya indriyāṇām viṣayāṇām ca manaā āśritā hi viṣayā ātmanaḥ  bhogya tvam pratipadyante manaḥ saṃkalpa vaśāni ca indriyāṇi pravartante nivartante ca atas  mana āyatanam indriyāṇām atas  darśana anurūpeṇa phalam āyatanam svānām bhavati āyatanam janānām ya evam veda yaḥ  ha vai prajātim veda prajāyate ha prajayā paśubhiḥ ca sampannaḥ  bhavati retaḥ  vai prajātiḥ retasā prajanana indriyam upalakṣyate tad vijñāna anurūpam phalam prajāyate ha prajayā paśubhiḥ ya evam veda te heme prāṇā vāc ādayaḥ  ahaṃśreyase aham śreyā an iti etasmai prayojanāya vivadamānā biruddham vadamānā brahma jagmuḥ brahma gatavantaḥ  brahma śabda vācyam prajāpati gatvā ca tad brahma ha ūcuḥ uktavantaḥ kaḥ  naḥ asmākam madhye vasiṣṭhaḥ kaḥ  asmākam madhye vasati ca vāsayati ca tad brahma taiḥ pṛṣṭam sadhā uvācoktavat yasmin vaḥ  yuṣmākam madhya utkrānte nirgate śarīrāt idam śarīram pūrvasmāt atiśayena pāpīyaḥ pāpataram manyate lokaḥ śarīram hi nāma aneka aśuci saṃdhāta tvāt jīvataḥ  api pāpam eva tatas  api kaṣṭataram yasmin  utkrānte bhavati vairāgya artham idam ucyate pāpīya iti sa vaḥ  yuṣmākam madhye vasiṣṭhaḥ  bhaviṣyati jānan  api vasiṣṭham prajāpatirta uvācāyam vasiṣṭha iti itareṣām apriya parihārāya ta evam uktā brahmaṇā prāṇā ātmanaḥ  vīrya parīkṣaṇāya krameṇa ucca kramuḥ tatra vāc eva prathamam ha asmāt śarīrāt ucca krāma utkrāntavatī sā ca utkramya saṃvatsaram proṣya proṣitā bhūtvā punar āgatya uvāca katham aśakata śaktavantaḥ  yūyam mad ṛte mām vinā jīvitum iti ta evam uktā ūcuḥ yathā loke akalā mūkā avadantaḥ  vācā prāṇantaḥ prāṇana vya apāram kurvantaḥ prāṇena paśyantaḥ  darśana vyāpāram cakṣuṣā kurvantaḥ tathā śṛṇvantaḥ śrotreṇa vidvāṃsaḥ  manasā kārya akārya ādi viṣayam prajāyamānā retasā
