putrān utpādayanta evam ajīviṣma vayam iti evam prāṇaiḥ datta uttarā vāc ātmanaḥ  asmin  avasiṣṭha tvam buddhvā praviveśa ha vāc  tathā cakṣuḥ het cakrāma ityādi pūrvavat  śrotram manaḥ prajā atirita atha ha prāṇa utkramiṣyan  utkramamam kariṣyan  tadānīm eva sva sthānāt pracalitā vāc ādayaḥ kim iva iti āha yathā loke mahān  ca asau suhayaḥ ca mahāsu hayaḥ śobhanaḥ  hayaḥ  lakṣaṇa upetaḥ  mahān parimāṇataḥ sindhu deśe bhavaḥ saindhavaḥ  abhijanataḥ paḍvīśa śaṅkūn pāda bandhana śaṅkūn paḍvīśāḥ ca te śaṅkavaḥ ca tān saṃvṛhet udyacchet yugapad utkhanet aśva āroha ārūḍhe parīkṣaṇāya evam ha eva ima anvāc ādīn prāṇān saṃvavarhet yatavān sva sthānāt bhraṃśitavān te vāc ādayaḥ  ha ūcuḥ he bhagavaḥ  bhagavat mā utkram īryasmāt na vai śakṣyāmaḥ tvad ṛte tvām vinā jīvitum iti yadi evam mama śreṣṭha tā vijñātā bhavadbhiḥ aham atra śreṣṭhaḥ tasya u me mama balim karam kuruta karam prayacchata iti ayam ca prāṇa samvādaḥ kalpitaḥ  viduṣaḥ śreṣṭha parīkṣaṇa prakāra upadeśaḥ anena hi prakāreṇa vidvān kaḥ nu khalu atra śreṣṭha iti parīkṣaṇam karoti sa eṣa parīkṣaṇa prakāraḥ samvāda bhūtaḥ kathyate na hi anyathā saṃhatyakāriṇām satām eṣām añjasā eva saṃvatsara mātram eva ekaikasya nirgamana ādi upapadyate tasmāt vidvān eva anena prakāreṇa vicārayati vāc ādīnām pradhāna bubhutsurupāsanāya balim prārthitāḥ santaḥ prāṇāḥ tathā iti pratijñātavantaḥ sā ha vāc prathamam bali dānāya pravṛttā ha kila uvācā uktavatī yad vā aham vasiṣṭhā asmi yad mama vasiṣṭha tvam tad tava eva tena vasiṣṭha guṇena tvam tad vasiṣṭhaḥ  asi iti yad vā aham pratiṣṭhā asmi tvam tad pratiṣṭhaḥ  asi yā mama pratiṣṭhā sā tvam asi iti cakṣuḥ samānam anyat  sampad ā āyatana prajā atitva giṇān krameṇa samarpitavantaḥ yadi evam sādhu balim dattavantaḥ  bhavantaḥ  brūta tasya u ma evaṅguṇa viśiṣṭasya kim annam kim vāsa iti āhuḥ itare yad idam loke kiñca kiñcid annam nāma āpyā śvabhya ā kṛmibhya ā kīṭa pataṅgebhyaḥ yad ca śva annam kṛbhyannam kīṭa pataṅga annam ca tena saha sarvam eva yad kiñcitprāṇibhiḥ adyamānam annam tad sarvam tava annam sarvam prāṇasya annam iti dṛṣṭiḥ atra vidhīyate kecitu sarva bhakṣaṇe doṣa abhāvam vadanti prāṇān na vidaḥ tad asat  śāsra antareṇa pratiṣiddha tvāt  tena asya vikalpa iti ced  na avidhāyaka tvāt  na ha vā asya anannam jagdham bhavati iti sarvam prāṇasya annam iti etasya vijñānasya vihitasya stuti artham etad  tena eka vākyata āpatteḥ na tu śāsra antara vihitasya bādhane sāmarthyam anya para tvāt asya prāṇa mātrasya sarvam annam iti etad darśanam ihi vidhitsitam na tu sarvam bhakṣayet iti yad tu sarva bhakṣaṇe doṣa abhāva jñānam sat mithyā eva pramāṇa abhāvāt  viduṣaḥ prāṇa tvāt sarvān na upapatteḥ sāmarthyāt adoṣa  eva iti ced  na aśeṣān natva anupapatteḥ satyam yadi api vidvān prāṇaḥ  yena kāryata karaṇa saṃghātena viśiṣṭasya vidvattā tena kārya karaṇa saṃghātena kṛmi kīṭa deva ādi aśeṣa anna bhakṣaṇam na upapadyate tena tatra aśeṣa anna bhakṣaṇe doṣa abhāva jñāpanam anarthakam aprāpta tvāt aśeṣa anna bhakṣaṇa doṣasya nanu prāṇaḥ sanbhakṣayati eva kṛmi kīṭa ādi annam api bāḍham kintu na tad viṣayaḥ pratiṣedhaḥ  asti tasmāt daiva raktam kiṃśukam tatra doṣa abhāvaḥ atas tad rūpeṇa doṣa abhāva jñāpanam anarthakam aprāpta tvāt aśeṣa anna bhakṣaṇa deṣasya yena tu kārya karaṇa saṃghāta sambandhena pratiṣedhaḥ kriyate tad sambandhena tu iha na eva pratiprasavaḥ  asti tasmāt tad pratiṣedha atikrame doṣa eva syāt anya viṣaya tvāt na ha vā iti ādeḥ na ca brāhmaṇa ādi śarīrasya sarvānnatva darśanam iha vidhīyate kintu prāṇa mātrasya eva yathā ca sāmānyena sarva annasya prāṇasya kiñcid anna jātam kasyacid jīvana hetuḥ yathā viṣam viṣa jasya krimeḥ tad eva anyasya prāṇa annam api sat dṛṣṭam eva doṣam utpādayati maraṇa ādi lakṣaṇam tathā sarva annasya api prāṇasya pratiṣiddha anna bhakṣaṇe brāhmaṇatva ādi deha saṃbandhāt doṣa eva syāt  tasmāt mithyājñānam eva abhakṣya bhakṣaṇe doṣa abhāva jñānam āpaḥ  vāsa iti āpaḥ  bhakṣamāṇā vāsaḥ sthānīyāḥ tava atra ca prāṇasyā apaḥ vāsa iti etad darśanam vidhīyate na tu vāsaḥ kārye āpaḥ  viniyoktum śakyāḥ tasmāt yathāprāpte abbhakṣaṇe darśana mātram kartavyam na ha vā asya sarvam prāṇasya annam iti evaṃvidaḥ  anannam anadanīyam jagdham bhuktam na bhavati ha yadi api anena ānadanīyam bhukta madanīyam eva bhuktam syāt na tu tad kṛta doṣeṇa lipyata iti etad vidyā āstutiḥ iti avocāma tathā na anannam pratigṛhītam yadi api apratighrāhyam hastyādi pratigṛhītam syāt tad api annam eva pratigrāhyam syāt tatra api apratigrāhya pratigraha doṣeṇa na lipyata iti stuti artham eva ya evam etad anasya prāṇasya annam veda phalam tu prāṇa ātmabhāva eva na tu etad phala abhiprāyeṇa kim tarhi stuti abhiprāyeṇa iti nanu etad eva phalam kasmāt na bhavati na prāṇa ātma darśinaḥ prāṇa ātmabhāva eva phalam tatra ca prāṇa ātma bhūtasya sarva ātmanaḥ  anadanīyam api ādyam eva tathā apratigrāhyam api pratigrāhyam eva iti yathāprāptam eva upādāya vidyā stūyate atas  na eva phala vidhi sarūpa tā vākyasya yasmāt āpaḥ vāsaḥ prāṇasya tasmāt vidvāṃsaḥ  brāhmaṇāḥ śrotriyā adhīta vedāḥ  aśiṣyantaḥ  bhokṣyamāṇā ācāmanti apaḥ  aśitvā acāmanti bhuktyā ca uttara kālam apaḥ bhakṣayanti tatra teṣām ācāmatām kaḥ  abhiprāya iti āha etam eva anam prāṇam anagnam kurvantaḥ  manyante asti ca etad yoyasmai vāsaḥ  dadāti sa tam anagnam karomi iti hi manyate prāṇasya cā apaḥ  vāsa iti hi uktam yad apaḥ pibāmi tad prāṇasya vāsaḥ  dadāmi iti vijñānam kartavyam iti evam artham etad  nanu bhokṣyamāṇaḥ  bhuktavān  ca prayataḥ  bhaviṣyāmi iti ācāmati tatra ca prāṇasya anagna tā karaṇa artha tve ca dvi kārya tā acamanasya syāt  na ca kārya dvayam ācamanasya ekasya yuktam yadi prāyatya artham na anagnatā artham atha anagnatā artham na prāyatya artham yasmāt evam tasmāt dvitīyam ācamana antaram prāṇasya anagna tā karaṇāya bhavatu na kriyā dvitva upapatteḥ dve hi ete kriye bhotryamāṇasya bhuktavataḥ ca yad ācamanam smṛti vihitam tad prāyatya artham bhavati kriyā mātram eva na tu tatra prāyatyam darśana ādi apekṣate tatra cā acamana aṅga bhūtāsu apsu vāsaḥ vijñānam prāṇasya iti kartavya tayā codyate na tu tasmin kriyamāṇa  ācamanasya prāyatyartha tā vādhyate kriyā antara tvāt ācamanasya tasmāt bhokṣyamāṇasya bhuktavataḥ ca yad ācamanam tatra āpaḥ  vāsaḥ prāṇasya iti darśana mātram vidhīyate aprāpta tvāt anyatas  śvetaketuḥ ha vā āruṇeyaḥ iti asya saṃbandhaḥ khila adhikāraḥ  ayam tatra yad anuktam tad ucyate saptama adhyāya ante jñāna karma samuccaya kāriṇā agneḥ mārga yācanam kṛtam agne naya supatha iti tatra anekeṣām pathām sadbhāvaḥ  mantreṇa sāmarthyāt pradarśitaḥ supatha iti viśeṣaṇāt  panthānaḥ ca kṛta vipāka pratipatti mārgāḥ vakṣyati ca yad kṛtvā ityādi tatra ca kati karma vipāka pratipatti mārgā iti sarva saṃsāra gati upasaṃhāra arthaḥ  ayam ārambhaḥ etāvatī hi saṃsāra gatiḥ etāvān karmaṇaḥ  vipākaḥ svābhāvikasya śāsrīyasya ca sa vijñānasya iti yadi api dvayā ha prājāpatyā iti atra svābhāvikaḥ pāpmā sūcitaḥ na ca tasya idam kāryam iti vipākaḥ pradarśitaḥ śāsrīyasya eva tu vipākaḥ pradarśitaḥ tri anna ātma pratipatti antena brahma vidyā ārambhe tad vairāgyasya vivakṣita tvāt  tatra api kevalena karmaṇā pitṛ lokaḥ  vidyayā vidyā saṃyuktena ca karmaṇā deva loke  iti uktam tatra kena mārgeṇa pitṛ lokam pratipadyate kena vā deva lokam iti na uktam tad ca iha khila prakaraṇe aśeṣataḥ vaktavyam iti ata ārabhyate ante ca sarva upasaṃhāraḥ śāsrasya iṣṭaḥ api ca etāvat amṛta tvam iti uktam na karmaṇaḥ  amṛtatva aśā asti iti ca tatra hetuḥ na uktaḥ tad arthaḥ ca ayam ārambhaḥ yasmāt iyam karmaṇaḥ  gatiḥ na nitye amṛta tve vyāpāraḥ  asti tasmāt etāvat eva amṛtatva sādhanam iti sāmarthyāt hetu tvam saṃpadyate api ca uktam agnihotre na tu eva enayoḥ tvam utkrātim na gatim na pratiṣṭhām na tṛptim na punarāvṛtim na lokam pratyutthāyinam vettha iti tatra prativacane te vā ete āhutī hute utkrāmata ityādinā āhuteḥ kāryam uktam tad ca etad kartuḥ āhuti lakṣaṇasya karmaṇaḥ phalam na hi kartāram anāśrityā ahuti lakṣaṇasya karmaṇaḥ svātantryeṇa utkrānti ādi kārya ārambha upapadyate kartṛ artha tvāt karmaṇaḥ kārya ārambhasya sādhana āśraya tvāt ca karmaṇaḥ tatra agnihotra stuti artha tvāt agnihotrasya eva kāryam iti uktam ṣaḍ  prakāram api iha tu tad eva kartuḥ phalam iti upadiśyate ṣaṣ prakāram api karma phala vijñānasya vivakṣita tvāt  tad dvāreṇa ca pañca agni darśanam iha uttara mārga pratipatti sādhanam vidhitsitam evam aśeṣa saṃsāra gati upasaṃhāraḥ karma kāṇḍasya eṣā niṣṭhā iti etad dvayam didarśayiṣuḥ ākhyāyikām praṇayati śvetaketuḥ nāmataḥ  aruṇasya apatyam āruṇiḥ tasya apatyam āruṇeyaḥ ha śabda aitihya arthaḥ vai niścaya arthaḥ pitrā anuśiṣṭaḥ san  ātmanaḥ  yaśaḥ prathanāya pañcālānām pariṣadam āgatya jitvā rājñaḥ  api pariṣadam jeṣyāmi iti garveṇa sa ājagāma jīvalasya apatyam jevalim pañcāla rājam pravāhaṇa nāma anaṃsu abhṛtyaiḥ paricārayamāṇam ātmanaḥ paricaraṇam kārayantam iti etad  sa rājā pūrvam eva tasya vidyā abhimāna garvam śrutvā vinetavyaḥ  ayam iti matvā tam udīkṣya utprekṣyā agata mātram eva abhyuvāda abhyuktavān kumārā iti saṃbodhya bhartsana arthā plutiḥ evam uktaḥ sa pratiśuśrāva bhoiti bhoitya pratirūpam api kṣattriyam pratyuktavān kruddhaḥ san anuśiṣṭaḥ  anuśāsitaḥ  asi bhavasi kim pitrā iti uvāca rājā pratyāha itara oṃm iti bāḍham anuśiṣṭaḥ  asmi pṛccha yadi saṃśayaḥ te yadi evam vettha vijānāsi kim yathā yena prakāreṇa imāḥ prajāḥ prasiddhāḥ prayatyaḥ  mriyamāṇā vipratipadyanta aiti vipratipadyante vicāraṇa arthā plutiḥ samānena mārgeṇa gacchantīnām mārga dvaividhyam yatra kāścid prajā anyena mārgeṇa gacchanti kāścid anyena iti vipratipattiḥ yathā tāḥ prajā vipratipadyante tad kim vetthā iti arthaḥ na iti ha uvāca itaraḥ tarhi vettha u yathā imam lokam punar āpadyantauiti punar āpadyante yathā punar āgacchanti imam lokam na iti ha eva uvāca śvetaketuḥ vetthaḥ  yathā asau lokaḥ evam prasiddhena nyāyena punar  punar asakṛt prayadbhiḥ mariyamāṇaiḥ yathāyena prakāreṇa na saṃpūryatāiti na saṃpūryate asau lokaḥ tad kim vettha na iti ha eva uvāca vetthaḥ  yatithyām yad saṃkhyā kāyām āhutyām āhutau hutāyāmāpaḥ puruṣa vācaḥ puruṣasya yā vāc sā eva yāsām vāktāḥ puruṣa vācaḥ  bhūtvā puruṣa śabda vācyā vā bhūtvā yadā puruṣa ākāra pariṇatāḥ tadā puruṣa vācaḥ  bhavanti samutthāya samyak utthāya udbhūtāḥ satyaḥ  vadantī iti na iti ha eva uvāca puruṣa ākāra pariṇatāḥ tadā puruṣa vācaḥ  bhavanti samutthāya samyak utthāya udbhūtāḥ satyaḥ  vadantī iti na iti ha eva uvāca yadi evam vettha u deva yānasya pathaḥ  mārgasya pratipadam pratipadyate yena sā pratipattām pratipadam pitṛyāṇasya vā pratipadam pratipad chabda vācyam artham āha yad karma kṛtvā yathā viśiṣṭam karma kṛtvā iti arthaḥ deva yānam vā panthānam mārgam pratipadyante pitṛyāṇam vā yad karma kṛtvā pratidyante tad karma pratipad icyate tām pratipadam kim vettha deva loka pitṛ loka pratipatti sādhanam kim vetthā iti arthaḥ api atra asya arthasya prakāśakam ṛṣeḥ mantrasya vacaḥ  vākyam naḥ śrutam asti mantraḥ  api asya arthasya prakāśakaḥ  vidyata iti arthaḥ kaḥ  asau mantra iti ucyate dve sṛtī dvau mārgau  aśṛṇavam śṛtavān asmi tayoḥ ekā pitṛṇām prāpikā pitṛ loka saṃbaddhā tayā sṛtyā pitṛ lokam prāpnoti iti arthaḥ aham aśṛṇavam iti vyavahitena saṃbandhaḥ devānām utāpi devānām saṃbandhini anyā devān prāpayati sā ke punarubhābhyām sṛtibhyām pitṝn devān  ca gacchanti iti ucyate uta api martyānām manuṣyāṇām saṃbandhinyau manuṣyā eva hi sṛtibhyām gacchanti iti arthaḥ tābhyām sṛti hyām idam viśvam samastam etad gacchat sameti saṃgacchate te ca dve sṛtī yad antarā yayoḥ antarā yad antarā pitaram mātaram ca mātā pitroḥ antarā madhya iti arthaḥ kau tau mātā pitarau dyāvāpṛthivī āvaṇḍa kapāle iyam vai mātā asau pitā iti hi vyākhyātam brāhmaṇena aṇḍa kapālayoḥ madhye saṃsāra viṣaye eva ete sṛtī nā atyantika amṛtatva gamanāya itara āha na aham atas  asmāt praśna samudāyāt ekañcana ekam api praśnam na veda na aham veda iti ha uvāca śvetaketuḥ atha anantaram apanīya vidyā abhimāna garvam enam prakṛtam śvetaketum vasatyā vasati prayojanena upamantrayāñcakre iha vasantu bhavantaḥ pādyam arpyam cā anīyatām iti upamantraṇam kṛtavān rājā anādṛtya tām vasatim kumāraḥ śvetaketuḥ pradudrāva pratigatavān pitaram prati sa cā ajagāma pitaram āgatya ca uvāca tam katham iti vāva kila evam kila naḥ asmān bhavān purā samāvagatavān pitaram prati sa cā ajagāma pitaram āgatya ca uvāca tam katham iti vāva kila evam kila naḥ asmān bhavān purā samāvartana kāle anuśiṣṭān sarvābhiḥ vidyābhiḥ avocaḥ avocat iti sa upālambham putrasya vacaḥ śrutvā aha pitā katha kena prakāreṇa tava duḥkham upajātam he sumedhaḥ śobhanā medhā yasya iti sumedhāḥ śṛṇu mama yathā vṛttam pañca pañca saṃkhyākān praśnāt mā mām rājanya bandhū rājanyā bandhavaḥ  yasya iti paribhava vacanam etad rājanyabandhuḥ iti aprākṣīt pṛṣṭavān  tatas tasmāt naikañcana ekam api na veda na vijñātavān asmi katame te rājñāḥ pṛṣṭāḥ praśnā iti pitrā uktaḥ putra ime ta iti ha pratīkāni mukhāni praśnānām udājahāra udāhṛtavān sa ha uvāca pitā putram kruddham upaśamayan  tathā tena prakāreṇa naḥ asmān  tvam he tāta vatsa jānīthā gṛhṇīthā yathā yad aham kiñca vijñāna jātam veda sarvam tatubhyam avocam iti eva jānīthāḥ kaḥ  anyaḥ  mama priya taraḥ  asti tvad taḥ  yad arthaṃrakṣiṣye aham api etad na jānāmi yad rājñā pṛṣṭam tasmāt prehya āgaccha tatra pratītya gatvā rājñi brahmacaryam vatsyāvaḥ  vidyā artham iti sa āha bhavān eva gacchatu iti na aham tasya mukham nirīkṣitum utsahe sa ājagāma gautamaḥ  gotrataḥ  gautama āruṇiḥ yatra pravāhaṇasya jaivalerāsā asanam āsthāyikā ṣaṣṭhī dvayam prathamam āsthāne tasmai gautamāyāḥ agatāyā asanam anurūpam āhṛtya udakam bhṛtyaiḥ āhāra yāñcakāra atha ha asmā ardhyam purodhasā kṛtavān mantravat madhuparkam ca kṛtvā ca evam pūjām tam ha uvāca varam bhagavate gautamāya tubhyam dadbha iti gaḥ śva ādi lakṣaṇam sa ha uvāca gautamaḥ pratijñātaḥ  me mama eṣa varaḥ tvayā asyām pratijñāyām dṛḍhī kurva ātmānam yām tu vācam kumārasya mama putrasya ante samīpe vācam abhāṣathāḥ praśna rūpām tām eva me brūhi sa eva naḥ vara iti sa ha uvāca rājā daiveṣu vareṣu tad vai gautama yaḥ tvam prārthayase mānuṣāṇām anyatamam prārthaya varam sa ha uvāca gautamaḥ  bhavatā api vijñāyate ha mama asti saḥ na tena prārthitena kṛtyam mama yam tvam ditsasi mānuṣam varam yasmāt mama api asti hiraṇyasya prabhūtasya apāttam prāptam gaḥ aaśvānānām āpāttam asti iti sarvatra anuṣaṅgaḥ  dāsīnām pravārāṇām parivārāṇām paridhānasya ca na ca yad mama vidyamānam tad tvattaḥ prārthanīyam tvayā vā deyam pratijñātaḥ ca varaḥ tvayā tvam eva jānīṣe yad atra yuktam pratijñā rakṣaṇīyā tava iti mama punar ayam abhiprāyaḥ  mā bhūt naḥ asmān abhyasmān eva kevalān prati bhavān sarvatra vadānyaḥ  bhūtvā avadān yaḥ  mā bhūt kadaryaḥ  mā bhūt iti arthaḥ bahoḥ prabhūtasya anantasya ananta phalasya iti etad  aparyantasya aparisamāptikasya putra pautra ādi gāmikasya iti etad  īdṛśasya vittasya mām pratyeva kevalam ādātā mā bhūdbhavān na ca anyatra ādeyam asti bhavataḥ evam ukta āha sa tvam vai he gautama tīrthena nyāyena śāsra vihitena vidyām matta icchāsā icchā anvāptum iti uktaḥ  gautama āha upaimi upagacchāmi śiṣya tvena aham bhavantam iti vācā ha sma eva kila pūrva brāhmaṇāḥ kṣattriyān vidyā arthinaḥ santaḥ  vaiśyān vā kṣattriyā vā vaiśyān āpadyupayanti śiṣya vṛttyā hi upacchanti na upāyana śuśrūṣā ādibiḥ atas  sa gautamaḥ  ha upāyana kortyā upagamana kīrtana mātreṇa eva uvāsa uṣitavān na upāyanam cakāra evam gautamenā apad antara ukte sa ha uvāca rājā pīḍitam matvā kṣāmayan  tathā naḥ asmān prati mā aparādhā aparādham mā kārṣīḥ asmadīyaḥ  aparādhaḥ  na grahītavya iti arthaḥ tava ca pitāmahā asmad pitāmaheṣu yata aparādham na jagṛhuḥ tathā pitāmahānām vṛttam asmāsu api bhavatā rakṣaṇīyam iti arthaḥ yathā iyam vidyā tvayā prārthitetaḥ tvad saṃpradānāt pūrvam prāk na kasmin  api brāhmaṇa uvāsa uṣitavatī tathā tvam api jānīṣe sarvadā kṣattriya param parayeyam vidyā agatā sā sthitiḥ mayā api rakṣaṇīyā yadi śakyata iti uktam daiveṣu gautama tad vareṣu mānuṣāṇām brūhi iti na punar tava ādeyaḥ  vara iti itaḥ para na śakyate rakṣitum tām api vidyām aham tubhyam vakṣyāmi kaḥ  hi anyaḥ  api hi yasmāt evam bruvantam tvām arhati pratyākhyātum na vakṣyāmi iti aham punar  katham na vakṣye tubhyam iti asau vai lokaḥ  agniḥ gotama ityādi caturthaḥ praśnaḥ prāthamyena nirṇīyate krama bhaṅgaḥ tu etad nirṇaya āyatta tvāt itara prasna nirṇayasya asau dyauḥ lokaḥ  agniḥ he gautama dyu loke agni dṛṣṭiḥ anagnau vidhīyate yathā yoṣit puruṣayoḥ tasya dyu loka agneḥ āditya eva samidh samindhanāt  ādityena hi samidhyate asau lokaḥ raśmayaḥ  dhūmaḥ samidha uththāna sāmānyāt  ādityāt hi raśmayaḥ  nirgatāḥ samidhaḥ ca dhūmaḥ  loka uttiṣṭhati ahararciḥ prakāśa sāmānyāt  diśaḥ  aṅgārā upaśama sāmānyāt  avāntara diṣaḥ  visphuliṅgā visphuliṅgavat vikṣepāt  tasmin  etasmin  evaṅguṇa viśiṣṭe dyu loka agnau devāḥ  indra ādayaḥ śraddhām juhvati āhuti dravya sthānīyām prakṣipanti tasyāḥ  āhutyā āhuteḥ somaḥ  rājā pitṝṇām brāhmaṇānām ca saṃbhavati tatra ke devāḥ katham juhvati kiṃvā śraddhā ākhyam haviḥ iti ata uktam asmābhiḥ saṃbandhe na tu eva enayoḥ tvam utkrāntim iti ādi padārtha ṣaṭka nirṇaya artham agnihotra uktam te vā ete agnihotra āhutī hute satyau  utkrāmataḥ te antarikṣam āviśataḥ te antarikṣam āhavanīyam kurvāte vāyum samidham marīcīḥ eva śukrām āhutim te antarikṣan tarpayataḥ te tatas  utkrāmataḥ te divam āviśataḥ te divam āhavanīyam kurvāte ādityam samidham iti evamādi uktam tatra agni hotra āhutī sa sādhane eva utkrāmataḥ yathā iha yaiḥ sādhanaiḥ viśiṣṭe ye jñāyete āhavanīya agni samiddhūma aṅgāra visphuliṅga āhuti dravyaiḥ te tathā eva utkrāmataḥ asmāt lokāt amum lokam tatra agniḥ agni tvena samidh samittvena dhūmaḥ  dhūma tvena aṅgārā aṅgāra tvena visphuliṅga tvenā ahuti dravyam api paya ādya āhuti dravya tvena eva sarga ādau  avyākṛta avasthāyām api pareṇa sūkṣmeṇā atmanā vyavatiṣṭhate tad vidyamānam eva sa sādhanam agnihotra lakṣaṇam karma apūrveṇā atmanā vyavasthitam sat tad punar vyākaraṇa kāle tathā eva antarikṣa ādīnām āhavanīya ādi agni ādi bhāvam kurvat vipariṇamate tathā eva idānīm api agnihotra ākhyam karma evam agni hotra āhuti apūrva vipariṇāma ātmakam jagat sarvam iti āhutyoḥ eva stuti artha tvena utkrānti ādyā lokam pratyutthāyinā antāḥ ṣaḍ  padārthāḥ karma prakaraṇe adhastāt nirṇītāḥ iha tu kartuḥ karma vivakṣāyām dyu loka agni ādi ārabhya pañca agni darśanam uttara mārga pratipatti sādhanam viśiṣṭa karma phala upabhogāya vidhitsitam iti dyu loka agni ādi darśanam prastūyate tatra ya ādhyātmikāḥ prāṇā iha agnihotrasya hotāraḥ ta evā adhidaivika tvena pariṇatāḥ santa indra ādayaḥ  bhavanti ta eva tatra hotāraḥ  dyu loka agnau te ca iha agnihotrasya phala bhogāya agni hotram hutavantaḥ ta eva phala pariṇāma kāle api tad phala bhoktṛ tvāt tatra tatra hotṛ tvam pratipadyante tathā tathā vipariṇamamānā deva śabda vācyāḥ santaḥ atra ca yad payaḥ dravyam agnihotra karma āśraya bhūtam ihā ahavanīye prakṣiptam agninā bhakṣitam adṛṣṭena sūkṣmema rūpeṇa vipariṇatam saha kartrā yajamānena amum lokam dhūma ādi krameṇa antarikṣāt dyulokam āviśati tāḥ sūkṣmā āpa āhuti kārya bhūtā agnihotra samavāyinyaḥ kartṛ sahitāḥ śraddhā śabda vācyāḥ soma loke kartuḥ śarīra antara ārambhāya dyu lokam praviśantyaḥ  hūyante iti ucyante tāḥ tatra dyu lokam praviśya soma maṇḍale kartuḥ śarīram ārabhante tad etad ucyate devāḥ śraddhām juhvati tasyāḥ  āhutyai somaḥ  rājā saṃbhavati iti śraddhā vā āpaḥ iti śruteḥ vettha yatithyām āhutyām hutāyāmāpaḥ puruṣa vācaḥ  bhūtvā samutthāya vadantoti praśnaḥ tasya ca nirṇaya viṣaye asau vai lokaḥ  agniḥ iti prastutam tasmāt āpaḥ karma samāvāyinyaḥ kartuḥ śarīra ārambhikāḥ śraddhā śabda vācyā iti niścīyate bhūyas tvādāpaḥ puruṣavāca iti vyapadeśaḥ  na tu itarāṇi bhūtāni na santi iti karma prayuktaḥ ca śarīra ārambhaḥ karma ca apsamavāyi tatas ca apām prādhānyam śarīra kartṛ tve tena cā apaḥ puruṣavāca iti vyapadeśaḥ karma kṛtaḥ  hi janma ārambhaḥ sarvatra tatra yadi api agnihotra āhuti stuti dvāreṇa utkrānti ādayaḥ prastutāḥ ṣaṣ padārthā agnihotre tathā api vaidikāni sarvāṇi eva karmāṇi agnihotra prabhṛtīni lakṣyante dāra agni saṃbaddham hi pāṅktam karma prastutya uktam karmaṇā pitṛ loke  iti vakṣyati ca atha ye yajñena dānena tapasā lokān jayanti iti parjanyaḥ  vā agniḥ gautama dvitīya āhuti ādhāra āhutyoḥ āvṛtti krameṇa parjanyaḥ  nāma vṛṣṭi upakaraṇa abhimānī devatā ātmā tasya saṃvatsara eva samidh  saṃvatsareṇa hi śarad ādibhiḥ grīṣma antaiḥ sva avayavaiḥ va parivartamānena parjanyaḥ  agniḥ dīpyate abhrāṇi dhūmaḥ dhūma prabhava tvāt dhūmavat upalakṣya tvāt vā vidyut arciḥ prakāśa sāmānyāt  aśaniḥ aṅgārāḥ upaśānta kāṭhinya sāmānyābhyām hrādunayaḥ  hlādunayaḥ stanayitnu śabdā visphuliṅgāḥ vikṣepa anekatva sāmānyāt tasmin  etasmin  iti āhuti adhikaraṇa nirdeśaḥ devāḥ  iti ta eva hotāraḥ somam rājānam juhvati yaḥ  asau dyu loka agnau śraddhāyām hutāyām abhinirvṛttaḥ somaḥ sa dvitīye parjanya agnau hūyate tasyāḥ ca soma āhuteḥ vṛṣṭiḥ saṃbhavati ayam vai lokaḥ  agniḥ gotama ayam loka iti prāṇi janma upabhoga āśrayaḥ kriyā kāraka phala viśiṣṭaḥ sa tṛtīyaḥ  agniḥ tasya agneḥ pṛthivī eva samidh  pṛthivyāḥ  hi ayam lokaḥ  aneka prāṇi upabhoga saṃpannayā samidhyate agniḥ dhūmaḥ pṛthivī āśraya utthāna sāmānyāt pārthivam hi indhana dravyam āśritya agniḥ uttiṣṭhati yathā samidh āśrayena dhūmaḥ rātriḥ arciḥ samidh saṃbandha prabhava sāmānyāt  agneḥ samidh saṃbandhena hi arciḥ saṃbhavati tathā pṛthivī samidh saṃbandhena śarvarī pṛthivī chāyām hi śārvaram tam ācakṣate candramā aṅgārāḥ tad prabhavatva sāmānyāt  arciṣaḥ  hi aṅgārāḥ prabhavanti tathā rātrau candramāḥ upaśāntatva sāmānyāt vā nakṣatrāṇi visphuliṅgāḥ bisphuliṅgavat vikṣepa sāmānyāt  tasmin  etasmin  ityādi pūrvavat  vṛṣṭim juhvati tasyāḥ  āhuteḥ annam saṃbhavati vṛṣṭi prabhavatu asya prasiddha tvāt vrīhi yava ādeḥ annasya puruṣaḥ  vā agniḥ gautama prasiddhaḥ śiraḥ pāṇi ādimān puruṣaḥ caturthaḥ  agniḥ tasya vyāttam vivṛtam mukham samidh  vivṛtena hi mukhena dīpyate puruṣaḥ  vacana svādhyāya ādau yathā samidhā agniḥ prāṇaḥ  dhūmaḥ tad utthāna sāmānyāt  mukhāt hi prāṇa uttiṣṭhati vākya śabdaḥ  arciḥ vyañjakatva sāmānyāt  arciḥ ca vyañjakam tathā vāc śabdaḥ  abhidheya vyañjakaḥ cakṣuḥ aṅgārā upaśama sāmānyāt prakāśa āśraya tvāt vā śrotram visphuliṅgā vikṣepa sāmānyāt  tasmin  annam juhvati nanu na eva devāḥ  annam iha juhvataḥ  dṛśyante na eṣa doṣaḥ prāṇānām devatva upapatteḥ adhidaivam indra ādayaḥ  devāḥ te  eva adhyātmam prāṇāḥ te ca annasya puruṣe prakṣeptāraḥ tasyāḥ  āhute retaḥ saṃbhavati anna pariṇāmaḥ  hi retaḥ yoṣā vā agniḥ gautama yoṣa iti srī pañcamaḥ  homa adhikaraṇaḥ  agniḥ tasyāḥ  upastha eva samidh  tena hi sā samidhyate lomāni dhūmaḥ tad utthāna sāmānyāt  yoniḥ arciḥ varṇa sāmānyāt yad antar  karoti te aṅgārā antar  karaṇam maithuna vyāpāraḥ te aṅgārā vīrya upaśama hetutva sāmānyāt  vīrya ādi upaśama kāraṇam maithunam tathā aṅgāra bhāvaḥ  agneḥ upaśama kāraṇam abhinandāḥ sukha lavāḥ kṣudratva sāmānyāt visphuliṅgāḥ tasmin retaḥ  juhvati tasyāḥ  āhuteḥ puruṣaḥ saṃbhavati evam dyuparjanyāyaṃloka puruṣa yoṣa agniṣu kramema hūyamānāḥ śraddhā soma vṛṣṭi anna retaḥ bhāvena sthūla tāratamya kramam āpadyamānāḥ śraddhā śabda vācyā āpaḥ puruṣa śabdam ārabhante yaḥ praśnaḥ caturthaḥ  vettha yatithyām āhutyām hutāyāmāpaḥ puraṣavācaḥ  bhūtvā samutthāya vadantī iti sa eṣa nirṇītaḥ pañcamyām āhutau yoṣa agnau hutāyām retaḥ bhūtā āpaḥ puruṣa vācaḥ  bhavanti iti sa puruṣa evam krameṇa jātaḥ  jīvati kiyantam kālam iti ucyate yāvat jīvati yāvat asmin śarīre sthiti nimittam karma vidyate tāvat iti arthaḥ atha tad kṣaye yadā yasmi kāle mriyate atha tadā enam mṛtam agnaye agni artham eva antyāhutyai haranti śratvijaḥ tasyāḥ ahuti bhūtasya prasiddhaḥ  agniḥ eva homa adhikaraṇam na parikalpyaḥ  agniḥ prasiddhā eva samidh samidh dhūmaḥ  dhūmaḥ  arciḥ arciḥ aṅgārā aṅgārā visphuliṅgā visphuliṅgā yathāprasiddham eva sarvam iti arthaḥ tasmin puruṣam antya āhutim juhvati tasyāḥ  āhutyā āhuteḥ puruṣaḥ  bhāsvara varṇaḥ  atiśaya dīptimān niṣeka ādibhiḥ anti āhuti antaiḥ karmabhiḥ saṃskṛta tvāt saṃbhavati niṣpadyate idānīm prathama praśna nirākaraṇa artham āha te ke ya evam yathā uktam pañca agni darśanam etad viduḥ evam śabdāt agni samiddhūma arciḥ aṅgāra visphuliṅga śraddhā ādi viśiṣṭāḥ pañca agnayaḥ  nirdiṣṭāḥ tān evam etān pañca agnīn viduḥ iti arthaḥ nanu agni hotra āhuti darśana viṣayam eva etad darśanam tatra hi uktam utkrānti ādi padārtha ṣaṭka nirṇaye divam evā ahavanīyam kurvāte ityādi iha api amuṣya lokasya agni tvam ādityasya ca samit tvam ityādi bahu sāmyam tasmāt tad śeṣam eva etad darśanam iti na yatithyām iti prasna prativacana parigrahāt  yatithyām iti asya praśnasya prativacanasya yāvat eva parigrahaḥ tāvat eva evaṃśabdena parāmraṣṭum yuktam anyathā praśna anarthakyān nirjñāta tvāt ca saṃkhyāyāḥ  agnaya eva vaktavyāḥ atha nirjñātam api anūdyate yathā prāptasya eva anuvadanam yuktam na tu asau lokaḥ  agniḥ iti atha upalakṣaṇa arthaḥ tathā api ādyena antyena ca upalakṣaṇam yuktam śruti antarāt ca samāne hi prakaraṇe chāndogya śrutau pañca agnīn veda iti pañca saṃkhyāyā eva upādānāt anagnihotra śeṣam etad  pañca agni darśanam yad tu agni samidh ādi sāmānyam tad agnihotra stuti artham iti avocāma tasmāt na utkrānti ādi padārtha ṣaṭka parijñānāt arcira ādi pratipattiḥ evam iti prakṛta upādānena arciḥ ādi pratipatti vidhānāt ke punar te ya evam viduḥ gṛhasthā eva nanu teṣām yajña ādi sādhanena dhūma ādi pratipattiḥ vidhitsita na anevaṃvidām api gṛhasthānām yajña ādi sādhana upapatteḥ bhikṣuvānaprasthayoḥ ca araṇya saṃbandhena grahaṇāt  gṛhastha karma saṃbaddha tvāt ca pañca agni darśanasya atas  na api brahmacāriṇa evam viduḥ iti gṛhyante teṣām tu uttare pathi praveśaḥ smṛti prāmāṇyāt  aṣṭāśīti sahasrāṇām ṛṣīṇām ūrdhvaretasām uttareṇa āryamṇaḥ panthāḥ te amṛta tvam hi bhejire iti tasmāt ye gṛhasthā evam agnijaḥ  aham agni apatyam iti evam krameṇa agnibhyaḥ  jātaḥ  agni rūpa iti evam ye viduḥ te ca ye cāmī araṇye vānaprasthāḥ parivrājakāḥ ca araṇya niṣṭhāḥ śraddhām śraddhā yuktāḥ snataḥ satyam brahma hiraṇyagarbha ātmānam upāsate na punar  śraddhām ca upāsate te sarve arciḥ abhisaṃbhavanti yāvat gṛhasthāḥ pañca agni vidyām satyam vā brahma na viduḥ tāvat śraddhā ādi āhuti krameṇa pañcamyām āhutau hutāyām tatas  yoṣa agneḥ jātāḥ punar lokam pratyutthāyinaḥ  agnihotra ādi karma anuṣṭhā tāraḥ  bhavanti tena karmaṇā dhūma ādi krameṇa punar  pitṛ lokam punar  parjanya ādi krameṇa imam āvartante punar yoṣa agneḥ jātāḥ punar  karma kṛtvā iti evam eva ghaṭīyantravat gati āgatibhyām punar  punar āvartante yadā tu evam viduḥ tatas  ghaṭīyantra bhramaṇāt vinirmuktāḥ santaḥ  arciḥ abhisaṃbhavanti arciḥ iti na agni jvālā mātram kim tarhi arciḥ abhimāninī arciḥ śabda vācyā devatā uttara mārga lakṣaṇā vyavasthitā eva tām abhisaṃbhavanti na hi parivrājakānām agni arciṣā eva sākṣāt saṃbandhaḥ  asti tena devatā eva parigṛhyate arciḥ śabda vācyā atas  ahar devatām maraṇa kāla niyama anupapatteḥ ahar śabdaḥ  api devatā eva āyuṣaḥ kṣaye hi maraṇam na hi evaṃvidāhani eva martavyam iti ahar maraṇa kālaḥ  niyantum śakyate na ca rātrau pretāḥ santaḥ  ahar  pratīkṣante sa yāvat kṣipyet manaḥ tāvat ādityam gacchati iti śruti antarāt ahna āpūryamāṇa pakṣam ahar devatayā ativāhitā āpūryamāṇa pakṣa devatām pratipadyante śukla pakṣa devatām iti etad āpūryamāṇa pakṣa ādyān ṣaṣ māsān udaṅṅuttarām diśam ādityaḥ savitā eti tān māsān pratipadyante śukla pakṣa devatayā ativāhitāḥ santaḥ māsān iti bahuvacanāt saṃgha cāriṇyaḥ ṣaṣ uttarāyaṇa devatāḥ tebhyaḥ  māsebhyaḥ ṣaṣ māsa devatābhiḥ ativāhitā deva loka abhimāninīm devatām pratipadyante deva lokāt ādityam ādityāt vaidyutam vidyut abhimāninīm devatām pratipadyante vidyut devatām prāptān brahma loka vāsī puruṣaḥ  brahmaṇā manasā sṛṣṭaḥ  mānasaḥ kaścid etyāḥ agatya brahma lokān gamayati brahma loka aniti adhara uttara bhūmi bhedena bhinnā iti gamyante bahuvacana prayogāt  upāsana tāratamya upapatteḥ ca te tena puruṣeṇa gamitāḥ santaḥ teṣu brahma lokeṣu parāḥ prakṛṣṭāḥ santaḥ svayam parāvataḥ prakṛṣṭāḥ samāḥ saṃvatsarān anekān vasanti brahmaṇaḥ  anekān kalpān vasanti iti arthaḥ teṣām brahma lokam gatānām na asti punarāvṛttiḥ asmin saṃsāre na punar āgamanam iha iti śākhā antara pāṭhāt  iha iti ākṛti mātra grahaṇam iti ced śvaḥ bhūte paurṇamāsīm iti yadvat  na iha iti viśeṣaṇā narthakyāt yadi hi nā avartanta eva iha grahaṇam anarthakam eva syāt  śvobhūte paurṇamāsīm iti atra paurṇamāsyāḥ śvobhūta tvam anuktaṃna jñāyata iti yukta viśeṣayitum na hi tatra śvaākṛtiḥ śabda arthaḥ  vidyata iti śva śabdaḥ  virarthaka eva prayujyate yatra tu viśeṣaṇa śabde prayukte anviṣyamāṇe viśeṣaṇa phalam ced na gamyate tatra yuktaḥ  nirarthaka tvena utsraṣṭum viśeṣaṇa śabdaḥ  na tu satyām viśeṣaṇa phala avagatau tasmāt asmāt kalpāt ūrdhvam āvṛttiḥ gamyate atha punar ye na evam viduḥ utkrānti ādi agnihotra saṃbandha padārtha ṣaṭkasya eva veditāraḥ kevala karmiṇaḥ  yajñena agnihotra ādinā dānena bahis vedi bhikṣamāṇeṣu dravya saṃvibhāga lakṣaṇena tapasā bahis vedi eva dīkṣā ādi vyatiriktena kṛcchra cāndrāyaṇa ādinā lokān jayanti lokān iti bahuvacanāt tatra api phala tā ramyam abhipretam te dhūmam abhisaṃbhavanti uttara mārga iva iha api devatā eva dhūma ādi śabda vācyāḥ dhūma devatām pratipadyanta iti arthaḥ ātivāhika tvam ca devatānām tadvat eva dhūmāt rātrim rātri devatām tatas  apakṣīyamāṇa pakṣa devatām tatas  yān ṣaṣ māsān dakṣiṇām diśam āditya eti tān māsa devatā viśeṣān pratipadyante māsebhyaḥ pitṛ lokam pitṛ lokāt candram te candram prāpya annam bhavanti tān  tatra anna bhūtānyathā somam rājānam iha yajña ṛtvija āpyāyasvāpakṣīyasva iti bhakṣayanti evam enān  candram prāptān karmiṇaḥ  bhṛtyān iva svāminaḥ  bhakṣayanti upabhuñjate devāḥ āpyāyasvāpakṣīyasva iti na mantraḥ kim tarhi āpyāyyā apyāyya camasa stham bhakṣaṇena apakṣayam ca kṛtvā punar  punar bhakṣayanti iti arthaḥ evam devāḥ  api soma loke labdha śarīrān karmiṇa upakaraṇa bhūtān punar  punar viśrāmayantaḥ karma anurūpam phalam prayacchantaḥ tad hi teṣām āpyāyanam somasyā apyāyanam iva upabhuñjata upakaraṇa bhūtān devāḥ teṣām karmiṇām yadā yasmin kāle tad yajña dāna ādi lakṣaṇam soma loka prāpakam karma paryavaiti parigacchati parikṣīyata iti arthaḥ atha tadā imam eva prasiddham ākāśam abhiniṣpadyante yāḥ tāḥ śraddhā śabda vācyā dyu loka agnau hutā āpaḥ soma ākāra pariṇatā yābhiḥ soma loke karmiṇām upabhogāya śarīram ārabdham ap mayam tāḥ karma kṣayāt himapiṇḍa ivā atapa saṃparkāt pravilīyante pravilīnāḥ sūkṣmā ākāśa bhūtā iva bhavanti tad idam ucyata imam eva aakāśam abhiniṣpadyanta iti te punar api karmiṇaḥ tad śarīrāḥ santaḥ purovāta ādinā itāḥ ca amutas ca nīyante antarikṣa gāḥ tad āha ākāśāt vāyum iti vāyoḥ vṛṣṭim pratipadyante tad uktam parjanya agnau somam rājānam juhvati iti tatas  vṛṣṭi bhūtā imām pṛthivīm patanti te pṛthivīm prāpya vrīhi yava ādi annam bhavanti tad uktam asmin  loke agnau vṛṣṭim juhvati tasyāḥ  āhutyā annam saṃbhavati iti te punar  puruṣa agnau hūyante anna bhūtā retaḥ sici tatas  retaḥ bhūtā yoṣa agnau hūyante tatas  jāyante lokam pratyutthāyinaḥ te lokam pratyuttiṣṭhantaḥ  agnihotra ādi karma anutiṣṭhanti tatas  dhūma ādinā punar  punar  soma lokam punar imam lokam iti ta evam karmiṇaḥ  anuparivartante ghaṭīyantravat cakrībhūtā baṃbhram anti iti arthaḥ uttara mārgāya sadyas muktaye vā yāvat brahma na viduḥ iti nu kāmayamānaḥ saṃsarati iti uktam atha punar ya uttaram dakṣiṇam ca etau panthānau na viduḥ uttarasya dakṣiṇasya vā pathaḥ pratipattaye jñānam karma vā na anutiṣṭhanti iti arthaḥ te kim bhavanti iti ucyate te kīṭāḥ pataṅgā yad idam yad ca idam dandaśūkam daṃśam aśakam iti etad bhavanti evam hi iyam saṃsāra gatiḥ kaṣṭa āsyām nimagnasya punar uddhāra eva durlabhaḥ tathā ca śruti antaram tāni imāni kṣudrāṇi asakṛt āvartīni bhūtāni bhavanti jāyasva mriyasva iti tasmāt sarva utsāhena yathāśakti svābhāvika karma jñāna hānena dakṣiṇa uttara mārga pratipatti sādhanam śāsrīyam karma jñānam vā anutiṣṭhet iti vākya arthaḥ tathā ca uktam atas  vai khalu durniṣprapataram tasmāt jugupseta iti śruti antarāt mokṣāya prayateta iti arthaḥ atra api uttara mārga pratipatti sādhana eva mahān yatnaḥ kartavya iti gamyate evam eva anuparivartanta iti ukta tvāt  evam praśnāḥ sarve nirṇītāḥ esau vai loka iti ārabhya puruṣaḥ saṃbhavati iti caturthaḥ praśnaḥ  yatithyām āhutyām ityādiḥ prathamyena pañcamaḥ tu dvitīya tvena deva yānasya vā pathaḥ pratipadam pitṛyāṇasya vā iti dakṣiṇa uttara mārga pratipatti sādhana kathanena tena eva ca prathamaḥ  api agneḥ ābhya kecid arciḥ pratipadyante kecid dhūmam iti vipratipattiḥ punarāvṛttiḥ ca dvitīyaḥ praśna ākāśa ādi krameṇa imam lokam āgacchanti iti tena eva asau lokaḥ  na saṃpūryate kīṭa pataṅga ādi pratipatteḥ ca keṣāñcid iti tṛtīyaḥ  api praśnaḥ  nirṇītaḥ sa yaḥ kāmayeta jñāna karmaṇoḥ gatiḥ uktā tatra jñānam svatantram karma tu daiva mānuṣa vitta dvaya āyattam tena karma artham vittam upārjanīyam tad ca apratyavāya kāriṇā upāyena iti tad artham mantha ākhyam karmā arabhyate mahattva prāptaye mahat tve ca satyartha siddham hi vittam tad ucyate sa yaḥ kāmayeta sa yaḥ  vitta arthī karmaṇi adhikṛtaḥ  yaḥ kāmayeta kim mahat mahat tvam prāpnuyām mahān syām iti iti arthaḥ tatra mantha karmaṇaḥ  vidhitsitasya kālaḥ  abhidhīyate udagayana ādityasya tatra sarvatra prāptau  āpūryamāṇa pakṣasya śukla pakṣasya tatra api sarvatra prāptau puṇya ahe anukūla ātmanaḥ karma siddhi kara iti arthaḥ dvādaśa aham yasmin puṇye anukūle karma cikīrṣati tatas  prāc puṇya aham evā arabhya dvādaśa aham upasadvratī upasatsu vratam upasadaḥ prasiddhā jyotiṣṭome tatra ca stana upacaya apacaya dvāreṇa payaḥ bhakṣaṇam tad vratam atra ca tad karma anupasaṃhārāt kevalam itikartavya tā śūnyam payaḥ bhakṣaṇa mātram upādīyate nanu upasadaḥ  vratam iti yadā vigrahaḥ tadā sarvam itikartavya tā rūpam grāhyam bhavati tad kasmāt na parigṛhyata iti ucyate smārta tvāt karmaṇaḥ smārtam hi idam mantha karma nanu śruti vihitam sat katham smārtam bhavitum arhati smṛti anuvādinīhi śrutiḥ iyam śrauta tve hi prakṛti vikāra bhāvaḥ tatas ca prākṛta dharma grāhi tvam vikāra karmaṇaḥ  na tu iha śrauta tvam ata eva cā avasathya agnau  etad karma vidhīyate sarvā cā avṛtsmārtā eva iti upasadvratī bhūtvā payaḥ vratī sannīti arthaḥ audumbara udumbara vṛkṣa maye kaṃse camase vā tasya eva viśeṣaṇam kaṃsa ākāre camasa ākāre vaudumbara eva ākāre tu vikalpaḥ  na audumbara tve etra sarva auṣadham sarvāsām oṣadhīnām samūham yathāsambhavam yathāśakti ca sarvā oṣadhīḥ samāhṛtya tatra grāmyāṇām tu daśa niyamena grāhyā vrīhi yava ādyā vakṣyamāṇāḥ adhika grahaṇe tu na doṣaḥ grāmyāṇām phalāni ca yathāsambhavam yathāśakti ca iti śabdaḥ samasta sambhāra upacaya pradarśana arthaḥ anyat api yad sambharaṇīyam tad sarvam saṃbhṛtya iti arthaḥ kramaḥ tatra gṛhya uktaḥ  draṣṭavyaḥ parisamūhana parilepane bhūmi saṃskāraḥ agnim upasamādhāya iti vacanāt āvasathye agnau  iti gamyate eka vacanāt upasamādhāna śravaṇāt ca vidyamānasya eva upasamādhānam paristīrya darbha anāvṛtā smārta tvāt karmaṇaḥ sthālīpāka āvṛt parigṛhyate tayā ajyam saṃskṛtya puṃsā nakṣatreṇa puṃnāmnā nakṣatreṇa puṇyāha saṃyuktena mantham sarva auṣadha phala piṣṭam tatra audumbare camase dadhani madhuni ghṛte ca upasicya ekayā upamanthanya upamaṃmathya saṃnīya madhye saṃsthāpya audumbareṇa sruveṇā avāpa sthāna ājyasya juhoti etaiḥ mantraiḥ yāvantaḥ  devāḥ  ityādyaiḥ jyeṣṭhāya svāhā śreṣṭhāya svāhā iti ārabhya dve dve āhutī hutvā manthe saṃsravam avanayati sruva avalepanam ājyam manthe saṃsrāvayati etasmāt eva jyeṣṭhāya śreṣṭhāya ityādi prāṇa liṅgāt jyeṣṭha śreṣṭha ādi prāṇa vida eva asmin karmaṇi adhikāraḥ retasa iti ārambha eka ekām āhutim hutvā manthe saṃsravam avanayati aparayā upamanthanyā punar mathnāti atha enam abhimṛśati bhramat asi iti anena mantreṇa atha enam ucchati saha pātreṇa haste gṛhṇāti ām aṃsya amaṃhi te mahi iti anena atha enam ācāmati bhakṣayati gāyatryāḥ prathama pādena madhumatyā ekayā vyāhṛtyā ca prathamayā prathama grāsam ācāmati tathā gāyatrī dvitīya pādena madhumatyā dvitīyayā dvitīya yā ca vyahṛtyā dvitīyam grāsam tathā tṛtīyena gāyatrī pādena tṛtīyayā madhumatyā tṛtīyayā ca vyāhṛtyā tṛtīyam grāsam sarvām sāvitrīm sarvāḥ ca madhumatīruktvā aham eva idam sarvam bhūyāsam iti ca ante bhūrbhavaḥ svar  svāhā iti samastam bhaśrayati yathā caturbhiḥ grāsaiḥ tad dravyam sarvam parisamāpyate tathā pūrvam eva nirupyet  yad pātra avaliptam tad pātram sarvam nirṇijya tūṣṇīm pivet  pāṇī prakṣālya apa ācamya jaghanena agnim paścāt agneḥ prāc śirāḥ saṃviśati prātar  saṃdhyām upāsyā adityam upatiṣṭhate diśām eka puṇḍarīkam iti anena mantreṇa yathetam yathāgatam etyā agatya jaghanena agnim āsīnaḥ  vaṃśam japati etam u ha eva vājasaneyaḥ  yājnavalkyaḥ  madhukāya paiṅgyāya antevāsina uktvā uvāca api ya enam śuṣke sthāṇau niṣiñcej jāyerañ chākhāḥ praroheyuḥ palāśāni iti bhrhūp etam u ha eva madhukaḥ paiṅgyaś cūlāya bhāga vittaye antevāsina uktvā uvāca api ya enam śuṣke sthāṇau niṣiñcej jāyerañ chākhāḥ praroheyuḥ palāśāni iti bhrhūp etam u ha eva cūlaḥ  bhāga vittiḥ  jānakaya āyaḥ sthūṇāya antevāsina uktvā uvāca api ya enam śuṣke sthāṇau niṣiñcej jāyerañ chākhāḥ praroheyuḥ palāśāni iti bhrhūp etam u ha eva jānakir āyasthūṇaḥ satyakāmāya jābālāya antevāsina uktvā uvāca api ya enam śuṣke sthāṇau niṣiñcej jāyerañ chākhāḥ praroheyuḥ palāśāni iti bhrhūp tam ha etam uddālaka ityādi satya kāmaḥ  jābālaḥ  antevāsibhya uktvā uvāca api ya enam śuṣke sthāṇau niṣiñcet jāyeran  eva asmin śākhāḥ praroheyuḥ palāśāni iti evam antam enam mantham uddālakāt prabhṛti ekaika ācārya krama āgatam satyakāma ācāryaḥ  bahubhyaḥ  antevāsibhya uktvā uvāca kim anyat uvāca iti ucyate api ya enam śuṣke sthāṇau gata prāṇe api enam mantham bhakṣaṇāya saṃskṛtam niṣiñcet prakṣipet jāyeu an  utpadyeran  eva asmin sthāṇau śākhā avayavā vṛkṣasya praroheyuḥ ca palāśāni parṇāni yathā jīvataḥ sthāṇoḥ kim uta anena karmaṇā kāmaḥ sidhyet iti dhruva phalam idam karma iti karma stuti artham etad  vidyā adhigame ṣṭa tīrthāni teṣām iha sa prāṇa darśanasya mantha vijñānasya adhigame dve eva tīrthe anujñāyete putraḥ ca antevāsī ca catur audumbaraḥ  bhavati iti vyākhyātam daśa grāmyāṇi bhavanti grāmyāṇām tu dhānyānām daśa niyamena grāhyā iti avocāma ke ta iti nirdiśyante vrīhi yavāḥ tila māṣā aṇu priyaṅgavaḥ  aṇavaḥ ca aṇu śabda vācyāḥ kvacid deśe priyaṅgavaḥ prasiddhāḥ kaṅgu śabdena khalvā niṣpāvā valla śabda vācyā loke khala kulāḥ kulatthāḥ etad vyatirekeṇa yathāśakti sarva auṣadha yaḥ grāhyāḥ phalāni ca iti avocāma aya ajñikāni varjayitvā sarvebhyaḥ  aṅgebhyaḥ tejaḥ saṃbhūtam iti śruti antarāt yata evam sarva bhūtānām sāratamam etad retaḥ  atas  kā nu khalu asya yogyā pratiṣṭhā iti sa ha sraṣṭā prajāpatiḥ ī kṣāñcake īkṣām kṛtvā sa sriyam sasṛje tām ca sṛṣṭvā adha upāsta maithuna ākhyam karma adhaupāsanam nāma kṛtavān tasmāt sriyam adha upāsīta śreṣṭha anuśrayaṇā hi prajāḥ atra vājapeya sāmānyakḷptim āha sa etam prāñcam prakṛṣṭa gati yuktam ātmanaḥ  grāvāṇam soma abhiṣava upala sthānīyam kāṭhinya sāmānyāt prajanana indriyam udapārayat utpūritavān srī vyañjanam prati tena enām sriyam abhyasṛjat abhisaṃsargam kṛtavān etad ha sma vai tad vidvān uddālaka āruṇirāha adhā upahāsa ākhyam maithuna karma vājapeya sampannam vidvān iti arthaḥ tathā nākaḥ maudgalyaḥ kumārahāritaḥ ca kim ta āhuḥ iti ujyate bahavaḥ  maryā maraṇa dharmiṇaḥ  manuṣyā brāhmaṇā ayanam yeṣām te brahmaṇā ayanā brahmabandhavaḥ  jāti mātra upajīvina iti etad  nirindriyā viśliṣṭa indriyā visukṛtaḥ  vigata sukṛta karmāṇaḥ  avidvāṃsau maithuna karma āsaktā iti arthaḥ te kim asmāt lokāt prayanti para lokāt paribhraṣṭā iti maithuna karmaṇaḥ  atyanta pāpa hetu tvam darśayati ya idam avidvāṃsaḥ  adhopahāsam caranti iti śrīmantham kṛtvā patnyā ṛtu kālam brahmacaryeṇa pratīkṣate yadi ida rataḥ skandati bahu vā alpam vā suptasya vā jāgrataḥ  vā rāga prābalyāt  etad ha sma vai tad vidvān uddālaka āruṇirāha adhā upahāsa ākhyam maithuna karma vājapeya sampannam vidvān iti arthaḥ tathā nākaḥ maudgālya kumārahāritaḥ ca kim ta āhuḥ iti ucyate bahavaḥ  maryā maraṇa dharmiṇaḥ  manuṣyā brāhmaṇā ayanam yeṣām te brāhmaṇāyanā brahmabandhavaḥ  jāti mātra upajīvina iti etad  nirindriyā viśilaṣṭa indriyā visukṛtaḥ  vigata sukṛta karmāṇaḥ  avidvāṃsau maithuna karma āsaktā iti arthaḥ te kim asmāt lokāt prayanti para lokāt paribhraṣṭā iti maithuna karmaṇaḥ  atyanta pāpa hetu tvam darśayati ya idam avidvāṃsaḥ  adhopahāsam caranti iti śrīmantham kṛtvā patnyā śratu kālam brahmacaryeṇa pratīkṣate yadi ida rataḥ skandati bahu vā alpam vā suptasya vā jāgrataḥ  vā rāga prābalyāt  tad abhimṛśet anumantrayeta vā anujapet iti arthaḥ yadā abhimṛśati tadā anāmikā aṅguṣṭhābhyām tad reta ādade iti evam antena mantreṇa punar mām iti etena nimṛjyāt antareṇa madhye bhruvau bhruveḥ vā stanau stanayoḥ vā atha yadi kadācid udaka ātmānam ātma  chāyām paśyet tatra api atri mantrayeta anena mantreṇa mayi teja iti śrīḥ ha vā eṣā patnā srīṇām madhye yadi asmāt mala udvāsā udgata malavat vāsāḥ tasmāt tām mala udvāsasam yaśasvinīm śrīmatīm abhikramya abhigatya upamantrayeta idam adyā avābhyām kāryam yad putra utpādanam iti tri rātra anta āplutām sā ced asmai na dadyāt maithunam kartum yad putra utpādanam iti tri rātra anta jñāpayet  tathā api sā na eva dadyāt kāmam enām yaṣṭyā vā pāṇinā vā upahatya atikrāmet maithunāya śāpsyāmi tvām durbhagām kariṣyāmi iti prakhyāpya tām anena mantreṇa upagacchet indriyeṇa te yaśasā yaśa ādada iti sā tasmāt tad abhiśāpāt vandhyā durbhagā iti khyātāyaśā eva bhavati sā ced asmai dadyāt anuguṇa eva syāt bhartuḥ tadā anena mantreṇa upagaccha indriyeṇa te yaśasā yaśa ādadhāmi iti tadā yaśasvinau  eva ubhau  api bhavataḥ sa yām sva bhāryām icchet iyam mām kāmayeta iti tasyām artham prajanana indriyam niṣṭhāya nikṣipya mukhena mukham saṃdhāya upastham asya abhimṛśya japet imam mantram aṅgāt aṅgāt iti atha yām icchet na garbham dadhīta na dhārayet garbhiṇī mā bhūt iti tasyām artham iti pūrvavat  abhiprāṇya abhiprāṇanam prathamam kṛtvā paścāt apānyāt indriyeṇa te retasā reta ādada iti anena mantreṇa āretā eva bhavati na garbhiṇī bhavati iti arthaḥ atha yām icchet dadhīta garbham iti tasyām artham ityādi pūrvavat  pūrva viparyayeṇa apānya abhiprāṇyāt indriyeṇa te retasā reta ādadhāmi iti garbhiṇī eva bhavati atha punar yasya jāyāyai jāra upapatiḥ syāt tam ced dviṣyāt abhicariṣyāmi enam iti manyeta tasya idam karma āma pātre agnim upasamādhāya sarvam pratilomam kuryāt tasmin  agnau  etāḥ śara bhṛṣṭīḥ śara iṣīkāḥ pratilomāḥ sarpiṣā aktā ghṛta abhyaktā juhuyāt mama samiddhe ahauṣīḥ iti ādyā āhutīrante sarvāsām asau  iti nāma grahaṇam pratyekam sa eṣa evaṃvidyā brāhmaṇaḥ śapati sa visukṛtaḥ  vigata puṇya karmā praiti tasmāt evaṃvid śrotrisya dāreṇa na upahāsam icchet narmā api na kuryāt kim uta adha upahāsam hi yasmāt evaṃvid api tāvat paraḥ  bhavati śatruḥ bhavati iti arthaḥ atha yasya jāyām ārtavam vindet ṛtu bhāvam prāpnuyāt iti evamādi granthaḥ śrīḥ ha vā eṣā srīṇām iti atas  pūrvam draṣṭavyaḥ sāmarthyāt  tri aham kaṃsena pibet ahata vāsāḥ ca syāt  na enām snātām asnātām ca vṛṣalaḥ  vṛṣalī vā na upahanyāt na upaspṛśet  tri rātra ante tri rātra vrata samāptau  āplutya snātvā hata vāsā syāt iti vyavahitena saṃbandhaḥ tām āplutām vrīhīn avaghātayet vrīhi avaghātāya tām eva viniyuñjyāt  sa ya icchet putraḥ  me śuklaḥ  varṇataḥ  jāyeta vedam ekam anubruvīta sarvam āyuḥ iyāt varṣa śatam kṣīra odanam pācayitvā sarpiṣmantam aśnīyātām āśvarau samarthau janayitavai janayitum dadhi odanam dadhnā carum pācayitvā dvidevam ced icchati putram tadā evam aśana niyamaḥ kevalam eva svābhāvikam odanam udagrahaṇam anya prasaṅga nivṛtti atham duhituḥ pāṇḍityam gṛha tantra viṣayam eva vede anadhikārāt  tila odanam kṛtaram vividham gītaḥ  vigītaḥ prakhyāta iti arthaḥ samitiṅgamaḥ sabhām gacchati iti pragalbha iti arthaḥ pāṇḍityasya pṛthak grahaṇāt  śuśrūṣitām śrotum iṣṭām ramaṇīyām vācam bhāṣitā saṃskṛtāyāḥ  arthavatyā vācaḥ  bhāṣitā iti arthaḥ māṃsa miśram odanam māṃsa odanam tad māṃsa niyama artham āha aukṣem vā māṃsena ukṣā secana samarthaḥ puṅgavaḥ tadīyam māṃsam ṛṣabhaḥ tatas  api adhikavayāḥ tadīyam ārṣabham māṃsam atha āmi prātar eva kāle avaghāta nirvṛttān  taṇḍulān ādāya sthālī pāka āvṛtā sthālīpāka vidhinā ajyam ceṣṭitvā ajya saṃskāram kṛtvā carum śrapayitvā sthālī pākasya āahutīḥ juhoti upaghātam upahatya upahatya agnaye svāhā ityādyāḥ gārhyaḥ sarvaḥ  vidhiḥ draṣṭavyaḥ  atra hutvā uddhṛtya caru śeṣam prāśnāti svayam prāśya itarasyāḥ patnyai prayacchati ucchiṣṭam prakṣālya pāṇī ācamya uda pātram pūrayitvā tena udakena enām tris abhyukṣatyena mantreṇa uttiṣṭhāta iti sakṛt mantra uccāraṇam atha enām abhimantrya kṣīra odana ādi yathā apatya kāmam bhuktvā iti kramaḥ  draṣṭavyaḥ saṃveśana kāle amaḥ  aham asmi ityādi mantreṇa abhipadyate atha asya ūrū vihāpayati vijihīthām dyāvāpṛthivī iti anena tasyām artham ityādi pūrvavat  tris ena am śiraḥ prabhṛti anulomām anumārṣṭi viṣṇuḥ yonim ityādi pratimantram ante nāma gṛhṇāti asau  iti tasyāḥ soṣyantīm adbhiḥ abhyukṣati prasava kāle sukha prasavana artham anena mantreṇa yathā vāyuḥ puṣkariṇīm samiṅgayati sarvatas  eva te garbha ejatu iti atha jātakarma jāte agnim upasamādhāya aṅka  ādhāya putram kaṃse pṛṣadājyam saṃmīya saṃyojya dadhi ghṛte pṛṣadājyasya upaghātam juhoti asmin sahasram iti ādi āvāpa sthāne atha asya dakṣiṇam karṇam abhinidhāya svam mukham vāc vāk iti tris japet  atha dadhi madhu ghṛtam saṃnīya anantarhitena avyavahitena jātarūpeṇa hiraṇyena prāśayati etaiḥ mantraiḥ pratyekam atha asya nāmadheyam karoti vedaḥ  asi iti tad asya tad guhyam nāma bhavati veda iti atha enam mātre pradāya sva aṅka stham stanam prayacchati yaḥ te stana ityādi mantreṇa atha asya mātaram abhimantrayata ilā asi iti anena tam vā etam āhuḥ iti anena vidhinā jātaḥ putraḥ pitaram pitāmaham ca atiśeta iti śriyā yaśasā brahmavarcasena paramām niṣṭhām prāpat iti evam stutyaḥ  bhavati iti arthaḥ yasya ca evaṃvidaḥ  brāhmaṇasya putraḥ  jāyate sa ca evam bhavati iti adhyāhāryam atha idānīm samasta pravacana vaṃśaḥ srīprādhānyāt  guṇavān putraḥ  bhavati iti prastutam atas  srī viśeṣaṇena eva putra viśeṣaṇāt ācārya paramparā kīrtyate tāni imāni śuklāni iti avyāmiśrāṇi brāhmaṇena athavā yāni imāni yajūṃṣi tānī śuklāni śuddhāni iti etad  prajāpatim ārabhya yāvat pautimāṣī putraḥ tāvat adhomukhaḥ  niyata ācārya pūrva kramaḥ  vaṃśaḥ samāna māsāṃjīvīputrāt  brahmaṇaḥ pravacana ākhyasya tad ca etad brahma
